### [1] [Dissipation-Selected Resonant Fronts in a Driven-Dissipative Bose-Hubbard Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21900)
*Wei-Guo Ma,Heng Fan*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过广义Gross-Pitaevskii模拟，证明在二维驱动-耗散Bose-Hubbard晶格中，结构化的空间耗散梯度与Stark诱导失谐斜坡结合，可以产生非线性共振切片并形成钉扎密度前沿。该前沿表现出Airy-like宽度标度，且通过调节共振条件可实现Peierls-Nabarro脱钉、离散横向模式锁定、时空混沌和最小损耗局域化等丰富动力学相行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索超越哈密顿量控制（Hamiltonian control）的驱动量子物质组织方式，即利用结构化耗散（structured dissipation）作为可重构输运势垒和非平衡界面（nonequilibrium interfaces）的调控机制。

Method: 在二维驱动-耗散Bose-Hubbard晶格模型中，施加耗散梯度（dissipation gradient）与Stark诱导失谐斜坡（Stark-induced detuning ramp），并通过广义Gross-Pitaevskii方程进行数值模拟。利用质心（center-of-mass）和广义不平衡度（generalized-imbalance）诊断量绘制动力学相图（dynamical phase diagram）。

Result: 耗散梯度与失谐斜坡的结合在晶格中选出非线性共振切片（nonlinear resonance slice），产生钉扎密度前沿（pinned density front）；前沿位置由共振条件固定，其Airy-like剖面的宽度标度由隧穿刚度（tunneling stiffness）和有效失谐斜率（effective detuning slope）决定。调节共振至最小损耗侧可产生Peierls-Nabarro脱钉步骤、离散横向模式锁定、时空混沌和最小损耗局域化等动力学现象。

Conclusion: 结构化耗散可作为可编程玻色晶格（programmable bosonic lattices）中可重构输运势垒和非平衡界面的有效控制机制，为超越传统哈密顿量框架的量子物质组织提供新途径。

Abstract: Spatially structured dissipation organizes driven quantum matter beyond Hamiltonian control. We show that a dissipation gradient combined with a Stark-induced detuning ramp selects a nonlinear resonance slice in a two-dimensional driven-dissipative Bose-Hubbard lattice, producing a pinned density front in generalized Gross-Pitaevskii simulations. The underlying resonance condition fixes the front position, while its Airy-like profile obeys a width scaling set by tunneling stiffness and the effective detuning slope. Treating the front as an emergent interface explains how tuning the selected resonance toward the minimum-loss side yields Peierls-Nabarro depinning steps, discrete transverse pattern locking, spatiotemporal chaos, and minimum-loss localization. Center-of-mass and generalized-imbalance diagnostics map these outcomes into a dynamical phase diagram as detuning-ramp slope and dissipation-gradient strength vary. The results suggest structured dissipation as a mechanism for reconfigurable transport barriers and nonequilibrium interfaces in programmable bosonic lattices.

</details>


### [2] [Multipolar exchange in a many-body homonuclear mixture of atoms in different internal states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22375)
*M. Bulakhov,A. S. Peletminskii,Yu. V. Slyusarenko*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一种通用方法，用于构建描述占据不同总角动量或量子数的同核原子混合物的多体哈密顿量（many-body Hamiltonian），并利用不可约球张量算符（irreducible spherical tensor operator）形式使其具有显式的物理结构，涵盖所有散射通道和多极交换相互作用（multipolar exchange interactions）。该哈密顿量为研究玻色和费米原子气体中的多种量子多体现象提供了统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构建一个通用的多体哈密顿量，以统一描述占据不同总角动量或其他量子数的同核原子混合物中的成对相互作用，并克服现有形式无法显式体现物理结构、涵盖所有散射通道的局限。

Method: 采用不可约球张量算符（irreducible spherical tensor operator）形式体系，构造描述同核原子混合物的成对相互作用的多体哈密顿量。该形式可显式赋予哈密顿量物理结构，涵盖所有散射通道，并包含对应于角动量投影和总角动量交换的多极交换相互作用（multipolar exchange interactions）。

Result: 得到的哈密顿量是一个通用框架，能够描述玻色和费米原子气体中的多种量子多体现象。此外，该工作还分析了该通用哈密顿量在超冷气体（ultracold gases）物理中常用的若干具体实现形式。

Conclusion: 该通用哈密顿量框架为研究玻色和费米原子气体中广泛的量子多体现象提供了统一的理论基础。

Abstract: We develop a general method for constructing the many-body Hamiltonian of pairwise interactions describing homonuclear mixtures of atoms occupying states with different total angular momenta or other quantum numbers. The advantage of the irreducible spherical tensor operator formalism is demonstrated: these operators give the Hamiltonian an explicit physical structure, account for all scattering channels, and include multipolar exchange interactions. The latter correspond to the exchange of both angular-momentum projections and the total angular momentum. Particular realizations of the general Hamiltonian, widely used in the physics of ultracold gases, are also analyzed. The resulting Hamiltonian provides a universal framework for investigating a broad range of quantum many-body phenomena in bosonic and fermionic atomic gases.

</details>


### [3] [Interaction-enabled metal-insulator phase transition in a driven quantum gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22449)
*Camilo Cantillano,Karthick Ramanathan,Zekai Chen,Ang Yang,Emilio Aguilera-Valdes,Lei Ying,Manuele Landini,Hanns-Christoph Nägerl,Yanliang Guo*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文在三维驱动量子气体中，通过可调相互作用实验揭示了局域化与扩散能量吸收之间的尖锐动力学边界，绘制了局域化-退局域化相图，并观察到多体动力学局域化（MBDL）、亚扩散输运及经典扩散行为，展示了一种由相互作用驱动的Floquet多体系统中的动力学相变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 相互作用通常促进遍历性（ergodicity）和扩散行为，但量子干涉（quantum interference）可抑制输运和能量吸收。两者如何竞争是一个基础性未解问题。本文旨在通过实验研究相互作用与量子相干性在周期性驱动系统（periodically driven system）中的竞争机制。

Method: 实验采用具有可调相互作用（tunable interactions）的三维（3D）驱动量子气体。通过调控驱动振幅（driving amplitude）和相互作用强度，结合有限时间标度分析（finite-time scaling）表征局域化-退局域化边界，并测量动量空间中的输运行为。

Result: 发现在参数空间中存在一个尖锐的动力学边界（dynamical boundary），分离局域化与扩散能量吸收。在绝缘侧观察到宽参数范围内的多体动力学局域化（many-body dynamical localization, MBDL），动量空间中输运被抑制。接近边界时输运变为亚扩散（subdiffusive），而在退局域化区域观察到经典扩散（classical diffusion），呈现出金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator transition）。

Conclusion: 该结果展示了一个封闭Floquet多体系统（Floquet many-body system）中由相互作用驱动的动力学相变（dynamical phase transition），阐明了相干性与相互作用如何共同主导量子到经典（quantum-to-classical）的转变。

Abstract: Particle transport and energy flow are central for our understanding of a wealth of phenomena in physics and the natural sciences. Interactions are generically expected to promote ergodicity and diffusive behavior, yet quantum interference can arrest transport and prevent energy absorption, defying classical expectations. How interactions and quantum coherence compete remains a fundamental open question. Here, we experimentally investigate their interplay in a periodically driven, three-dimensional (3D) quantum gas with tunable interactions. Strikingly, we find that interactions give rise to a sharp dynamical boundary that separates localization from diffusive energy absorption. By tuning the driving amplitude and interaction strength, we map the localization-delocalization phase diagram and characterize the boundary via finite-time scaling. On the insulating side, we observe many-body dynamical localization (MBDL) for a wide range of parameters, finding arrested transport in momentum space. Near the boundary, transport becomes subdiffusive, whereas in the delocalized regime we observe classical diffusion, yielding a metal-insulator transition that we interpret in terms of localization in many-body Hilbert space. Our results exemplify an interaction-enabled dynamical phase transition in a closed Floquet many-body system and clarify how coherence and interactions jointly govern the quantum-to-classical transition.

</details>


<div id='hep-ex'></div>

# hep-ex [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Patch Hierarchical Attention Transformer for Efficient Particle Jet Tagging](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21789)
*Aaron Wang,Zihan Zhao,Alan Xia,Chang Sun,Abhijith Gandrakota,Jennifer Ngadiuba,Richard Cavanaugh,Javier Duarte*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种面向实时触发系统（trigger system）的喷注标记（jet tagging）模型 PHAT-JeT（Patch Hierarchical Attention Transformer），通过结合物理启发的几何消息传递模块与分层补丁注意力机制，在严格计算预算下实现了比现有高效 Transformer 变体更优的分类精度与背景抑制能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型强子对撞机（Large Hadron Collider）的实时触发系统对延迟（latency）与精度有严格限制，但 Transformer 架构的二次自注意力（quadratic self-attention）计算成本过高，无法直接部署；现有高效变体虽降低计算开销，却牺牲了分类性能。

Method: PHAT-JeT 包含两种核心机制：(1) 物理启发的几何消息传递模块（geometric message-passing module），用于编码探测器平面上的局部结构；(2) 分层补丁注意力机制（hierarchical patch-based attention），在小型粒子组内计算精确注意力，并通过轻量级补丁令牌通信保留全局上下文。

Result: 在 hls4ml、JetClass、Top Tagging 和 Quark–Gluon 四个基准数据集上，PHAT-JeT 在资源受限预算下均达到了所有现有资源约束喷注标记模型中最优的分类精度（state-of-the-art accuracy）与背景抑制（background rejection）。

Conclusion: PHAT-JeT 证明在严格推理预算下，通过物理先验与高效注意力设计的结合，可以在不牺牲性能的前提下实现实时喷注标记，为高吞吐量探测器触发系统提供了可行的深度学习方案。

Abstract: Real-time jet tagging is critical for identifying short-lived particle decays in the high-throughput detectors of the Large Hadron Collider, where real-time trigger systems responsible for deciding which collision events to store impose strict latency and accuracy constraints. While transformer architectures achieve the highest jet tagging accuracy when compute is unconstrained, their quadratic self-attention cost makes inference restrictive on trigger budget. Existing efficient variants reduce the computational cost, but hinder the classification performance. To address this limitation, we introduce the Patch Hierarchical Attention Transformer (PHAT-JeT), which combines two mechanisms: a physics-inspired geometric message-passing module that encodes local detector-plane structure, and a hierarchical patch-based attention scheme that computes exact attention within small particle groups while preserving global context through lightweight patch-token communication. Within a restricted budget, PHAT-JeT achieves state-of-the-art accuracy and background rejection among all resource-constrained jet tagging models on four benchmarks (\textsc{hls4ml}, JetClass, Top Tagging, and Quark--Gluon). Our code is available at https://github.com/aaronw5/PHAT-JeT.

</details>


### [5] [Measurements of the absolute branching fractions of $D^0\toγ\bar K^{*0}$ and $D^0\toγφ$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22670)
*BESIII Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 基于BESIII探测器在质心能量3.773 GeV处收集的20.3 fb⁻¹正负电子对撞数据，首次测量了辐射衰变D⁰→γK̄*⁰和D⁰→γφ的绝对分支比，分别为(3.81±0.18_stat.±0.20_syst.)×10⁻⁴和(2.51±0.44_stat.±0.11_syst.)×10⁻⁵，统计显著性分别为26.8σ和7.9σ，且CP不对称性测量结果与CP守恒一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 首次对D⁰介子辐射衰变D⁰→γK̄*⁰和D⁰→γφ的绝对分支比进行实验测量，为检验标准模型（Standard Model）和寻找超出标准模型的新物理（new physics）提供关键输入。

Method: 基于BESIII探测器在质心能量（center-of-mass energy）3.773 GeV处采集的20.3 fb⁻¹正负电子对撞（e⁺e⁻ annihilation）数据，通过分析辐射衰变过程进行绝对分支比测量。

Result: D⁰→γK̄*⁰和D⁰→γφ的绝对分支比分别为(3.81±0.18_stat.±0.20_syst.)×10⁻⁴和(2.51±0.44_stat.±0.11_syst.)×10⁻⁵，统计显著性分别为26.8σ和7.9σ。CP不对称性（CP asymmetry）ACP(D⁰→γK̄*⁰)=(-0.7±5.0_stat.±4.1_syst.)%与CP守恒（CP conservation）一致。

Conclusion: 测得分支比与世界平均值（world average values）相符，CP不对称性测量未发现CP破坏（CP violation）迹象，结果支持标准模型预测。

Abstract: By analyzing a sample of 20.3 fb$^{-1}$ of $e^+e^-$ annihilation data collected at the center-of-mass energy of 3.773~GeV with the BESIII detector, we have made a first measurement of the absolute branching fractions of the radiative decays $D^0\toγ\bar K^{*0}$ and $D^0\toγφ$ to be $(3.81 \pm 0.18_{\rm stat.} \pm 0.20_{\rm syst.})\times 10^{-4}$ and $(2.51 \pm 0.44_{\rm stat.} \pm 0.11_{\rm syst.})\times 10^{-5}$, respectively.
  The statistical significances of $D^0\toγ\bar K^{*0}$ and $D^0\toγφ$ are $26.8σ$ and $7.9σ$, respectively. The obtained branching fractions are consistent with the corresponding world average values. In addition, the measured $C\!P$ asymmetry $\mathcal{A}_{C\!P}(D^0\toγ\bar K^{*0})=(-0.7\pm5.0_{\rm stat.} \pm4.1_{\rm syst.})\%$ is consistent with $C\!P$ conservation.

</details>


### [6] [New constraints on physics within and beyond the standard model from the latest CONUS datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22815)
*N. Ackermann,H. Bonet,A. Bonhomme,C. Buck,1 K. Fülber,J. Hakenmüller,J. Hempfling,G. Heusser,T. Hugle,M. Lindner,W. Maneschg,S. Mertens,K. Ni,D. Piani,M. Rank,T. Rink,E. Sanchez Garcia,I. Stalder,H. Strecker,R. Wink,J. Woenckhaus*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: CONUS合作组利用反应堆反中微子（antineutrino）在德国布罗克多夫和瑞士莱布施塔特两座核电站的观测数据，将相干弹性中微子-核散射（CEνNS）确立为标准模型（SM）内外的研究工具。实验在莱布施塔特站点以3.7σ的显著性观测到CEνNS信号，与SM预言吻合。基于完整系统误差的分析，研究改进了中微子磁矩（μ_ν<5.18·10⁻¹¹μ_B）和毫电荷（q_ν<1.76·10⁻¹²e₀）的极限，将新物理标度提升至Λ_NSI=145 GeV，并将轻新中介子的耦合下限压低至4·10⁻⁷（90%置信度）。此外，利用CEνNS和反应堆反中微子确定的温伯格角（Weinberg angle）在动量转移约10 MeV下给出sin²θ_W=0.28⁺⁰·⁰³₋₀.₀₄。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CEνNS已成为超出标准模型（BSM）物理探索的重要工具。CONUS实验通过在紧凑屏蔽中近距离运行锗半导体探测器，旨在利用反应堆反中微子高精度测量CEνNS信号，并以此约束中微子磁矩、毫电荷、非标准相互作用（NSIs）以及新轻中介子等新物理参数。

Method: CONUS实验使用在布罗克多夫和莱布施塔特核电站反应堆附近紧凑屏蔽内的锗半导体探测器（Germanium semiconductor detectors）收集数据。分析利用实验分析框架，合并了布罗克多夫站点的最后数据集与莱布施塔特站点的首批数据，并将完整系统误差纳入结果。

Result: 在莱布施塔特站点以3.7σ显著性观测到CEνNS信号，与SM预言一致。中微子磁矩上限改进至μ_ν<5.18·10⁻¹¹μ_B，中微子毫电荷上限改进至q_ν<1.76·10⁻¹²e₀（90%置信度）。NSIs相关新物理标度提升至Λ_NSI=145 GeV，轻新中介子的耦合下限降至4·10⁻⁷（90%置信度）。温伯格角在动量转移约10 MeV下确定为sin²θ_W=0.28⁺⁰·⁰³₋₀.₀₄。

Conclusion: CONUS合作组通过最新数据进一步巩固了CEνNS作为标准模型内外物理研究工具的地位。改进后的新物理约束显著收紧了中微子磁矩、毫电荷、NSIs及新轻中介子参数空间，并在低动量转移区域提供了温伯格角的测量值。

Abstract: Its detections with pion-decay-at-rest, solar and recently with reactor antineutrinos by the CONUS collaboration render coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering (CE$ν$NS) an established tool for investigations within and beyond the Standard Model (SM). The CONUS experiment located at the nuclear power plants in Brokdorf (Germany) and Leibstadt (Switzerland) operates Germanium semiconductor detectors in a compact shield at close distance to the reactor core. An observation with $3.7 σ$ significance is reported at the Leibstadt site, showing good agreement with its SM prediction. Physics investigations performed with the last datasets collected at the Brokdorf reactor and with the first data obtained at the Leibstadt site are summarized. By using the experimental analysis framework, the presented results contain the full systematics that underlie the experiment. Previously determined limits with neutrino-electron scattering on the neutrino magnetic moment and a neutrino millicharge are improved to $μ_ν <5.18\cdot 10^{-11}μ_\mathrm{B}$ and $q_ν<1.76\cdot 10^{-12} e_0$ (90% C.L). Further, the scale of new physics related to NSIs is improved to $Λ_{\rm NSI}$=145 GeV and limits on the coupling of light new mediators are lowered down to $4 \cdot 10^{-7}$ (90% C.L.) with the new data. Finally, the determination of the Weinberg angle with CE$ν$NS and reactor antineutrinos yields $\sin^{2}θ_W= 0.28^{+0.03}_{-0.04}$ at a momentum transfer of $\sim 10 \ \mathrm{MeV}$.

</details>


<div id='quant-ph'></div>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [7] [Journey in quantum metrology and sensing from foundations to applications: a review](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21702)
*Priya Ghosh,Tanoy Kanti Konar,Debraj Rakshit,Aditi Sen De,Ujjwal Sen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了量子计量学（quantum metrology）与量子传感（quantum sensing）领域，涵盖其理论基础、参数估计方法、不同编码过程与估计策略，以及多种物理平台上的应用与实验实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子计量学旨在利用量子效应（如纠缠、压缩）超越经典测量精度极限（即标准量子极限）。本文旨在对该领域进行系统性综述，整合从基础理论到前沿应用的最新进展。

Method: 综述涵盖了频率学派（frequentist）与贝叶斯（Bayesian）两种参数估计方法；单参数与多参数估计；通过酉信道（unitary channels）与噪声信道（noisy channels）、量子测温（quantum thermometry）及因果序不确定（indefinite causal order）通道等不同编码过程进行估计；以及量子纠错（quantum error correction）辅助方法、储层工程（reservoir engineering）等估计策略。此外还讨论了量子Fisher信息（quantum Fisher information）在资源探测中的作用。

Result: 该综述展示了量子计量学在量子多体传感器（quantum many-body sensors）、原子系综传感协议、原子-光子与连续变量系统、量子成像（quantum imaging）、量子照明（quantum illumination）、原子钟（atomic clocks）与原子干涉仪（atom interferometry）等多个领域的应用，并在不同物理平台上实现了量子传感器的实验验证。

Conclusion: 量子计量学与量子传感已从理论基础走向广泛的应用与实验实现，持续推动测量精度的前沿突破，在诸多物理系统中展现出重要应用前景。

Abstract: We present a review on quantum metrology and sensing, from its foundations to current applications. Highlights of the review include consideration of both frequentist and Bayesian approaches to parameter estimation; single as well as multiparameter estimation; estimation for different encoding processes comprising unitary as well as noisy channels, quantum thermometry, and channels involving indefinite causal order; different estimation strategies incorporating also recent advances like quantum error correction-aided methods and reservoir engineering; usefulness of quantum Fisher information to detect resources; applications of quantum metrology in diverse arenas covering quantum many-body sensors, sensing protocols in atomic ensembles, atom-photon systems, and continuous-variable systems, quantum imaging, quantum illumination, atomic clocks and atom interferometry, etc; and experimental realizations of quantum sensors in different physical platforms.

</details>


### [8] [What We Talk About When We Talk About Dissipative Quantum Chaos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21628)
*Lucas Sá,Pedro Ribeiro,Sergey Denisov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了耗散量子混沌（dissipative quantum chaos）理论的发展历程、基础原理与近期进展。该理论将传统哈密顿量子混沌（Hamiltonian quantum chaos）的思想与方法从相干演化扩展到开放量子动力学（open quantum dynamics），并基于开放系统演化算符的谱性质（spectral properties）来区分混沌系统与可积系统，近十年来该领域获得了显著发展并开始得到实验验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统哈密顿量子混沌局限于相干演化，无法描述开放量子系统中的耗散与非平衡动力学。因此需要发展一套新理论，将混沌的概念、思想和方法学推广到开放量子系统，以区分混沌开放系统与可积开放系统，并提供混沌性（chaoticity）的定量度量。

Method: 该理论继承哈密顿量子混沌的路线，基于开放量子演化算符（如林德布拉德超算符，Lindbladian superoperator）的谱性质，通过分析特征值统计分布等方法来判定系统是否混沌。作者通过综述近年大量理论工作与近期实验验证，梳理了该领域的基础框架和最新进展。

Result: 该理论于20世纪80年代末奠定基础，随后经历了较长的沉寂期，近十年来相关出版物大幅增加，理论预测也已首次获得实验检验，表明耗散量子混沌正在成为一门活跃的学科。

Conclusion: 耗散量子混沌作为新兴理论，成功将量子混沌的核心理念从封闭系统拓展至开放系统，近期的实验验证进一步增强了其可信度，未来有望成为理解开放量子系统复杂动力学的重要工具。

Abstract: Dissipative quantum chaos is an emerging theory that is expected to extend the ideas, concepts, and methodology of conventional Hamiltonian quantum chaos from coherent evolution to open quantum dynamics. The new theory should provide a set of tools to distinguish chaotic open quantum systems from integrable ones, as well as quantitative measures of their chaoticity (or, conversely, integrability). The foundations of this theory were laid in the late 1980s, and from the very start it was clear that, like its Hamiltonian predecessor, it had to be based on the spectral properties of the operators governing open quantum evolution. After these first steps, the field remained relatively quiet for many years and it is only over the last decade that the development of dissipative quantum chaos has received a strong boost, as confirmed by a large number of publications on this topic and, very recently, the first experiments performed to test its theoretical predictions. In this chapter, we review these recent developments and outline the basic foundations of dissipative quantum chaos.

### [9] [Completeness of the Klein-Gordon oscillator eigenfunctions via Hermite and Laguerre polynomials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21791)
*Kevin Hernández*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了Klein-Gordon谐振子（Klein-Gordon oscillator）本征函数在一维和三维空间中的完备性，基于Hermite多项式、广义Laguerre多项式以及球谐函数的完备性建立了闭包关系。与Dirac谐振子相比，论证因Klein-Gordon场的标量性质而更为简洁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 证明Klein-Gordon谐振子本征函数的完备性（completeness），填补该领域中尚未严格论证的空白。

Method: 通过建立本征函数满足的闭包关系（closure relations），利用Hermite多项式（Hermite polynomials）和广义Laguerre多项式（generalized Laguerre polynomials）的标准性质；在三维情形中额外依赖球谐函数（spherical harmonics）的完备性。

Result: 成功证明了一维和三维空间中Klein-Gordon谐振子本征函数的完备性。

Conclusion: Klein-Gordon场的标量性质使得该完备性证明比Dirac谐振子的对应证明更为简洁，无需进行非对角相消（off-diagonal cancellation）操作。

Abstract: Completeness of the Klein--Gordon oscillator eigenfunctions is proved in one and three spatial dimensions. The proofs establish the closure relations satisfied by the eigenfunctions and are based on standard properties of the Hermite and the generalized Laguerre polynomials, supplemented in three dimensions by the completeness of the spherical harmonics. The scalar nature of the Klein--Gordon field renders the argument strictly simpler than the analogous proof for the Dirac oscillator: no off-diagonal cancellation is required.

### [10] [Long-range nonstabilizerness of topologically encoded states from mutual information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22424)
*David Aram Korbany,Tyler D. Ellison,David T. Stephen,Lorenzo Piroli*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究长程非稳定子性（long-range nonstabilizerness, LRN），即用浅层局域量子电路无法消除的非稳定子性质。在二维拓扑有序系统的环面晶格模型中，通过分析非重叠区域（含非收缩环）的互信息（mutual information）及其在模变换下的变化来诊断LRN。以环面码（toric code）和非阿贝尔弦网模型（string-net model with doubled Fibonacci topological order）为例，发现互信息在环面码中能完全分类所有编码非稳定子态的LRN，但在非阿贝尔模型中仅能排除具有特殊模群变换性质的有穷子集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对一维系统中互信息（mutual information）已被证明是诊断LRN的有效工具，本文将其推广到二维拓扑有序系统的编码态，探索互信息是否能作为二维情形下LRN的诊断依据。

Method: 在环面（torus）上的晶格模型中，分析包含非收缩环（non-contractible loops）的非重叠区域之间的互信息，以及该互信息在模空间实空间变换（modular real-space transformations）下的变化，以此诊断LRN。

Result: 在环面码中，互信息提供了完全分类，能够认证所有编码非稳定子态（non-stabilizer states）的LRN；在双斐波那契拓扑序的非阿贝尔弦网模型中，互信息能检测除具有特殊模群（modular group）变换性质的有穷子集之外的所有态的LRN。

Conclusion: 本文关于LRN的结果约束了在环面上能够容错实现（fault-tolerantly implemented）的逻辑门（logical gates）。

Abstract: We study long-range nonstabilizerness (LRN), namely the obstruction to remove nonstabilizerness with shallow-depth local quantum circuits. In one-dimensional settings, the mutual information between disconnected spatial regions has proven to be a powerful tool to diagnose LRN. In this work, we focus on encoded states of two-dimensional topologically-ordered systems, and explore the ability of the mutual information to serve as a diagnostic of LRN. Focusing on the concrete setting of lattice models defined on a torus, we show that information about LRN can be gained from the analysis of the mutual information between non-overlapping regions containing non-contractible loops, and of the change of such mutual information under modular real-space transformations. We exemplify this idea in the toric code and the non-abelian string-net model with doubled Fibonacci topological order. In the former case, we show that the mutual information provides a full classification, certifying LRN for all encoded non-stabilizer states. In the latter case, instead, our approach does not lead to a full classification, as it detects LRN for all states except from a finite subset with special transformation properties under the modular group. Finally, we discuss how our results on LRN constrain the logical gates that can be implemented fault-tolerantly on the torus.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过将问题约化为一个无线性跳跃项的离散晶格模型，利用非线性相互作用（nonlinear interactions）来驱动模式的动力学行为；特别地，研究了对应Gross-Pitaevskii方程呼吸子解的二聚体模式族。

Result: 在负散射长度（negative scattering lengths）条件下，呼吸子表现为稳定；而在正散射长度（positive scattering lengths）且非线性较弱到中等强度时，也能观察到呼吸子的局域化（localization）和稳定传播。

Conclusion: 准周期势中的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体可以在无线性跳跃的情况下，仅通过非线性相互作用支持稳定的呼吸子模式，其稳定性取决于散射长度的符号和非线性强度。

Abstract: A quasi-one-dimensional Bose-Einstein condensate loaded into a quasi-periodic potential created by two sub-lattices of comparable amplitudes and incommensurate periods is considered. Although the conventional tight-binding approximation is not applicable in this setting, the description can still be reduced to a discrete model that accounts for the modes below the mobility edge. In the respective discrete lattice, where no linear hopping exists, solutions and their dynamics are governed solely by nonlinear interactions. Families of nonlinear modes, including those with no linear limit, are described with a special focus on dimers, which correspond to breather solutions of the Gross-Pitaevskii equation with a quasi-periodic potential. The breathers are found to be stable for negative scattering lengths. Localization and stable propagation of breathers are also observed for positive scattering lengths at relatively weak and moderate nonlinearities.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用分束器（beamsplitter）将调制激光探针制备成两个叠加分支，使其在 pancake 状玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的两个不同位置相交，然后通过另一个分束器重新合束。对其中一个输出进行外差探测（heterodyning），通过差拍光电流功率谱（difference photocurrent power spectrum）提取响应函数。使用压缩光以超越标准量子极限运行。

Conclusion: 该方案为在实验室中实验验证相对论性量子场中位置叠加态探测器的响应提供了可行路径，且压缩光技术能够有效提升信号提取质量。

Abstract: We propose a realizable experiment to test the response of a particle detector prepared in a superposition of locations interacting with a relativistic quantum field. Using a beamsplitter to prepare two superposed branches of a modulated laser probe, these branches are directed to intersect a pancake-shaped Bose-Einstein condensate at two separate locations. The branches are then recombined with another beamsplitter. Heterodyning one of the outputs, the response function corresponding to an Unruh-deWitt detector in a superposition of locations interacting with a (2+1)-dimensional massless scalar field is shown to appear in the difference photocurrent power spectrum. Operating beyond the standard quantum limit using squeezed light, we estimate the signal-to-noise ratio $SNR\gtrsim 10$ for extracting the response function over a broad set of baseband frequencies.

Abstract: We introduce a matrix product operator (MPO) encoding of the Magnus expansion and the Dyson series for one-dimensional quantum lattice models with time-dependent Hamiltonians. The MPO construction can be made accurate up to arbitrary order in the time step, it can be applied to both finite and infinite systems, and it can handle long-range interactions. The resulting MPO can be combined with state-of-the-art time evolution algorithms based on matrix product states, allowing for drastic improvements in simulating evolution under time-dependent Hamiltonians. Our MPO construction can also be used for the optimization of quantum circuits in the context of quantum simulation of time-dependent Hamiltonians.

### [15] [Factorization rule for multitime correlations in non-Markovian open quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22386)
*Thomas K. Bracht,Moritz Cygorek*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，对于时间无关哈密顿量和有限记忆时间 $\tau_c$ 的非马尔可夫开放量子系统，存在一种精确因子化规则，可将高阶多时间关联函数表示为低阶关联函数的乘积，从而极大简化计算效率并实现半解析求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子系统实验中常测量多时间关联函数（multitime correlation functions）。对于弱耦合系统，可利用量子回归定理（QRT）约化到约化密度矩阵演化，但一般非马尔可夫（non-Markovian）开放量子系统缺乏QRT，因此需要寻找新的精确因子化机制来简化多时间关联函数的计算。

Method: 论文在时间无关哈密顿量和有限记忆时间 $\tau_c$ 的假设下，推导出一个精确因子化规则（exact factorization rule），将高阶多时间关联函数关联到低阶关联函数的乘积。同时，该规则表明重构 $n$ 时间关联函数所需的信息包含在 $\mathcal{O}(\tau_c^n)$ 的时间体积（temporal volume）内。

Result: 以耦合声子（phonons）的量子点（quantum dots）为例，数值计算表明该因子化规则使得多时间关联函数的数值计算极为高效，并在标准QRT失效的系统中仍可实现半解析求解（semianalytical solutions）。

Conclusion: 该精确因子化规则为非马尔可夫开放量子系统中的多时间关联函数计算提供了一种通用的高效方法，突破了标准量子回归定理的局限性。

Abstract: Experiments performed on quantum systems often measure multitime correlation functions. When quantum systems are weakly coupled to their environment, the time evolution of such correlation functions can be reduced to that of the reduced density matrix by the quantum regression theorem (QRT). While no QRT is available for general non-Markovian open quantum systems, we show that for time-independent Hamiltonians and finite memory times $τ_c$, an exact factorization rule exists that relates higher-order multitime correlations to products of lower-order correlations. Consequently, all information needed to reconstruct $n$-time correlations is contained in a temporal volume of $\mathcal{O}(τ_c^n)$. On the example of quantum dots coupled to phonons, we demonstrate that this factorization makes numerical calculations of multitime correlations extremely efficient and even enables semianalytical solutions in systems where the standard QRT breaks down.

</details>


### [16] [Geometric Origin of the Non-Adiabaticity Parameter and Self-Limiting Instability in Driven Nonlinear Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22796)
*A. M. Tishin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了非绝热参数（non-adiabaticity parameter）在Fubini-Study度规下的射影希尔伯特空间（projective Hilbert space）中的直接几何解释，将其等同于驱动量子态的瞬时演化速度。与传统的渐近方法不同，该框架提供了一个严格的局部几何判据，能够连续评估驱动演化各阶段的非绝热不稳定性及其非线性抑制。进一步证明，依赖于占据数的非线性调节器（nonlinear regulator）可抑制有效几何演化速度，从而产生有界的低占据动力学，最终给出驱动非线性玻色系统中自限非绝热不稳定性的紧凑交叉参数判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统处理非绝热不稳定性多采用渐近方法，缺乏能够连续评估演化各阶段不稳定性的局部几何判据。论文旨在从微分几何角度为非绝热参数赋予直接的几何意义，并建立可适用于非线性玻色系统的严格局部判据。

Method: 通过在射影希尔伯特空间中引入Fubini-Study度规，将非绝热参数重新解释为量子态的瞬时几何演化速度。引入依赖于占据数的非线性调节器来抑制有效几何演化速度，并推导出交叉参数（crossover parameter）作为自限非绝热不稳定性的紧凑判据。

Result: 该框架提供了严格局部的几何判据，能够连续评估驱动演化各阶段的非绝热不稳定性。非线性调节器可有效抑制有效几何演化速度，导致低占据动力学有界。交叉参数给出了驱动非线性玻色系统中自限非绝热不稳定性的紧凑判据。

Conclusion: 非绝热参数具有直接的几何解释，新框架突破了传统渐近方法的局限，为理解和控制非线性玻色系统中的非绝热不稳定性提供了连续、局部的几何判据。

Abstract: We establish that the non-adiabaticity parameter has a direct geometric interpretation as the instantaneous evolution speed of a driven quantum state in projective Hilbert space under the Fubini Study metric. In contrast to conventional asymptotic approaches, the proposed framework provides a strictly local geometric criterion that allows non-adiabatic instability and its nonlinear suppression to be evaluated continuously at each stage of the driven evolution. We further show that an occupation-dependent nonlinear regulator Usuppresses the effective geometric evolution speed, leading to bounded low-occupancy dynamics. The resulting crossover parameter provides a compact criterion for self-limited non-adiabatic instability in driven nonlinear bosonic systems.

</details>

### [17] [Gravitational wave detectability range informed by external messengers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21578)
*S. Ronchini,A. Chopra,T. Dal Canton,B. Banerjee,A. L. De Santis,M. Branchesi*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为“目标可探测性距离（Targeted Detectability Range, TDR）”的方法，用于在外来信使（如电磁或中微子信号）与引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）事件相关联的假设下，以最小计算代价快速评估致密双星并合（compact binary coalescence）的引力波可探测性。该方法将外来信使的观测先验信息（如天区定位、倾角约束、质量边界）纳入评估，优于基于平均源参数的标准引力波范围，并在LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作的前三次观测运行期间的所有伽马射线暴（gamma-ray bursts）上进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 快速估计与天体瞬变现象（astronomical transients）相关联的引力波可探测性，对于优化多信使（multi-messenger）后续观测策略以及约束瞬变本身的物理起源至关重要。现有标准引力波范围（standard GW range）基于平均源参数，无法充分利用外来信使提供的先验信息，因此需要更高效、更具针对性的评估方法。

Method: 引入目标可探测性距离（TDR），该方法以最小计算代价评估致密双星并合在关联外部信使（如电磁或中微子信号）假设下的可探测性。TDR不采用平均源参数，而是纳入来自外来信使观测的先验信息，包括天区定位（sky localization）、倾角约束（inclination constraints）以及成分质量（component masses）的物理边界。

Result: 报告了LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作前三次观测运行期间所有长、短两类伽马射线暴的可探测性距离。通过与建模目标引力波搜索（modeled targeted GW searches）提供的90%排除距离进行系统比较，验证了该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: TDR能够以极低计算代价快速评估与外来信使关联的引力波源可探测性，其有效性通过系统比较得到验证，可用于优化多信使观测策略和约束瞬变起源。

Abstract: A rapid estimate of gravitational-wave (GW) detectability associated with astronomical transients is crucial for optimizing multi-messenger follow-up strategies and for constraining the physical origin of the transient itself. We introduce here the Targeted Detectability Range (TDR), designed to evaluate with minimal computational effort the detectability of compact binary coalescences under the hypothesis of association with an external messenger, such as an electromagnetic or neutrino signal. Unlike the standard GW range, which is based on averaged source parameters, the TDR incorporates prior information from observations of the external messenger, including sky localization, inclination constraints, and physically motivated bounds on component masses. We report the detectability range of all gamma-ray bursts, short and long duration, observed during the first three observing runs of the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA collaboration. The method is validated by performing a systematic comparison with the 90$\%$ exclusion distances provided by modeled targeted GW searches.

</details>


### [18] [Generation of Quantum Turbulence by Neutrino Cooling in Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22768)
*J. A. Sauls*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文探讨中子星内部中子超流体（neutron superfluid）和质子超导体（proton superconductor）中拓扑缺陷（topological defects）的形成，特别是在中微子冷却导致的非平衡条件下，基于Kibble-Zurek机制（KZM）预测量子涡旋（quantized vortices）和磁通线（quantized flux lines）的高密度生成，并指出这将在三维空间中形成随机涡旋网络，即量子湍流（quantum turbulence）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星内部壳层和大部分液体核心被认为是由中子超流体、质子超导体和相对论性电子液体组成的量子液体混合物。理解这些超流态在年轻中子星中如何形成，是揭示中子星内部结构及演化过程的关键问题。

Method: 采用Kibble-Zurek机制（KZM）描述非平衡相变中的拓扑缺陷形成，从接近临界温度T_c的库珀对涨落传播子（Cooper pair fluctuation propagator）出发，推导缺陷形成的标度关系（scaling relations）。基于Urca和修正Urca冷却机制，针对不同的超流能隙（superfluid gap）和转变温度模型，计算中子星核心中子超流体中的涡旋密度。

Result: 在所有研究的模型中，KZM均预测中子星冷凝相（condensate phase）中会产生高密度的拓扑缺陷。在三维空间中，这些缺陷表现为涡旋线和涡旋环的随机网络，即量子湍流（quantum turbulence）。

Conclusion: 中子星内部超流态的非平衡相变由中微子冷却速率驱动，必然伴随大量拓扑缺陷的产生。KZM预测的高密度涡旋网络意味着量子湍流的存在，这对理解中子星内部的输运性质、磁场演化及冷却行为具有重要物理意义。

Abstract: The interior crust and much of the liquid core of neutron stars is believed to be a quantum liquid mixture of neutron and proton superfluids and a relativistic electron liquid. Quantized vortices in the neutron superfluid and quantized flux lines in the proton superconductor are topological defects of these hadronic condensates. I consider the formation of the superfluid state in young neutron stars under non-equilibrium conditions imposed by the neutrino cooling rate. The nonequilibrium phase transition implies that the onset of superfluidity is accompanied by the generation of quantized vortices based on the mechanism envisioned by Kibble in the context cosmic string formation in an evolutionary models of an expanding universe, and further developed by Zurek for nonequilibrium phase transitions in quantum liquids such as \Hefour. I discuss the Kibble-Zurek mechanism (KZM) and scaling relations for topological defect formation starting from the Cooper pair fluctuation propagator for temperatures approaching $T_c$. I then calculate the predicted vortex densities based on Urca and modified Urca cooling mechanisms in the cores of neutron stars for several models of the superfluid gap and transition temperature of the interior neutron superfluid. In all cases studied the KZM leads to a large density of topological defects in the condensate phase, which in 3D form a random network of vortex lines and loops, i.e. the generation of quantum turbulence.

</details>

### [19] [Klein tunneling of the laser coherence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22033)
*Konstantin Manannikov,Sagie Gadasi,Ekaterina Mironova,Eran Bernstein,Andrei Poliakov,Nir Davidson,Alexander N. Poddubny*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本研究理论分析了由光谱失谐势垒分隔的两组激光阵列的锁相同步（lasing synchronization）行为，发现当工作在狄拉克点（Dirac point）时，同步能够跨越比常规抛物型色散（parabolic dispersion）或纯耗散耦合（purely dissipative coupling）阵列高一个数量级的势垒。该效应被解释为激光相干性的克莱因隧穿（Klein tunneling）。线性化本征模（linearized eigenmodes）的去局域化分析支持了数值结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有复模式色散（complex mode dispersion）的激光阵列在存在光谱失谐势垒（spectrally detuned barrier）时的同步行为，尤其是寻找超越常规色散结构的同步增强机制。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，研究两组激光阵列通过光谱失谐势垒耦合时的锁相同步条件；对比了狄拉克点色散、抛物型色散和纯耗散耦合三种情况；通过线性化本征模的去局域化（delocalization）分析对数值结果进行理论支撑。

Result: 在狄拉克点工作的激光阵列能够跨越比抛物型色散或纯耗散耦合阵列高一个数量级的势垒高度仍保持同步。该稳健同步效应源于激光相干性通过势垒的克莱因隧穿。

Conclusion: 狄拉克点色散可显著增强激光阵列的抗势垒同步能力，其物理机制是克莱因隧穿，这为设计具有更强鲁棒性的耦合激光系统提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We study theoretically the lasing synchronization of the two arrays of lasers with the complex mode dispersion, separated by a spectrally detuned barrier. We demonstrate that for lasing at the Dirac point, the synchronization persists for an order of magnitude higher barriers than in the arrays with a usual parabolic dispersion or a purely dissipative coupling. We interpret this effect as the Klein tunneling of the laser coherence through the barrier. Our numerical findings are supported by an analysis of the delocalization of the linearized eigenmodes of the arrays, which enhances the synchronization.

### [20] [A Metric-Deformed $q$-Gauge Dirac Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21508)
*Julio César Jaramillo Quiceno*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于变形 d'Alembert 算符引入的 q-狄拉克算符，通过将度规张量分量视为时空依赖的背景场，构造了一族度规变形的规范理论，包括变形的协变导数、场强以及相应的杨-米尔斯理论和费米子极小耦合的规范不变作用量，为 q-变形规范理论提供了基于度规的数学基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为近期提出的 $q$-Dirac 算符 $D_q = γ^μ\sqrt{|g^{μμ}|}\partial_μ$（源于变形 d'Alembert 算符 $\Box_q$）建立相应的规范理论框架，填补从度规视角构建 $q$-变形规范理论的数学基础空白。

Method: 将变形参数 $q$ 与度规分量关联 ($q_μ= \sqrt{|g^{μμ}|}$)，并将 $g^{μμ}(x)$ 推广为时空依赖的背景场，定义变形的协变导数 $D_μ^{(q)} = \partial_μ+ ieA_μ(x)/\sqrt{|g^{μμ}(x)|}$，进而计算对应的场强 $F_{μν}^{(q)} = [D_μ^{(q)}, D_ν^{(q)}]$。

Result: 变形场强 $F_{μν}^{(q)}$ 获得了正比于 $\partial_μ(1/\sqrt{|g^{νν}|})$ 的新项，这些项在度规为常数时消失；成功写下了变形杨-米尔斯理论以及费米子极小耦合到 $D_μ^{(q)}$ 的规范不变作用量。

Conclusion: 该工作从度规视角为 $q$-变形规范理论提供了严格的数学基础，表明度规的时空依赖性自然地引入规范理论中的额外结构。

Abstract: We construct a family of metric-deformed gauge theories based on a recently introduced $q$-Dirac operator $D_q = γ^μ\sqrt{|g^{μμ}|}\partial_μ$, which arises from a deformed D'Alembertian $\Box_q = |g^{00}|\partial_t^2 - \sum_i |g^{ii}|\partial_i^2$. The deformation parameter $q$ is related to the metric components via $q_μ= \sqrt{|g^{μμ}|}$. By promoting $g^{μμ}(x)$ to spacetime-dependent background fields, we define a deformed covariant derivative $D_μ^{(q)} = \partial_μ+ ieA_μ(x)/\sqrt{|g^{μμ}(x)|}$ (no sum over $μ$). The corresponding field strength $F_{μν}^{(q)} = [D_μ^{(q)}, D_ν^{(q)}]$ acquires new terms proportional to $\partial_μ(1/\sqrt{|g^{νν}|})$, which vanish for constant metrics. We write down gauge-invariant actions for deformed Yang-Mills theory and for fermions minimally coupled to $D_μ^{(q)}$. This work provides a mathematical foundation for $q$-deformed gauge theories from a metric perspective.

</details>


### [21] [Landau-Ginzburg models of generalised Dubrovin-Zhang form and pole collision: Dynkin-type A](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21749)
*Alessandro Proserpio,Karoline van Gemst*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文推广了将Dubrovin-Zhang Frobenius流形（Frobenius manifolds）构造为仿射Weyl群（affine Weyl groups）扩充的正则轨道空间（regular orbit spaces）上一维Landau–Ginzburg镜像的方法，在Dynkin A型中分类了由此产生的Frobenius流形结构，并通过Hurwitz空间边界上的分层（stratification）和极点碰撞框架（pole-collision framework）解释了这些结构，最终证明了Ma–Zuo关于双扩充仿射Weyl群预势（prepotential）形式的猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前期工作（arXiv:1711.05958, arXiv:2103.12673）构建了仿射Weyl群扩充的正则轨道空间上的Dubrovin-Zhang Frobenius流形的一维Landau–Ginzburg镜像，本文旨在推广该方法的适用范围，并在Dynkin A型中系统分类所得Frobenius流形结构，同时验证Ma–Zuo关于预势形式的猜想。

Method: 推广前期构造方法，对Dynkin A型中的Frobenius流形结构进行分类；引入Hurwitz空间边界上的分层（stratification）解释结果，并建立极点碰撞框架（pole-collision framework）以比较不同分层内的Frobenius结构；利用arXiv:2412.05165中的公式，在任意秩和维度下取合适的重整化极限（renormalised limit），证明预势层面的结构结果。

Result: 在Dynkin A型中完成了Frobenius流形结构的分类；通过分层和极点碰撞框架获得了不同分层间Frobenius结构的比较；证明了任意秩和维度下预势的结构性结果；作为推论，证明了Ma–Zuo关于与双扩充仿射Weyl群（doubly-extended affine Weyl groups）相关的预势形式的猜想。

Conclusion: 本文推广的方法有效分类了Dynkin A型中由仿射Weyl群扩充导出的Frobenius流形结构，并通过极点碰撞框架揭示了Hurwitz空间边界上的分层结构关联，最终验证了Ma–Zuo猜想。

Abstract: In arXiv:1711.05958, arXiv:2103.12673, the authors derive one-dimensional Landau-Ginzburg mirrors of Dubrovin-Zhang Frobenius manifolds constructed on regular orbit spaces of an extension of affine Weyl groups. We generalise the method employed, and classify the resulting Frobenius manifold structures in Dynkin type A. We interpret our results in terms of a stratification on the Hurwitz space boundary, and develop a pole-collision framework to compare the Frobenius structures within different strata. With this, we can prove a structural result at the level of the prepotential, for arbitrary rank and dimension, as a suitable renormalised limit of the formulae in arXiv:2412.05165. As a corollary, a conjecture of Ma and Zuo regarding the form of prepotentials related to doubly-extended affine Weyl groups is proven.

### [22] [Lie symmetries of a generalized Fisher equation in cylindrical coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21890)
*Bayarjargal Batsukh,Uuganbayar Zunderiya*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用李对称方法（Lie symmetry method）研究了柱坐标下的广义Fisher方程，确定了当扩散函数为指数函数时，除时间平移对称性外，何种源函数能使该方程具有其他李对称性，并推导了相应的约化常微分方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义Fisher方程在生物数学和反应扩散系统中具有重要应用，但柱坐标下该方程的对称性结构及其约化条件尚未被充分研究。本文旨在通过李对称分析，系统探究不同源函数形式下该方程对称性的存在条件。

Method: 采用李对称方法（Lie symmetry method）对柱坐标下的广义Fisher方程进行对称性分析。研究扩散函数为指数函数时，源函数需满足何种条件才能使得方程具备除时间平移对称性（time translation symmetry）之外的其他李对称性，并进一步通过对称性约化获得相应的常微分方程（ordinary differential equations）。

Result: 确定了当扩散函数为指数函数时，柱坐标下广义Fisher方程存在额外李对称性所对应的源函数类型，并推导了与这些李对称性相对应的约化常微分方程。

Conclusion: 李对称方法能够有效分析柱坐标下广义Fisher方程的对称性结构，特定源函数形式可赋予该方程更丰富的对称性，从而通过约化得到更易处理的常微分方程。

Abstract: In this work we studied a generalized Fisher equation in cylindrical coordinate using Lie symmetry method. We have determined for what type of source function the generalized Fisher equation has Lie Symmetries other than time translation symmetry when the diffusion function is given by an exponential function. Also the reduced ordinary differential equations are obtained corresponding to Lie symmetries of the generalized Fisher equation.

### [23] [Asymptotics of the IDS for Schrödinger operators with singular potentials and Gibbs point processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22023)
*Yuta Nakagawa*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有单点势（满足essinf V = -∞）的随机薛定谔算子（random Schrödinger operators）的积分态密度（integrated density of states, IDS）的渐近行为。在底层点过程为具有排斥性成对相互作用的吉布斯点过程（Gibbs point process）的假设下，采用周期近似方法确定了当E → -∞时log N(E)的领头阶，并发现排斥相互作用导致比泊松情形显著更快的衰减，且在吉布斯设定中多团簇构型可主导IDS贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解具有非有界下单点势的随机薛定谔算子在低能极限下积分态密度的渐近行为，特别是排斥性成对相互作用如何影响态密度的衰减速率。

Method: 采用周期近似方法（periodic approximation method）分析吉布斯点过程（Gibbs point process）框架下的积分态密度渐近行为。

Result: 排斥性成对相互作用导致log N(E)在E → -∞时比泊松情形衰减显著更快；在吉布斯框架下，多团簇构型（multiple clusters）可对积分态密度提供主导贡献，这与泊松模型中典型的单团簇主导（single-cluster dominance）形成对比；针对含有多重奇点的特定势能类别，给出了领头常数的精细估计。

Conclusion: 点过程间的排斥相互作用能从根本上改变随机薛定谔算子低能态密度的渐近行为，导致更快的指数衰减，同时改变了主导态密度的构型特征（从单团簇转为多团簇）。

Abstract: The asymptotic behavior of the integrated density of states (IDS), \(N(E)\), is investigated for random Schrödinger operators with a single-site potential \(V\) satisfying \(\mathrm{essinf}\, V = -\infty\). Under the assumption that the underlying point process is a Gibbs point process with repulsive pairwise interactions, the leading term of \(\log N(E)\) as \(E \to -\infty\) is determined using a periodic approximation method. It is shown that repulsive pairwise interactions lead to a significantly faster decay of \(N(E)\) compared to the Poisson case. Furthermore, configurations with multiple clusters can provide the dominant contribution to the IDS in the Gibbs setting, contrasting with the single-cluster dominance typically observed in Poisson models. Finally, refined estimates of the leading constants are provided for specific classes of potentials, including those with multiple singularities.

</details>


### [24] [Global exponential stability for the three-dimensional Navier-Stokes equations on hyperbolic space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22212)
*Zhi-Wei Wang,Samuel L. Braunstein*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明，在三维双曲空间 $\HH^3$ 上，带有变形拉普拉斯算子（deformation Laplacian）的不可压缩纳维-斯托克斯方程（Navier-Stokes equations），对于 $L^3(\HH^3)$ 中足够小的初值存在唯一全局温和解（global mild solution），且该解以指数速率衰减到零；而平坦空间 $\R^3$ 上的相应结果仅为代数衰减。指数稳定性源于负曲率提供的谱隙（spectral gap）。同时指出，$L^2$ 范数在 $\HH^3$ 上仍是超临界的（supercritical），因为热核（heat kernel）的局域紫外标度（ultraviolet scaling）对全局几何不敏感。曲率能够改善的边界恰好位于 Fujita-Kato 积分收敛性的临界指数处：当 $p \geq 3$（Kato 临界空间）时积分有界且谱隙贡献指数衰减；当 $p < 3$ 时积分发散，与曲率无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典纳维-斯托克斯方程在平坦空间 $\R^3$ 上的小初值全局适定性已有 Kato 型结果，但解仅呈代数衰减。一个自然的问题是，将方程置于具有负曲率的双曲空间 $\HH^3$ 上，能否借助几何曲率带来的谱隙（spectral gap）改善解的大时间行为（long-time behavior），甚至获得指数衰减（exponential decay），从而深化对几何与流体方程稳定性之间关系的理解。

Method: 采用 $L^p$-$L^q$ 框架下的 Kato 型迭代论证（Kato-type iteration argument），分析双曲空间 $\HH^3$ 上变形拉普拉斯算子的谱性质（spectral property），利用其有效谱隙（effective spectral gap）$\lambda_{\Def}^{(3)} = 26/9$ 结合动态粘度（dynamic viscosity）$\mu$ 得到指数衰减率 $\mu \lambda_{\Def}^{(3)}$。同时通过热核（heat kernel）的局域紫外标度分析（ultraviolet scaling analysis），检验 $L^2$ 范数的临界性（criticality）以及不同 $p$ 值下 Fujita-Kato 积分（Fujita-Kato integral）的收敛行为。

Result: 在 $\HH^3$ 上，对 $L^3(\HH^3)$ 中足够小的初值，方程存在唯一全局温和解，且解以指数速率 $\mu \lambda_{\Def}^{(3)} = 26\mu/9$ 衰减到零。$L^2$ 范数在 $\HH^3$ 上仍是超临界的，因为热核的局域紫外标度对全局几何不敏感。Fujita-Kato 积分的标度指数（scaling exponent）为 $1/2 - 3/(2p)$，仅依赖于初值可积性（integrability），与流形几何无关：当 $p \geq 3$ 时积分有界且谱隙贡献指数衰减；当 $p < 3$ 时积分在 $t=0$ 处发散（$p \leq 2$ 时对任意 $t>0$ 严格发散），与曲率无关。

Conclusion: 负曲率通过提供谱隙，在宏观尺度上将解的大时间行为从代数衰减改善为指数衰减，这是全局几何效应（global geometric effect）的体现。然而，曲率无法改善局域紫外标度行为（local ultraviolet scaling behavior），因此 $L^2$ 超临界性等由短距离（short-distance）发散引起的障碍仍然存在。曲率改善与不改善的精确分界线由 Fujita-Kato 积分的标度指数 $1/2 - 3/(2p)$ 刻画，对应 $p=3$ 这一 Kato 临界空间（Kato critical space）阈值。

Abstract: We prove that the three-dimensional incompressible Navier-Stokes equations with the deformation Laplacian on hyperbolic 3-space $\HH^3$ admit a unique global mild solution for sufficiently small initial data in $L^3(\HH^3)$, and that this solution decays exponentially to zero. The exponential decay rate is $μλ_\Def^{(3)}$, where $μ$ is the dynamic viscosity and $λ_\Def^{(3)} = 26/9$ is the effective spectral gap of the deformation Laplacian in $L^3$. On flat $\R^3$, the corresponding Kato-type result gives only algebraic decay. The exponential stability is a macroscopic consequence of the spectral gap provided by negative curvature. We also show that the $L^2$ norm is supercritical on $\HH^3$ (as on $\R^3$), with the obstruction arising from the local ultraviolet scaling of the heat kernel, which is insensitive to global geometry. The boundary between what curvature can and cannot improve is located exactly: the Fujita-Kato integral has a scaling exponent $1/2 - 3/(2p)$ that depends only on the integrability of the initial data, not on the geometry of the manifold. For $p \geq 3$ (the Kato critical space), the integral is bounded and the spectral gap contributes exponential time decay. For $p < 3$, the integral diverges at $t = 0$ (and strictly diverges for all $t>0$ when $p \le 2$) regardless of the curvature.

</details>


### [25] [A perturbative approach to the Wetterich equation for Bosonic and Fermionic interacting fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22436)
*Beatrice Costeri*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文在微扰代数量子场论（pAQFT）框架下，研究了弯曲时空上相互作用量子场的洛伦兹维特里希重整化群（Wetterich RG）流方程。针对两类模型——全局双曲时空上的两个互作用标量场和自旋背景上的自相互作用狄拉克场——在局域势近似下推导了RG流方程并计算了相关耦合的贝塔函数。此外，证明了这两类模型流方程解的局部存在唯一性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将重整化群方法拓展到弯曲时空背景下的相互作用量子场论，特别是建立洛伦兹代数RG方法与随机场论模型之间的潜在联系。

Method: 在微扰代数量子场论框架下，采用局域势近似（Local Potential Approximation）推导洛伦兹维特里希重整化群流方程，并基于纳什-莫泽定理（Nash-Moser theorem）证明解的局部存在唯一性。

Result: 推导了两个互作用标量场和自相互作用狄拉克场的RG流方程，计算了相应耦合参数的贝塔函数（beta functions）；对于标量模型，发现了一个形式上类似于马丁-西吉亚-罗斯描述（Martin-Siggia-Rose description）的不对称相互作用势；证明了标量场和狄拉克场两类模型的流方程均具有局部存在唯一解。

Conclusion: 洛伦兹代数RG方法可有效应用于弯曲时空上的相互作用量子场，且与随机场论模型之间存在潜在联系。流方程的局部良定性（local well-posedness）得到了严格证明。

Abstract: We study the Lorentzian Wetterich Renormalization Group (RG) flow equation for interacting quantum fields on curved backgrounds within the framework of perturbative Algebraic Quantum Field Theory (pAQFT). Specifically, we consider two classes of models: two mutually interacting scalar fields on globally hyperbolic spacetimes without boundary and, under the further assumption that the underlying background is spin, self-interacting Dirac fields. In both cases, we derive the corresponding RG flow equations within a Local Potential Approximation and compute the beta functions for the relevant couplings. For the scalar model, we also discuss an asymmetric interaction potential which is formally reminiscent of the Martin-Siggia-Rose description of a stochastic dynamics, thereby indicating a possible connection between Lorentzian algebraic RG methods [DDP+24] and stochastic field-theoretic models, [Duc25]. In addition, we address the local well-posedness of the resulting flow equations. Adapting the strategy detailed in [DP23] and based on the the Nash-Moser theorem, we prove local existence and uniqueness of solutions for both the scalar and the Dirac models.

</details>

### [26] [Long-lived quasinormal modes of Asymptotically de Sitter Black Holes in Generalized Proca Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21533)
*S. V. Bolokhov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过高阶WKB计算和时域演化，系统分析了广义Proca理论中渐近德西特黑洞的大质量标量扰动，发现标量质量增加会导致频率进入实部线性增长、阻尼率趋近几何依赖常数的大质量区，不存在准共振现象，并探讨了该结果对强宇宙审查猜想的含义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究广义Proca理论中渐近德西特（de Sitter）黑洞的大质量标量扰动（massive scalar perturbations），揭示原初毛发（primary hair）、视界结构（horizon structure）和场质量（field mass）之间的相互作用。

Method: 采用高阶WKB（Wentzel–Kramers–Brillouin）近似计算，辅以时域演化（time-domain evolution）方法，分析代表性黑洞背景，并将完整黑洞拟正规模谱（quasinormal mode spectrum）与精确的纯德西特基准解进行对比。

Result: 增加标量质量会使频率进入一个简单的大质量区，实部线性增长，阻尼率趋近非零且依赖于几何结构的常数，在所研究参数范围内未出现真正的准共振（quasi-resonance）。频谱随黑洞大小和Proca毛（Proca hair）发生偏移。

Conclusion: 推导出一个紧凑的大质量解析公式，并指出德西特型扇区（de Sitter-like sector）对带电荷三视界区间的强宇宙审查猜想（strong cosmic censorship）具有潜在影响。

Abstract: Massive scalar perturbations of asymptotically de Sitter black holes in generalized Proca theory display a sharp interplay between primary hair, horizon structure, and field mass. Using high-order WKB calculations supplemented by time-domain evolution, we analyze representative black-hole backgrounds and compare the full black-hole spectrum with the exact pure de Sitter benchmark. We show that increasing the scalar mass drives the frequencies into a simple large-mass regime in which the real part grows linearly while the damping rate approaches a nonzero geometry-dependent constant, so true quasi-resonances do not occur within the regime studied here. We also identify how the spectrum shifts with black-hole size and Proca hair, derive a compact analytic large-$μ$ formula, and comment on the implications of the de Sitter-like sector for strong cosmic censorship in the charged three-horizon regime.

</details>


### [27] [The Relativistic Gravitational Field of a Spherically Symmetric Extended Body](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21551)
*Y. Friedman,S. I. Klimovsky*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在扩展相对论（Extended Relativity, ER）框架下，通过叠加原理推导了延展对称球体的度规，发现其外部场依赖于内部质量分布的高阶修正，并在中子星和地球附近产生可测量的效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在标准广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）中，史瓦西外部解与牛顿壳层定理均表明球对称延展体的外部引力场与内部质量分布无关。本文旨在检验这一结论在扩展相对论框架下是否仍然成立，并探讨内部结构对引力场的修正效应。

Method: 作者在闵可夫斯基背景上的扩展相对论框架中，利用推迟引力场的相对论叠加原理（relativistic superposition principle），通过对质量元的贡献进行积分，推导出一个延展球对称体的显式度规，并分析了相应的允许速度几何（admissible-velocity geometry）及测试粒子的运动方程。

Result: 所得度规在适当极限下再现了点源引力时间膨胀效应并符合经典GR检验，但其外部场依赖于内部质量分布的高阶修正。这些修正随距离快速衰减，但在致密天体附近变得显著。对于中子星，修正明显改变了表面附近的局部光速结构；对于地球，修正虽小，但在往返光传播时间上对国际空间站（International Space Station, ISS）产生可测量差异。

Conclusion: 该形式体系为延展引力源提供了清晰的相对论描述，并建立了一个研究强场与精密测量条件下因内部结构导致的相对论修正的框架。

Abstract: We investigate the gravitational field of an extended spherically symmetric body within the framework of Extended Relativity (ER), a Lorentz-covariant formulation of relativistic gravity on a Minkowski background. Using a relativistic superposition principle for retarded gravitational fields, we derive an explicit metric for an extended body by integrating the contributions of its mass elements.
  The resulting metric reproduces the standard gravitational time dilation of a point source and agrees with the classical tests of General Relativity in the appropriate limits. However, unlike the exact Newtonian shell theorem and the Schwarzschild exterior solution, the external field depends weakly on the internal mass distribution through higher-order corrections. These corrections decay rapidly with distance but become significant near compact objects.
  We analyze the corresponding admissible-velocity geometry, derive the motion equations for test particles, and compare the predictions of extended-body and point-source models. For neutron stars, the corrections noticeably modify the local light-velocity structure near the surface. For the Earth, the corrections are small but produce measurable differences in round-trip light travel times to the International Space Station.
  The formalism provides a transparent relativistic description of extended gravitational sources and offers a framework for studying relativistic corrections due to internal structure in strong-field and precision-measurement regimes.

</details>


### [28] [Astrophysical Objects in Modified Theories of Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21564)
*Sneha Pradhan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本论文系统地研究了在基于挠率（torsion）和非度量性（nonmetricity）的修正引力理论（如 \(f(Q)\) 和 \(f(T)\) 引力）中，中子星和奇异星的内部结构、平衡与稳定性。通过共形对称性、MIT口袋模型（MIT Bag model）以及引力退耦（gravitational decoupling）技术构建了带电各向同性及各向异性（anisotropic）致密星模型，并结合贝叶斯统计框架利用NICER等观测数据约束模型参数。结果表明，修正引力能在与观测保持一致的前提下显著影响致密星的最大质量、半径及稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在广义相对论之外探索修正引力理论（modified theories of gravity）对致密天体性质的影响，检验其理论预测与天体物理观测的兼容性。

Method: 在 \(f(Q)\) 引力中采用共形对称性（conformal symmetry）和MIT口袋状态方程（MIT Bag equation of state）构建带电各向同性致密星模型，并与Bardeen外部时空匹配。在 \(f(T)\) 引力中利用最小和完全几何变形（minimal and complete geometric deformation）的引力退耦技术生成各向异性奇异星模型。通过能量条件、因果性约束、广义Tolman–Oppenheimer–Volkoff方程及Herrera开裂判据（Herrera's cracking criterion）检验物理可行性与稳定性。采用贝叶斯统计框架（Bayesian statistical framework）结合NICER质量–半径观测数据约束模型参数，并使用贝叶斯因子（Bayes factor）分析识别可行的引力扩展。

Result: 修正引力能够显著改变致密星的最大质量、半径和稳定性，同时仍与天文观测结果保持兼容。

Conclusion: 该工作为超越广义相对论（general relativity）的致密星研究提供了系统的理论与观测分析。

Abstract: This thesis investigates compact astrophysical objects within modified theories of gravity, focusing on neutron stars and strange stars. The work studies their internal structure, equilibrium, and stability in gravitational frameworks based on torsion and nonmetricity, which provide the foundation for theories such as \(f(Q)\) and \(f(T)\) gravity. Charged isotropic compact star models are constructed in \(f(Q)\) gravity using conformal symmetry and the MIT Bag equation of state, with matching to the Bardeen exterior spacetime.
  Gravitational decoupling techniques, including minimal and complete geometric deformation methods, are employed in \(f(T)\) gravity to generate anisotropic strange star models. These approaches enable the inclusion of additional gravitational sources, dark matter effects, and spacetime deformations. Exact analytical solutions are obtained under suitable physical conditions such as regularity and vanishing complexity. The models are examined using energy conditions, causality constraints, the generalized Tolman--Oppenheimer--Volkoff equation, and Herrera's cracking criterion to ensure physical viability and stability.
  The influence of modified gravity parameters on stellar mass, radius, compactness, and stability is analyzed in detail. A Bayesian statistical framework is applied to constrain model parameters using observational data, including NICER mass--radius measurements. Bayes factor analysis is further used to identify viable gravitational extensions consistent with astrophysical observations.
  The results show that modified gravity can significantly affect the maximum mass, radius, and stability of compact stars while remaining compatible with observations. This work provides a systematic theoretical and observational study of compact stars beyond general relativity.

</details>


### [29] [Astrophysical Signature and Optical Appearance of Weyl--Corrected Einstein--Maxwell Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21571)
*Hassan Hassanabadi,Mrinnoy M. Gohain,Kalyan Bhuyan,Farokhnaz Hosseinifar*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Weyl修正（Weyl correction）这一由时空曲率与电磁场非最小耦合（non-minimal coupling）产生的修正框架下，带电黑洞的物理性质如何被改变。

Method: 通过重新推导Hawking温度、熵和热容等热力学量分析热稳定性与相变；运用环绕数方法（winding number method）对热力学态进行拓扑分类；研究两种光子极化（photon polarization）下的零测地线（null geodesics）与阴影（shadow）；计算吸积盘（accretion disk）的能量通量、光谱光度及微分光度。

Result: Weyl修正参数重塑了黑洞的热稳定性和相变图景；拓扑分类揭示了Weyl修正对黑洞普适分类的影响；通过对两种光子极化阴影的分析获得了黑洞参数约束；吸积盘的辐射特征显示出Weyl修正在观测光谱中留下了可探测的痕迹。

Conclusion: Weyl修正不仅在理论上改变了黑洞的热力学与拓扑结构，还在天体物理学层面通过对阴影和吸积盘辐射的影响提供了潜在的可观测信号，有助于进一步约束修正引力理论。

Abstract: In this work, we delve into the physics of charged black holes modified by Weyl corrections, a framework that emerges from the subtle non--minimal coupling between spacetime curvature and electromagnetism. We begin by revisiting the thermodynamics of these cases, where we derive the Hawking temperature, entropy, and heat capacity to see how the Weyl correction parameter reshapes the landscape of thermal stability and phase transitions. Then, we apply the winding number method to classify the thermodynamic states of the system from a topological perspective and show the effect of the Weyl modifications on the universal classification of the Wey--corrected black hole. Moving beyond pure theory and into the realm of astrophysics, we study the motion of massless particles affected by the Weyl correction for the two photon polarization, and by exploring the shadow, we find constraints of the black hole parameters. Also, we study the null trajectories for the two photon polarization of the Weyl--corrected black hole. Finally, we model the accretion disk around these black holes. By calculating the energy flux, spectral luminosity, and differential luminosity, we show how these corrections leave a detectable trace on the light we might observe.

### [30] [Wave-optics gravitational wave lensing in modified gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21584)
*Alice Garoffolo,Gianmassimo Tasinato*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文首次在修正引力（modified gravity）框架内研究了波光学（wave-optics）区间的引力波透镜效应，发现曲率耦合传播方程导致红外（infrared）动力学与广义相对论（GR）定性不同——零频极限下放大因子不再趋近于1，需用含相互作用的静态格林函数（static Green function）和分波展开（partial-wave formulation）描述，并可用畸变波（distorted-wave）和散射振幅（scattering amplitudes）语言重新诠释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有引力波透镜研究多基于广义相对论（general relativity, GR）的几何光学（geometric-optics）近似，波光学效应在修正引力中的行为尚属空白。本文旨在探索曲率耦合传播方程下引力波透镜在低频波光学区间的全新动力学特征。

Method: 采用唯象（phenomenological）框架，设定引力波振幅满足曲率耦合传播方程（curvature-coupled propagation equation）。通过分析该方程在几何光学与波光学区间的渐近行为，引入含相互作用的静态格林函数和分波展开方法处理低频区域，并建立畸变波诠释（distorted-wave interpretation）和散射振幅（scattering amplitudes）形式体系。

Result: 标准观点中放大因子（amplification factor）在零频极限下趋于1的结论在修正引力中不再成立；低频区标准菲涅尔（Fresnel）处理失效，需代之以静态格林函数和分波方法；该结构等价于畸变波图像——曲率相互作用被吸收进修饰参考传播基（dressed reference propagation basis），残余透镜效应由有限频相移（finite-frequency phase shifts）编码。这些现象可用散射振幅语言自然解释。

Conclusion: 波光学引力波透镜效应能够探测到修正引力中传播级（propagation-level）偏离广义相对论的行为，而这些偏离在几何光学近似下完全不可见。该结果为利用引力波透镜检验修正引力理论提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: We initiate the study of gravitational-wave lensing in the wave-optics regime within modified gravity. We consider a phenomenological setup in which the gravitational-wave amplitude obeys a curvature-coupled propagation equation. This framework reproduces the standard GR behaviour in the geometric-optics regime, while leading to qualitatively different infrared dynamics. In particular, the usual argument implying that the amplification factor approaches unity in the zero-frequency limit no longer applies. This is due to the persistence of curvature-induced interactions in the infrared, which modify the natural propagation basis itself. As a result, the standard Fresnel treatment ceases to be valid at sufficiently low frequency. The correct infrared regime is instead controlled by an interacting static Green function, with a finite-frequency completion provided by a partial-wave formulation. We show that this structure admits an equivalent distorted-wave interpretation, in which the curvature interaction is absorbed into a dressed reference propagation basis, while the residual lensing effect is encoded in finite-frequency phase shifts. We further demonstrate that these phenomena admit a natural interpretation in the language of scattering amplitudes. Wave-optics lensing can therefore probe propagation-level departures from GR that remain entirely invisible in geometric optics.

</details>


### [31] [Gravitational Wave Hyperbolic Catalog: Reanalyzing High-Mass Gravitational Wave Signals Using Hyperbolic Waveforms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21640)
*Jacob Lange,Danilo Chiaramello,Peter Lott,Chad Henshaw,Alessandro Nagar,Richard O'Shaughnessy,Laura Cadonati*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用双曲构型引力波波形模型重新分析LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA目录中的高质重事件，发现除GW190521显著支持动力学捕获（dynamical capture）场景外，其余事件均倾向准圆进动（quasi-circular precessing）解释；进一步分析表明GW190521可能处于高质重束缚进动信号与动力学捕获信号难以区分的参数空间区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞之间的近距离双曲交汇（hyperbolic encounters）会产生形态上不同于准圆旋进（quasi-circular inspiral）的引力波爆发信号，这些信号在致密星团环境通过动力学相互作用产生，可探测孤立双星演化无法触及的质量范围与形成通道，因此成为当前及下一代探测器的重要目标。

Method: 使用\dali波形模型的双曲构型重新分析LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA目录中的高质重事件，通过与同一模型的准圆进动构型进行比较，计算贝叶斯因子（Bayes factor）评估数据更支持哪种描述；对GW190521进一步采用不同构型（准圆非进动、偏心非进动、偏心进动）以及数值相对论替代模型（numerical relativity surrogate model）\nrsur进行分析验证。

Result: 大多数事件强烈或轻度支持准圆进动场景，但GW190521的最佳拟合为动力学捕获波形，其贝叶斯因子$\ln \mathcal{B}^{\rm hyp}_{\rm prec}=3.71^{+0.11}_{-0.11}$；另一高质重信号GW231123则显著支持准圆进动场景，$\ln \mathcal{B}^{\rm hyp}_{\rm prec}=-15.80^{+0.24}_{-0.24}$；对模拟信号的分析提示GW190521可能处于高质重束缚进动信号与动力学捕获信号难以区分的参数空间区域。

Conclusion: GW190521是当前目录中唯一显著支持动力学捕获双曲构型的高质重事件，但其参数空间位置表明高质重束缚进动信号与动力学捕获信号之间存在分辨困难，这为未来引力波事件分类和波形建模提出了重要挑战。

Abstract: Close hyperbolic encounters between black holes produce distinctive bursts of gravitational radiation with a time-frequency morphology that is qualitatively different from that of quasi-circular inspirals. Expected to arise in dense stellar environments through dynamical interactions, these encounters probe formation channels and mass ranges inaccessible to isolated binary evolution, making them a compelling target for current and next-generation detectors. In this work, we reanalyze \totalevents high-mass events from the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA catalogs using the hyperbolic configuration of the~\dali~waveform model. We compare these with analyses using the quasi-circular, precessing configuration of the same model, computing Bayes factors to evaluate which description is favored by the data. We find that most events strongly to mildly favor the quasi-circular, precessing scenario, except for GW190521. For this event, we find that the signal is best fit by a dynamical capture waveform, with Bayes factor $\ln \mathcal{B}^{\rm hyp}_{\rm prec}=3.71^{+0.11}_{-0.11}$. We confirm this preference via further analyses with~\dali~in different configurations (quasi-circular, non-precessing; eccentric, non-precessing; and eccentric, precessing), as well as one using the quasi-circular, precessing numerical relativity surrogate model \nrsur. We also highlight the results we obtain for GW231123, another high-mass signal linked to evidence of strong precession, for which we find strong preference for the quasi-circular, precessing scenario, with $\ln \mathcal{B}^{\rm hyp}_{\rm prec}=-15.80^{+0.24}_{-0.24}$. The analysis of mock signals generated with the best fitting waveforms for GW190521 and GW231123 suggest that the former might belong to a region of parameter space where high-mass, bound, precessing signals can be hard to distinguish from dynamical captures in parameter estimation.

</details>


### [32] [Relativity for Retired Engineers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21660)
*David Garfinkle*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对狭义相对论（special relativity）中的常见误解，通过提供指导和示例来澄清。这些误解通常源于试图用牛顿力学（Newtonian mechanics）的术语来表达狭义相对论的真理，而非使用更符合狭义相对论自身特性的语言。该概念立场也有助于更好地理解广义相对论（general relativity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多人对狭义相对论存在普遍误解，这些误解往往是因为使用牛顿力学的概念框架来理解相对论所导致的。因此，需要提供系统的指导和实例来帮助澄清这些错误认识。

Method: 本文采用概念分析与示例说明相结合的方法，通过提供引导性说明和具体实例来识别和纠正关于狭义相对论的常见误解。

Result: 研究指出，改用更符合狭义相对论自身特性的术语和概念框架来表述其原理，能够有效澄清常见的误解。

Conclusion: 采用狭义相对论自身的自然语言来理解其真理，不仅能有效消除常见误解，还有助于进一步深化对广义相对论的理解。

Abstract: We provide some guidance and examples to clear up common misconceptions about special relativity. These misconceptions often come from trying to express the truths of special relativity in Newtonian terms rather than in terms more natural to special relativity itself. This conceptual stance can also help in attaining a better understanding of general relativity.

### [33] [Maximal extension of Schwarzschild-like spacetimes in Lorentz gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21823)
*Mohsen Fathi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了洛伦兹规范理论（Lorentz gauge theory, LGT）中类史瓦西黑洞解的最大解析延拓，构建了Kruskal-Szekeres图及Carter-Penrose紧致化，发现该解与经典史瓦西黑洞具有相同的因果拓扑（causal topology），但在几何上不等价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在洛伦兹规范理论的框架下，类史瓦西黑洞解的完整几何结构尚未被充分分析。作者旨在通过构造该解的Kruskal-Szekeres延拓和Carter-Penrose图，揭示其因果结构与经典史瓦西解的异同。

Method: 首先利用Schwarzschild-Droste（SD）图和内行Eddington-Finkelstein（IEF）图分析径向零曲线（radial null curves），然后针对LGT几何构造改良的Kruskal-Szekeres（KS）图，最后给出标准的和正则的Carter-Penrose（CP）紧致化。

Result: KS延拓包含两个外部区域、一个黑洞区域和一个白洞区域。虽然共形骨架（conformal skeleton）与史瓦西解相似，但视界（horizon）的物理尺度、表面引力（surface gravity）以及恒定半径曲线均由参数$A_0$控制。当$A_0\neq1$时，该解在几何上与史瓦西解不等价，但具有相同的因果拓扑。

Conclusion: 该LGT黑洞解尽管在因果拓扑上与经典史瓦西黑洞一致，但由于参数$A_0$对几何量的调控，两者在几何上是不同的，这凸显了规范理论框架下黑洞解的独特性质。

Abstract: We study the maximal analytic extension of the Schwarzschild-like black hole solution in Lorentz gauge theory. The lapse function is $f(r)=A_0^{-2}-2\m/r$, so the horizon is located at $r_+=2\m A_0^2$ and the non-affinity coefficient of the horizon generator is $κ=1/(4\m A_0^4)$. We first analyze the radial null curves in the Schwarzschild-Droste (SD) and ingoing Eddington-Finkelstein (IEF) charts, and then construct the Kruskal-Szekeres (KS) chart adapted to the LGT geometry. The KS extension contains two exterior regions, a black-hole region and a white-hole region. We also present the standard and regular Carter-Penrose (CP) compactifications. The conformal skeleton is Schwarzschild-like, but the physical scale of the horizon, the surface gravity and the constant-radius curves remain controlled by $A_0$. Hence the solution has the same causal topology as Schwarzschild, while it is geometrically inequivalent to it when $A_0\neq1$.

### [34] [Quantitative Black Hole Imaging Laboratory with the Black Hole Vision App: I. Schwarzschild Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21887)
*Lior M. Burko*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推动广义相对论教育的教学范式转变，利用智能手机应用程序将移动设备转化为教育性相对论成像工具，使学生能够通过定量分析模拟黑洞成像来深入理解广义相对论核心概念。

Method: 研究采用层次化模块化设计，基于施瓦西时空实施定量分析：通过独立探针三角测量模拟施瓦西质量；利用雅可比映射表征各向异性坐标变换；通过积分坐标长度检验全局数值一致性；测量模拟李雅普诺夫指数量化近束缚轨道的指数不稳定性；运用亚像素偏心度约束限制时空对称性。

Result: 通过整合上述统计框架，研究实现了对模拟黑洞成像中物理信号与仪器噪声的有效区分，并建立了基于计量学协议的教学评估方法。

Conclusion: 该研究为广义相对论教育提供了创新的定量分析工具和教学范式，使学生能够借助智能手机应用和统计学方法，在模拟环境中探索黑洞物理的关键特征。

Abstract: This paper utilizes the {\it Black Hole Vision} smartphone application to catalyze a pedagogical shift in General Relativity education through the quantitative analysis of simulated black hole imaging. Presented here for the Schwarzschild spacetime, the investigation is designed with a hierarchical modularity suitable for undergraduate students, with an expanded version intended for graduate courses in General Relativity or Relativistic Astrophysics. By transforming the mobile device into an educational relativistic imaging tool, we triangulate the simulated Schwarzschild mass through independent probes and characterize anisotropic coordinate transformations via a Jacobian map. Global numerical consistency is investigated through integrated coordinate length, while the exponential instability of nearly bound orbits is quantified through a measurement of the simulated Lyapunov exponent. Finally, symmetry is constrained through a sub-pixel constraint on eccentricity in the simulated spacetime. By integrating this statistical framework, the paper enables students to explore the distinction between physical signatures and instrumental noise using established metrological protocols.

### [35] [Vacuum breakdown in a misaligned magnetized Kerr spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21910)
*Ruixin Yang,Songbai Chen,Jiliang Jing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）浸入与自旋轴倾斜的均匀磁场时的真空击穿现象，通过电磁不变量识别了由多个瓣状结构组成的动力学区（dyadoregion），分析了其随磁场倾角的变化，并估算了可用于正负电子对产生的电磁能量、束因子（beaming factor）以及等离子体的热力学性质，发现非对齐磁场比对磁场更有利于正负电子对产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解致密天体周围真空击穿产生正负电子对（electron-positron pair）的机制，该过程被认为是为伽马射线暴（gamma-ray bursts, GRBs）等高能天体物理暂现事件供能的关键。现有研究多考虑对齐磁场情形，而实际天体中的磁场方向可能与自旋轴存在夹角，因此需要系统研究倾斜磁场下的真空击穿特性。

Method: 通过电磁不变量（electromagnetic invariants）识别动力学区——即感应电场超过临界值$E_{\text{c}}=m_{e}^{2}c^{3}/(e\hbar)$的区域。分析该区域在不同磁场倾角下的形态变化，并计算可用于对产生的电磁能量。引入束因子（beaming factor）实现本征动力学区能量与观测到的各向同性能量（observed isotropic energy）之间的转换。同时评估所产生的正负电子-光子等离子体（$e^{+}e^{-}γ$ plasma）的热力学性质。

Result: 动力学区由多个瓣状结构（lobes）组成，其数量、大小和方向随磁场倾斜角度变化。等离子体初始状态以磁能为主导（magnetic dominance）。非对齐（misaligned）磁场普遍比对对齐（aligned）磁场更有利于正负电子对产生。

Conclusion: 非对齐磁场配置能更有效地促进真空击穿与正负电子对产生，这为理解伽马射线暴等高能暂现事件的能量来源提供了新的理论依据。相关结果有助于将本征的动力学区能量与观测到的各向同性能量进行转换，从而更准确地解释观测数据。

Abstract: Electron-positron ($e^{+}e^{-}$) pair creation by vacuum breakdown around compact objects is believed to power high-energy astrophysical transients like gamma-ray bursts (GRBs). In this work, we focus on vacuum breakdown around a Kerr black hole (BH) immersed in an asymptotically uniform magnetic field that is inclined with respect to the BH spin axis. The dyadoregion, the region where the induced electric field exceeds the critical value $E_{\text{c}}=m_{e}^{2}c^{3}/(e\hbar)$, is identified via the electromagnetic invariants. It is found that the dyadoregion consists of several lobes whose number, size, and orientation vary with the inclination. We also estimate the electromagnetic energy available for pair creation and derive a beaming factor that allows a conversion between the intrinsic dyadoregion energy and the observed isotropic energy. The thermodynamic properties of the resulting electron-positron-photon ($e^{+}e^{-}γ$) plasma are included, revealing an initial magnetic dominance. The evaluation of the minimum magnetic field required shows that misaligned magnetic fields generally favor pair creation more than aligned ones.

### [36] [On the Presence of a Tertiary Compact Object in GW190814](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21955)
*Lalit Pathak,Hemantakumar Phurailatpam,Achamveedu Gopakumar*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文通过对GW190814事件的32秒数据进行贝叶斯推断，分析视向加速度（LOSA）与残余轨道偏心率对引力波波形的联合影响。研究发现LOSA单独分析未发现显著信号（贝叶斯因子约0.22），联合分析得到非零参数估计（a/c≈-2.8×10⁻³ s⁻¹, e₀≈0.11），但贝叶斯因子约0.64不支持统计显著性；LOSA与偏心率之间存在强简并，非零估计值可能源于该简并性，而非物理信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视向加速度（line-of-sight acceleration, LOSA）与残余轨道偏心率（residual orbital eccentricity）对引力波旋近波形傅里叶相位的领头阶贡献呈现相似的频率依赖性，这使得小偏心率可能混淆并模拟LOSA效应。该研究旨在区分两者对GW190814事件的贡献，验证是否存在真正的LOSA信号。

Method: 采用IMRPhenomXPHM波形族作为LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA基线波形模型，并在其基础上加入领头阶LOSA修正与残余偏心率修正。使用GW190814事件的32秒数据，分别进行LOSA单独分析和LOSA与偏心率联合分析的贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）。

Result: LOSA单独分析中，相对于基线模型的贝叶斯因子（Bayes factor）约为0.22，未发现非零LOSA效应证据，与Hendriks等人的结果一致，但与Yang等人仅用4秒数据得到的结论相矛盾。联合分析中得到a/c≈-2.8×10⁻³ s⁻¹和e₀≈0.11的后验分布，但贝叶斯因子约为0.64，表明32秒数据不支持显著的LOSA或偏心率信号。贝叶斯运行显示LOSA与偏心率参数之间存在强相关性，表明两者的波形印迹存在显著简并（degeneracy）。

Conclusion: GW190814事件的32秒数据未提供支持LOSA或残余偏心率的显著证据；联合分析中得到的非零参数估计最可能源于LOSA与偏心率参数间的强简并性，而非真实的物理信号。这一结论与理论论证一致。

Abstract: Gravitational waves from merging compact binaries are sensitive to line-of-sight acceleration (LOSA) induced by a massive companion in their vicinity. Interestingly, the leading-order contributions of LOSA and residual orbital eccentricity to the Fourier phase of the inspiral waveform exhibit similar frequency dependence, raising the possibility that a small eccentricity could mimic LOSA effects in transient GW events such as GW190814. We perform Bayesian inference using the IMRPhenomXPHM waveform family as the baseline LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA waveform model, augmented with leading-order LOSA and residual eccentricity corrections while using 32 seconds of data associated with GW190814. For a LOSA-only analysis, we find no evidence for a non-zero LOSA effect in GW190814, with a Bayes factor relative to the baseline model of approximately 0.22, consistent with the findings of Hendriks et al. and in tension with the claim by Yang et al., who employed only 4 seconds of GW190814 data. In a joint analysis that includes both leading-order LOSA and eccentricity effects, we obtain informative posteriors for both parameters, with representative values a/c approximately -2.8 x 10^{-3} s^{-1} and e_0 approximately 0.11. However, the corresponding Bayes factor relative to the baseline model is approximately 0.64, suggesting that the 32-second data do not provide significant evidence for either LOSA or residual eccentricity in GW190814. Further, our Bayesian runs reveal a strong correlation between the LOSA and eccentricity parameters, indicating a significant degeneracy in their imprint on the inspiral phase. This finding is consistent with our theoretical arguments and most likely explains the non-zero parameter estimates obtained in the joint analysis.

### [37] [Thermodynamic acceptability of spherically symmetric perfect-fluid solutions in general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21990)
*Dina Demissenova,Nurzada Beissen,Kuantay Boshkayev,Hernando Quevedo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文将经典的爱因斯坦方程静态球对称理想流体解的物理可接受性条件扩展至热力学领域，提出一套基于相对论平衡热力学、熵泛函和Tolman温度关系的热力学可接受性判据，并以Tolman IV解为例验证其满足有限正熵泛函与Tolman平衡条件。该工作表明热力学一致性是Delgaty-Lake可接受性方案的自然扩展，可作为相对论内部解分类的必要判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 爱因斯坦方程的静态球对称理想流体解在相对论天体物理和恒星结构理论中具有核心地位。尽管存在大量数学上精确的解，但其中仅有少数满足正则性、物质变量正性和因果声速传播等物理可接受条件。本研究旨在将经典物理可接受性概念扩展至热力学层面，为相对论恒星模型建立一套热力学可接受性判据。

Method: 本研究采用相对论平衡热力学（relativistic equilibrium thermodynamics）框架，引入熵泛函（entropy functionals）和Tolman温度关系（Tolman temperature relation），构建热力学可接受性条件的系统表述。随后以Tolman IV解作为显式算例，验证该解是否满足这些热力学条件。

Result: 分析表明，Tolman IV解具有有限且为正的平衡熵泛函，并与Tolman平衡条件一致。这一结果证实了热力学可接受性判据在具体解上的可应用性。

Conclusion: 热力学一致性为Delgaty-Lake可接受性方案提供了自然扩展，并可能构成相对论内部解分类中的一项必要判据。

Abstract: Static spherically symmetric perfect-fluid solutions of Einstein's equations play a central role in relativistic astrophysics and stellar structure theory. While many exact solutions satisfy Einstein's equations mathematically, only a limited subset satisfies physically acceptable conditions such as regularity, positivity of matter variables, and causal sound propagation. In this work, the classical concept of physical acceptability is extended to include thermodynamic considerations. Using relativistic equilibrium thermodynamics, entropy functionals, and the Tolman temperature relation, we formulate a set of thermodynamic acceptability conditions for relativistic stellar models. The Tolman IV solution is analyzed as an explicit example. We show that this solution admits a finite and positive equilibrium entropy functional consistent with the Tolman equilibrium condition. This analysis suggests that thermodynamic consistency provides a natural extension of the Delgaty-Lake acceptability program and may constitute an essential criterion in the classification of relativistic interior solutions.

### [38] [Classical Renormalization Group Equations for General Relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22037)
*F. Gutiérrez,K. Falls,A. Codello*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文为经典重整化群（RG）流方程建立了严格的数学基础，证明Legendre变换将经典Polchinski方程精确映射到该RG方程，从而确立了引力有效作用量等效精确RG方程之间的对偶性，为广义相对论两体问题和引力波物理奠定了严格的形式化框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 前序工作arXiv:2510.27676以启发式方式推导了一个非微扰经典重整化群（renormalisation group, RG）流方程，用于处理广义相对论中的强相互作用问题（尤其是两体问题）。尽管该方程已展示出复现后闵可夫斯基展开（Post-Minkowskian, PM）和1PN后牛顿（Post-Newtonian）作用量的计算效率，但其形式推导尚不严格，需要建立正式的数学基础。

Method: 本文通过数学推导证明，经典Polchinski方程经Legendre变换（Legendre transform）后精确等价于此前提出的经典RG流方程。这一变换建立了两种精确RG方程（exact RG equations）之间的对偶关系（duality），使得引力有效作用量（gravitational effective action）的重整化群流获得严格表述。

Result: 建立了经典Polchinski方程与经典RG流方程之间的精确对偶性，为引力有效作用量的重整化群流提供了严格的形式化基础。

Conclusion: 结合arXiv:2510.27676的成功应用，本文工作巩固了经典RG框架作为广义相对论两体问题及引力波物理（gravitational wave physics）中一种强大且严格的新方法。该对偶性证明表明，经典RG方程具备严谨的理论根基，适用于强引力系统的非微扰处理。

Abstract: In a companion paper arXiv:2510.27676, we introduced a non-perturbative classical renormalisation group (RG) flow equation as a novel method for treating strongly interacting problems in general relativity, with a prominent application to the two-body problem. While we demonstrated that it reproduces perturbation theory, via the Post-Minkowskian (PM) expansion, and its computational efficiency in reproducing the 1PN Post-Newtonian action, its derivation was heuristic. In this work, we place this flow equation on a firm formal foundation. In particular, we demonstrate that a Legendre transform maps the classical analogue of the Polchinski equation precisely to our classical RG equation. This establishes a duality between equivalent, exact RG equations for the gravitational effective action. The result, combined with the successful applications in arXiv:2510.27676, solidifies the classical RG framework as a powerful and rigorous new approach to the general relativistic two-body problem and gravitational wave physics.

</details>


### [39] [Landauer entropy of spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22172)
*J. M. Isidro,B. Koch,A. Rincon*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于朗道尔原理（Landauer's principle）为静态球对称时空（static, spherically symmetric spacetime）的熵给出几何定义，通过测地线汇（congruence of geodesics）的表面积分定义熵，并在温和假设下建立了该熵函数（Landauer 熵）的第二定律（second law），并将其与贝肯斯坦-霍金熵（Bekenstein-Hawking entropy）联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为静态球对称时空的熵提供基于朗道尔原理的几何定义，并建立其与已有黑洞熵概念（如贝肯斯坦-霍金熵）的联系。

Method: 基于朗道尔原理，考虑穿过某一曲面的测地线汇，将构成测地线汇的每条测地线的熵在曲面上积分，从而定义整个测地线汇的熵（即 Landauer 熵）。

Result: 在若干温和假设下，证明了所定义的 Landauer 熵函数满足第二定律，并将其与贝肯斯坦-霍金熵进行了关联。

Conclusion: 该工作为时空熵提供了一种几何化的定义方式，并证明了其热力学一致性，拓展了朗道尔原理在广义相对论（general relativity）中的应用。

Abstract: Based on Landauer's principle, we provide a geometrical definition for the entropy of a given static, spherically symmetric spacetime. Considering a congruence of geodesics across a surface, one defines the entropy of a congruence as the surface integral of the entropy of the constituent geodesics. Under certain mild assumptions, we establish a second law for the entropy function thus defined (Landauer entropy), and relate it to Bekenstein-Hawking entropy.

### [40] [Holographic Dark Energy with Hubble Radius as an Infrared Cutoff in Einstein-Cartan Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22143)
*Yongjun Yun,Jungjai Lee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在 Einstein-Cartan 引力框架下，以哈勃半径作为红外截断研究非相互作用的全息暗能量（HDE），通过引入自旋流体导出扭率标量的标度行为 $Φ\sim a^{-3}$，发现扭率效应使状态方程向负值偏移，可穿越幻影分界线，且预测宇宙加速逐渐减弱，与 DESI 观测潜在一致；同时导出了存在扭率时宇宙距离对偶关系的修正形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有全息暗能量模型在引入扭率标量时往往依赖人为 ansatz 确定其演化行为，缺乏第一性原理推导；同时，Einstein-Cartan 引力中扭率对暗能量动力学的影响尚未被系统研究。

Method: 从作用量原理导出 Einstein-Cartan 方程，引入扭率标量（torsion scalar）得到类弗里德曼方程；采用 Weyssenhoff 自旋流体（Weyssenhoff spin fluid）模型，在不引入额外假设的条件下确定扭率标量的标度行为 $Φ\sim a^{-3}$。

Result: 扭率标量将全息暗能量的状态方程从无扭率时的类尘埃值推向负值，在弱扭率 regime $|Φ/H| < 1$ 下可接近 $ω_X \simeq -1$ 并穿越幻影分界线（phantom divide）；模型预测宇宙加速逐渐减弱，与 DESI 观测潜在一致；宇宙距离对偶关系修正为 $d_L = d_A (1+z)^2 (1+η)$，其中偏差参数 $η\sim \int_{t_S}^{t_O} dt a^{-3}$。

Conclusion: Einstein-Cartan 引力框架下的全息暗能量模型具有可行性，为后续似然分析（likelihood analyses）提供了理论框架。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate non-interacting holographic dark energy (HDE) with the Hubble radius as the infrared cutoff in Einstein-Cartan gravity. We derive the Einstein-Cartan equations from the action principle and obtain Friedmann-like equations by introducing a torsion scalar. Considering a Weyssenhoff spin fluid, we determine the scaling behavior of the torsion scalar as $Φ\sim a^{-3}$ without introducing an ad hoc ansatz, resolving the ansatz problem of previous torsion scalar scenarios. In the absence of interactions between dark matter and dark energy, the torsion scalar shifts the equation of state for holographic dark energy toward negative values from the dust-like value obtained in HDE without torsion, making cosmic acceleration possible. In particular, the resulting equation of state can approach $ω_X \simeq -1$ and cross the phantom divide within the weak torsion regime $|Φ/H| < 1$. The model predicts a dynamical equation of state in which cosmic acceleration gradually weakens, potentially consistent with recent DESI observations. In spacetimes with torsion, the cosmic distance duality relation between the luminosity distance $d_L$ and the angular diameter distance $d_A$ is modified as $d_L = d_A (1+z)^2 (1+η)$. In the presence of the torsion scalar, we show that the standard relation between redshift and the scale factor is preserved, while the deviation parameter arising from torsion effects is determined as $η\sim \int_{t_S}^{t_O} dt a^{-3}$, where $t_S$ and $t_O$ denote the emission time at the source and the observation time at the observer, respectively. Overall, our results support the feasibility of the model and provide a theoretical framework for preparing likelihood analyses.
