### [41] [Vector modes in Type 3 New GR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22329)
*Alexey Golovnev*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文反驳了近期关于New GR模型中标量-矢量-张量分解（scalar-vector-tensor decomposition）中矢量模式被遗漏的论断，指出其错误根源在于将约束方程（constraint equations）代入拉格朗日量（Lagrangian）进行分析，而非基于运动方程（equations of motion）。以第三类New GR的矢量模式为例，作者证明这些模式实际上是非动力学的（non-dynamical）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清近期关于New GR模型中线性化弱引力极限（linearised weak gravity limit）下动力学模式计数（degree-of-freedom count）的争议，指出相关批评者因分析方法不当导致的错误结论。

Method: 选取第三类New GR（New GR of Type 3）中的矢量模式作为基本案例，对比分析基于运动方程与基于将约束方程代入二次拉格朗日密度（quadratic Lagrangian density）这两种方法所得结果的差异，从而揭示后者的错误。

Result: 批评者认为被遗漏的动力学位模式实际上是非动力学的，其错误源于将约束方程代入拉格朗日量进行分析，而非直接考察运动方程。

Conclusion: 核心结论是：在对约束系统（constrained system）进行分析时，不应将约束方程直接代入拉格朗日量，否则会导致对模式动力学性质的错误判断。

Abstract: Some time ago, we published the full count of degrees of freedom in the linearised weak gravity limit of arbitrary New GR models. We did it by considering the linear equations of motion and presented a thorough analysis with no ambiguity left. A bit later, we generalised it to linear cosmological perturbations and discussed the strong coupling issues that appear already at this level. Recently, there were claims that some dynamical modes had been missed in our work. However, the authors of the new claims did not look at the equations of motion and analysed the quadratic Lagrangian densities instead. In this paper, I take one of the most elementary cases, namely the vector modes in New GR of Type 3, and show what was their mistake that had led them to claiming that those were dynamical. The main message: Do not substitute constraint equations into a Lagrangian.

### [42] [Analytical solutions for timelike orbits around Damour-Solodukhin wormholes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22187)
*Shao-Chen Ho,Yo-Chung Ko,Tien Hsieh,Da-Shin Lee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该文对 Damour-Solodukhin 虫洞的类时测地线进行了完整的解析研究，揭示了喉道处根的简并性如何导致 ISCO、轨迹发散行为以及可观测特征，并给出了包括螺旋内落与穿越轨道在内的精确解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究 Damour-Solodukhin 虫洞周围的时间型测地线（timelike geodesics）动力学，特别是与 Schwarzschild 黑洞的可观测区分特征。

Method: 利用 Mino 时间参数化（Mino-time parametrization），将粒子轨迹解析为不完全椭圆积分（incomplete elliptic integrals）的闭合形式解，并分析径向势的根结构及其退化配置。

Result: 虫洞喉道（throat）在特定参数下与径向势的其它根形成二重、三重甚至四重简并；三重根配置决定了最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit, ISCO）；当喉道对应重根时，粒子的方位角和坐标时间在趋近喉道时出现对数或幂律发散；当喉道为单根时，粒子可平滑穿越两个渐近平直区域；推导了喉道附近的同宿解（homoclinic solutions）及相应的 Lyapunov 指数。

Conclusion: 虫洞喉道处势根的简并结构是产生区别于黑洞的观测特征（如 ISCO 位置变化、方位角发散、穿越轨道）的关键；解析解为未来引力波或天体测量实验中的虫洞识别提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We investigate timelike geodesics around Damour-Solodukhin wormholes, which are Schwarzschild-like geometries characterized by a deformation parameter $λ$ that determines the radius of the throat, $r_{\rm th}$. The radial potential admits four roots, including the throat radius itself, allowing the throat to merge with other roots and form double, triple, and quartic degeneracies. In particular, triple-root configurations associated with the throat determine the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO), providing a potential observational distinction from Schwarzschild black holes. Using the Mino-time parametrization, we derive particle trajectories with closed-form analytical solutions in terms of incomplete elliptic integrals for both bound and unbound motion. In particular, we focus on double or triple roots are located at the throat, the azimuthal angle and coordinate time exhibit logarithmic or power-law divergences as the particle approaches the throat. By contrast, trajectories remain regular when the throat corresponds to a simple root, allowing particles to traverse smoothly between the two asymptotically flat regions. We also derive exact homoclinic solutions associated with the throat and compute the corresponding Lyapunov exponent. In addition, inspiral and plunge trajectories through the throat are analyzed. These results provide analytic insights into particle dynamics and possible observational signatures of the wormholes.

### [43] [Constraints on Schwarzschild Black Hole in a Generalized Dehnen-Type $(1,4,γ)$ Dark Matter Halo via the S2 Star Orbit around Sgr A$^\star$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22210)
*Tursunali Xamidov,Sanjar Shaymatov,Qiang Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文通过广义的Schwarzschild–Dehnen黑洞-暗物质晕系统模型，利用S2星的轨道进动数据和MCMC分析，首次在任意暗物质晕参数γ下对Sgr A*周围的暗物质分布进行了观测约束，得到了最佳拟合参数和95%置信上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超大质量黑洞（supermassive black hole）周围的暗物质（dark matter, DM）晕分布可能对星系中心附近的恒星动力学留下可观测的印记。已有研究仅限于暗物质晕参数γ的特定取值，缺乏一般性。

Method: 采用广义的Schwarzschild–Dehnen黑洞-暗物质晕（Schwarzschild–Dehnen BH-DM）解，推导了任意γ参数下的S2星运动方程和单轨道周期内的近日点进动（perihelion shift）；利用Do等人和Gillessen等人两组S2星观测数据，通过马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）方法对模型参数进行约束。

Result: Do等人数据组的最佳拟合值为$γ=1.18^{+1.03}_{-0.81}$, $ρ_s=0.37^{+0.42}_{-0.29}$, $r_s=0.05^{+0.05}_{-0.03}$；Gillessen等人数据组的最佳拟合值为$γ=1.23^{+1.01}_{-0.85}$, $ρ_s=0.31^{+0.44}_{-0.26}$, $r_s=0.14^{+0.18}_{-0.10}$。95%置信上限分别为$γ<2.66(2.67)$, $ρ_s<0.93(0.92)$, $r_s<0.16(0.52)$。

Conclusion: 精确的恒星轨道测量可以对超大质量黑洞周围的暗物质晕分布提供有意义的观测约束，并为银河系中心Sgr A*的暗物质环境提供新的认识。

Abstract: The distribution of dark matter (DM) halo around supermassive black holes (BHs) may leave observable imprints on stellar dynamics near galactic centers. Motivated by this, we investigate the orbital motion of the S2 star in the spacetime of a recently derived generalized Schwarzschild BH solution embedded in a Dehnen-type $(1,4,γ)$ DM halo, considering it as a possible model for Sgr A$^{\star}$ at the center of the Milky Way. Unlike previous studies restricted to specific values of the halo parameter $γ$, the present solution describes the fully generalized case with arbitrary $γ$. We derive the corresponding equations of motion and obtain the associated perihelion shift over one orbital period. Using observational data of the S2 star, we constrain the parameters of the Schwarzschild--Dehnen BH-DM system through a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) analysis. Our results yield the best-fit values $γ= 1.18^{+1.03}_{-0.81}$ $(1.23^{+1.01}_{-0.85})$, $ρ_s = 0.37^{+0.42}_{-0.29}$ $(0.31^{+0.44}_{-0.26})$, and $r_s = 0.05^{+0.05}_{-0.03}$ $(0.14^{+0.18}_{-0.10})$ for observational data of Do et al.~\cite{Do19} and Gillessen et al.~\cite{Gillessen17ApJ}, respectively. We further obtain the corresponding 95\% confidence upper bounds: $γ< 2.66$ $(2.67)$, $ρ_s < 0.93$ $(0.92)$, and $r_s < 0.16$ $(0.52)$. These results demonstrate that precise stellar orbit measurements can provide meaningful constraints on the DM halo distributions surrounding supermassive BHs and may offer insights into the DM environment of Sgr A$^{\star}$ at the center of the Milky Way.

### [44] [Dark Energy in Ghost-free non-local Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22348)
*S. D. Odintsov,V. K. Oikonomou,G. S. Sharov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究检验了无鬼非定域引力（ghost-free non-local gravity）在晚期宇宙动力学中的表现，发现其在与Pantheon+、DESI、重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillations）和哈勃参数$H(z)$数据对比时与$Λ$CDM模型相当，但加入宇宙微波背景辐射（cosmic microwave background, CMB）数据后表现不佳；相比之下，广义指数$F(R)$引力模型在所有数据组合测试中均更优，其有效暗能量状态方程（equation of state）从幽灵（phantom）相演化至精粹（quintessence）相。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究的动机在于探索无鬼非定域引力模型在晚期宇宙动力学（late-time dynamics）中的可行性，并利用多种最新的天文观测数据对其进行严格的观测检验与比较。

Method: 研究方法包括将无鬼非定域引力模型的可行解与Pantheon+ Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernovae）目录、暗能量光谱仪（Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument, DESI）、重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillations）测量以及$H(z)$哈勃参数估计等观测数据进行对比检验，并最终引入CMB数据进行联合测试。

Result: 无鬼非定域引力模型在仅使用Pantheon+、DESI和$H(z)$数据时表现成功，但与$Λ$CDM模型可比；然而当加入CMB数据后该模型遇到困难。广义指数$F(R)$模型在所有数据（含CMB）的测试中更为成功，其有效暗能量状态方程（effective dark energy equation of state）从幽灵（phantom）相演化至精粹（quintessence）相，而无鬼非定域模型仅表现出精粹行为。

Conclusion: 无鬼非定域引力模型仅在部分观测数据（Pantheon+、DESI、$H(z)$）下成立；在包含CMB的全部数据测试中，广义指数$F(R)$模型优于$Λ$CDM模型（依据$χ^2$统计量（chi-square statistics）和信息准则（information criteria）），且满足可行性条件（viability conditions）。

Abstract: Ghost-free non-local gravity is investigated with regards to its late-time dynamics. Viable solutions in this model are confronted with the observational data including the Pantheon+ catalogue of Type Ia supernovae, the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument, the measurements of baryon acoustic oscillations and the Hubble parameter estimations $H(z)$. The ghost-free non-local gravity is found to be successful in these tests in comparison to the $Λ$CDM model and can be also comparable with the generalized exponential $F(R)$ gravity scenario. However the model encounters difficulties when the data from the above observations and the cosmic microwave background radiation data are combined. In tests with the whole set of Pantheon+, DESI, $H(z)$ and CMB data, the generalized exponential $F(R)$ model is essentially more successful. This success is related with the dynamical behavior of its effective dark energy equation of state evolving from a phantom to a quintessence phase during the late-time epoch, whereas the ghost-free non-local model demonstrates only a quintessence behavior. Hence the ghost-free non-local gravity scenario is successful only when the Pantheon+, DESI and $H(z)$ data are considered. The generalized exponential $F(R)$ model satisfies the viability conditions and in tests with all observational data including CMB surpasses the $Λ$CDM model in $χ^2$ statistics and also with information criteria.

### [45] [Black Hole Entropy Beyond the Wald Term in Nonminimally Coupled Gravity: A Covariant Phase Space Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22429)
*Jia-Zhou Liu,Shan-Ping Wu,Shao-Wen Wei,Yu-Xiao Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用协变相空间形式（covariant phase space formalism）研究了具有非最小物质-曲率耦合的微分同胚不变理论（diffeomorphism-invariant theories）中静态球对称黑洞的熵。对于物质场无法光滑延拓至正则分叉面（regular bifurcation surface）的情况，黑洞视界表面荷变分（horizon surface charge variation）可能包含Wald熵密度（Wald entropy density）未涵盖的有限贡献，文章给出了完整的第一定律熵分解 \(S_{\mathrm H}=S_{\mathrm W}+S_1+ΔS\)，并通过Kalb-Ramond、bumblebee和扩展Gauss-Bonnet黑洞实例验证了各修正项的存在与否。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在具有非最小物质-曲率耦合的微分同胚不变引力理论中，标准的Wald熵构造要求物质场在正则分叉面上光滑可延拓，但许多实际模型（如Kalb-Ramond场、bumblebee场等）不满足这一条件，因此需要检验Wald熵密度是否仍然足够，或者是否需要使用完整的视界面荷变分来定义黑洞熵。

Method: 采用协变相空间形式（covariant phase space formalism），在直接变分作用量并扣除普通功项（work terms）后，将进入热力学第一定律的黑洞熵分解为三部分：Wald熵 \(S_{\mathrm W}\)、Noether荷的非Wald部分 \(S_1\) 以及视界面荷变分的剩余可积部分 \(ΔS\)。然后将该判据应用于Kalb-Ramond、bumblebee和扩展Gauss-Bonnet三种具体黑洞模型进行检验。

Result: 对于正则Kalb-Ramond分支，有 \(S_{\mathrm H}=S_{\mathrm W}\)，即仅Wald熵足够；bumblebee分支要么出现 \(S_1=0\) 且 \(ΔS\neq0\)，要么 \(S_1\) 与 \(ΔS\) 相互抵消；Weyl-vector扩展Gauss-Bonnet例子则需要同时包含 \(S_1\) 和 \(ΔS\) 两项修正。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个直接判据，用于检验在非最小耦合且物质场无法光滑延拓的正则分叉面上，是否仅需Wald熵密度即可定义黑洞熵，还是必须使用完整的视界面荷变分。

Abstract: We study the entropy of static, spherically symmetric black holes in diffeomorphism-invariant theories with nonminimal matter--curvature couplings, using the covariant phase space formalism. For regular bifurcate Killing horizons, the Iyer--Wald construction gives the standard Wald entropy. If a matter field cannot be smoothly extended to the regular bifurcation surface, however, the horizon surface charge variation can contain finite contributions that are not included in the Wald entropy density. In the representative obtained by directly varying the action, and after ordinary work terms are subtracted, we decompose the entropy entering the first law of black hole thermodynamics as \(S_{\mathrm H}=S_{\mathrm W}+S_1+ΔS\). Here \(S_{\mathrm W}\) is the Wald entropy, \(S_1\) is the non-Wald part of the Noether charge, and \(ΔS\) is the remaining integrable part of the horizon surface charge variation. Applying this criterion to Kalb--Ramond, bumblebee, and extended Gauss--Bonnet black holes, we find that the regular Kalb--Ramond branch has \(S_{\mathrm H}=S_{\mathrm W}\), the bumblebee branches yield either \(S_1=0\) with \(ΔS\neq0\) or a cancellation between \(S_1\) and \(ΔS\), and the Weyl-vector extended Gauss--Bonnet examples require both corrections. This gives a direct test of whether the Wald entropy density is sufficient, or whether the full horizon surface charge variation has to be used.

</details>


### [46] [Entropic route to Brown-York tensor: A unified framework for null and timelike hypersurfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22434)
*Krishnakanta Bhattacharya,Bhera Ram,Bibhas Ranjan Majhi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 基于Padmanabhan熵泛函，本文证明其在不同引力理论（包括标量-张量理论）中均可统一导出Brown-York张量，揭示了准局域引力量的变分结构及其与边界动量的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Padmanabhan熵泛函最初用于导出爱因斯坦场方程并揭示引力的涌现（emergent）性质，但其适用性是否超越广义相对论尚不清楚。本文旨在验证该熵泛函在更广泛理论框架下的鲁棒性，并探索其与准局域引力量（quasi-local gravitational quantities）之间的深层联系。

Method: 采用相同的熵密度（entropy density）形式，通过变分方法在类时和类光超曲面上投影正则动量（canonical momentum）共轭于法向量，从而自然导出Brown-York (BY) 张量。进一步将该构造推广至标量-张量理论（scalar-tensor theories），检验熵泛函能否复现运动方程及相应的BY张量。

Result: Brown-York张量作为法向量共轭正则动量的投影在类时和类光超曲面上自然出现，并揭示了类光BY张量的非对称（non-symmetric）结构差异。在标量-张量理论中，熵公式成功复现了预期的运动方程及BY张量，同时阐明了非最小耦合标量场（non-minimally coupled scalar field）导致的BY张量非守恒（non-conservation）性质。

Conclusion: 熵基公式为准局域引力量提供了一致的变分解释（variational interpretation），揭示了连接体动力学（bulk dynamics）与边界动量（boundary momentum）的共同底层结构，表明Padmanabhan熵泛函具有超越广义相对论的广泛适用性。

Abstract: Building on Padmanabhan's entropy functional, originally introduced to derive Einstein's equations and highlight the emergent nature of gravity, we demonstrate its robustness in a broader context. Using the same entropy density, we show that the Brown-York (BY) tensor arises naturally as the projection of the canonical momentum conjugate to the normal vectors on the relevant hypersurface, thereby providing a common construction applicable to both timelike and null hypersurfaces. This perspective also offers insight into the structural differences of the null BY tensor, including its non-symmetric character. We further extend the analysis to scalar-tensor theories, showing that the entropy-based formulation reproduces the expected equations of motion along with the corresponding BY tensor, and, clarifies its non-conservation in the presence of additional scalar field which is non-minimally coupled. Our results provide a coherent variational interpretation of quasi-local gravitational quantities and reveal a common underlying structure linking bulk dynamics and boundary momentum.

</details>


### [47] [Black hole dark monopole system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22495)
*Marek Rogatko*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究可见和暗物质（dark matter）扇区中，位于磁单极（magnetic pole）或磁荷黑洞（magnetically charged black hole）附近的电荷系统的角动量特性，揭示静电荷在静态磁源周围仍可产生角动量，并在大尺度上表现为稳态轴对称磁荷黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索可见扇区与暗物质扇区中，静电荷在磁单极或磁荷黑洞附近时是否具有非平凡的角动量行为，并考察暗光子（dark photon）理论下电荷扰动的长程引力效应。

Method: 通过分析可见和暗物质扇区中静电荷在磁单极附近的角动量表达式，以及在暗光子理论框架下，将球对称静态磁荷黑洞外的电荷视为微扰（perturbation），研究其在大距离下的渐近行为。

Result: 发现即使电荷静止，系统仍具有非零角动量；在暗光子理论中，球对称静态磁荷黑洞外的静电荷扰动在大距离下等价于一个稳态轴对称（stationary axisymmetric）磁荷黑洞。

Conclusion: 静电荷在静态磁源附近可产生角动量，且暗光子理论中电荷微扰会导致黑洞的轴对称变形，暗示可见与暗物质扇区间的电磁耦合（electromagnetic coupling）可能具有重要的天体物理和理论意义。

Abstract: We scrutinize properties of electrical charges bounded to visible and dark matter sectors, in the vicinity of a magnetic poles of both sectors. It turns out that the considered system has an angular momentum despite the charges are at rest. On the other hand, investigation the behavior of electric charges of visible and hidden sectors held at rest outside a magnetically charged black hole, discloses that even if the electric charge are regarded as perturbations on a spherically symmetric magnetic static black hole in dark photon theory, at large distances it looks like a stationary axisymmetric magnetically charged black hole.

</details>


### [48] [Dynamics of Binary System around a Supermassive Black Hole :Binary Scattering and Eccentric vZLK Oscillations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22525)
*Kei-ichi Maeda,Hirotada Okawa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了围绕超大质量黑洞（SMBH）的双星动力学，涵盖非束缚轨道上的双星散射和束缚轨道上的偏心von Zeipel-Lidov-Kozai（vZLK）振荡。在非束缚轨道中识别出四种散射机制；束缚轨道中的vZLK机制呈现散射型振荡特征，与标准情况存在质的区别。研究提出了星系核中近心点驱动的潮汐动力学统一图景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解围绕超大质量黑洞（SMBH）的双星动力学行为，特别是非束缚轨道中的散射过程与束缚轨道中的偏心von Zeipel-Lidov-Kozai（vZLK）振荡，以建立星系核中潮汐相互作用的统一物理图像。

Method: 在Kerr时空的局部惯性系（local inertial frame）中描述运动，潮汐效应通过黎曼曲率（Riemann curvature）编码。分别分析了非束缚轨道（抛射和双曲轨道）和束缚偏心轨道（椭圆轨道）两种情形。

Result: 非束缚轨道中，根据双星半长轴识别出绝热、潮汐影响、混沌和潮汐瓦解四种散射机制；软双星在近心点附近的潮汐相互作用导致强偏心率激发和轨道参数大幅变化。束缚偏心轨道中，vZLK机制的z方向角动量近似守恒，但演化呈阶梯状变化，由重复的近心点通过驱动，表现为散射型vZLK振荡。SMBH的自转对振荡轮廓有影响，但小于初始轨道参数的影响。

Conclusion: 这些结果表明存在一个近心点驱动的潮汐动力学统一图景，适用于星系核中的双星系统。

Abstract: We study the dynamics of a binary orbiting a supermassive black hole (SMBH), focusing on both binary scattering in unbound orbits and eccentric von Zeipel-Lidov-Kozai (vZLK) oscillations in bound orbits. The motion is described in a local inertial frame in Kerr spacetime, where tidal effects are encoded in the Riemann curvature.
  For unbound (parabolic and hyperbolic) orbits, we identify four scattering regimes-adiabatic, tidally affected, chaotic, and disruptive-depending on the binary semi-major axis. As the binary becomes softer, tidal interactions near periapsis lead to strong eccentricity excitation, large changes in the orbital parameters, and eventually chaotic behavior or tidal disruption, with a sensitive dependence on the argument of periapsis.
  For eccentric bound (elliptic) orbits, the vZLK mechanism differs qualitatively from the standard one, although the $z$-component of the angular momentum in the local inertial frame remains approximately conserved. The evolution proceeds on a dynamical timescale and exhibits step-like changes driven by repeated periapsis passages, which can be interpreted as a sequence of scattering events. We refer to this behavior as scattering-type vZLK oscillations.
  The rotation of the SMBH also modifies the oscillation profiles, although its effect is less significant than the dependence on the initial orbital parameters. These results suggest a unified picture of periapsis-driven tidal dynamics in galactic nuclei.

</details>


### [49] [Cosmological Singularities and Quantum Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22623)
*Samuel W. P. Oliveira,Alexander Yu. Kamenshchik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了量子粒子穿越三类宇宙学奇点（big bang-big crunch, big rip, big brake）的可能性，通过求解狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）发现旋量粒子（spinors）的Fock空间可无奇异地构造，表明费米子（fermions）能够穿越这些奇点，而标量粒子（scalar particles）则无法实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验量子粒子是否能够穿越三类宇宙学奇点（大爆炸-大挤压、大撕裂、大刹车），以理解奇点附近基本粒子的行为。

Method: 对旋量场写出狄拉克方程（Dirac equation），选择合适的基函数参数化，得到对应的二阶微分方程并求解。

Result: 三类奇点情形下，二阶微分方程均有两个无奇异（non-singular）的独立解，从而可构造旋量粒子的Fock空间（Fock space）；但对标量粒子（scalar particles）无法实现，且更换参数化方式亦无效。

Conclusion: 费米子（fermions）在穿越宇宙学奇点时比玻色子（bosons）更具韧性，旋量粒子能够穿越三类奇点而标量粒子不能。

Abstract: We study if there is an opportunity to describe quantum particles in the vicinity of three types of cosmological singularities, big bang-big crunch, big rip and big brake. Writing down the Dirac equation for spinors, and choosing a convenient parametrization for basis functions of the spinor field, we show that the corresponding second-order differential equation has two independent solutions which are non-singular in the case of all three types of singularities. That permits us to construct the Fock space for the spinor particles and to interprete this fact as their opportunity to cross these cosmological singularities. We show also that this is impossible to do for scalar particles and changing the parametrization does not help. Thus, fermions look more resilient to the passage of the cosmological singularities than bosons.

</details>


### [50] [Topological Thermodynamics of Generalized Bardeen Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22686)
*A. A. M. Silva,M. H. Macedo,R. R. Landim*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用广义离壳亥姆霍兹自由能方法（generalized off-shell Helmholtz free energy method），在拓扑框架下研究了广义巴丁黑洞（generalized Bardeen black hole）的热力学性质，通过构造矢量场并分析其零点与绕数（winding number），揭示了正则化参数对热力学稳定性与相结构的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Neves 和 Saa 引入了一个包含 Hayward、Bardeen 和 Simpson-Visser 几何作为特例的双参数时空，本文旨在在此框架下系统地研究广义巴丁黑洞的热力学性质，并探讨正则化参数如何影响其热力学稳定性与相变行为。

Method: 采用广义离壳亥姆霍兹自由能方法（generalized off-shell Helmholtz free energy method），在拓扑框架下构造关联的矢量场，通过分析其零点并计算绕数（winding number）来对热力学分支进行分类，并识别与相变相关的临界点。

Result: 正则黑洞构型（regular black hole configurations）表现出两个拓扑缺陷（topological defects），绕数相反，导致总拓扑电荷（total topological charge）为零；而 Schwarzschild 情形则仅包含单个不稳定分支。

Conclusion: 研究结果展示了正则化参数如何影响时空的热力学稳定性与相结构。

Abstract: Neves and Saa introduced a two parameter spacetime that includes the Hayward, Bardeen, and Simpson-Visser geometries as particular cases. In this work, we employ the generalized off-shell Helmholtz free energy method to investigate the thermodynamic properties of the generalized Bardeen black hole within a topological framework. We construct the associated vector field and analyze its zeros, whose winding numbers allow us to classify the thermodynamic branches and identify critical points associated with phase transitions. The regular black hole configurations exhibit two topological defects with opposite winding numbers, resulting in a vanishing total topological charge, while the Schwarzschild case contains a single unstable branch. Our results demonstrate how the regularization parameters affect the thermodynamic stability and phase structure of the spacetime.

</details>


### [51] [Dimming of Photon Ring due to Photon-Axion Conversion around Kerr Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22696)
*Rahul Dhyani,Sauvik Sen,Indrani Banerjee,Ashmita Chakraborty,Arindam Chatterjee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了旋转克尔黑洞（Kerr black hole）附近的光子-轴子转换（photon-axion conversion）过程，发现强引力场将光子束缚在近圆形轨道上从而有效延长路径长度，增强了转换效率。通过数值计算光子路径长度，分析了各关键参数对转换概率及光子谱光度（spectral luminosity）减暗效应的影响，指出旋转黑洞比静态黑洞表现出更显著的减暗效应。未来高分辨率X射线/伽马射线望远镜若能观测到此类减暗，将为轴子质量及其与光子耦合提供有趣约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索旋转克尔黑洞附近强引力区域中光子-轴子转换的可观测信号，揭示这一过程对黑洞周围辐射特性的影响，并为暗物质候选者——轴子（axion）的存在提供间接探测途径。

Method: 基于数值方法计算靠近光子区域（photon region）的光子路径长度，系统分析光子频率（photon frequency）、轴子质量（axion mass）、光子-轴子耦合强度（photon-axion coupling）、磁场强度（magnetic field strength）、等离子体密度（plasma density）以及黑洞自旋（black hole spin）等参数对转换概率和光子谱光度减暗程度的影响。

Result: 转换在高频段（X射线和伽马射线）效率最高；有效转换的频率窗口随着光子-轴子耦合增强而变宽，随电子密度和轴子质量减小而变宽。光子谱光度减暗幅度主要取决于磁场、光子-轴子耦合强度以及黑洞自旋。旋转黑洞比静态黑洞表现出更显著的减暗效应。

Conclusion: 若未来分辨率达到约10^{-5}角秒的X射线/伽马射线望远镜观测到光子谱光度出现减暗，可为轴子质量及其与光子的耦合强度提供有意义的约束，从而推动轴子物理及相关暗物质研究的进展。

Abstract: We investigate photon-axion conversion in the vicinity of rotating Kerr black holes where strong gravity traps photons on near-circular trajectories, effectively enhancing the path length. We explore the observable signatures of such a conversion near the photon region. The process, driven by ambient magnetic fields, is significantly more efficient around supermassive black holes such as M87*, since the luminosity of photons increases with the mass of the BH. By numerically evaluating photon path lengths (on which the conversion depends), we analyze how key parameters-photon frequency, axion mass, photon-axion coupling, magnetic field strength, plasma density, and black hole spin-affect the conversion probability and the resultant dimming of photon spectral luminosity. We find that the conversion is most efficient at high frequencies (X-rays and gamma rays), while the frequency window associated with efficient conversion widens with an increase in the photon-axion coupling and a decrease in the electron density and the axion mass. The magnitude of dimming of the photon spectral luminosity depends primarily on the magnetic field, the photon-axion coupling and the BH spin. Our study reveals that rotating black holes generally exhibit enhanced dimming compared to static ones. Thus, if future telescopes achieving a resolution $\sim 10^{-5}$ arcsec in the X-ray/gamma-ray band detect a dimming of the photon spectral luminosity, then they can provide interesting constraints on the axion mass and its coupling with photons.

</details>


### [52] [Charged multi-sheet wormhole solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22799)
*Yusuke Makita,Keisuke Izumi,Daisuke Yoshida*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过哈里森变换（Harrison transformation）在四维爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-无质量幻影标量场体系（Einstein-Maxwell-massless phantom scalar system）中构造了具有偶数个渐近平坦区域的带电虫洞解，并系统分析了其参数空间与几何性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索存在多个渐近平坦区域的带电虫洞解的存在性及其参数空间边界，特别是超越传统哈里森变换直接生成的参数区域约束。

Method: 利用哈里森变换从已知种子解生成带电虫洞解；通过正则性条件（regularity condition）确定虫洞喉部半径；引入椭球坐标系（spheroidal coordinate system）简化解的表达式。

Result: 构造了一族由质量 $M$、电荷 $Q_\mathrm{e}$、磁荷 $Q_\mathrm{m}$、标量荷 $P$ 及片数 $2n$ 五个参数刻画的虫洞解。发现正则解存在的参数区域比哈里森变换直接生成的条件 $Q_{\mathrm{e}}^2 + Q_{\mathrm{m}}^2 < M^2$ 更广。椭球坐标系可覆盖一个完整渐近平坦区域及其相邻区域，并使解形式简洁。

Conclusion: 哈里森变换可有效构造多渐近平坦区域的带电虫洞解，且正则解存在更宽泛的参数范围，椭球坐标系为解析表达提供了便利。

Abstract: We construct charged wormhole solutions with an even number of asymptotically flat regions in the four-dimensional Einstein-Maxwell-massless phantom scalar system via the Harrison transformation. The solutions are characterized by five parameters: the mass $M$, the electric charge $Q_\mathrm{e}$, the magnetic charge $Q_\mathrm{m}$, the scalar charge $P$ and the number of sheets $2n$. The regularity condition then determines the throat radius. Although the Harrison transformation directly generates the solutions only in the parameter region $Q_{\mathrm{e}}^2 + Q_{\mathrm{m}}^2 < M^2$, we show that regular solutions exist in a wider parameter region beyond this bound. In addition, we introduce a spheroidal coordinate system that covers one complete asymptotically flat region and its adjacent ones, and allows the solution to be expressed in a simple form.

</details>


### [53] [Another Look at the Weak-Field Limit of Generalized Hybrid Metric-Palatini Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22801)
*Gustavo Melgarejo,Santiago Esteban Perez Bergliaffa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义混合度规-帕拉蒂尼理论（generalized hybrid metric-Palatini theories）的弱场框架下，线性化场方程并推导了牛顿极限下的引力势，包含两个由标量残差幅值决定的Yukawa修正项，并利用行星近日点进动数据对可行的标量质量层级参数空间进行了约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了在不依赖标量-张量表示（scalar-tensor representation）的情况下，系统分析广义混合度规-帕拉蒂尼引力理论在弱场线性化层面的稳定性、传播模式及其可观测的后牛顿效应，进而通过太阳系实验数据对理论参数进行约束。

Method: 在闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）背景上对\(f(R,\mathcal{R})\)型的广义混合度规-帕拉蒂尼理论的场方程进行线性化，推导无质量自旋-2模式和两个有质量标量模式的传播行为；通过牛顿极限（Newtonian limit）得到带两个Yukawa修正的引力势，并计算径向进动频率和反常近日点进动。

Result: 理论在弱场线性化层次上避免了快子（tachyonic）和鬼（ghostlike）不稳定性；引力势包含两个Yukawa修正，其幅值由标量残差（scalar residues）确定，有限尺寸效应由源依赖的形状因子（form factors）编码；推导了有效后牛顿参数\(\gamma_\Sigma\)以及径向epicyclic频率与反常进动表达式，并结合行星进动数据约束了层级标量质量参数。

Conclusion: 广义混合度规-帕拉蒂尼理论在弱场下可退化为含两个Yukawa修正的牛顿极限，通过后牛顿参数和行星进动数据可对理论参数进行有效约束；先前得到的一些条件被推广至更一般的导数约束形式。

Abstract: We investigate the weak-field regime of generalized hybrid metric-Palatini theories, described by a generic function \(f(R,\mathcal{R})\), where \(R\) is the metric Ricci scalar and \(\mathcal{R}\) is constructed from an independent torsionless connection. Linearizing the field equations about Minkowski spacetime, we show, without using the scalar-tensor representation, that the theory propagates the usual massless spin-2 mode and two massive scalar modes, with an effective gravitational coupling. The absence of tachyonic and ghostlike instabilities at the linearized level, together with the nondegeneracy of the scalar sector, is shown to impose algebraic restrictions on the derivatives of \(f(R,\mathcal R)\) evaluated on the Minkowski background, which generalize previously obtained conditions. The Newtonian limit for an extended static source is derived, yielding a gravitational potential with two Yukawa corrections whose amplitudes are fixed by the scalar residues, while finite-size effects are encoded in source-dependent form factors. We determine the conditions under which the usual Newtonian limit is recovered and derive the effective post-Newtonian parameter \(γ_Σ\) governing light propagation. Finally, we compute the radial epicyclic frequency and the corresponding anomalous periapsis advance, and compare it with planetary precession data to constrain the parameters of a viable hierarchical scalar-mass regime.

</details>

### [54] [Echoes of Nucleon Decay from Long-Lived Particles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21583)
*Patrick Adolf,Chandan Hati,Martin Hirsch,Volodymyr Takhistov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一类新的核子衰变（nucleon decay）观测量，涉及长寿命粒子（long-lived particles, LLPs），其特征为空间分离但时间关联的“回波”（echo）顶点，并论证了Super-Kamiokande、Hyper-Kamiokande和JUNO等实验在较宽的LLP衰变长度范围内可实现接近80%的几何接受度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 核子衰变搜索是探测重子数破坏（baryon number violation）及超越标准模型（Standard Model）物理的最灵敏探针之一，但传统瞬时（prompt）搜索无法捕捉空间分离但时间关联的“回波”信号。

Method: 针对矢量LLPs构建有效算符（effective operators）和紫外完备化（ultraviolet realizations）模型；通过几何接受度计算评估Super-Kamiokande、Hyper-Kamiokande和JUNO对回波信号的探测能力。

Result: Super-Kamiokande、Hyper-Kamiokande和JUNO在较宽的LLP衰变长度范围内可实现接近80%的几何接受度（geometric acceptance）。

Conclusion: 回波信号原则上可由任何可观测衰变的LLP产生，为核子衰变搜索提供了新的探测渠道。

Abstract: Nucleon decay searches provide uniquely sensitive probes of baryon number violation and physics beyond the Standard Model. We propose a new class of nucleon decay observables involving long-lived particles (LLPs), characterized by spatially separated but temporally correlated "echo" vertices not captured by conventional prompt searches. Focusing on vector LLPs, we construct effective operators and ultraviolet realizations, and show that Super-Kamiokande, Hyper-Kamiokande and JUNO can achieve geometric acceptances approaching 80% over a broad range of LLP decay lengths. Echo signatures could in principle arise from any visibly decaying LLP.

</details>


### [55] [Precision physics at the muon collider: $m_W$ and CKM matrix elements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21590)
*Ludovica Aperio Bella,Roberto Franceschini,Federico Meloni,Xing Wang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 分析了10 TeV轻子对撞机上多种W玻色子产生机制，聚焦于最丰富的有效γW→W过程（适用于同号与异号轻子对撞机）。分别评估轻子衰变道（leptonic channel）和强子衰变道（hadronic channel）的测量潜力，并讨论探测器响应精度对CKM矩阵元测定的影响。

Result: 轻子W衰变道因产率不足而难以与现有测量竞争。强子道具有超越当前强子对撞机~10 MeV精度的潜力。对强子探测器响应的精确理解可同时用于测定CKM矩阵元，尤其是涉及重夸克的耦合，预期精度远超现有水平，V_cb的测定可避开低能强子矩阵元知识不足的瓶颈。

Abstract: We examine the potential for a 10~TeV lepton collider to carry out precision measurements of the W boson mass and W boson couplings strength, i.e. the CKM matrix elements. We find that the leptonic W decay channel can hardly be competitive with present determinations, due to lack of rate. The hadronic channel has potential to improve over the current $\simeq$10~MeV from measurements at hadron colliders, motivating detector developments towards high-precision hadronic energy measurements. We find that the precision understanding of the detector response to hadrons can also lead to a determination of the CKM matrix elements. We expect determination of CKM matrix elements surpassing by far the present precision for couplings involving heavy quarks, notably $V_{cb}$, avoiding the present bottle-necks due to poor knowledge of hadronic matrix elements needed in low energy extractions of CKM matrix elements. Our findings motivate detector developments towards high-precision hadronic energy measurements and flavor tagging.

### [56] [Exploring the SMEFT landscape: Bayesian Model Selection for indirect discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21594)
*Luca Mantani*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于贝叶斯模型选择（Bayesian model selection）的框架，将标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）视为一个由不同算符子集（operator subsets）构成的假设空间，而非单一高维模型。通过遗传算法（genetic algorithm）高效搜索离散模型空间，并结合贝叶斯信息准则（BIC）近似计算贝叶斯证据，对LEP和LHC Run 2数据进行分析。结果显示无显著超出标准模型的证据，且贝叶斯模型平均（Bayesian Model Average）后验对Wilson系数的刻画能力优于传统全局拟合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准模型有效场论（SMEFT）的传统全局拟合将全部算符纳入单一高维模型，忽略了不同算符子集对应不同新物理低能实现的物理区分性。需要一种能够系统比较和选择算符子集的统计框架，从而更合理地识别可能偏离标准模型（Standard Model）的信号。

Method: 采用贝叶斯模型选择（Bayesian model selection）框架，将每个算符子集视为一个独立模型，计算其后验概率和算符的边缘包含概率（marginal inclusion probability）。使用遗传算法（genetic algorithm）高效搜索高维离散模型空间，并采用贝叶斯信息准则（Bayesian Information Criterion, BIC）近似计算贝叶斯证据（Bayesian evidence）。分析同时纳入线性阶和二次阶Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients），并系统包含单圈重整化群演化（one-loop renormalisation group evolution）。

Result: 对LEP电弱精确观测量（electroweak precision observables）以及LHC Run 2的Higgs、顶夸克和双玻色子测量数据的分析未发现任何统计上显著的超出标准模型的证据。贝叶斯模型平均（Bayesian Model Average, BMA）后验对Wilson系数的刻画能力显著优于传统全局拟合。算符相关矩阵（operator correlation matrix）揭示了共现于高后验模型中的算符对以及需要更多测量数据的平坦方向（flat directions）。所有结果对匹配标度（matching scale）$\mu_0$的敏感性均得到评估。

Conclusion: 该贝叶斯框架提供了一种在SMEFT模型中系统比较算符子集的统计方法，避免了传统全局拟合的局限性。将匹配标度提升为推断的连续参数被识别为该框架的自然扩展方向。

Abstract: We develop a framework for indirect discovery in the Standard Model Effective Field Theory (SMEFT) based on Bayesian model selection over operator subsets. We argue that SMEFT should be understood as a structured space of competing hypotheses rather than a single high-dimensional model, with each operator subset corresponding to a physically distinct low-energy realisation of new dynamics. Bayesian inference is applied at the level of model space itself, assigning posterior probabilities to operator subsets and marginal inclusion probabilities to individual operators. A genetic algorithm efficiently navigates the high-dimensional discrete model space, concentrating evaluations in the high-posterior region, while the Bayesian Information Criterion provides a tractable approximation to the Bayesian evidence. We apply this framework to a dataset comprising electroweak precision observables from LEP and Higgs, top-quark, and diboson measurements from LHC Run 2, at both linear and quadratic order in the Wilson coefficients, with one-loop renormalisation group evolution systematically included. The analysis finds no statistically significant evidence for any departure from the SM, and demonstrates that Bayesian Model Average posteriors on Wilson coefficients carry substantially improved characterisation potential compared to traditional global fits. The operator correlation matrix encodes the relational structure of the model posterior, identifying operator pairs that co-appear in high-posterior models and flat directions where additional measurements would be most valuable. The sensitivity of all results to the choice of matching scale $μ_0$ is assessed, and its promotion to a continuous parameter of inference is identified as a natural extension of the framework.

</details>


### [57] [The Higgs-top-$Z$ mass coincidence relation after NNLO matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21721)
*E. Torrente-Lujan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用2025年PDG最新电弱输入值和完整的NNLO阶匹配分析，重新审视了之前提出的Higgs质量巧合关系$M_H^2\simeq M_ZM_t$。结果显示，在极点（pole-level）层面该几何关系仍与实验数据相符（1.4σ），但在跑动耦合（running-coupling）边界条件$λ=g_Zy_t/(4\sqrt2)$下，在顶夸克能标处经完整NNLO $\overline{\mathrm{MS}}$匹配公式计算后与测量值不相容。论文由此提出，可能的对称性解释必须作用于极点阈值量，或提供一个有限的匹配因子$κ_{\rm th}=1.0340\pm0.0039$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 重新审视先前提出的非平庸Higgs质量巧合关系$M_H^2\simeq M_ZM_t$，利用最新的电弱实验输入值和方案自洽的匹配分析，检验该关系是否仍然成立，并探究其背后可能的对称性起源。

Method: 采用2025年PDG的$M_Z$、$M_W$、$M_H$值和ATLAS-CMS顶夸克直接质量联合值，计算极点层面的比值$ρ_{Zt}=M_ZM_t/M_H^2$；进一步在顶夸克能标$μ=M_t$处，使用完整的NNLO阶弱标度$\overline{\mathrm{MS}}$匹配公式（running-coupling matching），检验精确边界条件$λ=g_Zy_t/(4\sqrt2)$是否成立。

Result: 极点层面，$ρ_{Zt}=1.00362\pm0.00261$，与实验数据在1.4σ内一致；算术关系$ρ_{Wt}=(M_W+M_t)/(2M_H)=1.00994\pm0.00159$不构成可行的精确质量求和规则。在跑动耦合层面，$\widehatρ_{Zt}(M_t)=0.96714\pm0.00361$，精确边界条件预言$M_H=123.19\pm0.20\,\mathrm{GeV}$或$M_t=177.81\pm0.50\,\mathrm{GeV}$，与测量值不相容。所需的匹配因子为$κ_{\rm th}=1.0340\pm0.0039$。

Conclusion: 极点层面的几何关系仍与数据相容，但跑动耦合层面的精确边界条件已被排除。可能的对称性解释必须作用于极点阈值量（pole-level threshold quantities），或提供一个在电弱能标下有限的匹配因子。这一要求被表述为对规范对称性/顶-Higgs对称性或三性（triality）类对称性扩展的目标约束。

Abstract: The relation $M_H^2\simeq M_ZM_t$, previously proposed as a non-trivial Higgs mass coincidence, is reconsidered with present electroweak inputs and with a scheme-consistent matching analysis. With the 2025 PDG values for $M_Z$, $M_W$ and $M_H$, and the ATLAS-CMS direct top-mass combination, the pole-level ratio is $ρ_{Zt}=M_ZM_t/M_H^2=1.00362\pm0.00261$. Thus an exact pole-level geometric relation predicts either $M_H=125.426\pm0.120\,\mathrm{GeV}$ or $M_t=171.898\pm0.302\,\mathrm{GeV}$, which is still a $1.4σ$ test rather than an exclusion. By contrast, the companion arithmetic relation gives $ρ_{Wt}=(M_W+M_t)/(2M_H)=1.00994\pm0.00159$ and is not a viable exact mass sum rule. We then evaluate the complete NNLO weak-scale $\overline{\mathrm{MS}}$ matching formulae at $μ=M_t$. In the standard convention one obtains $\widehatρ_{Zt}(M_t)=\sqrt{g_2^2+g_Y^2}\,y_t/(4\sqrt2λ)=0.96714\pm0.00361$. Consequently, the exact running-coupling boundary condition $λ=g_Zy_t/(4\sqrt2)$ at the top scale would predict $M_H=123.19\pm0.20\,\mathrm{GeV}$, or equivalently $M_t=177.81\pm0.50\,\mathrm{GeV}$ when $M_H$ is held fixed. This is incompatible with the measured point. A possible symmetry explanation must therefore act on pole-level threshold quantities, or provide a finite matching factor $κ_{\rm th}=1.0340\pm0.0039$ at the electroweak scale. We formulate this requirement as a target for custodial/top-Higgs or triality-like symmetry extensions.

Although the charm sum rule is less precise than the relations in bottom-hadron decays, current low-energy and high-$p_T$ constraints on new physics restrict the actual deviation from the relation to below the percent level. The relation can therefore provide a useful consistency check of charm semileptonic measurements. Abstract: In this work, a comprehensive analysis for processes related to $b\to c\bar{u}q~(q=d, s)$ transitions are carried out, including new physics contributions.   <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Global fits of Beyond the Standard Model (BSM) physics often involve a two-way interplay between theory and experiment. Theoretical models provide guidance for experimental searches, while experimental results, in turn, constrain theoretical frameworks. A crucial aspect of this feedback loop is the direct inclusion of measurements and exclusion limits ``online'' global fits, i.e. during the parameter scans aspects of the global fits. However, incorporating the Large Hadron Collider (LHC) limits into such analyses has been computationally prohibitive, often due to time taken per parameter point exceeding the scales acceptable for global fit frameworks. In this study, we show that LHC limits can be incorporated ``online'' global fits by leveraging approximations derived from symbolic regression techniques. We utilize a dataset of ATLAS constraints from searches for electroweakino productions to derive a mathematical expression capable of classifying the phenomenological Minimal Supersymmetric Standard Model (pMSSM) parameter space as allowed or excluded. ### [61] [The Mass Gap Approach to QCD. II. The non-perturbative renormalization program for the massive gluon fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21547)
*V. Gogokhia,G. G. Barnafoldi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于QCD质量间隙方法，提出了一种适用于有质量胶子场的非微扰乘性重整化方案。该方案使胶子能够动态获得质量，完整分析了全胶子传播子的渐近性质与质量壳结构，并阐明了胶子无法成为质量壳上的物理粒子（即胶子禁闭），只能存在于真空中或强子内部。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在量子色动力学（quantum chromodynamics, QCD）中，胶子是否能够获得质量以及相应的非微扰重整化方案尚不明确。本文旨在基于先前建立的质量间隙方法（mass gap approach），构建一个非微扰的乘性重整化程序，以解决有质量胶子场的重整化问题，并修复规范规范（canonical gauge）中的不一致性。

Method: 采用非微扰乘性重整化（non-perturbative multiplicative renormalization）方案，基于前期构建的QCD质量间隙方法。该方法依赖于对QCD基态真实动力学与规范结构的新见解，使胶子能够动态获得质量（dynamical mass generation）。研究对全胶子传播子（full gluon propagator）进行了完整分析，并给出了适用于格点模拟（lattice simulations）的欧几里得度量表达式。

Result: 完整分析了有质量胶子全传播子的渐近性质，包括微扰论极限；讨论了有质量胶子传播子的质量壳结构奇异性；指出规范规范的不一致性已被修复；证明有质量解在胶子极点质量（gluon pole mass）形式化为零时，能正确退化为自由无质量胶子传播子。

Conclusion: 该方案不允许有质量胶子成为质量壳上的物体，从而阻止其出现在物理谱中（即实现了有质量胶子态的禁闭）。有质量胶子仅能存在于真空或强子内部。该工作为理解QCD中的胶子动态质量生成与胶子禁闭提供了非微扰理论框架。

Abstract: We present a non-perturbative multiplicative renormalization program for the massive gluon fields. This has been done within the previously formulated the mass gap approach to QCD. It is based on a new insights into its ground state true dynamical and gauge structures. Our approach makes it possible for gluons to acquire mass dynamically. The corresponding full gluon propagator has been investigated in full details. Its asymptotic properties have been analysed, including the perturbation theory limit. The peculiarities of the mass-shell structure of the full massive gluon propagator has been discussed. The inconsistency of the canonical gauge in QCD is fixed. Our approach does not allow the massive gluons to be the mass-shell objects. This prevents them to appear in the physical spectrum (confinement of massive gluon states). The massive gluons may exist in the vacuum or inside hadrons only. Expressions in Euclidean metric for the lattice simulations are also present. We have also shown that the massive solution has a correct limit to the free massless gluon propagator, when the exactly defined gluon pole mass is to be formally put zero.

</details>


### [62] [Symmetry Breaking as Quantum Gate: Entropy and Weak Mixing Angle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22070)
*Qing-Hong Cao,Yandong Liu,Haotian Qi,Hao Zhang,Haoran Zhao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在电弱对称性破缺（electroweak symmetry breaking, EWSB）相变过程的树级2→2弹性散射中，建立了两种独立熵探针——Rényi互信息（RMI）与稳定子Rényi熵（SRE）——之间的对应关系。在角度平均后，二者对sin²θ_W的依赖在每种中性流（neutral-current）道中完全相同，并追溯该对应起源于汤川质量插入（Yukawa mass insertion）在手征性（chirality）空间中充当−iY量子门。通过最小化所有过程的熵，得到的sin²θ_W值与纯轴矢类矢量（axial vector-like）Z玻色子交换耦合一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索电弱对称性破缺（electroweak symmetry breaking, EWSB）相变过程中，两种独立熵探针——Rényi互信息（RMI）与稳定子Rényi熵（SRE）——之间是否存在深层对应关系，并利用该对应解释弱混合角sin²θ_W的取值。

Method: 在树级2→2弹性散射中计算角度平均后的RMI（螺旋度基，helicity basis）与SRE（固定束基，fixed beam basis），并比较它们对sin²θ_W的依赖；通过在手征性（chirality）空间中引入汤川质量插入的−iY量子门操作追溯对应关系的物理起源。

Result: 在每种中性流（neutral-current）道中，RMI与SRE对sin²θ_W的依赖关系完全相同。最小化所有过程的熵后，得到的sin²θ_W值与纯轴矢类矢量（axial vector-like）Z玻色子交换耦合一致。

Conclusion: 汤川质量插入在手征性空间中充当−iY量子门是RMI与SRE对应的共同物理起源；熵的最小化可自然导出观测到的弱混合角（sin²θ_W）取值。

Abstract: We establish a correspondence between two independent entropic probes -- the variation of Rényi mutual information (RMI) across the electroweak symmetry breaking (EWSB) transition and the stabilizer Rényi entropy (SRE) -- in tree-level $2\to 2$ elastic scatterings. After angular averaging, the RMI (helicity basis) and the SRE (fixed beam basis) exhibit identical dependence on $\sin^2θ_W$ within each neutral-current channel. We trace this correspondence to a common physical origin that it's the Yukawa mass insertion acts as a $-\mathrm{i}Y$ quantum gate in chirality space. Minimizing entropies across all processes yields $\sin^2θ_W$ values matching purely axial vector-like couplings in $Z$ boson exchanged channel.

### [63] [Pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone inflation with $Z_N$ symmetric waterfall fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22464)
*Hyun Min Lee,Adriana G. Menkara*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种杂糅暴胀（hybrid inflation）模型，其中赝能戈德斯通玻色子（pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson）暴胀子通过与具有 $Z_N$ 对称性的 $N$ 个瀑布标量场（waterfall scalar fields）耦合，实现暴胀及后续的瀑布相变。研究表明，$Z_N$ 对称性可以消除瀑布扇区的二次发散，且当 $N>2$ 时对数发散也会消失，从而保证暴胀子势的辐射稳定性。文章分析了不同离散对称性下的参数空间、真空结构、再加热（reheating）过程及多组分暗物质的可能性，并指出可以避免畴壁问题（domain wall problem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在暴胀宇宙学中，如何构建一个辐射稳定且具有自然势能形式的暴胀子模型是一个关键问题。本文旨在利用离散对称性 $Z_N$ 来抑制源自瀑布扇区的量子修正，从而在杂糅暴胀框架中实现暴胀子势能的辐射稳定性，并解决再加热后对称性恢复及畴壁问题。

Method: 模型将赝能戈德斯通玻色子作为暴胀子，并将其与 $N$ 个具有 $Z_N$ 对称性的瀑布标量场耦合。基于科尔曼-温伯格势（Coleman-Weinberg potential）分析暴胀子的量子修正。具体研究了 $Z_2$、$Z_3$ 和 $Z_4$ 三种离散对称性情形，给出了暴胀参数空间，并借助 $Z_N$ 不变的 Higgs-portal 耦合分析再加热过程及真空结构。

Result: $Z_N$ 对称性可以消除瀑布扇区对暴胀子势的二次发散（quadratically divergent corrections），而仅在 $N>2$ 时对数发散（logarithmically divergent corrections）也完全消除，从而确保势能的辐射稳定性。对于 $Z_2$、$Z_3$ 和 $Z_4$ 情形，分别给出了成功暴胀所需的参数空间，并比较了不同离散对称性之间的差异。再加热温度可以低于瀑布场凝聚的质量，使得 $Z_N$ 对称性不再恢复，从而避免了畴壁问题。此外，$Z_N$ 对称性对应的伙伴场可能构成多组分暗物质（multi-component dark matter）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于 $Z_N$ 对称性的杂糅暴胀模型在辐射稳定性、参数可行性及宇宙学后果（如无畴壁问题、可具有多组分暗物质）方面均表现出良好的理论自洽性。该工作为利用离散对称性构建自然的暴胀模型提供了新的思路。

Abstract: We propose a hybrid inflation model where a pseudo-Nambu-Goldstone boson inflaton couples to $N$ waterfall scalar fields respecting a $Z_N$ symmetry. We identify the phases for the inflation and the consequent waterfall transition, concretely, in $Z_2$, $Z_3$ and $Z_4$ cases. From the Coleman-Weinberg potential for the inflaton, we show that the quadratically divergent corrections coming from the waterfall sector are cancelled due to the $Z_N$ symmetry, while the logarithmically divergent corrections are absent only for $N>2$, ensuring the radiative stability of the inflaton potential. We show the parameter space for a successful inflation with the loop-corrected inflaton potential in each model and compare the results between different discrete symmetries. We further analyze the vacuum structure of the models and the reheating process due to the $Z_N$-invariant Higgs-portal couplings for the waterfall fields. We find that the reheating temperature can be smaller than the mass of the waterfall field condensate such that the $Z_N$ symmetry is not restored after reheating and there is no domain wall problem in the models. We also comment on the possibility of multi-component dark matter from the $Z_N$ partners of the waterfall field condensate.

</details>

### [64] [A Utility-Driven Bounded-Confidence Model for Opinion Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21844)
*Alex Siebenmorgen,Juan G. Restrepo*

Main category: nlin.AO

TL;DR: 本文提出一种效用驱动的有界置信意见动力学模型，其中具有更高效用的意见施加更强的社会影响。推导了单聚类情形下平均意见的随机微分方程，其稳态分布呈吉布斯形式；对于多峰效用函数，动力学会出现亚稳态和意见状态间的自发切换。该降维随机描述还能捕捉多意见簇的演化与合并，与基于智能体的模拟结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的有界置信（bounded-confidence）意见动力学模型主要关注意见相似性对社交影响的约束，但缺乏对意见效用（utility）这一驱动因素的考量。本文旨在引入效用驱动的机制，使高效用意见具有更强的社会影响力，以更真实地刻画意见形成过程。

Method: 提出一个效用驱动的有界置信模型，该模型赋予高效用意见更大的社交影响力。在全体智能体（agents）归属于单一意见簇（opinion cluster）的机制下，推导出平均意见（mean opinion）的随机微分方程（stochastic differential equation）。通过数学分析得到稳态分布的形式，并利用基于智能体的模拟（agent-based simulations）验证多意见簇情形的演化行为。

Result: 当所有智能体属于单一意见簇时，平均意见的稳态分布呈吉布斯（Gibbs）形式，其有效势（effective potential）由效用景观（utility landscape）决定，而逆温度（inverse temperature）由学习率（learning rate）和智能体数量控制。对于多峰（multimodal）效用函数，动力学表现出亚稳态（metastability）和竞争意见状态之间的自发切换（spontaneous switching）。降维随机描述也能准确捕捉多个意见簇的演化与合并。

Conclusion: 该效用驱动模型为意见动力学提供了一种新的统计力学（statistical mechanics）视角，将效用景观与稳态分布联系起来，并揭示了亚稳态切换等集体行为。降维随机描述可以有效概括多智能体系统的宏观动力学特征，与微观模拟结果一致。

Abstract: We introduce a utility-driven bounded-confidence model of opinion dynamics in which opinions associated with higher utility exert stronger social influence. In the regime where all agents belong to a single opinion cluster, we derive a stochastic differential equation for the mean opinion and show that its stationary distribution is Gibbs-like, with an effective potential determined by the utility landscape and an inverse temperature controlled by the learning rate and the number of agents. For multimodal utility functions, the dynamics exhibit metastability and spontaneous switching between competing opinion states. The reduced stochastic description also captures the evolution and merging of multiple opinion clusters, in agreement with agent-based simulations.

</details>

### [65] [Identification and mitigation of memory block timing issue in ITk ABCStar during ASIC production](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22559)
*B. Ashmanskas,J. Botte,J. R. Dandoy,J. Dopke,N. Dressnandt,B. J. Gallop,J. J. John,P. T. Keener,T. Koffas,J. Kroll,R. P. McGovern,M. F. Newcomer,B. J. Norman,P. W. Phillips,C. Sawyer,R. Scouten,P. Vicente Leitao,M. Warren*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本论文描述了ATLAS ITk探测器ABCStar读出ASIC在预生产测试中发现的设计缺陷及其解决方案。该缺陷因逻辑时序问题导致某些批次晶圆良率从预期的90%骤降至最低2%。通过将核心工作电压从1.20V提升至1.25V并增加时钟占空比，验证了即使是最差批次晶圆的良率也可恢复至80%以上，从而避免了重新设计和工艺修改。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ABCStar是一款用于ATLAS ITk探测器条带传感器部分的前端读出专用集成电路（mixed-signal front-end readout ASIC），是High-Luminosity LHC升级项目的一部分。预生产测试中发现一个设计缺陷导致晶圆良率从预期的90%骤降至最低2%，急需找出根本原因并找到可行的缓解方案，以避免昂贵的重新设计和工艺变更。

Method: 通过分析确定缺陷根源为控制复用存储器模块的合成逻辑中的时序问题。提出了两种并行缓解方案：晶圆代工厂的制造工艺变更以及调整ABCStar在探测器中的工作参数。基于对现有工艺和最差晶圆测试结果的分析，提出将核心电压从1.20V提升至1.25V以加速晶体管。随后开展了涵盖ITk探测器全生命周期温度和辐射效应的广泛测试程序来验证该方案，并进一步通过增加时钟占空比提供额外可靠性裕量。

Result: 测试证明，即使是最差批次的晶圆在1.25V核心电压下良率也可超过80%，无需修改工艺或重新设计。进一步的时钟占空比调整提供了额外的可靠性裕量。所有ABCStar晶圆的测试已完成，探测器模块的生产已顺利推进。

Conclusion: 通过提升核心工作电压和调整时钟占空比，有效解决了ABCStar的时序缺陷问题，恢复了晶圆良率，确保了ATLAS ITk探测器模块的可靠生产，避免了重新设计和工艺变更等更昂贵的解决方案。

Abstract: The ABCStar is a mixed-signal front-end readout ASIC for the strips sensor portion of the ATLAS ITk detector being developed as part of the High-Luminosity LHC upgrade. In pre-production testing, a subtle design flaw was uncovered in the ABCStar that was reducing wafer yields in some manufactured lots from the expected 90% to as low as 2%. The root cause was determined to be a timing issue in the logic synthesized to control previously silicon proven memory blocks re-used for this ASIC. The solutions proposed included manufacturing process changes by the wafer foundry, changes to the operating parameters for the ABCStar in the detector, and the possibility that a redesign might be required. The two mitigation efforts were undertaken in parallel, with the process modification route a less desirable solution since already manufactured wafers would need to be scrapped in favour of the new ones. Based on a knowledge of the existing process, and testing done on the worst performing wafers, it was proposed that raising the core operating voltage of the ABCStar from 1.20V to 1.25V could address the timing issue by sufficiently speeding up its transistors. An extensive testing program that included the effects of temperature and radiation expected over the lifetime of the ITk detector was conducted to validate that approach. Those tests and studies proved that even the worst performing wafers would have yields over 80% with the 1.25V core voltage, and neither the modified process nor redesign would be required for ensuring reliable operation of the ITk. Based on testing, a further timing mitigation was implemented to provide an additional margin of reliability by increasing the duty cycle of the clock to the ABCStar. Testing of all ABCStar wafers has been completed and the production of the detector modules using these ASICs is now well underway as a result of the efforts detailed herein.

### [66] [Chiral superconductors from parent states with non-uniform Berry curvature: Momentum-space vortices, BdG topology, and thermal Hall conductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21618)
*L. David Le Nir,Asimpunya Mitra,Yong Baek Kim*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文研究了来自具有非均匀贝里曲率（Berry curvature）母体电子态的手性超导（chiral superconductivity），以菱方石墨烯多层膜实验为动机。通过连续λ_N模型求解完整BCS能隙方程，发现母体能带非均匀贝里曲率丰富了超导序参量，导致动量空间涡旋在能隙函数中形成。进一步证明母体能带陈数（Chern number）约束动量空间涡旋数量，并提供了计算连续模型Bogoliubov-de Gennes贝里曲率的规范不变公式。最后讨论了热霍尔测量用于探测动量空间涡旋形成的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期菱方石墨烯多层膜实验发现手性超导迹象，但非均匀贝里曲率对手性超导的具体影响尚不清晰。本文旨在揭示贝里曲率非均匀性如何塑造手性超导序参量及其拓扑约束。

Method: 采用连续λ_N模型作为可调平台，独立调控贝里曲率分布；在连续陈能带（Chern band）上求解完整BCS能隙方程，超越弱耦合极限；推导规范不变的Bogoliubov-de Gennes（BdG）贝里曲率公式，并分析动量空间相位电流及其环绕数。

Result: 非均匀贝里曲率使超导能隙函数产生动量空间涡旋；存在涡旋成核与涡旋数饱和的不同区间，涡旋成核倾向于降低凝聚能（condensation energy）；母体能带陈数严格约束动量空间涡旋数量，与λ_N模型细节无关；BdG贝里曲率由动量空间相位电流决定，该电流在占据区涡旋周围的环绕数决定了BdG陈数。

Conclusion: 贝里曲率在塑造手性超导中起关键作用；动量空间涡旋的形成可通过热霍尔测量进行实验探测；结果为指导菱方石墨烯等体系中手性超导的识别提供了理论原则。

Abstract: We investigate chiral superconductivity emerging from parent electronic states with non-uniform Berry curvature, motivated by recent experiments in rhombohedral graphene multilayers. Using the continuum $λ_N$-model-a tunable platform with independently controllable Berry curvature profiles-we solve the full BCS gap equation on a continuum Chern band beyond the weak-coupling limit. We find that a non-uniform Berry curvature of the parent band enriches the superconducting order parameter, leading to the formation of momentum-space vortices in the gap function away from high-symmetry points. By tuning the Berry curvature profile, we identify distinct regimes associated with vortex nucleation and vortex number saturation, and show that the nucleation of momentum-space vortices tends to lower the condensation energy. We then show analytically that the parent band Chern number constrains the number of momentum-space vortices that can nucleate in the gap-independent of details of the $λ_N$-model. We also provide a gauge-invariant formulation for computing the Bogoliubov-de Gennes (BdG) Berry curvature for continuum models, and find that it is determined by a momentum-space phase current. The winding of this current around vortices in the occupied region in turn determines the BdG Chern number. Finally, we discuss how thermal Hall measurements can be used to probe the formation of momentum-space vortices. Our results highlight the crucial role of Berry curvature in shaping chiral superconductivity, and offer guiding principles for its identification in systems such as rhombohedral graphene.

</details>

Abstract: Tunneling spectroscopy and its evolution are crucial for elucidating the intricate electronic structure and emergent phenomena in quantum materials.Nevertheless, high-quality measurements -- specifically those tracking evolution across temperature and external fields -- remain a formidable challenge. We have fabricated a high-quality $\mathrm{TaO}_x$-based planar tunneling junction by using magnetron sputtering for van der Waals (vdW) superconductors. Using the vdW superconductor $\mathrm{Bi}_2\mathrm{Sr}_2\mathrm{CaCu}_2\mathrm{O}_{8+δ}$ (Bi2212) as a benchmark, this platform yields high-quality tunneling spectra, reproducing the electronic signatures obtained from scanning tunneling spectra acquired from atomically clean surfaces under ultra-high vacuum conditions. This architecture enables high-precision spectroscopy across extensive temperature and magnetic field ranges, offering a universal strategy for probing the electronic structures of diverse two-dimensional systems and facilitating future explorations of material properties.

### [68] [Quasiparticle GW for Superconductors: Toward a Unified Treatment of Electron-Phonon and Electron-Plasmon Couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21700)
*Catalin D. Spataru,Christopher Renskers,Elena R. Margine*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一个名为“s-qpGW”的新理论框架，将准粒子自洽GW方法扩展到超导相，并与Eliashberg处理结合，以同时描述声子和等离激元介导的配对相互作用，从而更准确地捕捉电子通道中的动态屏蔽效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有超导理论主要基于BCS框架，假设电声子相互作用是超导的主要机制，但无法定量解释二维材料（特别是少层石墨烯）中非常规超导的起源。近期研究表明等离激元（plasmon）配对机制可能起重要作用，但由于缺乏能准确处理电子通道中动态屏蔽效应（dynamical screening effects）的第一性原理框架，难以区分声子和等离激元介导配对的相对贡献。

Method: 本文提出一个名为“s-qpGW”的理论框架，将准粒子自洽GW方法（quasiparticle self-consistent GW method）扩展到超导相，并与Eliashberg理论（Eliashberg treatment）相结合，以同时处理声子（phonon）和等离激元（plasmon）介导的相互作用。

Result: s-qpGW方法在应用于块体金属时与最先进的Eliashberg超导理论结果一致，并正确预测了掺杂单层石墨烯（doped monolayer graphene）中不存在超导现象。通过一个态密度（density of states）人为增强的石墨烯模型系统，证明s-qpGW能捕捉到标准BCS理论无法处理的动态库仑屏蔽效应（dynamical Coulomb screening effects）。

Conclusion: s-qpGW为区分声子和等离激元介导的超导配对机制提供了新的第一性原理工具，能够准确处理电子通道中的动态屏蔽效应，弥补了传统BCS理论在二维非常规超导材料中的不足。

Abstract: Superconducting two-dimensional materials, and in particular few-layer graphene, offer an exciting platform for low-power electronics, yet the origin of their unconventional superconductivity remains an open question. Prevailing theories, primarily rooted in the Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer (BCS) framework that assumes electron-phonon interactions are the main mechanism of superconductivity, struggle to account quantitatively for the observed phenomena. Recent studies point to a plasmonic pairing mechanism in graphene systems; however, disentangling the relative contributions of phonon- and plasmon-mediated pairing remains challenging due to the lack of a satisfactory first-principles framework capable of accurately capturing dynamical screening effects in the electronic channel. Here, we present a new theoretical framework that extends the quasiparticle self-consistent GW method to the superconducting phase by coupling it with the Eliashberg treatment of both phonon- and plasmon-mediated interactions. Our approach, termed "s-qpGW", is on par with the state-of-the-art Eliashberg theory of superconductivity when applied to bulk metals, and correctly predicts the absence of superconductivity in doped monolayer graphene. To differentiate s-qpGW from conventional Eliashberg approaches, we study a simple model system, graphene with an artificially enhanced density of states, and demonstrate that s-qpGW captures dynamical Coulomb screening effects in ways that standard BCS theory cannot.

</details>


### [69] [Anomalous acoustoelectric signatures of chiral superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21936)
*A. N. Osipov,V. N. Ivanova,V. M. Kovalev,I. G. Savenko*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出异常声电效应（anomalous acoustoelectric effect）作为一种稳健的电学探针，用于检测二维材料中的手性p波超导配对对称性（chiral p-wave pairing symmetry）。研究表明，声波可在无外磁场条件下通过准粒子各向异性散射诱导横向直流电流，并在样品边界产生可测量的凝聚体相位差。该效应在临界温度附近占主导，且不受电子-空穴不对称因子抑制，因此可作为手性序参量的高灵敏度电学探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维材料中非常规配对（unconventional pairing）的识别是现代凝聚态物理学（condensed matter physics）的核心挑战。手性p波超导（chiral p-wave superconductivity）为拓扑量子计算（topological quantum computing）提供了有前景的平台，但由于光学探针在二维极限下的固有限制，其探测仍难以实现。因此，亟需一种替代性探测手段。

Method: 本文提出利用异常声电效应作为检测p波配对对称性的稳健替代方案。具体而言，通过声波（acoustic wave）在无外磁场条件下诱导横向直流电流，并基于准粒子各向异性散射（anisotropic scattering of quasiparticles）在样品边界产生可测量的凝聚体相位差（condensate phase difference），从而实现对配对对称性的电学表征。

Result: 分析表明，准粒子介导的声电响应（quasiparticle-mediated acoustoelectric response）在接近临界温度（critical temperature）时占主导地位；与超导凝聚体（superconducting condensate）不同，该响应不会受到电子-空穴不对称因子（electron-hole asymmetry factor）的抑制。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了异常声电效应作为手性序参量（chiral order parameter）的高灵敏度电学探针，为实验探测超导体中的非常规配对提供了一种有效工具。

Abstract: The identification of unconventional pairing in two-dimensional materials is a central challenge in modern condensed matter physics. While chiral p-wave superconductivity offers a promising platform for topological quantum computing, its detection remains elusive due to the inherent limitations of optical probes in the two-dimensional limit. We propose the anomalous acoustoelectric effect as a robust, alternative to optical signature of p-wave paring symmetry. We demonstrate that an acoustic wave induces a transverse dc current resulting in a measurable condensate phase difference on sample boundaries originating from the anisotropic scattering of quasiparticles in the absence of an external magnetic field. Crucially, the quasiparticle-mediated acoustoelectric response dominates near the critical temperature and, unlike the superconducting condensate, is not suppressed by electron-hole asymmetry factor. These results establish the anomalous acoustoelectric effect as a high-sensitivity electrical probe of the chiral order parameter, providing a tool for experimental detecting of unconventional pairing in superconductors.

</details>


### [70] [Superconductivity in doped spin multimer systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22128)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用解析与数值相结合的方法，以双近藤晶格模型（double Kondo lattice model）为研究对象，利用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group）方法进行数值模拟。

Conclusion: 研究结果为超导研究提供了有用的指导方针（useful guidelines），表明结合能是驱动超导配对的关键因素，且配对关联的建立对局域自旋关联细节具有鲁棒性（robustness）。

Abstract: Binding energy, which quantifies pair formation, is a key factor in the emergence of superconductivity. Here, we show that even when multiple spins are complexly coupled, hole-doped systems, which can be mapped onto the universal hardcore boson model in the strong-binding-energy limit, exhibit promising signatures of superconductivity. We analytically and numerically demonstrate this concept in the double Kondo lattice model. Using the density-matrix renormalization group method, we show that a pairing state is maintained via a crossover even for parameters away from the strong-coupling regime. Additionally, we find that once binding energies are sufficiently generated, pair correlations develop similarly regardless of the details of local spin correlations. Our findings suggest useful guidelines for research on superconductivity.

### [71] [Fabrication and transfer of ultra-thin YBa$2$Cu$3$O$_{7-x}$ film on SrTiO$_3$ nanomembrane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22303)
*J. S. Madhira,G. Potemkin,D. Grützmacher,T. Schäpers,M. Lyatti*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 制备独立的（free-standing）高温超导（high-Tc superconductor）超薄膜对于开发高工作温度的超导纳米线单光子探测器（superconducting nanowire single-photon detector）具有重要价值。当前缺乏一种可行方案，能将高质量YBCO超薄膜集成到SiO₂/Si光子平台上。

Result: 转移后的YBCO薄膜临界温度（critical temperature）为88.8 K，77 K下临界电流密度（critical current density）为6.8 MA/cm²；STO/YBCO纳米膜与SiO₂/Si基底之间的范德华界面热边界电导（thermal boundary conductance）在15–75 K范围内显著低于外延YBCO/体块STO体系，从而改写了能量弛豫（energy relaxation）特性并增强了瞬态电阻态（transient resistive states）的稳定性。

Conclusion: 本研究验证了在光学透明的STO纳米膜上制备超薄YBCO薄膜可作为一种集成平台，将高温超导器件与基于SiO₂/Si的光子结构（photonic structures）相结合，为发展高工作温度超导单光子探测器提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The fabrication of free-standing ultra-thin films from high-temperature (high-Tc) superconductors is of great interest for the development of superconducting nanowire single-photon detectors with high operating temperatures. We successfully fabricate a millimeter-sized, high-quality, ultra-thin YBa$2$Cu$3$O$_{7-x}$ (YBCO) film on an SrTiO$_3$/Sr$_{1.5}$Ca$_{1.5}$Al$_2$O$_6$ (STO/SCAO) bilayer using high-pressure sputtering. The STO nanomembranes with the YBCO films are released by dissolving the water-soluble SCAO sacrificial layer and transferred onto the SiO2/Si substrate. X-ray diffraction confirms that STO and YBCO crystallinity is preserved following transfer onto SiO2/Si substrates. Microbridges patterned from the transferred YBCO films exhibit a critical temperature of 88.8 K and a critical current density of 6.8 MA/cm2 at 77 K, demonstrating robust superconducting transport after transfer. The thermal boundary conductance across the van der Waals interface between the STO nanomembrane with YBCO film and the SiO2/Si substrate, measured over 15-75 K, is significantly reduced compared to that of epitaxial YBCO film on bulk STO leading to modified energy relaxation and enhanced stability of transient resistive states. These results establish ultra-thin YBCO films on optically transparent STO nanomembranes as a platform for integrating high-Tc superconducting devices with SiO2/Si-based photonic structures.

### [72] [Current-driven reduction of topological protection in multichannel superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22460)
*Alfonso Maiellaro*

Method: 引入依赖于电流诱导的准粒子动量（quasiparticle momentum）的有效哈密顿量；结合体拓扑不变量（bulk topological invariants）与实空间诊断（real-space diagnostics），包括边缘-边缘量子条件互信息（edge-edge quantum conditional mutual information, Iee）。

Result: 孤立梯子中存在的双模拓扑相（two-mode topological phase）在有限电流通量下表现脆弱，即拓扑保护被破坏。

Abstract: We investigate the robustness of topological phases in a Kitaev ladder composed of two coupled superconducting chains under the perturbing influence of a finite charge current. By introducing an effective Hamiltonian depending on the quasiparticle momentum induced by the current, we show that the two-mode topological phase, present in the isolated ladder, is fragile against a finite current flux. To characterize this behavior, we combine bulk topological invariants with real-space diagnostics, including the edge-edge quantum conditional mutual information Iee, which provides an entanglement-based signature of topological order. Our results provide an effective framework to describe how current injection and measurement processes can affect topological protection in superconducting nanostructures.

### [73] [Predicting intermediate-mass black hole formation in star clusters with machine learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21593)
*Konstantinos Kritos,Digvijay Wadekar,Emanuele Berti*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究利用神经网络（neural network）和随机森林回归器（random forest regressor），基于Rapster星团演化代码生成的合成星表，从星团可观测性质（总质量、半质量半径）预测最重黑洞质量。应用于邻近球状星团（globular cluster）和核星团（nuclear star cluster）后发现：球状星团几乎不可能包含超过~100 M⊙的黑洞（占据率约0.02）；部分核星团（如NGC 5102、NGC 5206）预测中心黑洞质量超100 M⊙，与运动学推断存在偏差；最后利用归一化流（normalizing flow）量化了单个球状星团早期碰撞逃逸（collisional runaway）的初始条件概率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中等质量黑洞（intermediate-mass black hole, IMBH）是否存在于邻近星团中，是数十年来悬而未决的争议问题。

Method: 在Rapster星团演化代码生成的合成星表上训练神经网络和随机森林回归器，将星团总质量、半质量半径等可观测性质映射到经多次并合形成的最重黑洞质量；随后对邻近球状星团和核星团应用模型进行预测，并使用归一化流量化单个球状星团初始条件有利于碰撞逃逸过程的似然。

Result: 球状星团不太可能包含质量超过~100 M⊙的黑洞，占据率（occupation fraction）约0.02，但可在上质量间隙（upper mass gap）内产生接近100 M⊙的遗迹；核星团中NGC 5102和NGC 5206等少数案例预测中心黑洞质量超过100 M⊙，与运动学推断估计存在对比差异。

Conclusion: 当观测声称的黑洞质量超过预测值时，暗示其形成历史涉及层次并合（hierarchical merger）之外的过程，最可能是气体和恒星吸积（accretion）。

Abstract: Whether intermediate-mass black holes reside in nearby star clusters has remained contested for decades. We address this question by training neural network and random forest regressors on synthetic catalogs generated with the {\sc Rapster} cluster evolution code, mapping observable cluster properties such as total mass and half-mass radius onto the mass of the heaviest black hole built up through repeated mergers. Applying these models to nearby globular and nuclear star clusters, we forecast the intermediate-mass black hole population that each system may host. Globular clusters are unlikely to contain black holes more massive than $\sim 100\,M_\odot$, with an occupation fraction near 0.02, although they can produce remnants within the upper mass gap with masses approaching $100\,M_\odot$. Among nuclear star clusters, a handful of cases, including NGC 5102 and NGC 5206, yield predicted central black hole masses above $100\,M_\odot$, which we contrast with kinematically inferred estimates. Where the observationally claimed masses exceed our predictions, the implication is that the assembly history involved processes beyond hierarchical mergers, most plausibly accretion of gas and stars. Finally, we employ a normalizing flow to quantify, for individual globular clusters, the likelihood that their initial conditions were favorable to a collisional runaway during the first few million years after formation.

</details>


### [74] [Silicate cosmic dust grain collisions in the interstellar medium: A molecular dynamics study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22225)
*C. J. Esmerian,S. R. Hashemi,W. M. C. Sameera,W. Vlemmings,S. Andersson,T. J. L. C. Bakx,K. K. Knudsen,S. Aalto,G. Nyman*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本研究通过分子动力学模拟，揭示了硅酸盐尘埃颗粒的碎裂阈值速度约为6 km/s，是基于经典值2.7 km/s的两倍，并否定了此前关于碎裂产物尺寸分布呈幂律的假设。这些更新表明星际尘埃颗粒可能比以往认为的更耐碎裂。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在预测星际尘埃种群演化模型中最重要的碰撞结果参数——碎裂阈值速度、汽化阈值速度以及碰撞后粒径分布，以改进天体物理尺度下的尘埃演化模型。

Method: 采用分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟，追踪尘埃颗粒中每个原子的动力学过程，模拟非晶SiO₂及Draine & Hensley (2021)提出的非晶硅酸盐材料，粒径a∈[5,50] Å、碰撞速度0.1-20 km/s下的碰撞结果。

Result: 两种材料的碎裂阈值均约为6 km/s，是经典值2.7 km/s（Jones et al. 1996）的两倍；该差异主要源于Tielens et al. (1994)速度阈值表达式中的错误。碎裂产物的尺寸分布不服从此前模型预测的幂律分布，且现有模型（Tielens et al. 1994；Hirashita & Kobayashi 2013）均无法拟合模拟中碎裂或汽化物质的比例。

Conclusion: 提供了更新的碎裂阈值速度，表明星际尘埃颗粒可能比以往假设的更耐碎裂。

Abstract: (abridged) We aim to predict the most important parameters for grain-grain collision outcomes for models of interstellar grain population evolution on astrophysical scales: the threshold velocity above which colliding grains shatter, the threshold for vaporization, and resulting distributions of grain sizes. We use molecular dynamics simulations which evolve the dynamics of each atom in a dust grain to explore the outcomes of collisions between silicate grains of radii $a \in [5,50]~Å$ at velocities $0.1-20$ km/s. We run simulations of grains with two materials: amorphous SiO$_2$ and an amorphous silicate of composition suggested by Draine \& Hensley (2021). With these simulations, we quantify the collision velocity dependence of shattered and vaporized mass fractions, and the resulting size distributions of shattering products. We find grain shattering thresholds are $\sim$6 km/s for both amorphous SiO$_2$ and astrodust material, which is a factor of $\sim$2 higher than the canonical value for silicates of 2.7 km/s from Jones et al. (1996). This discrepancy is mostly alleviated by correcting an error in the expression for these velocity thresholds derived in Tielens et al. (1994). We find that the size distributions of shattered products are generally not consistent with the power law distributions predicted by this previous model. We also find that their expression fails to predict the fraction of shattered or vaporized material observed in our numerical simulations. The model of Hirashita \& Kobayashi (2013) for the same quantities similarly fails to match the simulations. We provide updated shattering velocity thresholds for standard candidate grain materials to the astrophysics community. Broadly, our updated threshold velocities that astrophysical dust grains may be more robust to shattering in the interstellar medium than previously assumed.

</details>

### [75] [Semi-global symplectic invariant of the champagne bottle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21985)
*Ognyan Christov*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 该论文研究了一个具有$S^1$对称双阱势（champagne bottle势）的两自由度完全可积哈密顿系统，计算了其Birkhoff正规形和焦点-焦点奇点附近的非平凡作用量，并得到了半全局辛不变量（semi-global symplectic invariant），最后与球面摆的对应结果进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该系统的势场形式——香槟瓶势（champagne bottle potential）——是可积系统中最简单的具有非平凡单值性（monodromy）而导致全局作用量不存在（no global action variables）的成员（Bates, 1991）。然而，目前对焦点-焦点奇点附近半全局辛不变量（semi-global symplectic invariant, Vũ Ngọc, 2003）的计算实例仍然很少，因此有必要对该系统进行具体计算并与已知例子（如球面摆）进行对比。

Method: 研究了形式为 $V = - (x_1^2 + x_2^2) + (x_1^2 + x_2^2)^2$ 的$S^1$对称双阱势（double well）对应的两自由度哈密顿系统；计算了该系统的Birkhoff正规形（Birkhoff normal form）以及焦点-焦点奇点（focus-focus singularity）附近的非平凡作用量（nontrivial action），进而得到了半全局辛不变量。

Result: 成功计算了香槟瓶势系统的Birkhoff正规形和焦点-焦点奇点附近的非平凡作用量，并得到了该系统的半全局辛不变量。

Conclusion: 将计算结果与Dullin (2013)给出的球面摆（spherical pendulum）的半全局辛不变量进行了比较，为该类可积系统的辛几何结构提供了新的计算实例。

Abstract: We study a two degrees of freedom Hamiltonian system describing the motion of a particle in a potential field of the form of $S^1$ symmetric double well, namely $V = - (x_1^2 + x_2^2) + (x_1^2 + x_2^2)^2$, known also as a champagne bottle potential.
  This system is completely integrable. The champagne bottle is the simplest member of a class of integrable systems that have no global action variables due to a non-trivial monodromy, Bates (1991). Beyond that, the geometric and dynamical properties of the system near the equilibrium are of primary interest. We calculate the Birkhoff normal form and the nontrivial action near the focus-focus singularity and obtain the semi-global symplectic invariant near focus-focus point, which is introduced by Vũ Ng\d{o}c (2003). Examples of such calculations are still few. We compare our result with the semi-global symplectic invariant of the spherical pendulum, calculated by Dullin (2013).

</details>


### [76] [Moving Boundary Problems for a Cuspon Equation and Reciprocal Associates: Exact Solution via Painleve' Symmetry Reduction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22565)
*Colin Rogers,Sandra Carillo*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文证明了Stefan型移动边界问题可以通过Painlevé II对称性约化求解，涵盖尖波子理论中的非线性演化方程及新型互逆孤子方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Stefan型移动边界问题（moving boundary problems of Stefan-type）在尖波子理论（cuspon theory）的非线性演化方程及互逆孤子方程中的可解性问题。

Method: 通过Painlevé II对称性约化（Painlevé II symmetry reduction）方法，对两类方程进行求解分析。

Result: 证明了Stefan型移动边界问题在尖波子理论方程及互逆孤子方程中均可通过Painlevé II对称性约化获得可解性。

Conclusion: Painlevé II对称性约化为解决Stefan型移动边界问题提供了有效的分析框架，适用于尖波子方程与互逆孤子系统。

Abstract: Here classes of moving boundary problems of Stefan-type for both an established non-linear evolution equation of cuspon theory and novel reciprocally linked solitonic equations are shown to be solvable via Painleve' II symmetry reduction.

### [77] [MetaDNS: Enhancing Exploration in Discrete Neural Samplers via Well-Tempered Metadynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21722)
*Xiaochen Du,Juno Nam,Jaemoo Choi,Wei Guo,Sathya Edamadaka,Junyi Sha,Elton Pan,Yongxin Chen,Molei Tao,Rafael Gómez-Bombarelli*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出MetaDNS（Metadynamics Discrete Neural Sampler）框架，将良态元动力学（well-tempered metadynamics）集成到离散扩散（discrete diffusion）或自回归采样器（autoregressive sampler）中，通过在选定低维坐标上维护自适应历史依赖偏置势，强制模型探索之前无法到达的高能垒区域，从而解决离散神经采样器在多重模态和高能垒分布采样中的模式坍塌问题，并实现自由能重建。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有离散神经采样器（如MDNS）存在模式坍塌（mode collapse）问题，无法采样模态间的高能垒区域，而这对于自由能估计和相变理解至关重要。

Method: MetaDNS框架将良态元动力学（well-tempered metadynamics）引入离散扩散或自回归采样器，通过沿选定低维坐标维护自适应、历史依赖的偏置势（bias potential），驱动模型探索先前无法到达的区域。

Result: 在低温基准任务（包括Ising模型、Potts模型和铜金二元合金）上，MetaDNS成功再现了热力学分布；与基于马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）的元动力学相比，以更少的偏置沉积步数（bias deposition steps）实现了可比较的探索性能。

Conclusion: MetaDNS能够完成标准神经采样器因缺乏高能样本而无法实现的自由能重建，并有效克服模式坍塌问题。

Abstract: Sampling from discrete distributions with multiple modes and energy barriers is fundamental to machine learning and computational physics. Recent discrete neural samplers like MDNS suffer from mode collapse and fail to sample high-energy barrier regions between modes, which is critical for free energy estimation and understanding phase transitions. We propose Metadynamics Discrete Neural Sampler (MetaDNS), a general framework integrating well-tempered metadynamics into discrete diffusion or autoregressive samplers. By maintaining an adaptive, history-dependent bias potential along selected low-dimensional coordinates, MetaDNS forces exploration of previously inaccessible regions, enabling free energy reconstruction infeasible with standard neural samplers due to a lack of high-energy samples. On challenging low-temperature benchmarks including Ising, Potts, and the copper-gold binary alloy, MetaDNS reproduces the thermodynamic distribution. Compared to MCMC-based metadynamics, MetaDNS also achieves comparable exploration requiring fewer bias deposition steps.
