### [78] [Aggregation-Fragmentation Processes with Broken Detailed Balance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22383)
*P. L. Krapivsky*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究了聚合-碎裂过程中团簇（cluster）的成对聚合与分裂行为。在聚合与碎裂速率不依赖于团簇质量的情况下，详细平衡（detailed balance）不成立，但通过拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）的精确解仍可推导出非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady state）。当碎裂速率按质量幂律标度（mass^β）变化时，仅β=1满足详细平衡。对于β≥0，稳态行为与质量无关模型（β=0）相似；当β<0时，系统会发生伴随连续质量损失的瞬时碎裂相变（shattering transition）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解聚合-碎裂过程中，当聚合与碎裂速率不满足质量依赖的详细平衡条件时，系统能否以及如何达到非平衡稳态，并揭示不同标度行为下的相变特征。

Method: 采用拉普拉斯变换的精确求解方法推导非平衡稳态；对于远离可解情形（β≠1）的参数区域，运用渐近分析（asymptotic techniques）方法研究稳态行为。

Result: 当β≥0时，稳态行为与质量无关模型（β=0）具有相似性；当β<0时，系统出现瞬时碎裂相变，伴随质量的连续损失。

Conclusion: 聚合-碎裂过程在非详细平衡条件下仍可存在非平衡稳态，且碎裂速率的标度指数β决定了系统是否发生碎裂相变。

Abstract: We study aggregation-fragmentation processes in which pairs of clusters can aggregate, and each cluster can break into two fragments. If the rates of aggregation and fragmentation do not depend on the masses, detailed balance does not hold, but nonequilibrium steady states can still be deduced from an exact solution for the Laplace transform. For models in which aggregation rates remain constant but fragmentation rates scale as $(\text{mass})^β$, detailed balance holds only when $β=1$. Away from this solvable case, we employ asymptotic techniques and show that when $β\geq 0$, the steady states share similarities with those from the mass-independent ($β=0$) model. An instantaneous shattering transition with continuous mass loss occurs when $β<0$.

</details>


### [79] [Thermodynamic Irreversibility of Training Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21933)
*Liu Ziyin,Yuanjie Ren,Adam Levine,Isaac Chuang*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文针对AI训练算法中引入的非平衡动力学过程，建立了一个统一框架来定义和分析训练算法的不可逆性。研究表明，四种不同的不可逆性刻画方式——数值后向误差、时间重整化修正、微观时间反演不对称性和随机热力学熵产生——在步长η的首阶近似下是等价的。该不可逆性产生了一种破坏时间反演对称性的涌现力，该力会打破非等距连续重参数化对称性但保持正交对称性，并导致学习轨迹普遍偏好最小化熵产生率的路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解AI训练算法的不可逆性是掌握现代AI系统学习动力学的关键一步，因为训练算法本质上引入了远离平衡态（far-from-equilibrium）的动力学过程。现有缺乏一个统一的理论框架来刻画和量化这种不可逆性。

Method: 建立了一个通用的数学框架，将四种表征动力学过程不可逆性的方式——数值后向误差（numerical backward error φ_DE）、时间重整化修正（time-renormalized correction φ_TR）、微观时间反演不对称性（microscopic time reversal asymmetry φ_TA）和随机热力学熵产生（stochastic-thermodynamic entropy production φ_ST）——进行形式化定义与比较，并证明它们在步长η的首阶下等价。

Result: 四种不可逆性度量在步长η的首阶近似下等价；不可逆性会产生一种破坏时间反演对称性的涌现力（emergent force），该力会打破非等距连续重参数化对称性但保持正交对称性；训练轨迹呈现普遍偏好最小化熵产生率（entropy production rate）的路径。

Conclusion: 训练算法的不可逆性可以被统一量化，且与随机热力学的熵产生直接关联；该框架揭示了不可逆性对学习轨迹对称性和优化路径偏好的深刻影响，为从非平衡统计力学（non-equilibrium statistical mechanics）角度理解AI学习动力学提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The training algorithms for AI systems all introduce far-from-equilibrium dynamical processes, and understanding the irreversibility of these algorithms is a fundamental step towards understanding the learning dynamics of modern AI systems. In this work, we establish a general framework for defining and analyzing the irreversibility of training algorithms. We show that four different ways to characterize the irreversibility of dynamical processes are equivalent to leading order in the step size $η$: numerical backward error $φ_{\rm DE}$, time-renormalized correction $φ_{\rm TR}$, microscopic time reversal asymmetry $φ_{\rm TA}$, and the (regularized) stochastic-thermodynamic entropy production $φ_{\rm ST}$. The irreversibility gives rise to a time-reversal-symmetry-breaking emergent force that generically breaks non-isometric continuous reparametrization symmetries, preserves orthogonal symmetries, and leads to a universal preference for those learning trajectories that minimize the entropy production rate.

</details>


### [80] [Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless-type Transition in Site Percolation on the Diamond Hierarchical Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22103)
*Takehisa Hasegawa,Kazuki Wataya,Tomoaki Nogawa*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过精确生成函数分析研究菱形层级晶格（diamond hierarchical lattice）上的点渗流（site percolation），发现该系统不存在从非渗流相到渗流相的常规相变，而是出现一个非渗流相和一个临界相（critical phase），其中最大团簇尺寸呈次广延（subextensive）标度行为，且关联长度在临界点附近呈现BKT型本质奇异性（essential singularity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索有限维分形网络上点渗流是否能够呈现临界相（critical phase），以及该临界相是否依赖于指数级体积增长（exponential volume growth）这一条件。

Method: 采用精确生成函数分析（exact generating-function analysis）研究菱形层级晶格上的点渗流；利用重整化群（renormalization group）递归关系分析临界点附近的标度行为；通过有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）分析验证数据坍塌（data collapse）。

Result: 点渗流在该晶格上不存在从非渗流相到渗流相的常规转变；当 p>p_c 时系统处于临界相，最大团簇尺寸以 N^{ψ(p)} 标度，分形指数 ψ(p) 连续变化；当 p→p_c^- 时关联长度呈 ξ(p)∼exp(const/√(p_c−p)) 的BKT型本质奇异性。

Conclusion: 临界相可以在有限维网络（finite-dimensional networks）的渗流问题中涌现，且并不需要指数级体积增长作为必要条件；菱形层级晶格上的临界相源于点稀释（site dilution）在重整化下保持相关（relevant）。

Abstract: We study site percolation on the diamond hierarchical lattice, a finite-dimensional fractal network, using an exact generating-function analysis. In contrast to bond percolation, site percolation on this lattice does not undergo a transition from a nonpercolating phase to a percolating phase. Instead, the system exhibits a nonpercolating phase for $p<p_{\rm c}$ and a critical phase for $p>p_{\rm c}$. In the critical phase, the size of the largest cluster remains subextensive, scaling as $N^{ψ(p)}$, where the fractal exponent $ψ(p)$ varies continuously with $p$. By analyzing the renormalization-group recursion relation in the vicinity of $p_{\rm c}$, we show that the correlation length exhibits a Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless-type essential singularity, $ξ(p)\sim \exp \left({\rm const}/\sqrt{p_{\rm c}-p}\right)$ for $p \to p_{\rm c}^-$, which is further confirmed by finite-size scaling analyses showing excellent data collapse. These results demonstrate that critical phases in percolation can emerge even on finite-dimensional networks and that exponential volume growth is not necessary for such phases to appear. We argue that the critical phase on the diamond hierarchical lattice stems from site dilution remaining relevant under renormalization.

</details>


### [81] [The cell fluid model with Curie-Weiss interactions: special cases and analytical results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22520)
*O. A. Dobush,M. P. Kozlovskii,I. V. Pylyuk,R. V. Romanik,M. A. Shpot*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文对一个具有Curie-Weiss相互作用的细胞流体模型（cell fluid model）进行了可解析处理的特殊情况分析。研究聚焦于全局吸引（global attraction）与局域排斥（local repulsion）之间的竞争，推导了强排斥极限下的临界点参数、状态方程以及binodal和spinodal曲线的闭合表达式，结果与平均场近似下的范德瓦尔斯晶格气体（van der Waals lattice gas）完全一致。此外，通过变形指数函数（deformed exponential function）的渐近展开，将模型有效性拓展至热力学稳定性的边际情形（$J_1=J_2$），并提供了此前工作中系统回避的$J_1=J_2\neq0$情况下的数值数据和相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受先前关于具有Curie-Weiss相互作用的细胞流体模型的大规模数值研究的启发，本文旨在探索该模型中若干可解析求解的特殊情形，从而更深入地理解全局吸引与局域排斥竞争机制所导致的临界行为与相变特性。

Method: 采用解析分析方法，在理想气体极限（$J_1=J_2=0$）和强排斥极限（$J_2\gg J_1$）等极限情形下推导闭合解；利用变形指数函数的渐近展开，将模型有效性扩展至边际情形（$J_1=J_2$）；对$J_1=J_2\neq0$情形辅以数值模拟和相图分析。

Result: 在强排斥极限下，得到了临界点参数、状态方程以及binodal和spinodal曲线的闭合表达式；状态方程与范德瓦尔斯晶格气体完全一致，序参量满足标准的Curie-Weiss方程；临界点附近的Landau展开与平均场近似下经典晶格气体的形式和对称性相同。还获得了$J_1=J_2\neq0$边际情形下的数值数据和相图。

Conclusion: 该细胞流体模型在强排斥极限下与平均场近似下的范德瓦尔斯晶格气体完全等价，且在边际情形$J_1=J_2$下模型仍保持热力学稳定性。本文的解析结果增强了模型的可解释性，并补充了先前工作在参数空间中的空白区域。

Abstract: Inspired by previous extensive numerical studies of a cell fluid model with Curie-Weiss interactions, we concentrate on some analytically tractable special cases in its description. The key ingredient of the model is a competition between global attraction and local repulsion interactions between particles with coupling constants $J_1$ and $J_2$, respectively. We provide analytical results in several limiting cases, including the ideal-gas limit $J_1=J_2=0$ and the strong-repulsion limit $J_2\gg J_1$. For $J_2\gg J_1$, a detailed analytical study is presented. We derive explicit expressions for the critical point parameters, the equation of state, and the binodal and spinodal curves in closed form. The equation of state is found to be in full agreement with that of the van der Waals lattice gas, and the order parameter satisfies the standard Curie-Weiss equation. In a neighborhood of the critical point, a Landau expansion is shown to have the same form and symmetry as that of the classical lattice gas within the mean-field approximation. Moreover, based on the explicit knowledge of a few leading terms in the asymptotic expansion of the deformed exponential function governing the physics of the cell model, we extend its validity range to include the marginal case of thermodynamic stability, $J_1=J_2$. In particular, this extension makes a consideration of the ideal-gas limit $J_1=J_2=0$ formally legitimate. For the generic marginal case $J_1=J_2\ne0$ systematically avoided in previous works, we present numerical data and phase diagrams that augment their findings for $J_2>J_1$.

</details>

### [83] [Robust fluctuating intertwined charge stripes in the Emery model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21585)
*Rong Zhang,Sijia Zhao,Hong-Chen Jiang,Brian Moritz,Edwin W. Huang,Thomas P. Devereaux*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过互补的密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）和行列式量子蒙特卡洛（DQMC）方法，系统研究了Emery模型中的电荷条带（charge stripes）与向列性（nematicity），首次在多轨道模型中揭示了电荷条带的氧轨道结构特征及其与向列性的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单带Hubbard模型中交织的自旋/电荷条带与超导电性密切相关，但其是否等价于多带Emery模型的低能物理仍存争议；Emery模型中电荷条带与向列性的综合图像尚未建立。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（DMRG）方法计算基态性质，辅以行列式量子蒙特卡洛（DQMC）方法分析静态电荷关联函数的氧轨道结构，并测量键电荷向列磁化率（bond-charge nematic susceptibility）及动能各向异性。

Result: DMRG确认Emery模型参数下存在氧中心电荷条带但振幅减弱；DQMC揭示电荷条带的实空间模式，其中指向"电荷河流"的p轨道上电荷密度调制更强；在费米子符号最大的参数集下首次观测到纯单向自旋和电荷条带的形成趋势，B1g分量在键电荷向列磁化率中占主导，且与动能各向异性的掺杂依赖相关。

Conclusion: Emery模型中间交织的电荷条带与向列性存在密切关联，补充了单带Hubbard模型之外的多轨道图像，为理解高温超导相关现象提供了新的微观机制视角。

Abstract: The single-band Hubbard model is one of the most extensively studied models in condensed matter physics, giving rise to intertwined spin and charge stripes that coexist with, or lie in the vicinity of, superconductivity in the phase diagram. However, whether the low energy physics of the single-band Hubbard model is fully equivalent to the multi-band (multi-orbital) Emery model remains an unsettled question. While the intertwined stripes and nematicity have been studied in the single-band Hubbard model, a comprehensive picture in the Emery model is lacking. In this paper, we focus on the less investigated intertwined charge stripes using complementary density matrix renormalization group (DMRG) and determinant quantum Monte Carlo (DQMC) techniques. Our ground state DMRG confirms the presence of the oxygen-centered charge stripes at a reduced amplitude in the Emery model parameter regime widely used in the study of intertwined stripes. Close analysis of the oxygen orbital structure of the static charge correlation function from DQMC reveals the charge stripe pattern in real-space, showcasing stronger charge density modulation on $p$-orbitals pointing along ``the rivers of charge'', consistent with DMRG. For the parameter set with the largest fermion signs, we managed to reach a temperature where the system first demonstrated tendencies to form purely unidirectional spin and charge stripes, and the $B_{1g}$ component becomes dominant in the bond-charge nematic susceptibility. This observation correlates with the doping dependence of the kinetic energy anisotropy, suggesting a close relation between the nematicity and charge stripes in the Emery model.

</details>


### [84] [Large-flavor route to a stable U(1) Dirac spin liquid on the maple-leaf lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21587)
*Yunchao Zhang,Andreas Feuerpfeil,Subir Sachdev,Ronny Thomale,Yasir Iqbal*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本论文表明，枫叶晶格（maple-leaf lattice）中的狄拉克自旋液体（Dirac spin liquid）可实现具有 $N_f=12$ 狄拉克费米子的 QED$_3$，远多于三角晶格和 kagome 晶格的 $N_f=4$。通过分类单体子（monopole）的对称性性质，发现存在五个对称性平凡的电荷-1 自旋单态单体子，其稳定性取决于动力学是否相关。枫叶晶格为检验紧致 QED$_3$ 在量子磁体中的稳定性提供了具体的大味数（large-flavor）平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维自旋哈密顿量中 $\mathrm{U}(1)$ 狄拉克自旋液体能否作为稳定基态存在是悬而未决的问题。紧致规范场（compact gauge field）的单体子事件可能会增殖并禁闭自旋子（spinon），破坏自旋液体。本文旨在寻找一种能规避该问题的具体晶格实现。

Method: 在枫叶晶格上构造狄拉克自旋液体，得到 QED$_3$ 理论，其中费米子味数 $N_f=12$。在完整微观对称群下对基本单体子进行分类，确定了五个对称性平凡的电荷-1 自旋单态单体子。利用大-$N_f$ 展开和蒙特卡洛估计计算单体子的反常维度（anomalous dimension），并判断其是否处于相关阈值（relevance threshold）附近。

Result: 枫叶晶格中的狄拉克自旋液体拥有 $N_f=12$ 狄拉克费米子。在微观对称性下，存在五个电荷-1 自旋单态单体子，它们在晶格对称性、时间反演和自旋旋转下均为平凡的。这些单体子的反常维度接近 $(2+1)$ 维中的相关阈值。此外，单体子分类还直接给出了单态、三重态和五重态单体子激发应出现的对称性扇区（symmetry sectors）的数值预测。

Conclusion: 枫叶晶格为检验紧致 QED$_3$ 在量子磁体中的稳定性提供了一个具体的、大味数的平台。该单体子分类结果可直接通过对称性分辨的精确对角化（symmetry-resolved exact diagonalization）和变分研究加以检验，从而为验证 $N_f=12$ 狄拉克自旋液体提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The $\mathrm{U}(1)$ Dirac spin liquid provides a useful organizing framework for frustrated magnets: it offers an algebraic parent state from which competing orders, confinement patterns, and low-energy spectral features can be understood. Whether such a state can occur as a stable ground state of a two-dimensional spin Hamiltonian remains an open question, because monopole events of the compact gauge field can proliferate and confine the spinons. Here, we show that the maple-leaf lattice provides a distinct route to this problem. Its Dirac spin liquid realizes QED$_3$ with $N_f=12$ Dirac fermions, substantially more than the $N_f=4$ theories of the triangular and kagome lattices. We classify the fundamental monopoles under the full microscopic symmetry group and find five charge-one spin-singlet monopoles that are trivial under lattice symmetries, time reversal, and spin rotation. The phase is therefore not protected by symmetry in the usual sense: its stability depends on whether these allowed monopoles are dynamically irrelevant. Available large-$N_f$ and Monte Carlo estimates place the charge-one monopole dimension close to the relevance threshold in $(2+1)$ dimensions, making the maple-leaf lattice a concrete large-flavor platform for testing the stability of compact QED$_3$ in a quantum magnet. The same monopole classification gives direct numerical predictions, identifying the symmetry sectors in which singlet, triplet, and quintet monopole excitations should appear. This provides a route to testing the $N_f=12$ Dirac spin liquid through symmetry-resolved exact diagonalization and variational studies of maple-leaf spin Hamiltonians.

</details>


### [85] [Observation of Altermagnetic Order Switching in Bulk MnTe by Polarized Neutron Diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21616)
*Zheyuan Liu,Shinichiro Asai,Shingo Takahashi,Hiraku Saito,Taro Nakajima,Takatsugu Masuda*

TL;DR: 本文利用极化中子衍射直接探测了MnTe中的交变磁序（altermagnetic order），观测到显著的核-磁干涉项，提供了体单晶中净Néel矢量的直接证据；同时发现由相对论性自旋-轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）产生的弱铁磁矩（weak ferromagnetic moment, WFM）与交变磁序耦合，二者均可通过毫特斯拉量级的磁场冷却实现翻转。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁序（altermagnetic order）即使在场论非相对论极限下也会破坏时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry, TRS），由此产生自旋极化与反常输运现象，但这些现象会被TRS连接的反相位畴（antiphase domains）互相补偿。因此，需直接探测交变磁序的存在并验证其净Néel矢量，以明确该有序态的本征特性。

Method: 采用极化中子衍射（polarized neutron diffraction）技术探测MnTe中的交变磁序，通过分析核-磁干涉项（nuclear-magnetic interference terms）检测Néel矢量的存在，并利用磁场冷却（magnetic field cooling）研究磁性翻转行为。

Result: 观测到显著的核-磁干涉项，直接证实了MnTe体单晶中存在净Néel矢量；同时发现由相对论性自旋-轨道耦合诱发的弱铁磁矩（WFM）与交变磁序耦合。毫特斯拉量级的磁场冷却即可同时翻转交变磁序与WFM。

Conclusion: 极化中子衍射能够直接探测交变磁序中的净Néel矢量，表明该有序态在真实材料中并非完全被反相位畴补偿；弱铁磁矩与交变磁序的耦合及其低场可翻转性，为交变磁体的操控与潜在自旋电子学应用提供了新途径。

Abstract: Altermagnetic order, characterized by the Néel vector, breaks time-reversal symmetry (TRS) even in the nonrelativistic limit. Although spin-polarized and anomalous transport phenomena emerge with this order, they are mutually compensated by TRS-connected antiphase domains with opposite Néel vectors. Here we employ polarized neutron diffraction to directly probe the altermagnetic order in MnTe. Pronounced nuclear-magnetic interference terms were observed, providing direct evidence of a net Néel vector in the bulk crystal. Moreover, a weak ferromagnetic moment (WFM), originating from relativistic spin-orbit coupling, was found to be coupled with the altermagnetic order. Both the altermagnetic order and the WFM can be switched by milli-Tesla-scale magnetic field cooling.

### [86] [Diagrammatic Monte Carlo for Fermionic Rényi Entanglement Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21632)
*Boyuan Shi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于相互作用晶格费米子（interacting lattice fermions）Renyi纠缠熵的直接图解蒙特卡洛（diagrammatic Monte Carlo）框架。该方法基于费米子分级交换表示（fermionic graded-swap representation）将纠缠熵问题转化为具有混合时间边界条件的复制路径积分，并结合连接行列式求和与多构型马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛采样，实现了对大系统高阶修正的逐阶计算。基准测试表明该方法在3×3哈伯德团簇上与精确对角化结果一致，且主要系统尺寸限制来自内存而非符号问题（sign problem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）是量子多体系统中的重要物理量，但费米子体系中的直接量子蒙特卡洛（quantum Monte Carlo）采样在高相互作用区域或大系统下常面临符号问题（sign problem）或计算成本过高的问题。现有方法在处理大尺寸费米子纠缠熵时受到严重限制，亟需开发能够规避这些瓶颈的数值框架。

Method: 从费米子分级交换表示（fermionic graded-swap representation）出发，将Renyi熵转化为具有混合时间边界条件的复制路径积分（replicated path integral）。该表示中复制动量（replica momenta）发生半移位，且相互作用展开具有行列式（determinant）形式，适用于连接行列式求和（connected-determinant summation）。进一步结合多构型马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov-chain Monte Carlo）采样器，逐阶获得高阶修正。

Result: 在3×3哈伯德团簇（Hubbard cluster）上，逐阶系数与精确对角化（exact diagonalization）结果一致，验证了方法的有效性。然后在大周期晶格上对方形子区域进行了生产性计算，结果表明主要系统尺寸限制来自内存（memory）而非传统的辅助场符号问题（auxiliary-field sign problem）。

Conclusion: 该工作为在直接量子蒙特卡洛采样成本高昂或受符号问题限制的参量区域中，进行费米子纠缠可观测量（fermionic entanglement observables）的图解计算迈出了重要一步。

Abstract: We develop a direct diagrammatic Monte Carlo framework for the Renyi entanglement entropy of interacting lattice fermions. The method starts from the fermionic graded-swap representation of Z_n[A]=Tr_Aρ_A^n, which converts the entropy problem into a replicated path integral with mixed temporal boundary conditions on the entangling region. In this representation the replica momenta are half-shifted, q_m=(2m+1)π/n, and the interaction expansion has a determinant form suitable for connected-determinant summation. We combine this expansion with a many-configuration Markov-chain Monte Carlo sampler to obtain order-by-order corrections for very large systems to very high orders. As a benchmark, we compare the order-by-order coefficients of a 3*3 Hubbard cluster with exact diagonalization. We then report a production calculation for a large periodic lattice with a square subregions. The dominant system-size limitation is therefore memory rather than a conventional auxiliary-field sign problem. The results provide a step toward diagrammatic calculations of fermionic entanglement observables in regimes where direct quantum Monte Carlo sampling is costly or sign-problem limited.

### [87] [Conductivity of a Non-Galilean--Invariant Fermi Liquid: Exact Solution of the Kinetic Equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21774)
*Tatia Kiliptari,Vladimir I. Yudson,Dmitrii L. Maslov*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过求解包含屏蔽库仑和z=3 Pomeranchuk临界相互作用的动力学方程，得到了无序、非伽利略不变费米液体电导率的精确表达式，并揭示了电子-电子相互作用仅通过准粒子散射时间影响电导率，同时阐明了碰撞与非流体动力学区间的交叉行为以及光学响应特性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过求解包含屏蔽库仑相互作用（screened Coulomb interaction）和z=3 Pomeranchuk临界相互作用的动力学方程（kinetic equation），推导出电导率的精确表达式，并利用Eliashberg近似考虑质量重整化（mass renormalization）以保持动力学方程与Kubo形式方法的一致性。

Result: 电子-电子相互作用仅通过准粒子散射时间（quasiparticle scattering time）τ_ee进入电导率表达式；碰撞与非流体动力学区间的交叉发生在1/τ_ee大于杂质散射率与探测频率Ω中较大者时；精确解给出了微扰理论无法触及的流体动力学区（Ω≪1/τ_ee）的光学响应；在z=3 Pomeranchuk量子临界点附近，光学电导率在碰撞与非流体动力学区间的交叉发生在普朗克尺度（Planckian scale）Ω∼T。

Conclusion: 该精确解统一了此前渐近结果，并揭示了在Pomeranchuk量子临界点附近，动力学方程与Kubo方法的一致性要求恰当引入Eliashberg近似下的质量重整化，从而确保光学电导率的交叉尺度处于普朗克标度。

Abstract: We obtain an exact expression for the conductivity of a disordered,
  non-Galilean-invariant Fermi liquid by solving the kinetic equation with both screened Coulomb and $z=3$ Pomeranchuk critical interactions. While consistent with previous asymptotic results, our solution shows that electron-electron interactions enter the conductivity solely via the quasiparticle scattering time, $τ_\mathrm{ee}$. Accordingly, the crossovers between the collisionless and hydrodynamic regimes occur when $1/τ_\mathrm{ee}$ becomes comparable to the larger of the impurity scattering rate and the probe frequency, $Ω$. In addition, the exact solution yields the optical response in the hydrodynamic regime, $Ω\ll 1/τ_\mathrm{ee}$, which is inaccessible within perturbation theory. Near a $z=3$ Pomeranchuk quantum critical point, consistency between the kinetic-equation and Kubo approaches requires proper inclusion of mass renormalization within the Eliashberg approximation, which also ensures that the crossover between the collisionless and hydrodynamic regimes in the optical conductivity occurs at the Planckian scale $Ω\sim T$.

Abstract: The ternary transition-metal oxide Fe$_2$Mo$_3$O$_8$ is a polar magnet characterized by a layered structure of magnetic Fe honeycomb lattices and non-magnetic Mo kagome lattices. Whereas previous studies have primarily focused on the chemical substitution at the Fe sites to modulate the magnetic properties, the Mo sites have remained largely unexplored due to the strong spin-singlet trimerization of Mo$^{4+}$ ions. In this study, we investigated the effect of substituting non-magnetic Pb$^{4+}$ and Zr$^{4+}$ ions into the Mo sites to intentionally disrupt the Mo trimers. Our results reveal that the disruption of the Mo spin-singlet state induces active spins within the Mo layer, resulting in the emergence of a ferromagnetic-like behavior that persists even at room temperature. Quantitative analysis that takes into account the weight fraction of the main phase suggests an effective spin $S = 1/2$ state per active Mo ion upon trimer disruption. ### [90] [Emergent magnetic and charge ordered phases in freestanding ultrathin \ce{LaVO3}](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22415)
*Ashutosh Anand,Mukul Kabir*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）对自由站立超薄LaVO₃薄膜进行第一性原理计算，系统分析不同厚度下的磁结构及掺杂效应。

Abstract: Transition metal oxide perovskites are an ideal platform for exploring the interplay between spin, orbital, charge and lattice degrees of freedom. Among them, \ce{LaVO3} has been extensively studied in heterostructures and superlattices, where exotic phases have been reported. Motivated by the advances in freestanding oxide membranes, we investigate the intrinsic properties of freestanding ultrathin \ce{LaVO3} films using density functional theory. Our calculations reveal a sequence of magnetic phase transitions with thickness, starting from stripe-AFM in monolayer until the bulk like C-AFM is recovered. Beyond four layers, polar catastrophe driven charge transfer dopes the surface layers giving rise to stripe-AFM and ferromagnetic surface states while the central layers remain bulk like. We further explore this fact by studying charge doped monolayer, discovering that hole doping drives the system into ferromagnetic state. Doping also induced charge ordering in the system. A striped charge ordering pattern is observed at 0.5 h/fu, while a 3:1 stripe pattern emerges at 0.25 h/fu, indicating that the periodicity of the superstructure changes with doping concentration.

### [91] [Revisiting the high-field phase diagram of the topological cubic helimagnet SrFeO$_{3}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22517)

Method: 研究通过分析磁场方向依赖性（field-orientation dependence）的磁相图，并建立包含立方体单离子各向异性（cubic single-ion anisotropy）以及动量空间双线性（bilinear）和双二次（biquadratic）相互作用的有效自旋哈密顿量（effective spin Hamiltonian）来定量描述该体系。

Conclusion: 配体-空穴带（ligand-hole band）形成所导致的电子巡游性（electronic itinerancy）对于稳定多-Q相（multiple-Q phases）具有关键作用。

Abstract: The cubic perovskite SrFeO$_{3}$ is a prototypical centrosymmetric itinerant magnet that hosts a quadruple-${\mathbf Q}$ hedgehog-antihedgehog lattice and exhibits a complex magnetic-field-temperature phase diagram. Yet, the microscopic mechanism underlying the emergence of its versatile multiple-${\mathbf Q}$ phases remains unresolved. Here, we elucidate the field-orientation dependence of the magnetic phase diagram and establish an effective spin Hamiltonian for SrFeO$_{3}$ that incorporates a cubic single-ion anisotropy together with bilinear and biquadratic interactions in momentum space. In addition, we observe magnetoelastic signatures of a first-order valence transition upon entering the forced FM phase at 40 T, which would be attributed to the suppression of negative charge transfer. These findings emphasize the pivotal importance of electronic itinerancy arising from the formation of a ligand-hole band in stabilizing multiple-${\mathbf Q}$ phases.

</details>


### [92] [Competing incommensurability, electronic correlations, and superconductivity in a hybrid transition metal dichalcogenide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22522)
*Jean C. Souza,Moshe Haim,Lorenzo Crippa,Hyeonhu Bae,Edanel Fishbein,Jonathan Ruhman,Binghai Yan,Amit Kanigel,Roser Valentí,Nurit Avraham,Haim Beidenkopf*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy）在层状过渡金属二硫族化合物（transition-metal dichalcogenide）4Hb-TaS₂中发现了体相非公度势（incommensurate potential），该势场源于交替的1T和1H层之间的晶格失配。通过密度泛函理论（DFT）与动力学平均场理论（DMFT）结合，揭示了该非公度势通过调控层距、杂化和电荷转移，驱动体系进入掺杂莫特（Mott）绝缘体 regime，并产生零偏压共振（zero-bias resonance）。研究还表明体超导电性与此势场及电荷转移相互竞争，确立了非公度势作为混合型过渡金属二硫族化合物中一个先前被忽略的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管非公度性（incommensurability）在三维体系中普遍存在，但莫尔势（moiré potential）在体材料中的作用尚未得到充分探索。本文旨在填补这一空白，研究在体相过渡金属二硫族化合物中非公度势对电子关联、电荷密度波（charge-density wave）和非常规超导电性的影响。

Method: 实验上采用扫描隧道显微镜（scanning tunneling microscopy）直接观测体相4Hb-TaS₂中的非公度势；理论上结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）与动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT），分析晶格失配对层间距、杂化（hybridization）和电荷转移（charge transfer）的局域调控效应。

Result: 发现1T与1H层之间的晶格失配产生了非公度势，该势场与共存的非公度电荷密度波相互作用，抑制了其长程有序；局域层间距调制进而调节了关联的1T层与金属性1H层之间的杂化和电荷转移，导致电荷重新分布，驱动体系进入掺杂莫特（doped Mott） regime；剩余局域磁矩发生自屏蔽（self-screened），产生零偏压共振（zero-bias resonance）；体超导电性（bulk superconductivity）与上述势场景观和电荷转移之间存在竞争关系。

Conclusion: 研究确立了非公度势（incommensurate potential）是混合型过渡金属二硫族化合物中一个此前被忽视的关键要素，它在电子关联、电荷密度波序与非常规超导电性之间的相互竞争中扮演核心角色。

Abstract: The engineering of superlattices in two-dimensional van der Waals materials has enabled the realization of rich phase diagrams hosting topological and strongly correlated phases. While incommensurability is widespread in three-dimensional systems, the role of moiré potentials in bulk materials remains largely unexplored. Here, using scanning tunneling microscopy, we demonstrate that a bulk transition-metal dichalcogenide polytype, 4Hb-TaS$_2$, hosts an emergent incommensurate potential between its alternating 1T and 1H layers. Interplay with a concomitant incommensurate charge-density wave suppresses the long-range order of this potential, leading to intricate coupling with electronic correlations in the doped 1T surface layer. Combining density functional theory with dynamical mean-field theory, we show that the lattice mismatch locally modulates the interlayer distance, thereby tuning both hybridization and charge transfer between the correlated 1T and metallic 1H layers. This redistribution of charge drives the system towards a doped Mott regime, in which the remaining local moments become self-screened, giving rise to a zero-bias resonance. We further find that bulk superconductivity competes with both the underlying landscape and the associated charge transfer. Our results establish incommensurate potentials as a previously overlooked ingredient in hybrid transition-metal dichalcogenides, highlighting their central role in the interplay between electronic correlations, charge-density-wave order, and unconventional superconductivity.

### [93] [Nonlinear Magnon Magnetic Moment Transport in Triangular-Lattice f-Wave Antialtermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22614)
*Volodymyr P. Kravchuk,Kostiantyn V. Yershov,Bastián Pradenas,Robin R. Neumann,Rodrigo Jaeschke-Ubiergo,Ricardo Zarzuela,Jairo Sinova,Jeroen van den Brink,Alexander Mook*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 磁振子的非线性热输运效应（如Edelstein效应和自旋劈裂效应）为f波反交变磁体中磁振子的存在提供了清晰的实验可观测特征。

Abstract: We study the spin excitations in the frustrated coplanar 120-degree ground state of the triangular-lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet and demonstrate that they carry a magnetic moment perpendicular to the plane in which the spins order, despite the ground-state sublattice moments having no out-of-plane component. The symmetry of the momentum dependence of the magnetic moment and energy of the magnons renders the system an odd-parity f-wave magnet. Extending this model to a stack of antiferromagnetically coupled triangular layers provides a realization of magnons in a three-dimensional f-wave antialtermagnet. We show that nonlinear thermal transport effects of magnons, such as Edelstein and spin-splitter effects, provide clear experimental signatures of magnons in f-wave antialtermagnets.

### [94] [Simultaneously monitoring Ga adsorption and desorption kinetics on GaN(0001) using four in situ techniques](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22279)
*Huaide Zhang,Philipp John,Jingxuan Kang,Lutz Geelhaar,Yongjin Cho,Oliver Brandt*

Main category: physics.app-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解Ga在GaN(0001)表面的吸附与解吸动力学对优化GaN薄膜生长工艺至关重要，但此前缺乏多技术同步、覆盖度范围广泛的系统研究。

Method: 同步使用四种原位技术：反射高能电子衍射（reflection high-energy electron diffraction, RHEED）、激光反射测量（laser reflectometry）、视线四极质谱（line-of-sight quadrupole mass spectrometry）和光学高温测量（optical pyrometry）。在从亚单层到液滴区（droplet regime）的Ga覆盖度范围内进行通量和温度依赖实验；并基于Ga吸附、扩散和解吸过程建立统一的动力学模型（unified kinetic model），对四种技术的瞬态响应进行定量拟合。

Result: 尽管四种技术的瞬态响应特征各异，但其信号及随表面覆盖率的变化趋势均能被统一动力学模型定量复现。阿伦尼乌斯分析（Arrhenius analysis）给出Ga吸附层解吸的活化能（activation energy）为(2.87±0.04)eV。

Conclusion: 多原位技术的同步测量结合统一动力学模型，能够准确描述GaN(0001)表面Ga的吸附-解吸行为，获得的活化能值可为GaN薄膜生长工艺的精确调控提供定量依据。

Abstract: We present a systematic investigation of Ga adsorption and desorption kinetics on the wurtzite GaN(0001) surface using four in situ techniques operated simultaneously: reflection high-energy electron diffraction, laser reflectometry, line-of-sight quadrupole mass spectrometry, and optical pyrometry. Flux- and temperature-dependent experiments are performed for Ga coverages ranging from the submonolayer to the droplet regime. Despite their distinct transient responses, the signals from all four techniques and their trends with surface coverage are quantitatively reproduced by a unified kinetic model of Ga adsorption, diffusion, and desorption. An Arrhenius analysis of the Ga adlayer desorption yields an activation energy of (2.87 $\pm$ 0.04) eV.

### [95] [Constraining Spatial Curvature with Priors from Swampland Conjectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22362)
*Simran Arora,Hun Jang,Shinji Mukohyama*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在弦论启发的swampland理论先验下，研究了具有指数势的五元暗能量（quintessential dark energy）模型（允许非零空间曲率），通过Planck CMB、DESI BAO和Ia型超新星数据进行贝叶斯推断，发现该先验对曲率参数Ω_k的推断值产生轻微偏移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 弦论中的swampland猜想对有效场论施加了严格约束，例如de Sitter猜想（de Sitter conjecture）排除平坦势的ΛCDM极限，距离猜想（distance conjecture）限制场位移幅度。这些理论先验可能改变标准宇宙学参数推断结果，但现有研究对此探讨不足。

Method: 构建包含非零空间曲率的指数势五元暗能量模型的动力学系统，数值求解宇宙学演化并展示相空间行为；将swampland先验（包括对斜率参数λ的de Sitter猜想约束和场位移范围的距离猜想约束）引入贝叶斯推断，联合分析Planck CMB、DESI BAO和Ia型超新星数据。

Result: 在开放宇宙（Ω_k>0）中，曲率相关的不动点可在较陡势（与swampland兼容）下支持加速膨胀；swampland先验会使曲率参数Ω_k的后验推断值相较于理论无关先验（如宽平先验）产生轻微偏移。

Conclusion: 理论驱动的swampland先验对宇宙学参数推断具有可观测影响，尤其在曲率参数上体现为轻微偏移，表明弦论约束在宇宙学数据分析中不可忽视。

Abstract: We study a string-motivated theoretical prior on the quintessential dark energy model with exponential potential, \( V(φ) = V_0 e^{-λφ} \), allowing for non-zero spatial curvature. First, we formulate the corresponding dynamical system and investigate its cosmological evolution numerically, illustrating the phase-space behaviour and the influence of curvature on the background dynamics. In open universes (\( Ω_k > 0 \)), it has been suggested that a curvature-related fixed point may support accelerated expansion even for relatively steep potentials compatible with swampland considerations. Next, we explicitly impose swampland-motivated priors on the slope parameter $λ$, restricting it to values consistent with the de Sitter conjecture that excludes the (curved) $Λ$CDM limit. Furthermore, we restrict our considerations to the range of field excursion that is consistent with the swampland distance conjecture. Our primary interest is the possibility that such theoretically-motivated priors may shift values of cosmological parameters inferred by observational data, compared with the standard analysis based on theory-agnostic priors such as a sufficiently wide flat prior. We examine this possibility using a combination of Planck CMB data, DESI BAO measurements, and recent Type Ia supernova samples, performing a Bayesian inference of the model parameters. Our analysis indicates that the swampland-motivated prior mildly shifts the values of $Ω_k$.

Method: 利用标准模型隐藏扇区（hidden sector）中自然产生的暗光子（dark photon），通过将其与标准光子耦合（coupling dark photons with standard ones）实现磁生成（magnetogenesis）。

Result: 暗光子-标准光子耦合机制能够产生足够的宇宙磁场，且不存在现有模型中的局限性（如强耦合和反作用问题）。

Abstract: Magnetic fields observed across cosmic scales are difficult to explain within conventional physics. A primordial origin is, thus, often assumed. While a nonminimal coupling of the inflaton with the electromagnetic field could theoretically generate magnetic fields of about $10^{-13}$ G, this approach faces significant issues, including strong-coupling and backreaction problems. ``Dark photons", arising naturally in hidden-sector extensions of the Standard Model, provide a well-motivated framework for addressing various cosmic as well as particle physics issues. We demonstrate that coupling dark photons with standard ones can result in adequate magnetogenesis without the limitations of existing models. This minimal mechanism may also provide insights into unresolved cosmic mysteries.

### [97] [Signatures of Modified Gravity Below $\mathcal{O}(10)$ Mpc in a Dynamical Dark Energy Background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22309)
*Yo Toda,Adrià Gómez-Valent*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 基于CMB、重子声学振荡和Ia型超新星等宇宙学数据，本文在CPL参数化动态暗能量背景下，通过两个红移区间（0≤z<1和1≤z≤3）参数化晚期宇宙中有效引力耦合偏离牛顿常数的行为。研究发现，为实现低红移处结构增长的抑制并与CMB约束一致，修正引力效应需出现在共动尺度λ_c~O(10) Mpc以下；包含修正引力效应后，CPL背景模型相对于ΛCDM的偏好从中等增强至略强的水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）、重子声学振荡（baryon acoustic oscillations）和Ia型超新星数据表明，驱动宇宙加速膨胀的成分可能具有动力学特征（置信度约2.5-3σ），但标准CPL模型与红移空间畸变（redshift-space distortion）数据存在轻微张力，因此需要探索是否可通过修正引力（modified gravity）效应来缓解这一不一致性。

Method: 在CPL形式的动力学暗能量（dynamical dark energy）背景下，将有效引力耦合（effective gravitational coupling）偏离牛顿常数（Newton's constant）的行为参数化为两个红移区间（0≤z<1和1≤z≤3），并引入共动尺度截断λ_c。利用Planck PR4、DESI DR2、Pantheon+（或DES-Dovekie）及红移空间畸变数据，通过贝叶斯分析确定λ_c和引力偏离幅度的最优值。

Result: 为实现低红移处结构增长的必要抑制并满足CMB约束（主要来自低ℓ处的晚期ISW效应和高ℓ处的引力透镜效应），修正引力效应必须出现在小于λ_c~O(10) Mpc的尺度上。数据分析确认，标准引力下的CPL背景模型相对于ΛCDM具有中等偏好；引入修正引力后，该偏好增强至略强水平，CPL参数基本保持不变但略微移向quintom区域。

Conclusion: 晚期宇宙中小尺度（≤O(10) Mpc）的修正引力效应能够缓解CPL动力学暗能量模型与结构增长数据之间的张力，并提升相对于ΛCDM的统计偏好，但CPL参数本身未发生显著改变，而是被轻微推向quintom区域。

Abstract: Cosmological data from the cosmic microwave background (CMB), baryon acoustic oscillations, and Type Ia supernovae suggest that the component driving the accelerated expansion of the Universe may be dynamical at the $\sim 2.5$-$3σ$ CL. The best-fit CPL model produces a level of cosmic structure similar to that of $Λ$CDM, with both models exhibiting mild tension with redshift-space distortion data. In this {\it Letter}, we parametrize possible departures of the effective gravitational coupling from Newton's constant in the late Universe, below a comoving scale $λ_c$, using two redshift bins, $0 \leq z < 1$ and $1 \leq z \leq 3$. We then determine the optimal values of $λ_c$ and the amplitude of these deviations from General Relativity, assuming a background with dynamical dark energy in CPL form. We find that, in order to achieve the required suppression of structure growth at low redshifts while remaining consistent with CMB constraints -- primarily from the late-time ISW effect at low $\ell$ and lensing at high $\ell$ -- modified gravity effects must appear on scales smaller than $λ_c \sim \mathcal{O}(10)\,\mathrm{Mpc}$. Using Planck PR4, DESI DR2, Pantheon+ (or DES-Dovekie) and redshift-space distortions data we confirm that a CPL background with standard gravity is moderately preferred over $Λ$CDM; this preference strengthens to a mildly strong level when modified gravity effects are included. This enhancement leaves the CPL parameters largely unchanged, but shifts them slightly further into the quintom region.

### [98] [Primordial black holes in excursion set theory: Formation probabilities, mass functions, and window functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22789)
*Hayami Iizuka,Daiki Saito,Koki Tokeshi*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文基于 excursionset 理论，研究不同窗口函数（window function）对原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）质量函数（mass function）的影响，发现低质量端的质量函数与 Carr 公式存在偏差，该偏差源于关联噪声（correlated noise）的普遍性，但 Carr 公式在特征质量附近仍具有良好的近似效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在原初黑洞形成理论中，excursionset 框架下的粗粒化尺度（coarse-graining scale）变化会导致随机密度对比（stochastic density contrast）的响应由有色噪声（colored noise）描述。然而，文献中常用的不同窗口函数对 PBH 形成概率及最终质量函数的具体影响尚不明确，需要系统研究。

Method: 基于 excursionset 理论，将粗粒化尺度变化引起的随机密度对比响应建模为有色噪声。针对文献中常用的几种窗口函数，分别计算其对应的 PBH 形成概率（formation probability）及质量函数，并与 Carr 公式的结果进行比较。

Result: 研究发现，PBH 质量函数的低质量端（low-mass tail）与 Carr 公式的预测存在差异。该差异源于关联噪声（correlated noise）的普遍存在，使得不同窗口函数下的形成概率不再简并（degeneracy）。然而，当使用光滑的傅里叶空间窗口函数（smooth window function in Fourier space）时，Carr 公式在特征质量尺度（characteristic mass scale）附近仍能提供实用的估计。

Conclusion: 窗口函数的选择对 PBH 质量函数的低质量端有显著影响；关联噪声破坏了形成概率的简并性，导致与 Carr 公式的偏差。尽管如此，Carr 公式在特征质量附近仍是有效的近似工具，前提是采用傅里叶空间中的光滑窗口函数。

Abstract: We study the mass function of primordial black holes (PBHs) within the excursion-set theory, in which the response of the stochastic density contrast to the variation of the coarse-graining scale is described by colored noises. For several window functions often used in the literature, we investigate how this choice affects the formation probability as well as the resultant mass function of PBHs. It is found that the low-mass tail of the mass function differs from the one predicted from Carr's formula. The difference comes from the prevalence of correlated noises, by which degeneracy of the formation probabilities ceases to exist. Nevertheless, Carr's formula still provides a practical estimation in the vicinity of the characteristic mass scale, as long as a smooth window function in Fourier space is used.

### [99] [Dominant vibronic relaxation channels in a europium-based molecular qubit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21520)
*Neil Iyer*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过无拟合参数的DFT/TD-DFT与Redfield理论相结合的计算框架，成功复现了Eu核自旋量子比特Eu(dpphen)(NO3)3的纵向自旋-晶格弛豫时间T1，揭示了分子内振动耦合（vibronic coupling）主导的慢弛豫通道，并识别出dpphen摇摆模和硝酸根摇摆模为关键弛豫通道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分子自旋量子比特（molecular spin qubits）因其合成可调谐性和明确的电子结构，在量子信息处理中具有潜力。然而，理解并控制其自旋-晶格弛豫机制，特别是从第一性原理层面定量预测弛豫时间，仍是关键挑战。本文旨在建立无拟合参数的理论框架，以揭示Eu核自旋量子比特中纵向弛豫的微观机制。

Method: 采用无拟合参数的计算框架，将密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）、含时密度泛函理论（time-dependent DFT, TD-DFT）与Redfield理论（Redfield theory）相结合，基于单分子气相模型计算Eu(dpphen)(NO3)3核自旋量子比特的纵向自旋-晶格弛豫时间T1。

Result: 慢弛豫分量T1,long的计算值55.88 s（4.2 K）与实验值41.39 s吻合于1.4倍以内，而快弛豫分量T1,short的计算偏差达66倍，表明后者受缺失的晶格和分子间效应影响。5D0→7F0光学跃迁计算误差仅1.1%。识别出dpphen摇摆模（332.02 cm-1）为振动耦合主通道，硝酸根摇摆模（180.57 cm-1）为核自旋环境的主要调制者，与近最大四极不对称参数η=0.941一致。

Conclusion: 研究建立了单分子弛豫基线，表明分子内振动耦合主导慢弛豫通道，而快弛豫通道需考虑晶格效应。基于识别出的关键振动模式，建议通过配体刚性化（ligand rigidification）和取代策略抑制退相干，为分子自旋量子比特的设计提供理论指导。

Abstract: Molecular spin qubits offer a versatile platform for quantum information processing due to their synthetic tunability and well-defined electronic structure. Here, a fitted-parameter-free computational framework combining density functional theory (DFT), time-dependent DFT (TD-DFT), and Redfield theory is applied to investigate the longitudinal spin-lattice relaxation time $T_1$ of the Eu nuclear spin qubit Eu(dpphen)(NO3)3. Using a single-molecule gas-phase model, the experimental long relaxation component $T_{1,\mathrm{long}} = 41.39$ s is reproduced within a factor of 1.4 (calculated: 55.88 s at 4.2 K), indicating that the slow relaxation channel is governed by intramolecular vibronic coupling. In contrast, the calculated $T_{1,\mathrm{short}}$ deviates by a factor of 66, highlighting the importance of crystal lattice and intermolecular effects absent from the model. The experimental $^5D_0 \rightarrow {}^7F_0$ optical transition is reproduced to within 1.1%, supporting the accuracy of the electronic structure description. Vibrational analysis identifies a large-amplitude dpphen rocking mode at a frequency of $332.02~\mathrm{cm}^{-1}$ as the dominant vibronic coupling channel, while electric field gradient (EFG) derivative analysis independently identifies another nitrate-rocking mode at $180.57~\mathrm{cm}^{-1}$ as the primary modulator of the nuclear spin environment via nitrate motion. These results are consistent with a near-maximal quadrupole asymmetry parameter $η= 0.941$, which creates state mixing through off-diagonal quadrupolar terms. Overall, the results establish a single-molecule relaxation baseline and suggest targeted ligand rigidification and substitution strategies to suppress decoherence.

</details>

Abstract: High entropy oxides (HEOs) are a class of materials with vast compositional space and tunable properties, making them attractive for applications in thermoelectrics, magnetism, ionic conduction, and beyond. It is therefore essential to probe the local modulations in atomic, chemical, and electronic structure as a function of growth conditions. Here, advanced S/TEM techniques, including 4D-STEM combined with electron energy loss spectroscopy and energy-dispersive X-ray spectroscopy are used to investigate the effect of substrate temperature on structure and strain at the nanoscale regime in HEO thin films. Our results demonstrate that identical HEO compositions can accommodate distinct strain and defect states in thin film form and highlight how synthesis conditions can be leveraged to manipulate strain and Co valence. The Raman spectroscopic studies further confirm the cubic inverse spinel phase. The Magnetic properties were explored as a function of temperature, ranging from 10 to 300 K, a ferromagnetic behaviour was observed with the highest saturation magnetization of 75.87 emu g(-1) and a coercivity of 723 Oe at room temperature. The variation of the magnetic entropy was measured indirectly using the Maxwell approach with an increasing magnetic field. A maximum of Delta(S)=1.71 J K-1 was reached around 32 K. At 180 K, the associated adiabatic temperature change, Delta (Tmax), was 0.93 K, with a large RCP value of 7.58 J kg-1 was measured, which is reasonably high for the corresponding nanoparticles (NPs). This work may suggest that 1D CFO nanofibers offer a promising route for the production of nanostructured magnetic materials, potentially impacting various electronic and electromagnetic device applications at low temperatures.

### [103] [Uncovering Antipolar Ordering and Pressure-Tunable Phases in Hexagonal LaN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21767)
*Atanu Paul,Laurent Bellaiche,Charles Paillard*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理密度泛函理论预测了六方氮化镧（LaN）中存在反极性（antipolar）不稳定性，并揭示了极性（polar）与反极性相之间的压力驱动竞争，表明该二元氮化物体系具有类反铁电（antiferroelectric-like）行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索六方LaN中是否存在反极性不稳定性，并理解极性相与反极性相之间的竞争关系及其压力调控机制。

Method: 采用第一性原理密度泛函理论（first-principles density functional theory）进行计算，从非极性六方相出发，识别极性（polar）和反极性（antipolar）的布里渊区中心声子不稳定性（zone-center phonon instabilities），并分析不同相在不同压力下的相对稳定性。

Result: 在六方LaN中发现了竞争性的极性和反极性声子不稳定性，分别导致稳定的纤锌矿（wurtzite, WZ）相和六方反极性（hexagonal antipolar, AP）相。AP相在常温常压下相对于WZ相是亚稳态的，两相之间存在有限能垒。随着压力增加，WZ与AP相间的能垒降低，且AP相中的亚晶格极化（sublattice polarization）增大而WZ相中减小。在更高压力下，岩盐相（rock-salt）和四方相（tetragonal）变得比六方相更稳定。

Conclusion: 六方LaN中极性相与反极性相之间存在压力驱动的竞争，反极性相的实现在低压区更为有利；该体系表现出类反铁电行为，且通过AP中间态可能存在极化翻转（polarization-switching）路径。

Abstract: We predict an antipolar instability in hexagonal LaN using first-principles density functional theory. Starting from a nonpolar hexagonal phase, we identify competing polar and antipolar zone-center phonon instabilities. Condensation of the polar and antipolar modes stabilizes, respectively, dynamically stable wurtzite (WZ) phase and an hexagonal antipolar (AP) phase which is characterized by alternating local polarization and zero net macroscopic polarization within the unit cell. At ambient conditions, the AP phase is metastable with respect to the WZ phase, and a finite energy barrier exists between these phases, suggesting a possible polarization-switching pathway via the AP intermediate state. The energy barrier between the WZ and AP phases decreases with increasing pressure, indicating enhanced tunability between polar and antipolar states. The sublattice polarization increases with pressure in the AP phase, while it decreases in the WZ phase. We further find that, with increasing pressure, the rock-salt and tetragonal phases of LaN become more stable than the hexagonal phases (AP and WZ). Consequently, the realization of the AP phase is more favorable in the low-pressure regime, where hexagonal phases remain energetically competitive. These results demonstrate pressure-driven competition between polar and antipolar phases in LaN and point toward antiferroelectric-like behavior in this binary nitride system.

Abstract: Serpentinization of ultramafic rocks is a naturally occurring mineralogical process that can generate molecular hydrogen through the oxidation of ferrous iron during water-rock reaction. Although the resource potential is large, the natural reaction is kinetically limited, and practical hydrogen recovery requires methods that can accelerate conversion without imposing an energy penalty that exceeds the value of the hydrogen produced. This short communication reports a preliminary atmospheric-pressure microwave serpentinization experiment using a water-saturated 2 g crushed olivine sample. Microwave irradiation produced a rapid increase in measured hydrogen concentration compared with conventional hot-plate heating under otherwise similar conditions. The preliminary experiment showed approximately a 12-fold increase in hydrogen concentration and an apparent rate increase from about 2 ppb s$^{-1}$ for conventional heating to about 10 ppb s$^{-1}$ during microwave exposure. These results suggest that electromagnetic stimulation can enhance serpentinization kinetics, likely through rapid volumetric heating, selective coupling to iron-bearing phases, and localized thermal gradients. The result provides an initial experimental basis for evaluating microwave stimulation as a route to accelerated geologic hydrogen production and motivates follow-on measurements using calibrated gas analysis, absorbed-power measurements, dielectric characterization, and elevated-pressure testing.

Motivation: 联苯网络（biphenylene network, BPN）作为一种新型二维碳同素异形体（2D carbon allotrope），具有潜在的应用前景，但其与金属原子的相互作用机制及金属修饰对其物理性能的影响尚不清楚，有必要进行系统研究。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）对单层和双层BPN上Fe原子的吸附进行结构优化与吸附能分析，并评估了原始及Fe修饰BPN的力学性能和电导率。

Result: 单层BPN上Fe吸附随覆盖度升高而增强，最稳定构型出现在Fe/C比为50%时；双层BPN中Fe的最优吸附位在层间四元环中心，吸附能为-4.3 eV。Fe吸附对BPN的面内力学性能影响较小，但显著增强了双层BPN的面外力学响应：面外弹性常数C33从24.59 GPa提升至515.63 GPa（Fe/C=25%）。Fe修饰后的BPN表现出显著的电导各向异性，300 K下整体电导率达10^5 S/m量级。

Conclusion: Fe吸附可显著增强双层BPN的层间相互作用，大幅提升其面外刚度，且对BPN原有的面内优异力学稳定性影响微弱；Fe修饰后的BPN兼具高电导率和显著各向异性，在纳米电子和结构材料领域具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: Biphenylene network (BPN) is a 2D carbon allotrope that exhibits promising potential for applications. In this work, we systematically investigated the adsorption characteristics of Fe atoms on monolayer and bilayer BPN. Structural optimization and adsorption energy analysis reveal that, for monolayer BPN, the average adsorption gradually enhances with increasing Fe coverage, indicating a strengthening of Fe-substrate interactions. The most stable configuration is identified at an Fe/C ratio of 50 %. For bilayer BPN, the energetically preferred adsorption site for Fe atom is located at the center of the interlayer four-membered ring, with an average adsorption energy of -4.3 eV. Mechanical properties are further evaluated for pristine and Fe-decorated BPN. The results demonstrate that monolayer and bilayer BPN possess relatively high in-plane Young's and shear moduli, indicative of excellent in-plane mechanical stability. Fe adsorption is found to have only a minor effect on the in-plane mechanical properties of both monolayer and bilayer BPN, suggesting that the in-plane stiffness is predominantly governed by the intrinsic carbon framework. In contrast, the out-of-plane mechanical response of bilayer BPN is significantly affected by Fe incorporation. The effective out-of-plane elastic constant C33 of pristine bilayer BPN is calculated to be 24.59 GPa, indicating relatively weak interlayer interactions and facile deformation along the out-of-plane direction. Notably, this property can be substantially enhanced by interlayer Fe adsorption, with C33 increasing dramatically to 515.63 GPa upon an Fe/C ratio of 25 %. The calculations on pristine and Fe-decorated BPN reveal pronounced anisotropy in the conductivity, with the value along one direction being significantly higher than that along the other. At 300 K, the overall conductivity is on the order of 10^5 S/m.

</details>


### [107] [High-field Magnetotransport Studies of Surface Conducting Diamonds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22032)
*Kaijian Xing,Daniel L. Creedon,Golrokh Akhgar,Steve A. Yianni,Jeffrey C. McCallum,Lothar Ley,Dong-Chen Qi,Christopher I. Pakes*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用显著改进的理论磁输运模型，分别对表面导电氢-terminated金刚石（H-diamond）霍尔条器件和Al/Al₂O₃/V₂O₅/H-diamond MOSFETs的磁输运行为进行分析，该模型适用于所有表面导电金刚石的掺杂策略。

Conclusion: 该理论模型对多种掺杂策略均有效；高磁场下经典轨道磁阻效应优于SOI效应；观测到极高的低温空穴迁移率，表明金刚石基电子器件在低温下实现超高空穴迁移率是可能的。

Abstract: The observation of strong and tunable spin-orbit interaction (SOI) in surface conducting diamond opens up a new avenue for building diamond-based spintronics. Herein we provide a comprehensive method to analyze the magnetotransport behavior of surface conducting hydrogen-terminated diamond (H-diamond) Hall bar devices and Al/Al2O3/V2O5/H-diamond MOSFETs, respectively. By adopting a significantly improved theoretical magneto transport model, the reduced magnetoconductance can be accurately explained both within and outside the quantum diffusive regime. The model is valid for all doping strategies of surface conducting diamond tested. From this analysis, we find that the orbital magnetoresistance, a classical effect distinct from the SOI, dominates the magnetotransport in surface conducting diamond at high magnetic fields. Furthermore, local hole mobilities as high as 1000 ~ 3000 cm2/Vs have been observed in this work, indicating the possibility of diamond-based electronics with ultra-high hole mobilities at cryogenic temperatures.

### [109] [Theory-Guided, Machine-Learning-Accelerated Discovery of a 3D Carbon Nested Nodal-Surface Semimetal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22141)

Method: 提出一般性的对称性工程原理，通过受控的层叠和配准偏移（controlled layering and registry shift）将石墨烯的狄拉克锥转化为三维节面。同时，集成晶体扩散变分自编码器（Crystal Diffusion Variational Autoencoder, CDVAE）与Crystal Transformer，进行机器学习加速的逆设计（inverse design）。

Conclusion: Netsene提供了一个结构稳健的体材料平台，统一了超高载流子迁移率（ultrahigh carrier mobility）、拓扑节面和潜在关联物理（correlation physics），展示了理论指导的机器学习加速发现方法在工程化拓扑量子相（topological quantum phases）方面的能力。

Abstract: Extending the Dirac physics of two-dimensional (2D) graphene into three dimensions (3D) carbon allotropes with higher-dimensional band degeneracies remains a central challenge in topological materials science. Here, we propose a general symmetry-engineering principle that systematically transforms graphene's Dirac cone into a 3D nodal surface via controlled layering and registry shift, and employ this principle to guide a machine-learning-accelerated inverse design. By integrating a crystal diffusion variational autoencoder(CDVAE) with a Crystal Transformer, we discover a novel, dynamically and mechanically stable carbon allotrope named \textbf{Netsene} (bct-C$_{24}$), which crystallizes in the body-centered tetragonal \textit{I4/mcm} space group. First-principles calculations confirm that Netsene is a unique nested nodal-surface semimetal: it hosts a complex, double-bowl-shaped nodal-surface system around the Fermi level, protected by non-symmorphic symmetries, alongside Dirac-like linear crossings with Fermi velocities comparable to graphene ($\sim 9 \times 10^5$~m/s). Its non-trivial bulk topology manifests in drumhead surface states, including a nearly flat band. Netsene provides a structurally robust, bulk platform that unifies ultrahigh carrier mobility, topological nodal surfaces, and potential correlation physics, demonstrating the power of theory-guided, machine-learning-accelerated discovery for engineering topological quantum phases.

Abstract: We present a computational framework that integrates machine learning with high-throughput \textit{ab initio} calculations to screen over 2.8 million compounds for metallic transport. We identify several intermetallic candidates with predicted high conductivities comparable to that of aluminum ($36.59 \times 10^6$~S/m). We perform full electron--phonon coupling calculations for the top-performing materials, yielding results in excellent agreement with available experimental data. Our analysis reveals that while the noble metals (Ag, Au, Cu) define the practical ceiling for conductivity due to their unique electronic structure and low scattering, compounds like $\text{LiBePt}_2$ can achieve comparable performance by utilizing valence electrons from light elements to shift high-scattering $d$-states beneath the Fermi level. This study not only identifies novel high-performance conductors but also demonstrates the predictive power of combining statistical learning with detailed ab initio calculations.

### [111] [Toward the Rational Design of Molecular Field-Coupled Nanocomputing Candidates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22196)

Abstract: Molecular Field-Coupled Nanocomputing (MolFCN) is a promising beyond-CMOS paradigm in which information is propagated electrostatically rather than through charge transport, enabling ultra-low-power logic. Identifying molecules with stable logic states, efficient clock-field switching, and reliable information propagation, however, remains an open challenge. In this Letter, we introduce LUFFY (Layered Unified Framework for MolFCN systematic analYsis), a framework for the rational design and validation of molecular candidates for MolFCN architectures. Starting from 27 synthetically accessible molecules, we combine conformational sampling and electrostatic analysis in neutral and oxidized states to derive robust descriptors of molecular response. In particular, we extract the V${in}$-to-Aggregated-Charge Transcharacteristics (VACTs), capturing the field-induced charge response, and introduce energy-averaged models validated via ab initio molecular dynamics to account for conformational diversity. Finally, we use the resulting molecular responses to evaluate device-level propagation and demonstrate stable information transfer. These results directly link molecular structure to functional information flow, identifying conformationally robust electrostatic response as a key requirement for MolFCN operation. Overall, this work establishes a unified and transferable framework for the identification and validation of MolFCN molecular candidates, bridging molecular design and circuit-level functionality. By unifying previously fragmented approaches into a sustainable methodology, LUFFY enables rational and scalable molecular discovery and establishes a foundation for data-driven design strategies that accelerate the development of ultra-low-power information processing technologies.

Abstract: Advanced nanodevices require high-precision machining of thin films using ultrafast lasers. This work investigates the complex interplay between these factors in ultrafast laser-irradiated gold (Au) thin films using a hybrid Two Temperature Model-Molecular Dynamics simulations. We realized microstructure-informed atomistic models with varying grain topologies (randomized vs. equiaxed), grain sizes, and residual tensile/compressive stress configurations. Our results reveal a clear hierarchy of influence on laser-metal interaction: 1.) Microstructure configuration 2.) Topology 3.) Grain Size 4.) Crystallographic orientations. In fine-grained thin films, grain boundaries act as primary melting precursors, while local crystallographic orientation determines the melting extent in coarser grains. Residual tensile stresses contribute to higher melting and greater laser-induced expansion than unstrained films. Conversely, residual compressive stresses resist deformation, as deposited thermal energy is utilized to overcome lattice compression, leading to reduced expansion. We found that microstructure grain topology and size exert a stronger fingerprint on film expansion than the initial defect density.

### [113] [Virp: neural network-accelerated prediction of physical properties in site-disordered materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22234)
*Andy Paul Chen,Martin Hoffmann Petersen,Kedar Hippalgaonkar*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合排列虚拟胞生成算法、采样方案和热力学后处理的流水线（pipeline），能够高效地对位点无序（site-disordered）材料进行第一性原理计算分析，克服了传统方法需依赖大尺度蒙特卡洛模拟且成本高昂的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多金属合金、陶瓷甚至水冰等材料中的晶体有序性表现为概率性——一个或多个晶格位点可被多种元素或空位以特定概率占据，但主流的第一性原理材料模拟方法假设完美晶格有序，无法直接处理此类结构。现有的变通方案（如准随机结构和团簇展开）依赖于大尺度蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟，计算成本高且具有系统特异性。

Method: 提出一个多步骤流水线：（1）基于排列（permutation）的虚拟胞生成算法，用于枚举可能的位点占据构型；（2）系统性的采样方案；（3）热力学后处理（thermodynamic post-processing）。该方法替代传统的大超胞蒙特卡洛模拟，直接对虚拟胞进行采样和计算。

Result: 在超胞定义足够大的前提下，仅需采样400个虚拟胞即可充分覆盖庞大的构型空间（configurational space），显著提升了位点无序材料计算分析的可行性。

Conclusion: 该流水线有效降低了位点无序材料第一性原理计算的复杂度与成本，为这类材料的高通量计算提供了一个系统且可扩展的替代方案。

In such cases, one or more sites within a crystal can be occupied by multiple elements or vacancies, according to a set of probabilities. These crystal structures remain inaccessible to common first-principles materials simulation methodologies, which assumes perfect crystal order. Workaround strategies to this limitation include quasirandom structures and cluster expansion. These methods are system-specific and computationally expensive as they rely on large scale Monte Carlo simulations of enlarged unit cells. To address these limitations, we propose a pipeline combining a permutation-based virtual cell generation algorithm, sampling regime, and thermodynamic post-processing which greatly improves the feasibility of computation analyses for site-disordered materials. We demonstrate that the massive configurational space can be adequately sampled with 400 virtual cells, as long as the supercell definition is sufficiently large.

</details>


### [114] [Enrichment of rhombohedral stacking by mechanical exfoliation of graphite](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22282)

Method: 采用常规机械剥离和引入额外剪切的刀片辅助剥离（blade-assisted exfoliation）两种方法处理石墨样品；利用大区域拉曼2D带偏度映射（Raman 2D-band skewness mapping）定量测量ABC堆叠的面积分数；通过追踪单个样品在剥离前后的变化，结合褶皱与单轴应变分析AB-ABC畴壁的成核与移动机制。

Result: 原始源晶体的ABC含量为3%；常规机械剥离后提升至16%；刀片辅助剥离后进一步升至26%（厚层样品）。对于薄层样品（<20层），片内ABC面积分数在分布上尾可达75%。实验证实褶皱可成核AB-ABC畴壁，单轴应变能驱动这些畴壁移动。

Conclusion: 刀片辅助机械剥离（blade-assisted mechanical exfoliation）通过剪切与应变调控有效富集ABC堆叠含量，克服了制备富菱方石墨样品的关键瓶颈，为研究菱方石墨中的关联与拓扑电子相提供了可行的实验途径。

Abstract: Rhombohedral (ABC) graphite hosts a surface-localized flat band that supports correlated and topological electronic phases, but its experimental study is limited by the scarcity of ABC stacking in natural graphite, which is dominated by Bernal (AB) stacking. Here we show that the routine mechanical exfoliation step itself enriches the rhombohedral content of graphite flakes, and that a simple blade-assisted exfoliation step, which introduces additional shear, amplifies the effect further. Using large-area Raman 2D-band skewness mapping we measure ABC content at area fractions of 3\% in the pristine source crystal, 16\% after conventional exfoliation, and 26\% after blade-assisted exfoliation for thick flakes. In thin flakes ($<20$ layers) the per-flake area fraction reaches 75\% in the upper tail of the distribution. Tracking individual flakes before and after blade-assisted exfoliation shows that wrinkles seed AB-ABC domain walls, and uniaxial strain can move these walls. Blade-assisted mechanical exfoliation therefore removes one of the bottlenecks to the preparation of ABC-rich graphite samples for studies of correlated and topological phases in rhombohedral graphite.

Abstract: The coupling between ferroelectrics and magnetism presents a promising avenue for low-dissipation spintronic devices. Here, we identify a class of collinear antiferromagnetic multiferroics in which intra-sublattice Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya interaction (DMI) induces odd-parity chiral magnons that are reversible via ferroelectric switching. Leveraging the charge-neutral nature of magnons, such multiferroics enable non-volatile ferroelectric control over magnon spin splitting, Hall transport, and spin polarization in antiferromagnetic insulators. Remarkably, magnetic group analysis and spin wave calculations reveal that the chiral splitting adopts three planar odd-parity forms, f-wave, p-wave, and fully-gapped types, with an intriguing Néel vector dependence. The intermittency results in a dynamic shift of the electron spectra correlating with the photoelectron yield. Method: 首先通过紧束缚模型（tight binding model）揭示交替亚铁磁性源于交变磁体中未补偿的磁化强度。随后采用第一性原理计算（first principles calculations）与蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulations），在应变及Cr替代的V2Te2O体系中验证该磁相的稳定性及其物性。

Abstract: The discovery of altermagnetism offers new opportunities for exploring novel quantum states and developing spintronic devices for enabling momentum dependent spin splitting in compensated systems, while zero net magnetization limit its manipulability using conventional magnetic method. Here, we propose 2D alternating ferrimagnetism,a phase merging alternating momentum dependent spin splitting with a finite net magnetization. Abstract: Piezocatalysis, based on the piezoelectric properties of catalysts, breaks down the barrier between mechanical energy and chemical energy. It describes the use of charges induced by piezoelectricity to assist typical chemical processes while harvesting various forms of mechanical green energy. The performance of piezocatalysis is predominantly governed by the piezoelectric properties of materials. The main aim of this work is to evaluate and analyze the potential of potassium doped sodium bismuth titanate Na0.5-xKxBi0.5TiO3 abbreviated as NKxBT (0, 0.15, 0.20, and 0.25), as a piezocatalyst in the degradation of the organic dye Rhodamine B RhB under ultrasonic vibration. The piezocatalytic degradation results showed a total piezo-degradation in only 90 min and a rate constant 8 times higher than the undoped NK0BT. The enhanced piezocatalytic activity results from a synergistic effect of MPB presence, reduced particle size, optimal bandgap and high lattice strain. ### [119] [Generation of an anomalous linearly dispersing spin-polarized band in Bi-based topological insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22370)
*Matthias Kronseder,Thomas Mayer,Jan Minár,Magdalena Marganska,Hedwig Werner,Florian Schmid,Rebeca Diaz-Pardo,Ivana Vobornik,Jun Fuji,Cornelia Streeck,Alexander Gottwald,Hendrik Kaser,Bernd Kästner,Christian H. Back*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We report the generation of an anomalous linearly dispersing, spin-polarized band in Bi-based topological insulator (TI) thin films, induced by soft Ar-ion bombardment followed by annealing. This extra band -- which we call the anomalous linearly dispersing state (ALS) -- is superimposed on the regular band structure including the topological surface state (TSS), spans an unusually large energetic range of up to ${\sim}\,\SI{650}{\milli\electronvolt}$ at the $Γ$-point, and appears near the Fermi energy. Spin-resolved measurements indicate spin-momentum locking with a helicity \emph{opposite} to that of the regular TSS. The observation is reproducible across samples of varying thickness and was confirmed at two independent synchrotron radiation facilities. We discuss different mechanisms for the physical origin of the observed ALS including sputtering-induced TSS relocation, bi-layer formation by,e.g., chalcogen removal, and high-index surface relocation.

### [120] [Antiferromagnetic Ordering Enhanced Magnetic Damping in Mn2Au/CoFeB Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22382)
*Donghang Xie,Haozhe Wang,Zhe Zhang,Zishuang Li,Jiahua Lu,Ronghua Liu,Jun Du,Bo Liu,Yu Yan,Liang He,Jing Wu,Rong Zhang,Bo Liu,Tiejun Zhou,Yongbing Xu,Xuezhong Ruan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过铁磁共振（Ferromagnetic Resonance, FMR）实验，研究了Mn₂Au/CoFeB反铁磁/铁磁（AFM/FM）双层膜中的磁动力学，发现2纳米厚Mn₂Au的奈尔温度（Néel temperature）低至约40 K，远低于块材的1000 K以上；随着温度降低，CoFeB层的磁阻尼（magnetic damping）α从0.013增至0.047，交换耦合场同步增大，归因于Mn₂Au反铁磁有序增强导致的AFM-FM交换耦合及自旋角动量转移增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反铁磁体（antiferromagnet, AFM）在自旋电子器件中具有重要潜力，其与铁磁体（ferromagnet, FM）组成的双层膜中，AFM可调控FM的磁动力学，但该调控机制尚存争议。本研究旨在通过实验探究AFM/FM双层膜中磁动力学行为的物理机制。

Method: 实验采用铁磁共振（Ferromagnetic Resonance, FMR）技术，测量了Mn₂Au/CoFeB AFM/FM双层膜在不同温度下的磁动力学响应，提取了磁阻尼（magnetic damping）系数α和交换耦合场H_rot等关键参数。

Result: 实验发现，2纳米厚Mn₂Au薄膜的奈尔温度（Néel temperature）仅约40 K，远低于块材的1000 K以上。在Mn₂Au(2 nm)/CoFeB(4 nm)双层膜中，随温度从160 K降至10 K，CoFeB层的磁阻尼α从0.013增加至0.047，交换耦合场H_rot同步增大。

Conclusion: 磁阻尼α随温度降低而增大的现象归因于Mn₂Au反铁磁有序（antiferromagnetic ordering）增强，促进了AFM-FM交换耦合（exchange coupling），从而增强了CoFeB向Mn₂Au的自旋角动量转移（spin angular momentum transfer）。本研究深化了对AFM/FM磁动力学以及自旋电子存储技术的认识。

Abstract: Antiferromagnets (AFMs) hold significant potential for spintronic devices owing to their insensitivity to external magnetic fields and the absence of stray fields. Beyond these inherent advantages, an AFM can manipulate the magnetic dynamics of a ferromagnet (FM) layer in AFM/FM bilayers, whereas the mechanism of such manipulation remains controversial. Here, we investigate the magnetic dynamics of AFM/FM Mn2Au/CoFeB bilayers via Ferromagnetic Resonance (FMR). It is found that the Néel temperature of 2-nm-thick Mn2Au is as low as ~40 K, in sharp contrast to that of bulk Mn2Au, which exceeds 1000 K. In the Mn2Au(2 nm)/CoFeB(4 nm) bilayer, the magnetic damping $α$ of the CoFeB layer increases from 0.013 to 0.047 as temperature decreases from 160 K to 10 K, accompanied by a synchronous increase in the exchange coupling field H_rot. Such an increase in $α$ is attributed to the enhanced spin angular momentum transfer from CoFeB to Mn2Au, mediated through AFM-FM exchange coupling between Mn2Au and CoFeB, which is enhanced by the Mn2Au antiferromagnetic ordering as the temperature decreases. Our study provides deeper insights into AFM/FM dynamics and spintronic storage technology.

</details>


### [121] [Harnessing Linear and Nonlinear Optical Responses in Ferroelectric LaMoN$_3$ for Enhanced Photovoltaic Efficiency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22453)
*Surajit Adhikari,Sanika S. Padelkar,Jacek J. Jasieniak,Alexandr N. Simonov,Aftab Alam*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文基于第一性原理方法，系统研究了氮化物钙钛矿LaMoN₃在0–40 GPa高压下的相稳定性、电子结构、激子与极化子行为以及线性和非线性光学响应。研究发现该材料在40 GPa内保持动态稳定，带隙随压力减小，压力可增强光谱限值最大效率（SLME）并降低激子结合能，体光伏效应在15 GPa附近达到峰值。据此提出多结器件设计以提升太阳能转换效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氮化物钙钛矿（nitride perovskite）是一类新兴材料，具有多样功能特性，但因无氧氮化物合成困难而研究不足。LaMoN₃虽已被报道具有极性对称性和铁电性，但其高压下的相稳定性、线性和非线性光学响应、激子与极化子行为以及效率特性尚属空白。本文旨在通过高压手段系统调控其电子结构，识别适用于线性和非线性光学响应的优化相区。

Method: 采用第一性原理方法（first-principles methods），包括密度泛函理论（DFT）、密度泛函微扰理论（DFPT）、多体微扰理论（G₀W₀和Bethe-Salpeter方程，BSE），以及紧束缚近似模型（tight binding approximation model），在0–40 GPa范围内系统计算LaMoN₃的各项性质。

Result: LaMoN₃在40 GPa内保持动态稳定且为单相结构；间接带隙（indirect bandgap）在G₀W₀@PBE水平下从2.17 eV（0 GPa）降至1.45 eV（40 GPa）；压力增强SLME并降低激子结合能（exciton binding energy）；体光伏效应（bulk photovoltaic efficiency）随压力先升后降，在15 GPa附近达到峰值，归因于位移电流密度（shift current density）J_SC的变化。

Conclusion: 压力可调谐LaMoN₃的光电性能，识别出有利于光伏应用的优化压力区间。提出多结器件（multi-junction device）设计，将优化线性和非线性光学电流的吸收层结合，通过互补机制协同提升太阳能转换效率。

Abstract: Nitride perovskites are an emerging class of materials predicted to exhibit diverse functional properties, yet remain underexplored due to synthesis challenges of oxygen-free nitrides. Recently, LaMoN$_3$ has been reported as an oxygen-free nitride perovskite with polar symmetry, exhibiting excellent dynamic stability and ferroelectric properties under moderate pressure. However, its phase stability, linear and non-linear optical response, excitonic and polaronic behavior, and efficiency under high pressure remain unexplored. Applying pressure enables systematic tuning of the electronic structure properties, thereby facilitating the identification of phases optimized for either linear or nonlinear optical responses. Therefore, in this work, we systematically investigate these properties of LaMoN$_3$ up to 40 GPa using first-principles methods, including density functional theory, density functional perturbation theory, many-body perturbation theory (namely G$_0$W$_0$ and BSE), and tight binding approximation model. Our study shows that LaMoN$_3$ remains dynamically stable and retains its single-phase structure up to 40 GPa. The compound exhibits an indirect bandgap that decreases from 2.17 eV (0 GPa) to 1.45 eV (40 GPa) at the G$_0$W$_0$@PBE level. Using the BSE, we find that pressure enhances the SLME while lowering the exciton binding energy, both favorable for photovoltaic applications. The bulk photovoltaic efficiency trend with pressure mimics the behavior of the shift current density J$_SC$ , peaking near 15 GPa before declining at higher pressures due to a diminished nonlinear shift current response. These results highlight pressure-tuned regimes to enhance photovoltaic performance. We thereby propose multi-junction device, combining absorber layers optimized for linear and nonlinear optical currents, together boosting solar energy conversion through complementary mechanisms.

</details>

Conclusion: Zr₂SN₂证明了强光-物质相互作用（light-matter interaction）、光学透明性和电导率可以在单一材料平台中实现调和，揭示了一类新型高折射率透明导体（high-refractive-index transparent conductors）。

Abstract: With the rise of AI-assisted materials screening, extraordinary properties are now frequently predicted in experimentally uncharted material systems, highlighting the need to develop new synthesis methods for unconventional materials beyond the classic bulk powder form. Here, we establish the first thin-film growth route for any metal sulfonitride compound by realizing Zr2SN2 films with a rare and compelling combination of optical and electrical properties. Zr2SN2 is transparent across most of the visible range while exhibiting a very high average refractive index of 2.95 in the visible, exceeding expectations based on conventional refractive index-bandgap scaling. Importantly, the same Zr2SN2 film shows degenerate n-type conductivity with carrier density above 10^20 cm-3 and intragrain mobility above 8 cm2V-1s-1, approaching those of established transparent conductive oxides. Zr2SN2 thus demonstrates that strong light-matter interaction, optical transparency and electrical conductivity can be reconciled within a single material platform, revealing a new class of high-refractive-index transparent conductors.

### [123] [Observation of magnetically switchable quantum geometric photocurrents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22518)
*Qi Tian,Zhuoliang Ni,Matthew Cothrine,David G. Mandrus,Eugene J. Mele,Andrew M. Rappe,Charles L. Kane,Fernando de Juan,Liang Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文首次在范德华反铁磁体中实验证实了磁控线性注入电流与圆位移电流的存在，这两种光电流分别探测量子度量与几何挠率，可通过翻转奈尔向量实现开关控制，揭示了与量子几何直接相关的磁控光电流新机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非中心对称材料中，体光伏效应（bulk photovoltaic effect）产生的注入电流（injection current）和位移电流（shift current）已被发现与两态量子几何（two-state quantum geometry）密切相关。磁性晶体理论上预言了一类尚未观测到的磁控光电流，其中线性和圆偏振光的角色互换，产生探测量子度量（quantum metric）的线性注入电流和探测几何挠率（geometric torsion）的圆位移电流。本研究旨在首次实验验证此类光电流的存在。

Method: 在范德华反铁磁体（van der Waals antiferromagnet）中，通过翻转奈尔向量（Néel vector）实现光电流的开关控制，并测量光电流的频率依赖性和温度依赖性。

Result: 首次实验观察到磁性晶体中的线性注入电流和圆位移电流。通过翻转奈尔向量实现光电流的切换，且光电流的频率和温度依赖特性证实了圆位移电流和线性注入电流的归属。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了一种直接与量子几何（quantum geometry）相关联的磁控光电流新控制方式，在反铁磁自旋电子学（antiferromagnetic spintronics）和光捕获（light harvesting）领域具有潜在应用前景。

Abstract: In non-centrosymmetric materials, light can be rectified into two types of DC photocurrents, known as injection and shift currents, through the bulk photovoltaic effect. Recent theory has uncovered their deep relation with the two-state quantum geometry of resonant transitions: In non-magnetic crystals, where these currents have been routinely observed, the injection current responds to circular light and probes the Berry curvature, while the shift current responds to linear light and probes the geometric connection. Magnetic crystals have been predicted to show a new set of hitherto unobserved magnetically switchable photocurrents, with the roles of linear and circular light interchanged: A linear injection current, which probes the quantum metric, and a circular shift current, which probes the geometric torsion. In this work, we demonstrate the existence of such currents for the first time, demonstrating the switching of the current by flipping the Néel vector in a van der Waals antiferromagnet. Furthermore, their specific frequency and temperature dependence confirm the assignment of circular shift and linear injection currents. Our work demonstrates a new way to control photocurrents in magnets that are directly tied to geometry and have promising applications in antiferromagnetic spintronics and light harvesting.
