### [124] [Upscaling DFT-trained machine-learning interatomic potential toward Quantum Monte Carlo accuracy: Sulfur-vacancy migration in monolayer MoS$_2$ as a testbed](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22601)
*Adam Hložný,Ján Brndiar,Ye Luo,Ivan Štich*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出一种多保真度（multi-fidelity）训练策略，利用基准质量的量子蒙特卡洛（QMC）能量和合适的低层级DFT原子力，对等变消息传递MACE机器学习原子间势（MLIP）进行微调（fine-tuning），在MoS₂单层硫空位体系上实现接近QMC精度的能量与自由能迁移势垒计算，从而将QMC级精度模拟拓展至大规模原子体系与分子动力学构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子蒙特卡洛（QMC）方法虽具有基准级的计算精度，但因其随机性导致原子力（atomic force）确定复杂，难以直接应用于大规模模拟。作者旨在设计一种训练流程，使机器学习原子间势（MLIP）达到QMC精度，同时避开QMC力计算的复杂性。

Method: 采用多保真度（multi-fidelity）方法：将高层级QMC能量与经过适当处理的低层级DFT原子力结合，对等变消息传递MACE架构的MLIP的读出层（readout layers）进行微调（fine-tuning）。微调仅涉及模型读出层，基底为DFT训练的MLIP。

Result: 以单层MoS₂中的单空位和多空位硫缺陷为测试体系，在域内（in-domain）和域外（out-of-domain）测试中均展现出接近QMC的精度。仅需有限大小的QMC能量数据集即可显著改善基线DFT MLIP。在单空位和多空位硫缺陷的能量迁移势垒与自由能迁移势垒计算中验证了准确性。

Conclusion: 该方法打开了利用大规模原子数或分子动力学构型进行接近QMC精度模拟的窗口，而这是直接暴力应用QMC方法所无法实现的。

Abstract: We designed a procedure to train a machine learning interatomic potential (MLIP) at benchmark-quality quantum Monte Carlo (QMC) accuracy. To avoid the complexities of high-quality atomic force determination with the stochastic QMC methods, we use a multi-fidelity approach wherein high-level QMC energies are used alongside suitably processed low-level DFT atomic forces to train a QMC fine-tuned MLIP which significantly improves both the energetics and atomic forces over the baseline DFT-based MLIP. Fine-tuning is only applied to the readout layers of an equivariant message-passing MACE MLIP. We used sulfur mono- and multiple vacancies in monolayer MoS$_2$ as a testbed and demonstrate a near QMC accuracy of the model in a number of in- and out-of-domain tests. We show that a fairly limited dataset of QMC energies suffice to significantly improve the baseline DFT MLIP. The accuracy of our approach is demonstrated on energy and free energy migration barriers of mono- and multiple S-vacancy defects. The results open the window to large-scale near QMC quality simulations with large numbers of atoms and/or molecular dynamics configurations which would not be possible by a direct brute-force application of QMC methods.

</details>


### [125] [A Local Probe Mass Spectrometer for Localized and Sensitive Product Detection in Environmental Electron Microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22626)
*Saleh Firoozabadia,Timofei Ivanova,Frederik Stendera,Julian Grahlb,Stephan Schulzb,Christian Joossa,Tobias Meyera*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种集成像差校正环境透射电镜（aberration-corrected ETEM）的局域探针质谱仪（LPMS），通过去除MEMS芯片的SiN膜并采用微毛细管局域采样，克服了传统闭池和开池ETEM在空间分辨率与反应产物检测灵敏度之间的矛盾，实现了催化反应中原子尺度结构变化与产物分布的同时、定域检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ETEM方法中，闭池（closed-cell）结构因SiN窗的漫散射（diffuse scattering）导致空间分辨率和灵敏度下降；开池（open-cell）结构虽可保持高分辨率，但反应产物在输运至质谱仪（mass spectrometer, MS）过程中被显著稀释。因此，亟需开发一种既能保持原子级成像分辨率，又能实现反应产物高灵敏度局域检测的新技术。

Method: 研究将DENSsolution Stream样品杆与质谱仪集成，去除MEMS芯片的上下SiN膜以保留空间分辨率，同时利用ETEM腔体维持气体环境；通过置于催化剂附近的微毛细管（micro-capillary）局域采样，经样品杆气体管路将产物输送至MS。采用Co3O4纳米片（nanoplates）作为模型催化剂（其固有电子透明性无需FIB制备），并开发微穿梭转移（micro-shuttle transfer）策略，实现定数、定取向纳米片的可控放置。

Result: 在环境扫描电镜（environmental SEM）中的初步验证表明，该装置实现了对MS的可控气体输运。Co3O4纳米片无需FIB减薄即可实现原子级分辨率成像，避免了离子束损伤。微穿梭转移策略成功实现了特定数量及晶向纳米片在反应位点的精确定位。

Conclusion: LPMS-ETEM集成平台为实现定量结构-反应性关联（quantitative structure reactivity correlation）奠定了基础，可同时获取反应产物的空间分辨检测与原子尺度的结构动力学信息。

Abstract: Aberration-corrected environmental transmission electron microscopy (ETEM) enables atomic-resolution imaging of dynamic catalytic processes. Correlating atomic-scale structural changes with reaction products detected by mass spectrometry offers a powerful route to uncover catalytic mechanisms. However, current approaches face fundamental limitations: closed-cell ETEM setups suffer from diffuse scattering by SiN windows, degrading spatial resolution and sensitivity, while open-cell configurations enable high-resolution imaging and maintain high sensitivity but suffer from significant dilution of reaction products during transport to the mass spectrometer (MS). To overcome these challenges, we develop a Local Probe Mass Spectrometer (LPMS) integrated with aberration-corrected ETEM. The setup combines a DENSsolution Stream holder with a MS. To preserve spatial resolution, both top and bottom SiN membranes of the MEMS chip are removed, while the gas environment is maintained via the ETEM chamber. Reaction products are sampled locally via a micro-capillary positioned near the catalyst and connected to a holder gas line that delivers the gas to the MS. Initial validation in environmental SEM confirmed controlled gas delivery to the MS. Co3O4 nanoplates serve as a model catalyst due to their inherent electron transparency, enabling atomic-resolution imaging without FIB lamella preparation and associated ion-beam damage. A novel micro-shuttle transfer strategy enables controlled placement of a defined number of nanoplates at the reaction site with precise crystallographic orientation. This establishes the foundation for quantitative structure reactivity correlation by enabling simultaneous, spatially resolved detection of reaction products and atomic-scale structural dynamics.

</details>


### [126] [Atomic scale demonstration of ferromagnetism in a single layer FeCl2 on Au(111)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22783)
*Adriana E. Candia,Eliecer Peláez-Sifonte,Amitayush Jha Thakur,Sebastien E. Hadjadj,Samuel Kerschbaumer,Aymeric Saunot,Martina Corso,Maxim Ilyn,Jorge Lobo-Checa,Celia Rogero,David Serrate*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究利用自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜（spin-polarized scanning tunnelling microscopy, SP-STM）明确证实了Au(111)衬底上单层FeCl2具有铁磁有序（ferromagnetic ordering），并表征了其3.3 eV的宽绝缘带隙、1.5 eV处的强自旋极化导带，以及三角状原子尺度缺陷对电子能隙和自旋密度分布的显著调控作用，最终通过原子分辨磁滞回线确认了易面外各向异性的软铁磁基态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: FeCl2作为一种具有显著磁化率和绝缘特性的单层材料，可通过分子束外延（molecular beam epitaxy）在不同表面上生长，但其磁性与电子基态尚待确认，且衬底影响也未明确，这正是将其纳入范德华异质结构（van der Waals heterostructures）材料库所需解决的关键问题。

Method: 采用自旋极化扫描隧道显微镜（spin-polarized scanning tunnelling microscopy, SP-STM）对Au(111)衬底上的单层FeCl2进行磁性和电子结构表征；通过跟踪随外加磁场变化的自旋相关隧穿电导（spin-dependent tunnelling conductance）来记录原子分辨的磁滞回线（hysteresis loops）。

Result: 单层FeCl2表现出铁磁有序（ferromagnetic ordering）、约3.3 eV的宽绝缘带隙以及位于费米能级（Fermi level）上方1.5 eV处的强自旋极化导带（strongly spin-polarized conduction band）；三角形状原子尺度缺陷在1.6 nm范围内使导带局部抑制、隧穿磁电导（tunnelling magneto-conductance）降低至四分之一；原子分辨磁滞回线揭示了矫顽场（coercive field）在15-50 mT范围内的软铁磁基态（soft ferromagnetic ground state）及明显的易面外各向异性（out-of-plane anisotropy）。

Conclusion: 单层FeCl2在Au(111)上的铁磁基态和宽绝缘带隙得到明确证实，其电子和自旋性质受到原子尺度缺陷的显著调控，这为将该材料纳入功能范德华异质结构（functional van der Waals heterostructures）的设计提供了关键实验依据。

Abstract: FeCl2 is a promising single-layer material with sizeable magnetic susceptibility and insulating character that can be easily grown by molecular beam epitaxy on various surfaces. In order to include it into the select palette of van der Waals materials used to engineer functional heterostructures, it is necessary to confirm its magnetic and electronic ground states, and understand the influence of the supporting substrate. In this work, we unambiguously demonstrate ferromagnetic ordering in a single-layer FeCl2 on Au(111) by means of spin-polarized scanning tunnelling microscopy. The material features a relatively wide insulating gap of 3.3 eV and a strongly spin-polarized conduction band that emerges at 1.5 eV above the Fermi level. Atomic scale defects with triangular shape play a primary role in the electronic gap and spin density distribution. Specifically, in a region of 1.6 nm around each defect, the conduction band is locally suppressed and the tunnelling magneto-conductance is reduced a factor of four. By tracking the spin-dependent tunnelling conductance as a function of the applied magnetic field, we record atomically resolved hysteresis loops, revealing a soft ferromagnetic ground state with pronounced out-of-plane anisotropy and coercive fields in the range of 15-50 mT.

</details>

### [127] [Comment on "Entropic Costs of Extracting Classical Ticks from a Quantum Clock"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21833)
*Longyan Gong*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文对Wadhia等人声称利用双量子点（DQD）实现量子时钟的工作提出了两项根本性质疑：其系统仅表现经典行为且缺乏时间关联，不符合精确时钟标准；其热力学分析错误分配了熵产生（entropy production），混淆了放大（amplification）与测量（measurement），所报告的联合熵是工程耗散而非量子守时（quantum timekeeping）的基本代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 指出Wadhia等人发表于《物理评论快报》的量子时钟实验在物理机制和热力学分析两方面存在根本性缺陷，以澄清量子守时（quantum timekeeping）的基本条件与熵代价（entropy cost）的正确归属。

Method: 采用批评性分析（Comment）的形式，针对原始论文的两项核心主张——量子时钟的实现与热力学代价——逐一提出反证与理论辨析。

Result: 发现该“量子时钟”仅表现出经典行为（classical behavior），且各“滴答（tick）”之间缺乏内在时间关联（intrinsic temporal correlations），不足以作为精确时钟；热力学分析中错误地将工程耗散（engineering dissipation）归因为量子守时的基本熵代价，混淆了放大过程与测量过程。

Conclusion: 该双量子点系统并非真正的量子时钟，其熵分析也不能反映量子守时的基本热力学成本；需要更严格的量子时间测量（quantum timekeeping）判据与正确的热力学框架。

Abstract: A recent Letter by Wadhia et al. reports a realization of a quantum clock using a double quantum dot (DQD) [Phys. Rev. Lett. 135, 200407 (2005)]. This Comment identifies two fundamental issues: (I) the claimed ``quantum clock" exhibits only classical behavior and lacks intrinsic temporal correlations between ticks; it is not sufficient for accurate time as a good clock. (II) the thermodynamic analysis misassigns entropy production and conflates amplification with measurement; the reported combined entropy is an engineering dissipation, not a fundamental cost of quantum timekeeping.

</details>


### [128] [Spin torque driven mode hybridization and band engineering in nanopatterned magnonic crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21888)
*Nikhil Kumar*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过实验和理论计算，在纳米图案化的双组分磁子晶体（magnonic crystal）中展示了可调谐的模式耦合和能带杂化（band hybridisation），并利用自旋扭矩（spin torque）实现了对自旋波色散（spin-wave dispersion）的动态电学调控。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋波传播与动态控制对于可重构磁子（magnonic）和自旋电子（spintronic）器件至关重要，而现有方法在纳米尺度上实现灵活电学调控仍面临挑战。

Method: 采用平面波法（plane wave method）和包含类场力矩项（field-like torque term）的线性化朗道-利夫希茨方程（Landau Lifshitz equation）进行理论建模，体系为坡莫合金（Permalloy）/重金属双层薄膜上图案化的二维Co纳米点阵列构成的磁子晶体。

Result: 非均匀电流诱导的自旋扭矩产生磁子频率的周期性调制，实现动态色散调控；观察到局域模与传播的Damon Eshbach模之间存在明显的避免交叉（avoided crossing），形成可调谐的杂化能隙（hybridisation gap）、能带变形和增强的模式混合。

Conclusion: 自旋扭矩诱导的调制可实现可控的模式转换和可重构杂化磁子态，展现了纳米尺度自旋波动力学的高效电学调谐能力。

Abstract: Spin wave propagation and dynamic control are essential for reconfigurable magnonic and spintronic devices. Here, tunable mode coupling and band hybridisation are demonstrated in a nanopatterned bicomponent magnonic crystal consisting of a Permalloy/heavy metal bilayer patterned with a two dimensional array of Co nanodots. Using the plane wave method and the linearised Landau Lifshitz equation with a field like torque term, we show that inhomogeneous current induced spin torque produces periodic modulation of the magnonic frequency, enabling dynamic control of spin-wave dispersion. A pronounced avoided crossing between localised and propagating Damon Eshbach modes is observed, leading to tunable hybridisation gaps, band deformation, and enhanced mode mixing. The spin torque induced modulation enables controlled mode conversion and reconfigurable hybrid magnonic states, demonstrating efficient electrical tuning of nanoscale spin-wave dynamics.

### [129] [Nonlinear Photonic Tripartite Phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21983)
*Xiangrui Hou,Fangyu Wang,Zhaoxin Wu,Shuming Zhang,Shan-Zhong Li,Lei Ying,Haiqing Lin,Baile Zhang,Zhi Li,Shi-Liang Zhu,Zhaoju Yang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在非线性准周期光子晶格中实验实现了局域态、临界态和扩展态共存的三重相，并发现克尔非线性（Kerr nonlinearity）作为有效相互作用能够提供状态选择性（state-selective）进入临界窗口（critical window）的机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准周期系统理论上可以存在一个由迁移率边（mobility edges）界定的有限临界窗口（finite critical window），其中局域态、临界态和扩展态共存。然而，该区域的实验实现以及相互作用能否可控地进入这一窗口仍未解决。

Method: 在一个非线性准周期光子晶格（nonlinear quasiperiodic photonic lattice）中进行实验，利用克尔非线性作为有效相互作用，通过追踪波包动力学（wavepacket dynamics）区分局域、临界和扩展三种输运（transport）行为。

Result: 实验发现了状态选择性响应：弱非线性并非简单地通过自陷（self-trapping）增强局域化，而是将低能局域态驱动进入临界窗口；强非线性则将它们恢复为局域态。临界态、扩展态和高能局域态则单调地演变为自陷行为。

Conclusion: 实验结果揭示了一种状态选择性机制，通过相互作用可以对准周期系统中预先存在的临界窗口实现可控访问。

Abstract: Anderson localization is usually understood as a transition between extended and localized phases, with criticality confined to a single mobility edge. Recent advances predict that quasiperiodic systems can instead host a finite critical window bounded by mobility edges, in which localized, critical and extended states coexist. Yet both the experimental realization of this regime and whether interactions can provide controlled access to it remain unknown. Here, we realize such a tripartite phase in a nonlinear quasiperiodic photonic lattice and show that Kerr nonlinearity, acting as an effective interaction, enables state-selective access to the critical window. By tracking wavepacket dynamics, we distinguish localized, critical and extended transport regimes and uncover a state-selective response: rather than simply reinforcing localization through self-trapping, weak nonlinearity drives low-energy localized states into the critical window, whereas stronger nonlinearity restores localization. By contrast, critical, extended and high-energy localized states evolve monotonically towards self-trapped behaviour. Our results reveal a state-selective mechanism by which interactions provide controlled access to a pre-existing critical window in quasiperiodic systems.

</details>


### [130] [Direct observation of the transverse near field of an edge excitation and associated slow secondary dynamics in a fractional quantum Hall state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21989)
*Yunhyeon Jeong,Akinori Kamiyama,John N. Moore,Takaaki Mano,Ken-ichi Sasaki,Yuuki Sugiyama,Tokiro Numasawa,Masahiro Hotta,Go Yusa*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文通过时间分辨光致发光（photoluminescence, PL）显微镜与光谱学，在ν=1/3分数量子霍尔（fractional quantum Hall, FQH）态中观测到边缘激发的横向近场，揭示了边缘磁等离子体激元（edge magnetoplasmon, EMP）是一种空间扩展的集体激发，而非严格的准一维电荷密度振荡，并发现了多时间尺度的体态侧动力学响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的认知将边缘磁等离子体激元（EMP）视为准一维的电荷密度振荡，但这一图像可能过于简化。实验旨在通过高时空分辨的光学手段直接探测FQH态中边缘激发的空间结构，以验证EMP是否具有扩展性的体态耦合。

Method: 采用频闪时间分辨光致发光（stroboscopic time-resolved PL）显微镜与光谱学技术，采集时间分辨的y-t空间图，测量边缘激发在ν=1/3分数量子霍尔（FQH）态体相中的横向近场分布。

Result: 当边缘磁等离子体激元（EMP）通过台面边界时，观察到瞬时的光致发光（PL）响应向体相横向延伸超过30微米。这一长程近场响应的近瞬时特性表明其为非辐射的准静电近场，证明EMP是空间扩展的集体激发。此外还观察到区别于瞬时横向近场的次级体态侧响应，两种共存响应展现出广泛分离的时间尺度。

Conclusion: 边缘磁等离子体激元（EMP）并非准一维模式，而是具有长程横向扩展的集体激发；电学激发的边缘模式可在体相侧产生跨越多个时间尺度的动力学行为。这一发现修正了对FQH边缘激发本质的理解，并为体-边耦合动力学提供了新视角。

Abstract: We report stroboscopic time-resolved photoluminescence (PL) microscopy and spectroscopy revealing the transverse near field of an edge excitation in a $ν=1/3$ fractional quantum Hall (FQH) state. Time-resolved $y$-$t$ maps reveal an immediate PL response extending more than $30~μ\mathrm{m}$ into the bulk transverse to the edge when the edge magnetoplasmon (EMP) passes the mesa boundary. The nearly instantaneous nature of this long-range response identifies it as the non-radiative, quasi-electrostatic near field, revealing the EMP as a spatially extended collective excitation rather than a strictly one-dimensional charge-density oscillation. We also observe secondary bulk-side responses distinct from the immediate transverse near-field response. The coexistence of these immediate and secondary responses shows that electrically launched edge excitations produce bulk-side dynamics on widely separated time scales.

### [131] [Gyromagnetic Quantum Friction in Rayleigh Vorticity Baths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22135)
*Mamoru Matsuo,Ryotaro Sano,Ai Yamakage,Hiroshi Funaki,Tatsuhiko N. Ikeda*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 论文识别了一种近表面自旋在零温下通过与瑞利波涡度（Rayleigh-wave vorticity）的陀螺磁耦合（gyromagnetic coupling）产生的内禀弛豫通道。该通道不需要热声子，由瑞利涡度而非材料特定的g因子调制决定，表现为超欧姆（super-Ohmic）且随深度衰减的浴，导致自旋弛豫具有特定的场和深度标度关系，可被用于探测固体中瑞利波的声学量子摩擦（acoustic quantum friction）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有近表面自旋弛豫机制（如拉曼弛豫（Raman relaxation））依赖热声子，无法描述零温下的内禀损耗。论文旨在揭示一种不依赖热声子、由瑞利波涡度驱动的零温自旋弛豫通道，并解释其物理起源与标度行为。

Method: 论文从理论上分析了近表面自旋与瑞利波涡度之间的陀螺磁耦合，将瑞利波涡度建模为一个超欧姆且随深度呈指数衰减的量子浴（quantum bath），推导出自旋弛豫率随外磁场和自旋所处深度的标度关系。

Result: 发现瑞利波涡度浴是超欧姆型的，且其效应随深度呈蒸发（evanescent）衰减；自旋弛豫率表现出明确的磁场标度（field scaling）和深度标度（depth scaling）。

Conclusion: 该机制使得浅层自旋传感器（shallow spin sensors）和混合表面声波自旋界面（hybrid surface-acoustic-wave spin interfaces）可作为探测固体中瑞利波声学量子摩擦的实验平台。

Abstract: We identify an intrinsic zero-temperature relaxation channel for near-surface spins gyromagnetically coupled to Rayleigh-wave vorticity. This surface-mode contribution requires no thermal phonons, unlike Raman relaxation, and is fixed by Rayleigh vorticity rather than material-specific $g$-factor modulation. The Rayleigh-vorticity bath is super-Ohmic and evanescent with depth, producing field and depth scalings of spin relaxation. These scalings establish shallow spin sensors and hybrid surface-acoustic-wave spin interfaces as detectors of Rayleigh-wave acoustic quantum friction in solids.

### [132] [Quasinormal mode quantization of bound and propagating photons in complex lightguiding nanostructures for integrated devices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22153)
*Robert Meiners Fuchs,Marten Richter*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文为开放光学或等离子体谐振器中的准正则模（quasinormal modes）推导了普适边界条件，并提出了一个通用的量子化方案，涵盖多个相互作用的准正则模腔与量子发射体（quantum emitters）及非玻色子传播光子库（non-bosonic bath）的耦合，最终导出了可计算的光-物质相互作用及有效库介导关联函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先针对准正则模推导了适用于特定几何结构的普适边界条件（general boundary conditions）；随后提出了一个通用的量子化方案（quantization scheme），将多个相互作用的准正则模腔与量子发射体以及非玻色子传播光子库耦合起来；利用麦克斯韦求解器（Maxwell solvers）计算了系统-库哈密顿量（system-bath Hamiltonian）中的耦合元；定义了系统-库关联函数（system-bath correlation functions），以描述库介导的时滞相互作用。

Result: 得到了一个具有严格定义耦合元的系统-库哈密顿量，该哈密顿量可通过麦克斯韦求解器数值计算；定义了有效库介导的时滞相互作用关联函数，可作为模拟开放量子系统动力学（open quantum system dynamics）的核心输入。

Conclusion: 该工作为开放光学纳米结构中准正则模的量子化提供了通用理论框架，使得光-物质相互作用的计算和开放量子系统动力学的模拟在计算上变得可行。

Abstract: Open optical or plasmonic resonators are placed on and connected through surfaces or via waveguides, forming complex lightguiding nanostructures, e.g. for integrated photonic quantum devices. We derive general boundary conditions for quasinormal modes that account for the structure's specific geometry. We then present a general quantization scheme for multiple, interacting quasinormal-mode cavities coupled to quantum emitters and to a non-bosonic bath of propagating photons on waveguides or a surface. We derive a system-bath Hamiltonian with rigorously defined coupling elements that can be computed using Maxwell solvers, including light-matter coupling between the electromagnetic field and quantum emitters. We define system-bath correlation functions for an effective, bath-mediated, and time-delayed interaction between the quasinormal modes and quantum emitters, which is a main ingredient commonly used to simulate open quantum system dynamics.

### [133] [Nonlinear frequency shift and bistability of magnon-polarons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22157)
*Kevin Künstle,Matthias Wagner,Philipp Knaus,Yannik Kunz,Ephraim Spindler,Katharina Lasinger,Matthias R. Schweizer,Philipp Pirro,John F. Gregg,Mathias Weiler*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过微波反射测量与微聚焦布里渊光散射光谱学，实验研究了基于YIG/ZnO异质结的磁声谐振器中强耦合表面声波（SAWs）与自旋波（SWs）的非线性动力学，揭示了由交叉频移项主导的正频移非线性响应、双稳态折叠行为，并证明了SAW驱动的k≠0磁振子-声子杂化体系是非线性磁声学与波动信息处理的理想平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索强耦合表面声波与自旋波杂化体系中的非线性动力学行为，尤其是非线性频移的物理机制及其对磁振子-声子杂化体系非线性响应的影响。

Method: 采用微波反射测量与微聚焦布里渊光散射光谱学（microfocused Brillouin light scattering spectroscopy）结合，在YIG/ZnO异质结构构成的磁声谐振器（magnetoacoustic resonator）中进行实验测量，并利用非线性自旋波动力学的矢量哈密顿形式（vector Hamiltonian formalism）进行理论分析。

Result: 在线性区观察到驻波SAW腔模与有限波矢SWs的杂化导致的明显避让交叉（avoided crossings）。在高驱动功率下，杂化体系呈现场依赖的正频移非线性响应，且该频移由交叉频移项（cross-shift term）主导。在合适的场失谐条件下，非线性频移将SW模驱动至与SAW激励共振，导致磁振子布居数显著增强、宽带非线性散射以及双稳态折叠行为（bistable foldover behavior）。超过折叠阈值后，磁振子和声子响应均趋于稳定。

Conclusion: SAW驱动的k≠0磁振子-声子杂化体系为非线性磁声学与波动信息处理提供了一个有前景的平台。

Abstract: We investigate the nonlinear dynamics of strongly coupled surface acoustic waves (SAWs) and spin waves (SWs) in a magnetoacoustic resonator based on a YIG/ZnO heterostructure by combining microwave reflection measurements with microfocused Brillouin light scattering spectroscopy. In the linear regime, the electrical response reveals clear hybridization between standing SAW cavity modes and finite-wave-vector SWs, resulting in pronounced avoided crossings. At elevated drive powers, the hybrid system exhibits a strongly field-dependent nonlinear response characterized by a positive frequency shift of the driven SW mode. Using the vector Hamiltonian formalism for nonlinear spin-wave dynamics, we show that this shift is dominated by a cross-shift term. In our resonator geometry, this contribution becomes significant because the standing SAW cavity mode simultaneously excites counterpropagating SWs with wave vectors $+k$ and $-k$. For suitable field detuning, the nonlinear shift drives the SW mode into resonance with the SAW excitation, leading to a strong enhancement of the magnon population, broadband nonlinear scattering, and bistable foldover behavior. Beyond the foldover threshold, both the magnon and phonon responses stabilize. These results establish SAW-driven $k \neq 0$ magnon-phonon hybrids as a promising platform for nonlinear magnetoacoustics and wave-based information processing.

</details>


### [134] [Topologically Driven Giant Effective Spin Mixing Conductance in Antiferromagnetic FeSn/Py Heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22180)
*Kacho Imtiyaz Ali Khan,Nidhi Kandwal,Pankhuri Gupta,Deeksha Khandelwal,Akash Kumar,Johan Åkerman,Pranaba Kishor Muduli*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验制备了外延FeSn/Py（Ni₈₀Fe₂₀）异质结（epitaxial-FeSn/Py heterostructures），测量其自旋泵浦行为；并通过插入3 nm Al间隔层（spacer layer）进行对照实验，以确认界面效应的贡献。

Result: 测得了巨大的有效自旋混合电导（effective spin mixing conductance, g↑↓eff）为(116±7) nm⁻²，比标准Pt/Py异质结高近一个数量级；插入Al层后有效阻尼（effective damping）降低两倍；FeSn/Py体系中的逆自旋霍尔效应（inverse spin Hall effect）电压比Pt/Py参考样品高一个数量级。

Conclusion: 巨大的g↑↓eff源于Py层与外延FeSn的拓扑活性[001]-kagome表面的直接界面接触。这些发现确立了拓扑活性界面（topologically active interfaces）对于先进量子材料基自旋电子器件（quantum-material-based spintronic devices）的关键作用。

Abstract: The topological semimetal FeSn antiferromagnet, characterized by its kagome lattice, two-dimensional flat bands, and Dirac-like surface states, holds immense promise for spintronic applications. In this work, for the first time, we investigate the spin pumping behavior in epitaxial-FeSn/Py (Ni$_{80}$Fe$_{20}$) heterostructures. We report a giant effective spin mixing conductance (g$^{\uparrow \downarrow}_{\mathrm{eff}}$) of $(116\pm 7)$~nm$^{-2}$, which is nearly one order of magnitude higher than that of standard Pt/Py heterostructures. The insertion of a 3 nm Al spacer layer results in a two-fold reduction in the effective damping, confirming the interfacial origin of the large g$^{\uparrow\downarrow}_{\mathrm{eff}}$. Consistently, we observe an order-of-magnitude higher inverse spin Hall effect voltage in the FeSn/Py system compared to a reference Pt/Py film stack. We attribute the giant g$^{\uparrow\downarrow}_{\mathrm{eff}}$ to the direct interfacing of the Py layer with the topologically active [001]-kagome surface of epitaxial-FeSn. These findings establish the critical role of topologically active interfaces for advanced quantum-material-based spintronic devices.

### [135] [Quantum-metric Bloch oscillations in weakly inhomogeneous electric fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22227)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过理论分析弱非均匀电场对半经典波包动力学（semiclassical wavepacket dynamics）的影响，引入与量子度量相关的修正项；并采用倾斜狄拉克模型（tilted Dirac model）进行机制演示。

Result: 当贝里曲率为零时，非均匀电场仍可产生振荡的实空间贡献；输运响应分为本征部分和与散射时间相关的部分，在相对场不均匀性固定时，后者在高场下趋于有限饱和值。

Conclusion: 该效应为实现新型布洛赫振荡类比提供了量子度量驱动的新机制，实际平台可能需要在具有有限量子度量和适当带隙的人工合成超晶格（synthetically engineered superlattices）中实现。

Abstract: Geometric analogs of Bloch oscillations studied so far have relied on Berry curvature. We show that a weakly inhomogeneous electric field adds a distinct quantum-metric term to semiclassical wavepacket dynamics, generating an oscillatory real-space contribution even when the Berry curvature vanishes. The associated transport response comprises an intrinsic and a scattering-time-dependent part. In the regime studied, the latter can dominate and approach finite saturation at high field when the relative field inhomogeneity is held fixed. A tilted Dirac model illustrates the mechanism. Realistic platforms will likely require synthetically engineered superlattices, with a finite quantum metric and an adequate band gap.

### [136] [Topological semimetals: surface transport and spin effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22278)
*E. V. Deviatov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文综述了拓扑半金属（topological semimetals）中电荷与自旋输运的实验研究进展，重点关注Weyl半金属（Weyl semimetals）的表面态特性、自旋-动量锁定、非线性反常霍尔效应（non-linear anomalous Hall effect）以及超导邻近效应（superconducting proximity effect）等关键现象，并讨论了该类拓扑材料的潜在应用。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑半金属，尤其是Weyl半金属，因其拓扑保护的线性色散表面态（surface states）和手性（chirality）特征而受到广泛关注。然而，由于体态能谱无带隙（gapless bulk spectrum），在输运研究中区分表面态贡献成为核心难题。

Method: 本文采用综述（review）方法，系统梳理了拓扑半金属在电荷输运、自旋相关输运、表面态的磁响应以及非线性反常霍尔效应等方面的实验研究结果。

Result: Weyl半金属的表面态是手性的（chiral），类似于Chern绝缘体（Chern insulators），可被视为量子霍尔效应（quantum Hall effect）的三维类比。自旋-动量锁定（spin-momentum locking）使得该类材料在自旋相关效应中具有重要价值。非线性反常霍尔效应直接反映了非零贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的存在。

Conclusion: 拓扑半金属作为一类新型拓扑材料，在超导邻近器件、自旋输运和磁响应等方面展现出丰富的物理现象，具有潜在的应用前景。

Abstract: For the solid state physics, recent interest to topological systems is mostly connected with topological semimetals, in particular, to Weyl ones as the most representative semimetal type. Like other topological materials, e.g. topological and Chern insulators, topological semimetals acquire topologically protected surface states with linear dispersion. In contrast to helical surface states in topological insulators, the surface states are chiral for Weyl semimetals, similarly to Chern insulators, which allows to consider Weyl semimetals as the three-dimensional analog of the quantum Hall effect regime. Weyl semimetals are also interesting for spin-dependent effects, due to the spin-momentum locking in the topological surface states. For topological semimetals, the main problem of transport investigations is to reveal the surface states contribution in the material with gapless bulk spectrum. Here, we present review of experimental results on charge and spin transport in topological semimetals: charge transport in different superconducting proximity devices; spin-dependent transport; magnetic response of the topological surface states; non-linear anomalous Hall effect as the direct manifestation of the non-zero Berry curvature in topological semimetals. Possible applications are also considered for this new class of topological materials.

</details>

Method: 在hBN-石墨烯-hBN-SiO₂异质结中利用标准白光光源实现光诱导调制掺杂，结合光退火效应。采用Drude输运模型和Landauer输运模型对器件的输运性质进行分析，通过光调控实现迁移率和平均散射长度的可逆精确调节。

Result: 该技术能够以高精度可逆地调控石墨烯的迁移率和平均散射长度，使器件可在原位实现扩散输运与准弹道输运之间的切换。利用对局域无序的卓越控制，在初始质量不足以观测的器件中成功实现了量子霍尔等旋铁磁态。

Conclusion: 光诱导调制掺杂技术提供了对范德瓦尔斯异质结中载流子密度和电荷无序的精确操控手段，是一种高度易行的方法，可用于制备能够实现关联电子态（correlated electronic states）的高质量器件。

Abstract: Modulation doping, a well-established technique for traditional semiconductor heterostructures, is a promising approach for tailoring carrier concentration in 2D materials devices. In this letter we report on photoinduced modulation doping in hBN-graphene-hBN-SiO2 heterostructures utilizing standard white light sources and no additional fabrication complexity. We establish the use of this technique to both dope the channel material and to photoanneal devices, providing control over electronic doping and disorder in the graphene channel. We analyze the transport properties by employing Drude and Landauer transport models, highlighting the ability to reversibly tune the mobility and mean scattering length of the graphene with a high degree of accuracy. This tunability allows us to switch our device between the diffusive and quasi-ballistic transport regimes in situ. We utilize the exceptional control our technique provides over local disorder to realize quantum Hall isospin ferromagnetic states in a device whose initial quality would otherwise leave such states unobservable. These results demonstrate precise manipulation of carrier density and charge disorder in van der Waals heterostructures, providing a highly accessible approach to creating high-quality devices capable of realizing correlated electronic states.

### [138] [Entanglement Dynamics across a Monitored Quantum Point Contact](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22555)
*Anna Delmonte,Marco Schirò*

TL;DR: 本文研究了一个被监测的量子点接触（quantum point contact）中的纠缠动力学，发现单点局域监测会显著改变纠缠产生模式：纠缠熵先线性增长至体积律（volume-law scaling）最大值，随后缓慢衰减至零，与幺正情况下的对数增长形成鲜明对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索局域监测（local monitoring）对量子点接触中纠缠动力学的重塑作用，并理解其与幺正演化（unitary evolution）下纠缠行为的差异。

Method: 采用准粒子图像（quasiparticle picture）解释纠缠行为的交叉（crossover），并连接全计数统计（full counting statistics）与页面曲线（Page curve）研究及实验相关探针。

Result: 纠缠熵先呈线性增长至体积律标度的最大值，随后系统逐渐排空时缓慢衰减至零；该行为源于损失（losses）所建立的偏置电压（bias voltage）的涌现与衰减。

Abstract: We compute the entanglement dynamics across a monitored quantum point contact, where particle losses are recorded on a given site, and demonstrate how this single-site local monitoring substantially reshapes the entanglement production. Contrary to the unitary case, where entanglement entropy grows logarithmically in time, here we find first a linear growth, up to a maximum value displaying volume-law scaling, and then a slow decay to zero, as the system empties out. We capture this crossover using a quasiparticle picture, where the first linear growth arises due to an emergent bias voltage established by the losses, which eventually decays away as the system depletes. We connect our results to studies of the Page curve and to experimentally relevant probes, via full counting statistics of charge transfer across a subregion, with only a single channel to unravel leading to a favorable scaling of the postselection overhead. Natural platforms for this setting include mesoscopic systems and ultracold atoms.

### [139] [Quantum Batteries in two-dimensional material-based Josephson Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22582)
*V. Varrica,G. Gemme,F. M. D. Pellegrino,E. Paladino,M. Sassetti,D. Ferraro*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出并分析了一种基于二维材料约瑟夫森结（如石墨烯）与谐振腔电感耦合的类Dicke量子电池固态实现方案。安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound states）作为非简并二能级系统，系统支持单光子和双光子共振过程。LC电路磁通与超电流的耦合产生了传统Dicke模型中没有的纵向相互作用项，可在适当参数范围内增强能量存储。此外，该架构还允许通过调节结上超导相位差实现等效的充电协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索固态系统中类Dicke量子电池（Dicke-like quantum battery）的实验实现路径，利用二维材料约瑟夫森结（Josephson junction）与谐振腔的耦合结构，突破传统Dicke模型（conventional Dicke model）的限制，提升量子电池的能量存储性能。

Method: 以石墨烯（graphene）为代表材料，构建二维材料基约瑟夫森结与LC谐振腔电感耦合的固态架构。利用安德烈夫束缚态作为非相互作用、能量非简并的二能级系统（two-level systems），引入LC电路磁通与结超电流耦合产生的纵向相互作用项（longitudinal interaction terms），并探索单光子与双光子共振过程（single-photon and two-photon resonant processes）。

Result: 该固态架构中存在的纵向相互作用项在传统Dicke模型中无对应项，可在合适的参数范围内显著增强能量存储（enhance energy storage）。同时，该架构支持一种通过调节约瑟夫森结上超导相位差（superconducting phase difference）实现的替代性等效充电协议。

Conclusion: 基于二维材料约瑟夫森结的类Dicke量子电池方案在固态平台上具备可行性，其独特的纵向耦合机制为提升量子电池性能提供了新途径，且充电协议具有灵活的可调性。

Abstract: We investigate the solid-state implementation of a Dicke-like quantum battery consisting of a two-dimensional material-based Josephson junction inductively coupled to a resonator, using graphene as a representative example. In this configuration, Andreev bound states naturally act as non-interacting, energetically non-degenerate two-level systems, and the setup allows for both single-photon and two-photon resonant processes. The coupling between the LC-circuit flux and the supercurrent through the junction gives rise to peculiar longitudinal interaction terms that have no counterpart in the conventional Dicke model. These additional couplings can enhance energy storage for a proper range of parameters. The proposed architecture also enables an alternative, but equivalent, charging protocol that relies on tuning the superconducting phase difference across the junction.

### [140] [Spintronic Neuromorphic Hardware Using Domain Wall Based Neurons and Quantized Synapses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22625)
*Sakshi Kiran Bandekar,Arnab Ganguly,Debanjan Polley,Debasis Das*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过自旋轨道矩（spin-orbit torque）驱动的磁畴壁动力学，在重金属/铁磁（HM/FM）异质结纳米轨道中模拟了人工神经元和突触的功能，并构建了全连接人工神经网络（ANN）。采用3 ns电流脉冲模拟ReLU激活函数，利用10 ns电流脉冲下的畴壁钉扎实现可调突触权重，在MNIST和Fashion-MNIST数据集上分别达到~97%和~86%的准确率，经权重量化后仍保持~95%和~62%的准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统神经网络硬件实现面临能效和集成度瓶颈，亟需开发新型神经形态（neuromorphic）器件来模拟突触可塑性和神经元激活功能。自旋电子器件具有非易失性、低功耗和高可扩展性等优势，但如何在单一平台上同时实现神经元和突触功能仍具挑战。

Method: 采用重金属/铁磁（HM/FM）异质结构成的矩形磁性纳米轨道，利用横向磁畴壁（domain wall）动力学来模拟神经突触器件。神经元方面，通过3 ns电流脉冲驱动畴壁运动来模拟ReLU激活函数；突触方面，利用10 ns电流脉冲通过带有半圆形凹槽（notch）的波纹状纳米轨道，实现阶梯式畴壁钉扎，不同钉扎点的电导作为稳定的突触权重。并对训练后的权重进行离散量化以实现低内存占用的稀疏网络。

Result: 在MNIST和Fashion-MNIST数据集上，使用float32浮点权重的全连接ANN分别达到~97%和~86%的识别准确率。将权重量化为离散等级后，在两个数据集上分别保持~95%和~62%的准确率。实验还观察到阈值依赖的延迟效应（threshold-dependent delay effect），每个去钉扎事件受前序事件影响，成功模拟了突触记忆和适应性。

Conclusion: 基于自旋轨道矩（spin-orbit torque）的磁畴壁动力学可以在单一平台上同时实现人工神经元和突触功能，为构建低功耗、高能效的神经形态计算系统提供了可行方案。权重量化策略在显著降低内存占用的同时仍能保持较高的识别精度，尤其适用于MNIST数据集；但对于更复杂的Fashion-MNIST数据集，量化带来的精度下降更为明显。

Abstract: In this work, we simulate the functionality of artificial neuron and synapse using spin-orbit torque-based spintronic devices and implemented a fully connected artificial neural netwrok (ANN). These neuro-synaptic devices are emulated using transverse domain wall dynamics in a rectangular magnetic nanotrack comprised of heavy metal/ferromagnet (HM/FM) heterostructures. The ReLU activation function of the neuron has been mimicked using the domain wall motion induced by a 3 ns current pulse. The synapse has been modelled using current-induced domain wall (DW) dynamics through a corrugated HM/FM nanotrack under the influence of a 10 ns current pulse with varying current density. The semicircular corrugations are in the form of notches, which are symmetrically located on both sides of the nanotrack. By applying 10 ns current pulses of varying densities, we achieve controlled DW pinning, revealing a step-like motion caused by temporary pauses at each pinning center. The electrical conductance of the pinned DW across various pinning points, act as stable synaptic weights for our ANN. Furthermore, we observe a threshold-dependent delay effect where each depinning event is influenced by previous ones, successfully mimicking synaptic memory and adaptability in neuromorphic systems. The fully connected ANN has been modeled using the conventional float32 synaptic weights for the MNIST and Fashion MNIST datasets with an accuracy of ~97 % and ~86 %, respectively, which serves as a test bed of our neuromorphic simulations. With the aim of implementing a sparse and low memory footprint ANN, we quantize the trained synaptic weights into discrete quantized level and tested the network, which demonstrate an accuracy of ~95% and ~62%, for the MNIST and Fashion-MNIST dataset, respectively.

### [141] [Monitored quantum transport through a disordered one-dimensional conductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22701)
*J. Sánchez Fernán,J. Tworzydło,C. W. J. Beenakker*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对通过单模导体传播的电子的多粒子密度矩阵的量子主方程（quantum master equation），该方程结合了无序弹性散射与时间分辨投影测量（time-resolved projective measurements）。研究表明，监测会抑制导致一维局域化（one-dimensional localization）的相位相干性，使典型的透射概率随导体长度的衰减从指数衰减（$e^{-L/ξ}$）在长度$L\simeq \ell_φ$处交叉为欧姆型（Ohmic）$1/L$衰减。通过弱监测下的数值求解，发现相干长度$\ell_φ$与测量平均时间$τ_φ$之间存在对数依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论表明，无序导体中的量子相干性会导致一维局域化，但测量（measurement）如何破坏相位相干性并影响输运特性（如电导与散粒噪声）尚需定量刻画。本文旨在构建一个统一的量子主方程框架，以描述监测过程对电子传输统计行为的调控作用。

Method: 作者构建了电子在多粒子密度矩阵框架下的量子主方程，其中同时包含无序弹性散射（elastic scattering by disorder）和时间分辨投影测量（time-resolved projective measurements）。通过解该主方程，分析了透射电子的全计数统计（full counting statistics）及其随导体长度的演化行为。

Result: 透射电子的全计数统计呈二项分布（binomial distribution），其均值${\cal T}$和方差${\cal T}(1-{\cal T})$分别决定电导与散粒噪声功率（shot noise power）。典型透射概率随长度$L$的衰减在$L\simeq \ell_φ$处从指数衰减$e^{-L/ξ}$（局域化长度$ξ$）交叉为欧姆型$1/L$衰减。弱监测下，相干长度满足$\ell_φ\simeq ξ\ln(v_{\rm F}τ_φ/ξ)$，呈对数依赖关系。

Conclusion: 监测能有效抑制一维局域化所需的相位相干性，导致输运行为从局域化区间向欧姆区间交叉。该工作为理解测量诱导的退相干（decoherence）对量子输运的影响提供了定量理论工具。

Abstract: We formulate a quantum master equation for the many-particle density matrix of electrons propagating through a single-mode conductor, combining elastic scattering by disorder with time-resolved projective measurements that monitor the outcome of scattering events. The full counting statistics of transmitted electrons has a binomial distribution function, whose mean ${\cal T}$ and variance ${\cal T}(1-{\cal T})$ determine the conductance and shot noise power, respectively. Monitoring suppresses the phase coherence responsible for one-dimensional localization: The decay with conductor length $L$ of the typical transmission probability crosses over at $L\simeq \ell_φ$ from the exponential $e^{-L/ξ}$ (with localization length $ξ$) to the Ohmic $1/L$ decay. Numerical solution of the master equation gives, for weak monitoring, a logarithmic dependence $\ell_φ\simeq ξ\ln(v_{\rm F}τ_φ/ξ)$ of the coherence length $\ell_φ$ on the mean time $τ_φ$ between measurements.

</details>


### [142] [Signatures of quantum chaos in phonon-polariton billiards](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22753)
*Yinan Dong,Felix Liu,Ekrem Demirboga,Andrey Grankin,Dihao Sun,Yuchen Lin,Lukas Wehmeier,Matthew Fu,Cory R. Dean,Song Liu,James H. Edgar,Michael M. Folger,Victor M. Galitski,Dmitri N. Basov*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本论文利用扫描近场光学显微镜实验研究了六方氮化硼（hBN）弹子球台中的双曲声子极化激元，在可积和混沌几何结构中观察到量子疤痕、边界模式以及随机波特征，并通过数值框架和理论分析揭示了从泊松型到Wigner-Dyson型能级统计的交叉行为，建立了介观范德华弹子球台作为研究光-物质混合极化子混沌动力学的平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在介观尺度下，具有可积与混沌几何结构的六方氮化硼（hBN）弹子球台中双曲声子极化激元（hyperbolic phonon polaritons）的动力学行为，验证随机波猜想及量子疤痕（quantum scarring）等混沌系统中的关键现象。

Method: 采用扫描近场光学显微镜（scanning near-field optical microscopy）对hBN弹子球台进行实空间成像；基于亥姆霍兹方程（Helmholtz equation）构建数值框架，引入广义边界条件以编码角度依赖的反射相位偏移；利用耗散格林函数（dissipative Green's function）进行理论分析。

Result: 在Sinai弹子球台中观察到与量子疤痕一致的不规则模式以及对弱探针扰动的异常敏感性；随机波特征与非混沌的一维边界模式共存；随着边界复杂度增加，测量信号的傅里叶变换演化为环状结构，符合Berry随机波猜想；能级统计从可积弹子球台的泊松（Poisson）型行为过渡到混沌几何中的Wigner-Dyson型行为，但存在由非线性边界条件导致的小偏差。

Conclusion: 建立了介观范德华弹子球台（mesoscopic van der Waals billiards）作为研究光-物质混合极化子（hybrid light-matter polaritons）广义混沌动力学的有效平台。

Abstract: We use scanning near-field optical microscopy to image hyperbolic phonon polaritons in hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) billiards with integrable and chaotic geometries. In Sinai billiards, we observe irregular mode patterns consistent with quantum scarring, together with an unexpected sensitivity to weak probe perturbations. These random-wave features coexist with non-chaotic one-dimensional boundary modes arising from nontrivial polariton reflection at the billiard edge. As the billiard boundary becomes increasingly complex, the Fourier transforms of the measured signals evolve toward ring-like structures consistent with Berry's random-wave conjecture. We develop a numerical framework based on the Helmholtz equation with generalized boundary conditions that encode angle-dependent reflection phase shifts. The calculated level statistics exhibit a crossover from Poisson-like behavior in integrable billiards to Wigner-Dyson-like behavior in chaotic geometries, with small deviations from the canonical form arising from nonlinear boundary conditions that require self-consistent bulk-boundary analysis. Theoretical analysis based on dissipative Green's functions qualitatively reproduces the near-field data. These results establish mesoscopic van der Waals billiards as a rich platform for studying generalized chaotic dynamics of hybrid light-matter polaritons.

### [143] [Signatures of the Quantum Geometric Dipole of Interlayer Excitons in Counterflow Conductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22810)
*Fanuel I. Mendez,Luis Brey,H. A. Fertig*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出使用双层层间激子（interlayer excitons）的反向电流（counterflow electric currents）作为探针，测量其量子几何偶极矩（quantum geometric dipole, QGD），并在一维周期势与强垂直磁场的磁激子（magnetoexciton）能带中展示了该方案的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体电子系统的集体激发可携带内部结构，支撑新颖的量子几何与拓扑性质。其中激子（exciton）的量子几何偶极矩（QGD）直接对应内部极化，对于双层的层间激子表现为面内偶极矩，可通过面内电场驱动，但如何有效探测该QGD结构尚需研究。

Method: 本文构建了一个在强垂直磁场下叠加一维周期势的双层结构，产生具有QGD结构的磁激子能带。采用包含带间隧穿（inter-band tunneling）的玻尔兹曼方法（Boltzmann approach）建模激子输运，考虑强层反对称驱动场导致的非平衡动量分布。

Result: 对驱动场的层对称分量的线性响应可提供QGD信息，且通过改变层反对称场可探测激子能带的宽QGD结构。反向电导率（counterflow conductivity）可作为可调探针，反映层间激子携带的内部量子几何结构。

Conclusion: 反向电导率是探测多体激发量子几何结构的有效探针，将输运测量与激子的量子几何偶极矩联系起来。

Abstract: Collective excitations of many-body electron systems can carry internal structure, supporting novel quantum geometric and topological properties. Among these are a quantum geometric dipole (QGD), which for excitons have direct significance as an internal polarization. For interlayer excitons of a bilayer system, this represents an in-plane dipole moment, which can be used to drive them with in-plane electric fields. In this work, we consider counterflow electric currents associated with driven excitons in such a bilayer system as a probe of their QGD structure. As a simple but non-trivial example, we analyze a structure with a one-dimensional periodic potential in a strong perpendicular magnetic field. The resulting magnetoexciton bands host QGD structure that distinguishes it from the exciton QGD of a uniform system. To model exciton transport we adopt a Boltzmann approach that includes inter-band tunneling, allowing us to consider non-equilibrium momentum distributions that result from strong layer-antisymmetric driving fields. We show how linear response to a layer-symmetric component of the driving fields provide information about the QGD, and that the broad QGD structure of the exciton bands can be probed by the varying the layer-antisymmetric field. Our results demonstrate that counterflow conductivity serves as a tunable probe of the internal quantum geometric structure carried by the interlayer excitons, connecting transport to the quantum geometry of many-body excitations.

</details>

### [144] [Summarizing Time-Varying Digital Image Correlation Strain Fields Using Sankey Diagrams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22627)
*Victor Persson,Christofer Boo,Mohit Sharma,Ingrid Hotz*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于Sankey图的可视化摘要方法，通过跟踪冯·米塞斯等效应变场的超水平集连通分量，将高应变区域的演化（包括诞生、持续、合并与消失）压缩为单个全局时间图，从而补充传统逐帧空间可视化在捕捉时间模式上的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字图像相关法（DIC）能够获取材料变形过程中密集、时解析的表面应变场，揭示应变局域化与失效机制；然而，现有的应变场分析主要依赖逐帧空间可视化，难以从全局时间维度识别应变演化的时间模式。

Method: 提出一种基于超水平集（superlevel sets）的视觉摘要方法：从冯·米塞斯等效应变场中提取高应变区域，通过空间重叠（spatial overlap）追踪这些连通分量（connected components）随时间的变化，最终将各分量的诞生、持续、合并与消失编码为一张Sankey图。

Result: 在四种不同缺口几何形状的拉伸试验数据集上应用该方法，结果表明该方法能够紧凑地捕捉不同变形机制（deformation regimes）之间的差异以及失效的定性前兆（qualitative precursors to failure）。

Conclusion: 该方法为传统空间应变可视化提供了一种全局时间视角的补充，有助于更全面地理解应变局域化的演化过程。

Abstract: Digital Image Correlation (DIC) enables dense, time-resolved measurement of surface strain in deforming materials, providing insight into strain localization and failure mechanisms. However, the resulting strain fields are typically explored frame-by-frame through spatial visualizations, making global temporal patterns difficult to discern. We present a visual summarization approach that represents the evolution of high-strain regions as a single Sankey diagram constructed from superlevel sets of the von Mises equivalent strain field. By tracking connected components over time via spatial overlap, the diagram encodes the birth, persistence, merging, and disappearance of strain concentrations. Applied to four tensile test datasets with varying notch geometries, the approach compactly captures differences in deformation regimes and qualitative precursors to failure, complementing traditional spatial strain visualizations with a global temporal overview.

### [145] [Conditional Entropy of Heat Diffusion on Temporal Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21514)
*Samuel Koovely,Alexandre Bovet*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出将热扩散的条件熵（conditional entropy of heat diffusion）从静态图扩展到时序网络（temporal networks），证明其时间单调性（类似于热力学第二定律的信息论类比），并引入局部版本用于变点检测（change-point detection）。方法在合成基准和法国小学真实接触网络上得到验证，且检测到的变点可用于改进社区检测（community detection）的质量与可解释性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时序网络常常经历不同的结构阶段（structural phases），识别这些阶段之间的变点（change points）具有重要意义但具有挑战性。现有方法在连续时间时序网络中缺乏基于信息论视角的有效变点检测工具。

Method: 本文首先将静态图上的热扩散条件熵扩展到时序网络中，给出了其上界，并解释了非对称时序路径（asymmetric temporal paths）如何导致偏差。进一步证明了该量在时间上具有单调性，为时序网络上的非齐次扩散（inhomogeneous diffusion）提供了类似于热力学第二定律的信息论类比。然后，引入局部版本的条件熵，用于探测有限时间窗口上的扩散过程，并以此作为连续时间时序网络中变点检测的信号。

Result: 在合成基准上进行了变点检测的比较实验（包括与现有快照设置下非参数基线的对比），并在法国小学的真实时序接触网络上进行了应用验证。实验表明，该方法能够有效检测变点，且利用检测到的变点对子区间进行社区检测可提升聚类结果的质量和可解释性。

Conclusion: 提出的条件熵及其局部扩展为时序网络的变点检测提供了一种有效且具有信息论基础的新方法，并展示了其在社区检测任务中的实用价值。

Abstract: Many complex systems can be modeled by temporal networks, whose organization often evolves through distinct structural phases. Detecting the change points that delimit these phases is both important and challenging. In this work, we extend the conditional entropy of heat diffusion from static graphs to temporal networks and study its properties. We provide an upper bound and explain how discrepancies from it arise from the presence of asymmetric temporal paths. Moreover, we show that this quantity is monotone in time, yielding an information-theoretic analog of the second law of thermodynamics for inhomogeneous diffusion on temporal networks. We then introduce a local version of conditional entropy, designed to probe diffusion over finite temporal windows, and show that it provides an informative signal for change-point detection in continuous-time temporal networks. We evaluate the proposed methodology on synthetic benchmarks, including comparative experiments with existing nonparametric baselines in the snapshot setting, and then apply it to a real-world temporal contact network from a French primary school. Finally, we show how to use detected change points to perform community detection on targeted sub-intervals, improving the quality and interpretability of the clustering results.

### [146] [Chiral Electromagnetic Surface Waves on Chern-Simons Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21577)
*Nemanja Kaloper*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明了在无限空间常规真空电动力学中，嵌入一个余维为1的Chern-Simons界面即可支持手征电磁表面波，无需任何材料响应或几何约束。该模式是无能隙的手征表面光子，具有线性色散和由Chern-Simons系数决定的频率无关折射率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在无材料响应（material response）和几何约束（geometric confinement）的条件下，常规真空麦克斯韦理论（Maxwell theory）是否仍能支持局域化的手征表面电磁模式。

Method: 在无限空间真空电动力学中引入一个余维为1的Chern-Simons界面（codimension-$1$ Chern-Simons interface），并通过求解精确边值问题（exact boundary value problem）分析表面波的模式结构。

Result: Chern-Simons相互作用对沿界面的两种手征性（helicities）以相反符号作用，产生一个可归一化的局域界面模式。该模式为无能隙的手征表面光子（gapless chiral surface photon），具有线性色散和由Chern-Simons系数决定的频率无关折射率。

Conclusion: 即使在纯粹真空中，仅通过Chern-Simons界面即可产生手征电磁表面波，表明这种拓扑界面相互作用的效应可替代传统材料或几何结构来束缚和引导表面电磁波。

Abstract: We show that Maxwell theory with a codimension-$1$ Chern-Simons interface supports chiral electromagnetic surface waves on the interface, even when the bulk theory on both sides is conventional vacuum electrodynamics in infinite space. Solving the exact boundary value problem we find that the Chern-Simons interaction acts with opposite sign on the two helicities oriented along the interface, giving rise to one normalizable mode localized on the interface. This mode is a gapless chiral surface photon with linear dispersion and a frequency-independent index of refraction set by the Chern-Simons coefficient. This mode exists despite the absence of ambient material response or geometric confinement.

### [147] [Cosmological Collider in the Grassmannian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21581)
*Mattia Arundine,Guilherme L. Pimentel*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文利用宇宙学格拉斯曼（cosmological Grassmannian）将外部共形耦合标量粒子交换一般质量和自旋粒子时的四点波函数系数（four-point wavefunction coefficients）以超几何函数（hypergeometric functions）和勒让德多项式（Legendre polynomials）的闭合形式写出，通过普吕克坐标（Plücker coordinates）和曼德斯塔姆不变量（Mandelstam invariants）推导标准靴带微分方程（bootstrap differential equation），并通过无奇异性和动量空间运动学极限确定边界条件；该格拉斯曼空间表达式比动量空间对应形式更简洁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙学碰撞者物理（cosmological collider physics）在近德西特极限（near-de Sitter limit）下的现象学主要源于四点波函数系数，而该系数的详细计算是宇宙学靴带（cosmological bootstrap）的核心挑战。

Method: 利用宇宙学格拉斯曼，通过其普吕克坐标和曼德斯塔姆不变量基，将标准靴带微分方程改写，从而将s-通道关联子用S曼德斯塔姆的超几何函数表示，自旋信息则作为依赖于其他曼德斯塔姆变量的勒让德多项式整体因子出现；边界条件通过无奇异性和动量空间波函数运动学极限匹配来确定。

Result: 四点波函数系数以超几何函数和勒让德多项式的闭合形式给出，格拉斯曼空间中的公式比动量空间对应形式更简单。

Conclusion: 格拉斯曼作为宇宙学的运动学空间（kinematic space）展现了另一个有用应用，即简化关联子计算。

Abstract: We revisit the computation of four-point wavefunction coefficients for external conformally coupled scalars exchanging a particle of general mass and spin. Much of the phenomenology of cosmological collider physics in the near-de Sitter limit follows from this function. Computing it in detail is a central challenge in the cosmological bootstrap. Using the cosmological Grassmannian, we write this correlator in closed form using hypergeometric functions and Legendre polynomials. We achieve this by writing the standard bootstrap differential equation using the Plücker coordinates of the Grassmannian, and using the basis of Mandelstam invariants. The correlator in the s-channel can be written in terms of a hypergeometric function of the S Mandelstam, while the spin information appears as an overall Legendre polynomial factor that also depends on the other Mandelstams. We fix the boundary conditions by first demanding the absence of unphysical singularities, and by further matching to kinematic limits of the momentum-space wavefunction. Our formulae in Grassmannian space are much simpler than their counterparts in momentum space, demonstrating another useful application of the Grassmannian as a kinematic space for cosmology.

### [148] [Multipositivity Constrains the Chiral Lagrangian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21582)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用现代散射振幅程序中的工具（tools from the modern scattering amplitudes program），分析在平面极限（planar limit）下手征拉氏量中多粒子动力学的一致性条件，推导出耦合常数所需满足的约束关系，并引入一种适用于任意平面树图（planar tree-level）理论的多正性（multipositivity）约束的新表述。

Result: 在平面极限下，手征拉氏量的某些Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）存在由手征反常（chiral anomaly）所决定的下界；即这些系数受到手征反常的约束而无法低于某一数值。

Conclusion: 该结果揭示了强相互作用的反常扇区（anomalous sector）与非反常扇区（nonanomalous sector）之间此前未被注意到的微妙联系，并为任意平面树图理论的多正性约束提供了一种新的表述框架。

Abstract: The chiral Lagrangian is a cornerstone of modern particle physics, offering a systematic and quantitative description of low-energy pions. Using tools from the modern scattering amplitudes program, we show that consistent multiparticle dynamics impose novel constraints on the coupling constants of this theory. In the planar limit, these constraints imply that certain Wilson coefficients of the chiral Lagrangian are bounded from below by the chiral anomaly. Our results reveal a subtle connection between the anomalous and nonanomalous sectors of the underlying strong interactions, while introducing a novel formulation of multipositivity bounds that holds for any planar tree-level theory.

### [149] [Algebraic locality and non-invertible Gauss laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21591)
*Nicholas Holfester,Jonathan Sorce*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究2+1维闭合格点上非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetry）的高斯定律（Gauss law）下的代数局域性原理（algebraic locality principles）。结果表明，对于一大类非可逆在位对称性，Haag对偶性（Haag duality）仅在无尖角（cuspless）区域精确成立，尖角区域需加“领圈”（collar）后才成立弱形式；并证明了基于群的double模型中的不相交可加性（disjoint additivity）以及一般Hopf代数下的弱化版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前工作（arXiv:2509.03589）已分析了可逆对称性（invertible symmetry）下高斯定律对Haag对偶性和不相交可加性的影响，本文旨在将这一分析推广至非可逆对称性，探索代数局域性原理在更一般对称性结构下的保持程度。

Method: 采用代数方法分析2+1维闭合格点系统，分别处理两类模型：具有纯磁约束的double模型（double models with a purely magnetic constraint），以及更一般的由Hopf代数（Hopf algebra）在位作用诱导约束的框架，并具体处理一类扩展的string-net模型。

Result: 对于一大类非可逆在位对称性，Haag对偶性仅在无尖角区域精确保持；尖角区域仅满足需添加领圈的弱Haag对偶性（weak form of Haag duality）。对于基于群的double模型，不相交可加性成立；对于一般Hopf代数，仅成立弱化的不相交可加性。

Conclusion: 非可逆对称性下的代数局域性原理相较于可逆情形出现弱化：Haag对偶性在尖角区域需修正，不相交可加性在一般Hopf代数框架下仅以弱形式成立，表明非可逆对称性对局域结构产生更复杂的约束。

Abstract: We study algebraic locality principles on a 2+1D closed lattice in the presence of a Gauss law for a non-invertible symmetry. Prior work in arXiv:2509.03589 showed that when enforcing the Gauss law of an invertible symmetry, the principle of "Haag duality" is preserved exactly, and "disjoint additivity" is preserved after appropriate treatment of discreteness artifacts. Here we show that for a large class of non-invertible on-site symmetries, Haag duality is preserved exactly only for sufficiently nice, "cuspless" regions. For cusped regions, we instead have a weak form of Haag duality that requires adding a collar. Our results apply to double models with a purely magnetic constraint, and to the more general framework of constraints induced by the on-site action of a Hopf algebra. In particular, we treat a class of extended string-net models explicitly. We also demonstrate disjoint additivity for double models based on a group, and a weakened form of disjoint additivity in the setting of a general Hopf algebra.

### [150] [Dissipative stabilization of Ostrogradsky modes in non-equilibrium field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21689)
*Y. M. P. Gomes*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在开放系统Keldysh-Lindblad框架下研究高阶导数量子场论中的Ostrogradsky不稳定性问题。通过将鬼（ghost）扇区耦合到耗散库，自洽间隙方程生成非微扰有效质量和耗散宽度。超过临界耦合时，非平衡动力学出现分叉耗散分支，标志着耗散相变的发生。系统通过两种机制抑制鬼激发：一为大有效质量保留准粒子特征，另一为强耗散展宽通过过阻尼动力学破坏准粒子特征。结果表明耗散效应可能提供一种非平衡机制来抑制Ostrogradsky鬼。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶导数量子场论因Ostrogradsky不稳定性（Ostrogradsky instability）导致鬼（ghost）激发而受到困扰，该问题长期以来是量子场论和引力理论中一个根本性难题。本文旨在探索能否通过开放系统框架下的耗散效应来稳定这类不稳定性。

Method: 采用开放系统Keldysh-Lindblad框架，将鬼扇区耦合到耗散库（dissipative baths），通过自洽间隙方程（self-consistent gap equations）生成非微扰有效质量和耗散宽度。通过分析参数空间中的临界行为，研究非平衡动力学随耦合强度的演化。

Result: 存在一个临界耦合值，超过该阈值时系统出现分叉耗散分支（bifurcated dissipative branches），标志着耗散相变（dissipative phase transition）的发生。系统展现出两种不同的鬼抑制机制：一是动态生成的大有效质量保留准粒子（quasiparticle）特征；二是强耗散展宽导致的过阻尼（overdamped）动力学，完全破坏准粒子特征。

Conclusion: 耗散效应可能提供一种非平衡机制实现Ostrogradsky鬼的谱抑制（spectral suppression）。稳定机制与类鬼谱结构（ghost-like spectral structure）存在内在联系，该机制与健康扇区（healthy sector）的对比进一步支持了这一结论。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate higher-derivative quantum field theories and the problem of Ostrogradsky instability within an open-system Keldysh-Lindblad framework. Coupling the ghost sector to dissipative baths generates non-perturbative effective masses and dissipative widths through self-consistent gap equations. Above a critical coupling, the nonequilibrium dynamics develops bifurcated dissipative branches, signaling the emergence of a dissipative phase transition and a nontrivial critical structure in parameter space. We find that the resulting dissipative dynamics can suppress ghost excitations through two distinct mechanisms: in one branch, a large dynamically generated effective mass preserves a quasiparticle-like excitation, while in the second branch, strong dissipative broadening destroys the quasiparticle character through overdamped dynamics. Our results suggest that dissipative effects may provide a nonequilibrium mechanism for the spectral suppression of Ostrogradsky ghosts. The comparison with the healthy sector indicates that the stabilization mechanism is intrinsically tied to the ghost-like spectral structure.

</details>


### [151] [Universalities of Defects in Quantum Field Theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21755)
*Siwei Zhong*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文从对称性原理出发，系统研究了现代量子场论（quantum field theory）中缺陷（defect）的普适动力学行为，涵盖缺陷重整化群流（defect renormalization group flows）、有效弦论（effective string theory）以及原子量子气体中的杂质（impurities）等多个主题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺陷作为扩展算子（extended operators），如边界（boundaries）、杂质（impurities）和探测粒子（probe particles），在量子多体系统中既是丰富的物理对象，也是强大的理论工具，理解其动力学普适特性具有基础性意义。

Method: 采用对称性原理（symmetry principles）作为统一视角，将缺陷重整化群流、有效弦理论和原子量子气体中的杂质问题纳入同一分析框架，揭示缺陷动力学的普适方面（universal aspects）。

Result: 通过对称性分析，在缺陷重整化群流、有效弦理论以及原子气体杂质系统三个主题下，获得了关于缺陷动力学普适行为的理论结果。

Conclusion: 对称性原理是理解缺陷动力学普适行为的关键工具，能够将不同物理背景下看似独立的缺陷问题统一起来。

Abstract: Defects are both physically rich objects and powerful tools in modern quantum field theory. They are extended operators, such as boundaries, impurities, and probe particles, embedded in many-body systems. In this dissertation, we study the universal aspects of defect dynamics from the perspective of symmetry principles. We bring together several themes, including defect renormalization group flows, effective string theory, and impurities in atomic quantum gases.

</details>

Abstract: This talk introduces a Cartan-geometric framework for generalised geometries governed by a differential graded Lie algebra. In contrast to ordinary Cartan geometry, the tangent bundle is extended and qu both a global duality group and a local gauge group. This framework provides a systematic construction of generalised connections and their torsion and curvature tensors for generic generalised geometries. We also review the realisation of these algebraic structures on the phase space of branes in M-theory.

### [153] [New mechanism for fermion localization in $f(T,T_G)$-brane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21838)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用 Dirac 旋量与挠率不变量（torsional invariants）的非最小耦合（non-minimal coupling），导出描述 Kaluza-Klein 模的有效薛定谔类方程（Schrödinger-like equations），并利用香农熵和相对概率等信息论测度量化局域化程度。

Result: 遥平行高斯-博内项显著改变有效势的形态；零模仅有一个手征分量可在膜上局域化，且局域化程度依赖于模型选择；质量谱连续但出现共振态（resonant states）；香农熵和相对概率显示挠率修正导致信息非平庸再分布并增强局域化。

Conclusion: 高阶挠率项在膜世界场景中塑造费米子局域化和共振结构方面发挥关键作用。

Abstract: We investigate the localization of fermionic fields in a five-dimensional braneworld scenario within the framework of modified teleparallel gravity described by a general $f(T,T_G)$ function. Considering a non-minimal coupling between a Dirac spinor and the torsional invariants, we derive the effective Schrödinger-like equations governing the Kaluza-Klein modes. We showed that the contribution of the teleparallel Gauss-Bonnet term significantly modifies the effective potentials and, consequently, the localization properties. The zero-mode analysis reveals that only one chiral component can be localized on the brane, with the degree of confinement depending on the chosen model. In the massive sector, the spectrum is continuous, but resonant states arise due to the internal structure of the potentials. Additionally, we employ information-theoretic measures, such as Shannon entropy and relative probability, to quantify the localization mechanism. Our results show that the torsional modifications induce a nontrivial redistribution of information, exhibiting stronger localization. These findings highlight the role of higher-order torsional terms in shaping fermionic localization and resonance structures in braneworld scenarios.

### [154] [Stochastic inflation as an open quantum system II: open effective field theory and stochastic matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21929)
*Yue-Zhou Li*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文进一步发展了将随机暴胀（stochastic inflation）解释为开放量子系统的提议，通过构建长波长模式约化密度矩阵的开放有效场论（open effective field theory），揭示了该理论具有两条重整化群流动——传统的威尔逊通道和开放系统特有的随机通道，并系统分析了随机通道中的高斯与非高斯扩散、非局域威尔逊核、以及非马尔可夫泛函主方程，最后通过解析正规化（analytic regulator）初步实现了随机重整化（stochastic renormalization）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 进一步发展先前在 Phys. Rev. Lett. 136 071501 中提出的将随机暴胀视为开放量子系统的方案，澄清该开放有效场论所独有的重整化群结构，特别是随机通道的物理意义和数学形式。

Method: 采用硬截断方案（hard cutoff scheme）构建开放有效场论，通过匹配关联函数和形状因子（form factors）识别影响泛函（influence functional）中的高斯与非高斯扩散有效算符；利用时间上的区域法（method-of-region in time）处理匹配数据，并引入解析正规化代替硬截断以建立连续版本。

Result: 识别出高斯和非高斯扩散作为影响泛函中的有效算符，发现高斯阶以上的匹配数据不再是局域威尔逊系数而是非局域、非马尔可夫的威尔逊核（Wilson kernels）；推导出裸哈密顿密度及非局域泛函主方程，包括对角密度矩阵的福克-普朗克方程（Fokker-Planck equation）和维格纳泛函的克莱因-克雷默斯方程（Klein-Kramers equation）；以有质量标量场为例展示了随机重整化过程。

Conclusion: 开放有效场论框架能够系统地处理随机暴胀中的量子扩散效应，其随机通道的重整化结构不同于传统威尔逊有效场论，为理解暴胀时期的量子到经典过渡提供了更完善的理论工具。

Abstract: We further develop the proposal in Phys.\ Rev.\ Lett.\ \textbf{136} 071501 that interprets stochastic inflation as an open quantum system, by constructing the open effective field theory for the reduced density matrix of long wavelength modes. We clarify that this open effective field theory enjoys two renormalization group flows: the conventional Wilsonian channel, and a stochastic channel arising from the openness that has no counterpart in ordinary Wilsonian effective field theory. Focusing on the stochastic channel in the hard cutoff scheme, we identify both Gaussian and non-Gaussian diffusion as effective operators in the influence functional, and show that they are required by matching onto correlators and form factors of the perturbative full theory through a method-of-region in time. Beyond Gaussian order, the matching data are no longer local Wilson coefficients but nonlocal and non-Markovian Wilson kernels. We then obtain the bare Hamiltonian density of this open effective field theory and derive its nonlocal functional master equations, including the Fokker-Planck equation for the diagonal density matrix and the Klein-Kramers equation for the Wigner functional, with their zero-modess simplifications discussed. Finally, we take a first step toward a continuum version of this open effective field theory, replacing the hard cutoff by an analytic regulator in the stochastic channel, and demonstrate stochastic renormalization using a massive scalar as an example.

Method: 采用哈密顿量方法（Hamiltonian approach），通过显式构造孤子态来展开计算。孤子态被描述为压缩相干态（squeezed, coherent states）加上微扰修正，并引入适用于不可归一化动量本征态（non-normalizable momentum eigenstates）的内积。

Conclusion: 线性化孤子微扰理论（LSPT）为量子孤子计算提供了高效的新途径，能够处理态构造、质量修正及散射问题，并适用于畴壁孤子等更广泛的孤子类型。

Abstract: We give a pedagogical introduction to Linearized Soliton Perturbation Theory (LSPT), a new and efficient tool for calculations involving quantum solitons. It is a Hamiltonian approach with a focus on explicitly constructing the soliton states. These states are squeezed, coherent states plus perturbative corrections. We will describe multi-loop corrections to states and their masses. An inner product suitable for non-normalizable momentum eigenstates will be introduced and applied to kink-meson scattering. We will also discuss domain wall solitons.

### [156] [Entanglement viscosity to entropy density ratio for spin-3/2 theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22409)
*R. V. Khakimov,G. Yu. Prokhorov,O. V. Teryaev*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 针对Rarita-Schwinger-Adler（RSA）理论中的自旋-3/2场，计算其纠缠粘度；分别采用模哈密顿量展开法（modular Hamiltonian expansion method）和Zubarev密度算符两种方法计算熵密度。

Result: 在RSA理论中，自旋-3/2场的纠缠粘度为负值；模哈密顿量展开法得到的熵密度也为负，但粘熵比饱和KSS下限；Zubarev密度算符方法则得到正的熵密度。此外，RSA理论展现出共形场论的许多特征。

Conclusion: 自旋-3/2场的纠缠粘度为负的特殊行为表明，关于高自旋场中纠缠粘度普适性的理解需要进一步研究；不同熵密度计算方法的结果差异值得关注。

Abstract: It is known that the Minkowski vacuum appears as a thermal medium to an accelerated observer due to the renowned Unruh effect. More recently, it has been shown that at least for lower-spin fields this medium also exhibits a non-zero "entanglement" shear viscosity, which saturates the fundamental Kovtun-Son-Starinets (KSS) bound. We test the universality of this result for higher spins by computing the entanglement viscosity for spin-3/2 fields within the Rarita-Schwinger-Adler (RSA) theory. Strikingly, we obtain a negative viscosity. However, computing the entropy density using the modular Hamiltonian expansion method, we find it is also negative, and the viscosity to entropy ratio saturates the KSS bound. To clarify the origin of the negativity, we use another approach of Zubarev density operator, which gives positive entropy. We also show that RSA theory has many features of a conformal field theory.

### [157] [Shading A-polynomials via huge representations of $U_q(\mathfrak{su}_N)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22560)
*Dmitry Galakhov,Alexei Morozov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种基于Clebsh-Gordan（CG）弦（chords）形式论，将经典A-多项式（A-polynomials）从$SL(2,\mathbb{C})$推广到任意$SU(N)$李群，并借助双重缩放极限（double scaling limit）建立与量子A-多项式（quantum A-polynomials）的联系，同时给出了$\mathfrak{su}_3$下$3_1$、$4_1$和$5_1$三个纽结的显式例子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的A-多项式$A(\ell,m)$仅限于$SL(2,\mathbb{C})$群，而量子A-多项式$\hat A(\hat \ell,\hat m)$只能湮灭$SU(2)$下的琼斯多项式（Jones polynomials）。为了将这类重要的纽结不变量（knot invariants）推广到更高秩的$SU(N)$群以及更一般的表示（representations），需要一种系统的构造方案。

Method: 利用Clebsh-Gordan（CG）弦形式论，其中指标$a,b,c$取值范围为$1,\ldots,N-1$，该形式论可与二维WZW型共形场论（2d CFTs of WZW type）或量子群$U_q(\mathfrak{su}_N)$自然对应。通过双重缩放极限（$q=e^{\hbar}$，$\hbar\to 0$且表示权重分量$w_i\to\infty$使得$\hbar w_i\sim m_i$有限），将构造聚焦于经典A-多项式。

Result: 建立了与$SU(N)$李群关联的经典着色A-多项式（shaded A-polynomials）$A_a(\ell_b,m_c)$的构造框架。在$\mathfrak{su}_2$情形下，CG弦可与纽结接触同调（knot contact homology, KCH）框架中的Reeb弦（Reeb chords）对应。该形式论可自然推广到$\mathfrak{su}_N$及任意表示，从而将A(ugmentation)-多项式推广到一般情况。给出了$\mathfrak{g}=\mathfrak{su}_3$下$3_1$、$4_1$和$5_1$纽结的显式A-多项式例子。

Conclusion: CG弦形式论提供了一种将A-多项式从$SL(2,\mathbb{C})$推广到任意$SU(N)$李群的有效途径。该技术有望进一步推广到任意李（超）代数$\mathfrak{g}$，并可用于推导相应的量子A-多项式。

Abstract: Classical A-polynomials $A(\ell,m)$ define constraints on coordinates $\ell$ and $m$ in $SL(2,\mathbb{C})$ (a complexification of $SU(2)$) character varieties associated to knot complements $S^3\setminus K$. Quantum A-polynomials $\hat A(\hat \ell,\hat m)$ are difference operators annihilating Jones polynomials believed to represent wave functions of 3d Chern-Simons theory with gauge group $SU(2)$ on a toroidal pipe surrounding the knot $K$ strand -- a boundary of the knot complements $S^3\setminus K$. We suggest a construction of classical shaded A-polynomials $A_a(\ell_b,m_c)$ associated to Lie groups $SU(N)$. We exploit a formalism of Clebsh-Gordan (CG) chords, where indices $a$, $b$, $c$ run over $1,\ldots,N-1$. CG chords have a natural interpretation in terms of 2d CFTs of WZW type, or, alternatively, in terms of quantum group $U_q(\mathfrak{su}_N)$. In the case of $\mathfrak{su}_2$ CG chords could be associated to Reeb chords in a knot contact homology (KCH) framework. KCH suggests its own analogue of A-polynomials known as augmentation polynomials allowed to have extra spurious roots in principle. Yet the CG chord formalism could be easily extended to arbitrary $\mathfrak{su}_N$ allowing us to generalize the construction of A(ugmentation)-polynomials to arbitrary $\mathfrak{su}_N$ and arbitrary representation as well. Primarily we aim at classical A-polynomials by considering a double scaling limit when $q=e^{\hbar}$, $\hbar\to 0$ and the representations are huge, in particular, highest weight vector components $w_i\to \infty$ so that $\hbar w_i\sim m_i$ remain finite. Still we expect the presented techniques would be helpful in deriving quantum A-polynomials for arbitrary Lie (super)algebras $\mathfrak{g}$. Also we discuss explicit examples of A-polynomials for knots $3_1$, $4_1$ and $5_1$ for $\mathfrak{g}=\mathfrak{su}_3$.

### [158] [Ising surface defects can get dirty](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22628)
*António Antunes,Apratim Kaviraj,Baishali Roy*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究三维伊辛普适类（3d Ising universality class）中受边界和随机耦合影响的真实临界系统。通过在4-ε维度下考虑局域在二维表面上的随机磁场，利用复制方法（replica method）发现：无序下普通边界条件（ordinary boundary condition）保持稳定，同时存在一种可通过调节无序强度或局域温度达到的非平庸“脏”边界条件（dirty boundary condition），还探讨了缺陷谱（defect spectrum）的对数结构及其在复制形式论中的涌现机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实临界系统（如单轴铁磁体）必然受边界约束（boundary constraints）和随机耦合（random couplings）影响，理解无序与边界条件之间的相互作用是凝聚态物理中的核心问题。

Method: 采用威尔逊-费希尔不动点（Wilson-Fisher fixed point）在4-ε维度下的框架，引入局域在二维表面上的随机磁场；运用复制方法（replica method）处理无序场，分析边界条件的稳定性与相变行为。

Result: 普通边界条件在无序作用下稳定存在；发现了可通过调节无序强度或局域温度到达的非平庸“脏”边界条件；揭示了缺陷谱的对数结构（logarithmic structure）及其在复制形式论中的涌现机制。

Conclusion: 随机磁场可诱导出新的边界条件类型，扩展了对无序临界系统中边界行为（boundary behavior）的理解；复制方法能够有效捕捉缺陷谱中的对数结构，为研究类似无序界面问题提供了分析工具。

Abstract: Real critical systems, such as uniaxial ferromagnets in the 3d Ising universality class, are constrained by boundaries and subject to random couplings. We consider the Wilson-Fisher fixed point in $4-ε$ dimensions subject to a random magnetic field localized on a two-dimensional surface, which becomes co-dimension 1 in the physical $ε\to1$ limit. Using the replica method for the disordered field, we find that the ordinary boundary condition is stable under disorder but also discover a non-trivial ``dirty" boundary condition which can be reached by tuning the disorder strength or the local temperature. We also investigate the logarithmic structure of the defect spectrum and how it emerges via the replica formalism.

### [159] [Bottom-up open EFT for non-Abelian gauge theory with dynamical color environment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22822)
*Yoshihiko Abe,Kanji Nishii*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在Schwinger-Keldysh形式下为非阿贝尔规范理论构建了一种自下而上的开放有效场论（open effective field theory），通过保留慢速环境响应变量和引入动态颜色标架（color-frame）变量，实现了非局域非马尔可夫颜色响应的规范协变马尔可夫嵌入（Markov embedding），并自然重现了硬热圈（hard thermal loop）响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统开放有效场论需要完全积掉环境并处理非局域的影响泛函（influence functional），这给非阿贝尔规范理论中的非马尔可夫颜色响应和耗散效应描述带来困难。本文旨在发展一种局域化的系统-环境有效场论框架，以更简洁的方式捕捉颜色传输、记忆效应和涨落-耗散结构。

Method: 在Schwinger-Keldysh形式基础上，不彻底积掉环境，而是显式保留慢速环境响应变量，引入描述动态颜色标架的Stückelberg-like场及相关的颜色流（color-current）扇区，构建局域的系统-环境有效场论。随后通过带延迟边界条件（retarded boundary conditions）积掉保留的环境变量，还原出非局域耗散核（dissipative kernels）和随机源（stochastic sources）。

Result: 构建的框架实现了非局域非马尔可夫颜色响应的规范协变马尔可夫嵌入；硬热圈响应作为保留环境响应的一种特定实现自然出现；该框架提供了非阿贝尔等离子体中颜色传输、记忆效应和涨落-耗散结构的局域开放有效场论描述。

Conclusion: 本文为具有动力学环境的耗散Yang-Mills有效场论提供了一个系统的起点，可用于进一步研究非阿贝尔规范理论中的非平衡量子输运和介质效应。

Abstract: We develop a bottom-up open effective field theory (EFT) for non-Abelian gauge theories within the Schwinger--Keldysh formalism. Instead of integrating out the environment completely and starting from a nonlocal influence functional, we retain the slow environmental response variables explicitly and construct a local system-environment EFT. The environmental sector is described by a dynamical color-frame variable, Stückelberg-like field, and an associated color-current sector, which gives the nontrivial interactions and dissipation between the system and the environment. The resulting construction provides a gauge-covariant Markov embedding of nonlocal and non-Markovian color response. After integrating out the retained environmental variables with retarded boundary conditions, the reduced system theory acquires nonlocal dissipative kernels and stochastic sources. We show that the hard thermal loop response arises naturally as a particular realization of the retained environmental response. Our framework provides a local open-EFT description of color transport, memory effects, and fluctuation-dissipation structure in non-Abelian plasmas, and offers a systematic starting point for dissipative Yang--Mills EFTs with dynamical environments.

</details>

### [160] [DMFT analysis of Hopfield network with plasticity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22254)
*Yoshinori Hara,Yoshiyuki Kabashima*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文利用生成泛函形式（generating-functional formalism）推导了具有在线活动依赖突触可塑性的Hopfield型联想记忆网络（associative memory network）的动力学平均场理论（DMFT），发现适度可塑性通过延迟正反馈扩大吸引域并提高可检索记忆容量，但过强可塑性会导致虚假吸引子，从而产生最优可塑性强度的权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解神经状态与突触耦合在检索过程中协同演化的联想记忆网络的集体动力学行为，特别是活动依赖突触可塑性（activity-dependent synaptic plasticity）对记忆检索性能的影响。

Method: 采用生成泛函形式（generating-functional formalism）对大规模极限下存储大量随机模式的完全连接Hopfield网络（fully connected Hopfield-type network）进行严格推导，将多体动力学约化为一个有效的单点随机过程（single-site stochastic process），包含有色高斯串扰噪声（colored Gaussian crosstalk noise）和延迟反馈项（delayed feedback terms），并通过数值求解DMFT方程与直接模拟进行对比验证。

Result: 适当程度的可塑性通过产生正延迟反馈稳定检索以抵抗串扰噪声，扩大吸引域（basin of attraction）并提高最大可检索记忆负载（maximum retrievable memory load）；但过强可塑性导致网络将不完美的初始线索本身印记下来，产生虚假吸引子（spurious attractors）并降低检索性能。

Conclusion: 存在一个基于记忆稳定化与过早线索印记之间权衡的最优可塑性强度（optimal plasticity strength），该工作将联想记忆的DMFT描述推广至具有共演神经与突触动力学的网络。

Abstract: We study a fully connected Hopfield-type associative memory network with online activity-dependent synaptic plasticity, where neural states and synaptic couplings coevolve during retrieval. Using the generating-functional formalism, we derive a dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) in the large-system limit with extensively many stored random patterns, and show that the many-body dynamics reduces to an effective single-site stochastic process with colored Gaussian crosstalk noise and delayed feedback terms. Numerical solutions of the DMFT equations agree well with direct simulations. We find that moderate plasticity enlarges the basin of attraction and increases the maximum retrievable memory load by generating a positive delayed feedback that stabilizes retrieval against crosstalk noise. However, excessively strong plasticity causes the network to imprint the imperfect initial cue itself, leading to spurious attractors and degraded retrieval performance. Consequently, an optimal plasticity strength emerges from the trade-off between memory stabilization and premature cue imprinting. These results extend the DMFT description of associative memory to networks with coevolving neural and synaptic dynamics.

</details>


### [161] [Possible Topological Decoherence Transition in Relativistic Electron Beams Propagating through Coulomb-Disordered Media](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22316)
*Yury A. Budkov*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该论文通过重整化群分析证明，在库仑无序介质中，相对论电子束的互相干性由具有对数关联函数的有效二维紧致相位场控制，并存在一个临界样品厚度，在该厚度处会发生Berezinskii–Kosterlitz–Thouless相变，将代数退相干与指数退相干区域分开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解相对论电子束在库仑无序介质（如液体池或低温样品）中的相干性行为，特别是揭示其退相干机制与相变行为。

Method: 将电子束的互相干性映射为有效二维紧致相位场（compact phase field）的对数关联问题；通过高斯自由场作用量（Gaussian free-field action）描述其刚度与传播长度的反比关系；引入涡旋激发并将其相互作用视为二维库仑气体（two-dimensional Coulomb gas）；采用重整化群（renormalization-group）分析该气体系统的标度行为。

Result: 存在一个由基本微观参数表达的临界样品厚度 L_c，在此厚度下系统可能发生Berezinskii–Kosterlitz–Thouless (BKT) 相变：低于该厚度时对应代数退相干（algebraic decoherence）区域，高于该厚度时自由涡旋增殖导致相干性呈指数衰减。

Conclusion: 该临界厚度可通过透射电子显微镜（transmission electron microscopy）在液体池或低温样品中观测验证，为电子束相干性调控提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We show that the mutual coherence of a relativistic electron beam in a Coulomb-disordered medium is governed by an effective two-dimensional compact phase field with a logarithmic correlation function. The corresponding Gaussian free-field action exhibits a stiffness inversely proportional to the propagation length. When the compact nature of the phase is taken into account, the system supports vortex excitations that interact as a two-dimensional Coulomb gas. Renormalization-group analysis of this gas indicates the existence of a critical sample thickness $L_c$ at which a Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless (BKT) transition may occur, separating a regime of algebraic decoherence from one where free vortices proliferate and coherence is destroyed exponentially. The critical thickness is expressed through fundamental microscopic parameters and could be observed in transmission electron microscopy of liquid cells or cryogenic samples.

</details>


### [162] [Directed extended-range percolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22646)
*Wenbo Liu,Yiwen Zeng,Xueming Liu,Ginestra Bianconi*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文引入有向扩展范围渗流（Directed Extended-Range Percolation, DERP）模型，证明当连通性由长度 R≥2 的有向路径保障时，网络方向性通过阻止回溯（backtracking）能够显著降低渗流的复杂性。基于消息传递方法，作者在局部树状结构上精确确定了渗流阈值和反常临界指数，并在随机有向网络上发现临界行为对度关联（degree correlations）高度敏感，理论结果得到了蒙特卡洛模拟的验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准渗流（percolation）中，方向性被认为会增加组合复杂性；然而当连通性依赖长度 R≥2 的路径时，方向性对渗流复杂性的影响尚不清楚。本文旨在揭示在此条件下网络方向性反而能简化渗流行为，并引入 DERP 模型以回应量子通信等应用场景中对非互易边缘（non-reciprocal edges）有向长程连通性的需求。

Method: 提出有向扩展范围渗流（DERP）模型，在其框架中，消息传输可在由长度不超过 R 的有向路径连接的可信节点之间进行。采用消息传递方法（message-passing approach）在局部树状结构上精确推导渗流阈值与临界指数，并在随机有向网络上分析度关联对临界行为的影响，最后通过蒙特卡洛模拟（Monte Carlo simulation）验证理论预测。

Result: 在局部树状结构上，方向性使渗流阈值和反常临界指数能被精确确定。在随机有向网络上，DERP 的临界行为对度关联敏感依赖。蒙特卡洛模拟结果与理论分析一致，证实了方向性和关联对长程连通性的显著影响。

Conclusion: 当连通性由长度 R≥2 的有向路径保障时，方向性通过阻止回溯显著降低了渗流的复杂度；该结论以及关键临界参数可通过消息传递方法在树状结构上精确获得。实际有向网络中的度关联对临界行为具有重要调节作用，理论结果对量子通信等涉及长程有向连通性的应用具有参考价值。

Abstract: While for standard percolation directionality is known to increase the combinatorial complexity of percolation, here we show that when connectivity is ensured by paths of length $R\geq 2$, network directionality, impeding backtracking, can significantly reduce the complexity of percolation. To illustrate this finding, we introduce Directed Extended-Range Percolation (DERP), defined directed networks with non-reciprocal edges, motivated by applications in quantum communication. In this framework, message transmission is enabled between trusted nodes separated by a directed path of length at most $R$. Using a message-passing approach, we show that directionality enables an exact determination of the percolation threshold and the anomalous critical indices on locally tree-like structures. On random directed networks we find that the critical behavior of DERP depends sensitively on degree correlations. These analytical predictions are corroborated by extensive Monte Carlo simulations, highlighting the profound impact of directionality and correlations on long-range connectivity in complex networks.

</details>


### [163] [Spin Glass Mapping of the Parallel Minority Game](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22764)
*Aryan Tyagi,Soumyaditya Das,Soumyajyoti Biswas,Anirban Chakraborti*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文证明平行少数者博弈（parallel minority game, PMG）中的方差最小化问题等价于平均场极限下伊辛自旋玻璃（Ising spin glass）的基态寻找问题，即Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型，从而将PMG与自旋玻璃理论建立精确映射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平行少数者博弈中，在多选项且每位参与者仅限两个预定备选方案的条件下，最小化所有选项的人口方差是一个复杂的组合优化问题（combinatorial optimization problem），缺乏有效的理论分析工具。

Method: 将每个参与者的选择编码为自旋变量（spin variables），使得人口方差转化为一个包含淬火随机耦合（quenched random couplings）$J_{ij}$和随机场（random fields）$h_i$的二次哈密顿量（quadratic Hamiltonian），从而建立PMG与Sherrington-Kirkpatrick模型之间的精确等价关系。

Result: 方差最小化问题与平均场极限下伊辛自旋玻璃的基态（ground state）寻找问题完全等价，揭示了该系统内在的阻挫（frustration）特性。

Conclusion: 该映射将PMG与成熟的自旋玻璃理论（spin glass theory）联系起来，为理解随机策略中出现的冻结、次优构型（frozen, sub-optimal configurations）提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: The parallel minority game (PMG) extends the classical minority game to many choices, with each agent restricted to two predetermined alternatives. In this condition, minimizing the population variance across all choices is a complex combinatorial optimization problem. We show that this minimization is exactly equivalent to finding the ground state of an Ising spin glass in the mean-field limit, i.e., the Sherrington-Kirkpatrick model. By encoding the agent choices as spin variables, the variance becomes a quadratic Hamiltonian with quenched random couplings $J_{ij}$ and random fields $h_i$. This mapping reveals inherent frustration and connects the PMG to the well developed theory of spin glasses, providing a new perspective on the frozen, sub-optimal configurations observed in stochastic strategies.

</details>
