### [164] [Dropout Universality: Scaling Laws and Optimal Scheduling at the Edge-of-Chaos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21648)
*Lucas Fernandez Sarmiento*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文发展了一种将丢弃法（dropout）视为临界信号传播微扰的平均场理论，揭示了平滑激活函数与ReLU类激活函数属于不同的普适类（universality class），并由此导出了固定预算下的最优丢弃率调度策略，显著降低了测试损失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解丢弃法（dropout）对深度神经网络中信号传播的影响，特别是在临界初始化（critical initialization）条件下的动力学行为，并利用该理论指导实际训练中的调度策略。

Method: 发展了一种平均场理论（mean-field theory），将dropout视为对混沌边缘（edge of chaos）临界信号传播的微扰；推导了相关函数衰减的临界标度律（critical scaling laws）和交叉标度律（crossover scaling laws）；识别出平滑激活函数与ReLU类（kinked）激活函数属于不同的普适类（universality class），并给出普适的两参数标度塌缩（two-parameter scaling collapse）。

Result: 平滑激活与ReLU类激活具有不同的临界指数（critical exponents）；平滑激活的关联映射（correlation map）可做泰勒展开（Taylor expansion），而ReLU类激活存在带有普适非解析性（universal non-analyticity）的分支点（branch point）；由此导出的rank-flow tie-breaker选择前加载调度（front-loaded schedules），在无额外计算开销下显著降低了测试损失并附带精度提升。

Conclusion: 该理论框架不仅在MLP和Vision Transformer上验证了预测，还讨论了向CNN/ResNet的推广可能性，表明基于dropout临界动力学的理论分析能够有效指导实际训练策略设计。

Abstract: We develop a mean-field theory of dropout as a perturbation of critical signal propagation at the edge of chaos. Dropout shifts the perfect-alignment fixed point, making the depth scale for information propagation finite even at critical initialization. We derive critical and crossover scaling laws for correlation decay and establish that smooth activations and kinked, ReLU-like activations constitute distinct universality classes, with different critical exponents and a universal two-parameter scaling collapse in detuning and dropout strength. The distinction traces to the analytic structure of the correlation map: smooth activations admit a Taylor expansion near perfect alignment, while kinked activations develop a branch point with universal non-analyticity. As a corollary, the framework yields saturated dropout profiles under fixed budget; a rank-flow tie-breaker then selects front-loaded schedules, substantially reducing held-out test loss at no extra computational cost, with accuracy gains as a consistent secondary effect. We test the predictions in MLPs and Vision Transformers and discuss CNN/ResNet extensions.

</details>


### [165] [Beyond Scalar Objectives: Expert-Feedback-Driven Autonomous Experimentation for Scientific Discovery at the Nanoscale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21820)
*Ralph Bulanadi,Jefferey Baxter,Arpan Biswas,Hiroshi Funakubo,Dennis Meier,Jan Schultheiß,Rama Vasudevan,Yongtao Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为深度核成对学习（deep-kernel pairwise learning, DKPL）的方法，将人类专家知识与跨学科见解融入自主显微镜实验的主动学习循环中，通过成对比较替代传统标量目标函数，以解决贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization, BO）依赖预定义标量描述符而无法捕捉细微科学现象的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于贝叶斯优化（Bayesian optimization, BO）的自主实验框架依赖于预定义的标量描述符（scalar descriptors）来指导实验，但确定合适的标量描述符往往具有挑战性，且可能无法捕捉跨学科专家凭直觉所能识别的微妙但科学上重要的现象，这限制了自主实验室在复杂科学问题上的应用能力。

Method: 提出深度核成对学习（deep-kernel pairwise learning, DKPL），将人类专家知识与跨学科见解整合到主动学习循环中。专家直接评估哪一实验输出更优，DKPL从这些专家判断中学习一个潜在效用函数（latent utility function），进而指导后续的自主显微镜实验。

Result: 在使用已知真实值的实验模型数据集上，DKPL有效学习了具有物理意义的纳米尺度结构并优先选择高信息量测量区域。在铁电畴壁（ferroelectric domain walls）分析中，DKPL能够区分铋铁氧体中高、低特征畴壁角，并能发现铒锰矿中头对头（head-to-head）和尾对尾（tail-to-tail）两种畴壁特征。

Conclusion: DKPL建立了一种将专家知识整合到自主显微镜实验中的方法，展示了一条通往专家引导型自主实验室（expert-guided self-driving laboratories）的路径，能够解决超出标量度量驱动学习（scalar-metrics-driven learning）限制的科学问题。

Abstract: Self-driving laboratories or autonomous experimentation are emerging as transformative platforms for accelerating scientific discovery. Bayesian optimization (BO) is among the most widely used machine learning frameworks for these purposes, but these BO-based frameworks rely on predefined scalar descriptors to guide experimentation. In many situations, the determination of an appropriate scalar descriptor can be challenging, and may fail to capture subtle yet scientifically important phenomena apparent to experts with interdisciplinary insight. To overcome this limitation, here we develop deep-kernel pairwise learning (DKPL), an approach for autonomous microscopy experiments which incorporates human expertise and interdisciplinary scientific knowledge into an active learning loop. Instead of relying on explicit scalar objectives, DKPL enables experts to directly evaluate which experimental output is more promising using interdisciplinary knowledge. DKPL then learns a latent utility function from these expert judgements to guide subsequent autonomous microscopy experiments. We demonstrate DKPL's performance in learning physically meaningful nanoscale structures while effectively prioritizing high-information measurement regions using an experimental model dataset with known ground truth. We further apply DKPL to analyze the character of ferroelectric domain walls, where we find DKPL capable of distinguishing between high and low characteristic domain-wall angles in bismuth ferrite, and able to discover both head-to-head and tail-to-tail domain-wall character in erbium manganite. This development establishes an approach to integrate expert knowledge into autonomous microscopy experiments and demonstrates a pathway toward expert-guided self-driving laboratories capable of addressing scientific problems beyond the limits of scalar-metrics-driven learning.

</details>


### [166] [A Boundary-Layer Mechanism for One-Third Scaling in Online Softmax Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22341)
*Marcel Kühn,Yoon Thelge,Bernd Rosenow*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文在在线教师-学生（online teacher-student）模型中揭示，硬标签分类中使用平滑替代损失函数（如softmax交叉熵）会导致测试损失和泛化误差（generalization error）呈现幂律衰减，衰减指数为α⁻¹/³，远慢于贝叶斯最优的α⁻¹。通过调节学习率调度（learning-rate schedule），可将指数提升至α⁻¹/²。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硬标签分类通常使用平滑替代损失函数（如softmax交叉熵）进行训练，但平滑代理与离散标签之间的不匹配所带来的渐近影响尚不明确。本文旨在隔离并解析这一机制，解释其如何产生幂律学习曲线（power-law learning curves）。

Method: 采用在线教师-学生模型（online teacher-student model），在热力学极限（thermodynamic limit）下对中心化变量（centered variables）的动力学进行封闭分析：包括增长的中心化学生-教师对齐量D和残差学生方差Δ。利用固定学习率的在线梯度下降（online gradient descent）模拟噪声效应，并推导晚时间解的标度行为。

Result: 在晚时间阶段，远离教师决策边界的样本已被高置信度分类，仅宽度为O(D⁻¹)的边界层保持活跃。训练时间α的晚时间解给出测试损失和泛化误差ε_g均呈α⁻¹/³幂律衰减，远慢于贝叶斯最优的α⁻¹。引入学习率调度可将泛化误差改进至ε_g ∼ α⁻¹/²幂律。

Conclusion: 平滑代理与离散标签的不匹配是神经标度律（neural scaling laws）的一种渐近补充机制，而非对谱方法（spectral explanations）的替代。数据结构（如相关高斯输入和白化预训练特征）可以主导瞬态行为（transients），表明该机制在存在数据相关性时仍具有解释力。

Abstract: Hard-label classification is usually trained with smooth surrogate losses, most prominently softmax cross-entropy. We isolate an asymptotic mechanism by which this mismatch between smooth surrogate and discrete labels produces power-law learning curves in an online teacher-student model. After subtracting the mean logit, the thermodynamic-limit dynamics close in centered variables: a growing centered student-teacher alignment $D$ and the residual student variance $Δ$. At late times, examples away from teacher decision boundaries are already classified confidently and contribute exponentially little. Only boundary layers of width $O(D^{-1})$ remain active, while the noise of fixed-learning-rate online gradient descent maintains a nonzero $Δ$. As a function of the training time $α$ the late-time solution yields a $α^{-1/3}$ power law not only for the test loss but also for the generalization error $ε_g$, i.e., one minus test accuracy. This is much slower than the $α^{-1}$ Bayes-optimal reference for the same model. We further show that learning-rate schedules can improve the generalization error towards a $ε_g \sim α^{-1/2}$ power law. Simulations support the predicted order parameter dynamics and learning curves. Controlled experiments with correlated Gaussian inputs and whitened pretrained features show that data structure can dominate transients. Therefore, our result is an asymptotic, complementary mechanism rather than an alternative to spectral explanations of neural scaling laws.

</details>


### [167] [Posterior Collapse as Automatic Spectral Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22691)
*Johannes Hirn*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文揭示了β-VAE中的后验坍缩（posterior collapse）实质上是一种自动化的谱剪枝（spectral pruning）机制：潜在模式按贡献大小逐步解耦并坍缩，其阈值由超参数β控制；通过Landau稳定性分析，论文建立了有序参量并严格刻画了线性高斯情形下的坍缩谱与平均场行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解β-VAE中后验坍缩的底层机制，并将其形式化为一种受控的、有结构的谱剪枝过程，而非单纯的正则化副作用。

Method: 采用Landau稳定性分析（Landau stability analysis）从损失函数出发推导后验坍缩行为；定义了一个对潜在变量重新缩放（latent-rescaling）不变的序参量（order parameter），用于对活跃潜在模式排序并确定坍缩阈值。

Result: 在线性高斯情形下，坍缩谱（collapse spectrum）、效用谱（utility spectrum）与归一化PCA谱（normalized PCA spectrum）完全一致，且每次坍缩遵循平均场律（mean-field law）；在WorldClim数据集上验证了理论预测。

Conclusion: 后验坍缩可按潜在模式的有用性从低到高逐步发生，形成级联坍缩（cascade of collapses）；所提出的序参量与坍缩阈值可用于指导识别哪些有效变量应优先检查，为理解β-VAE的表示学习行为提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We show that posterior collapse in $β$-VAEs implements automatic spectral pruning. A latent mode collapses if its contribution to reconstruction is below the cutoff set by $β$. Equilibrium solutions with different $β$ thus reveal a cascade of collapses as latent modes decouple from least to most useful.
  We derive this as a consequence of the loss via a Landau stability analysis. We define a latent-rescaling-invariant order parameter that ranks active latent modes and whose collapse thresholds identify which effective variables to inspect first.
  In the linear Gaussian case, the collapse spectrum, utility spectrum, and normalized PCA spectrum coincide, and each collapse follows a mean-field law. We test these predictions on the WorldClim dataset.

</details>

### [168] [Fisher Information Velocity: A New Geometric Channel for Precision Glitch Identification in Gravitational-Wave Detectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21531)
*James Kennington,Zach Yarbrough*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出Fisher信息速度（Fisher information velocity）——一种基于黎曼几何（Riemannian geometry）的引力波探测器表征新方法，将功率谱密度（PSD）建模为流形上的点，通过外代数（exterior algebra）计算切空间散度（sinθ），从而将能量波动与频谱形变（spectral warp）数学解耦。在Advanced LIGO O4a数据的约40小时高采样率数据上验证，新方法相比标准BLRMS监测在74%的共检事件中显著性更高，将异常目录扩大了87%，并对天体物理信号具有稳健的免疫性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波探测器运行在本质非平稳（non-stationary）环境中，传统探测器表征框架（如形态学分类器或基于能量的投影，例如带限均方根BLRMS指标）会将全局振幅缩放与频谱物理重构混淆，难以有效区分仪器瞬变与天体物理信号。

Method: 将探测器的功率谱密度（PSD）建模为黎曼流形（Riemannian manifold）上的点，通过追踪噪声本底的运动学漂移（kinematic drift）并利用外代数（exterior algebra）计算切空间散度（sinθ），从数学上解耦简单能量激增与频谱形变（spectral warp）。该框架通过sgn-drift实时流处理管线对约40小时Advanced LIGO O4a高采样率数据进行了评估，获取了N=282,080个独立流形速度样本。

Result: 高分辨率相空间映射揭示了严重仪器非平稳性的双峰分类（bimodal taxonomy）：结构枢轴事件（structural pivots）占87.2%，各向同性激增事件（isotropic surges）占12.8%。在共检事件中，几何通道在74%的案例中显著高于标准BLRMS监测，中位敏感度比为Γ=1.65。两个通道检测到的主要是非重叠群体，总异常目录比单独使用BLRMS增加了87%。在10个已确认的GWTC-4.0事件和约5000次模拟注入上的系统验证表明，该方法对天体物理信号具有稳健的免疫性。

Conclusion: 该几何通道被确立为一种灵敏、互补且可安全用于否决（veto-safe）的诊断工具，适用于当前及下一代探测器网络，能够有效弥补传统能量型探测方法的盲区。

Abstract: Gravitational-wave detectors operate in inherently non-stationary environments, requiring robust detector characterization (DetChar) to distinguish instrumental transients from astrophysical signals. Traditional DetChar frameworks typically rely on morphological classifiers or energy-based projections, such as band-limited root-mean-square (BLRMS) metrics, which can conflate global amplitude scaling with physical reconfigurations of the spectrum. In this work, we introduce Fisher information velocity, a novel geometric channel that models the detector's power spectral density (PSD) as a point on a Riemannian manifold. By tracking the kinematic drift of the noise floor and utilizing exterior algebra to calculate tangent divergence ($\sin θ$), we mathematically decouple simple energy surges from spectral warps, or differential redistributions of power across frequency bands. Applying this framework via the sgn-drift streaming pipeline to ~40 hours of high-cadence Advanced LIGO O4a data, we evaluate N=282,080 independent manifold velocity samples. High-resolution phase space mapping reveals a bimodal taxonomy of severe instrumental non-stationarity, classifying events into structural pivots (87.2%) and isotropic surges (12.8%). Among co-detected events, the geometric channel achieves higher significance than standard BLRMS monitors in 74% of cases with a median sensitivity ratio of $Γ= 1.65$. The two channels detect largely non-overlapping populations, increasing the total anomaly catalog by 87% over BLRMS alone. Systematic validation on 10 confirmed GWTC-4.0 events and ~5,000 simulated injections demonstrates robust insensitivity to astrophysical signals, establishing this geometric channel as a sensitive, complementary, and veto-safe diagnostic for current and next-generation detector networks.

</details>

### [169] [Rheology and Programmable Gelation of DNA Origami Polymer Tadpoles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21741)
*Jennifer Harnett,Saminathan Ramakrishnan,Alice L. B. Pyne,Elizabeth P. Holmes,Davide Michieletto*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究设计了具有复杂拓扑结构的类DNA折纸（DNA origami）聚合物（线性、环形和"蝌蚪"形），并在致密条件下研究其流变学（rheology）与粘弹性（viscoelasticity）。结果表明，尽管拓扑不同，所有结构均遵循普适的流变标度律，但热退火后表现出显著差异，提示该类聚合物可用于构建具有拓扑依赖性可逆交联的热响应性复杂流体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DNA折纸虽能实现纳米尺度折叠结构，但产量低且多局限于单分子尺度研究；因此，本文旨在将DNA折纸原理拓展至宏观聚合物体系，探索拓扑结构对其在致密条件下的流变学与粘弹性行为的影响。

Method: 设计并纯化了三种拓扑不同的DNA纳米结构——线性、环形和"蝌蚪"形聚合物；通过流变学测量评估聚合物构型对缠结（entanglement）和流变行为的影响；进一步对块体样品进行热退火（thermal annealing）处理以观察行为变化。

Result: 所有拓扑结构均服从普适的流变标度律（universal rheological scalings），推测是由于聚合物长度较短所致；但在块体热退火后，不同拓扑结构的类DNA折纸聚合物表现出显著不同的行为。

Conclusion: 类DNA折纸聚合物可通过引入可逆且拓扑依赖的交联（topology-dependent crosslinking），用于设计具有热响应行为的复杂流体（complex fluids）。

Abstract: DNA origami is a powerful method to achieve nanoscale folded structures. Despite rapid improvements in folding and purification methods, DNA origami objects are still often produced in small quantities and studied at single molecule scale. Here, we design simple DNA origami-inspired polymers with complex topologies, and study their rheology and viscoelastic properties in dense conditions. First, we designed and purified topologically distinct DNA nanostructures, linear, circular, and "tadpole" polymers, to evaluate how polymer architecture influences entanglement and rheology. Despite their distinct topologies, we observe that all constructs obeyed universal rheological scalings, likely due to their short length. However, upon thermal annealing in the bulk, the DNA origami-like polymers displayed significantly different behaviours. Our results suggest that DNA origami-like polymers could be used to engineer thermoresponsive behaviours in complex fluids by introducing reversible and topology-dependent crosslinking.

### [170] [A diffuse-interface theory of active nematic interfaces: transport mechanisms and modal structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21826)
*Rodrigo C. V. Coelho,Mykola Tasinkevych,Margarida M. Telo da Gama*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文为活性向列相（active nematic）与各向同性流体（isotropic fluid）之间的平直界面建立了一个长波理论（long-wavelength theory）。通过将线性化动力学投影到少数界面自由度上，发现活性效应在扩散界面（diffuse-interface）区产生一个与 $q^2$ 成正比的局部贡献，该贡献与被动毛细松弛（$q^4$）竞争，构成了不同于经典Hele-Shaw输运的新型活性界面失稳机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解活性向列相与各向同性流体之间界面的线性稳定性（linear stability）机制，特别是活性效应如何在不依赖长程动量输运的情况下诱导界面失稳。

Method: 从耦合Brinkman屏蔽Stokes流体力学（Brinkman-screened Stokes hydrodynamics）的扩散界面Cahn–Hilliard–Landau–de Gennes描述出发，将线性化动力学投影到三个界面自由度上：守恒平移（高度）模、标量轮廓畸变（振幅）模以及指向矢旋转（transverse orientational mode）模；再消去有能隙的标量轮廓模，得到耦合高度模与横向取向模的约化界面算子。

Result: 活性效应在屏蔽扩散界面区（screened diffuse-interface regime）产生一个直接局部贡献，在高度模中正比于 $q^2$。该贡献与被动局部扩散毛细松弛（$q^4$ 阶）竞争，并定义了一个由扩散界面内部结构控制的局部活性界面通道。此机制不同于弱屏蔽Hele–Shaw/Saffman–Taylor型输运中由长程动量输运控制的 $|q|$ 和 $|q|q^2$ 项。

Conclusion: 该框架识别出一条通过扩散界面（diffuse-interface）途径实现活性界面失稳的机制，该机制可在均质活性向列相因流体动力学屏蔽（hydrodynamic screening）而保持线性稳定时运作，并为区分局部扩散界面失稳、体流驱动流体力学失稳以及混合区提供了基础。

Abstract: We develop a long-wavelength theory for the linear stability of a flat interface between an active nematic and an isotropic fluid. Starting from a diffuse-interface Cahn--Hilliard--Landau--de Gennes description coupled to Brinkman-screened Stokes hydrodynamics, we project the linearized dynamics onto a small set of interfacial degrees of freedom: the conserved translation, or height, mode; a scalar profile distortion or amplitude mode; and a transverse orientational mode associated with director rotations. Eliminating the gapped scalar profile mode gives a reduced interfacial operator coupling the conserved height mode to the transverse orientational mode. The main result is that activity generates, in the screened diffuse-interface regime, a direct local contribution proportional to $q^2$ in the height sector. This term competes with the passive local diffusive capillary relaxation, which enters at order $q^4$, and defines a local active interfacial channel controlled by the internal structure of the diffuse interface. This mechanism is distinct from the non-analytic $|q|$ and $|q|q^2$ terms characteristic of weakly screened Hele--Shaw/Saffman--Taylor-type transport, which are controlled by long-ranged momentum transport in the surrounding fluid. This framework identifies a diffuse-interface route to active interfacial instability that can operate while the homogeneous active nematic remains linearly stable because of hydrodynamic screening. It also provides a basis for distinguishing local diffuse-interface instabilities, bulk-flow-driven hydrodynamic instabilities, and mixed regimes in active nematic--isotropic interfaces.

</details>


### [171] [Defect Kinematics in 2D Nematics: Contributions from Surface Topology, Intrinsic and Extrinsic Geometry, Solitons, Defect Orientations, and Elastic Anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21855)
*Joseph Pollard,Richard G. Morris*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过几何场论（geometric field theory）刻画了向列相液晶中带电拓扑缺陷（topological defect）的类粒子运动学，指出其与电磁理论的关键区别在于缺乏规范不变性（gauge-invariance），并利用霍奇理论（Hodge theory）将缺陷相对取向与拓扑孤立子（topological soliton）统一为“调和”激发，进而展示了非零外曲率或弹性各向异性如何诱导超越两体相互作用的非阿贝尔式多体效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 向列相液晶中的拓扑缺陷运动学虽常与电磁学类比，但由于系统缺乏规范不变性（gauge-invariance），自由能极小化对约束条件更为敏感，因此需要建立一套更精确的理论框架来统一描述缺陷相对取向和拓扑孤立子（topological soliton）对运动学的影响。

Method: 采用几何场论（geometric field theory）构建电荷载体拓扑缺陷的类粒子运动学，与标准电磁理论进行对比；利用霍奇理论（Hodge theory）将缺陷间相互作用中的调和激发（harmonic excitation）加以形式化，并分析能量扰动（特别是引入Euler–Lagrange方程非线性的扰动）对缺陷相互作用的影响。

Result: 揭示了向列相中缺陷相互作用由依赖于全局拓扑或表面内蕴几何的传播子（propagator）主导；规范非不变性（gauge noninvariance）允许特定的能量扰动，这些扰动引入非线性Euler–Lagrange方程，导致缺陷相互作用超越两体形式，尽管底层U(1)对称性本质上是阿贝尔（abelian）的。这种多体效应在非零外曲率或弹性各向异性情况下得以显现。

Conclusion: 向列相液晶中的规范非不变性为多体相互作用的产生提供了独特机制，扩展了传统电磁类比所无法涵盖的物理现象，为深入理解复杂拓扑缺陷系统的集体运动提供了新的理论途径。

Abstract: We characterise the particlelike kinematics of charge-carrying topological defects in nematic media via a geometric field theory. This differs from the theory of electromagnetism, with which it is often compared, due to the absence of gauge-invariance. In both approaches, basic defect interactions are governed by a propagator, which depends upon the global topology and/or intrinsic geometry of the surface. For nematic materials, however, the minimisation of the free energy is sensitive to constraints that a gauge invariant theory would otherwise be indifferent to. Hodge theory is used to capture these as `harmonic' excitations, unifying two factors known to additionally affect the kinematics of defects in nematics: relative defect orientations and topological solitons. Perturbations to the form of the energy are also permitted in nematic materials due to gauge \emph{non}invariance. Those that introduce non-linearities in the corresponding Euler--Lagrange equations are shown to result in defect interactions that go beyond pairwise despite the otherwise abelian nature of the underlying U(1) symmetry. We show how this type of induced many-body effect manifests in the cases of non-zero extrinsic curvature and/or elastic anisotropy.

</details>


### [172] [Electrohydraulic Fields Generated by Active Transport at Tissue Interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22056)
*Amit Singh Vishen,Ahandeep Manna,Frank Jülicher*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个统一的电液耦合框架（electrohydraulic framework），将电场、渗透压和流体流动结合起来，解释了生物系统中离子输运如何产生大尺度电场和流体流动，并揭示了新的非线性效应和自发对称性破缺现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活细胞和组织能产生复杂的电场和流体流动模式，这些模式在生理学中具有重要作用，但缺乏一个统一的理论框架来理解电场、渗透压和流体流动之间的耦合关系。

Method: 发展了一个统一的电液耦合框架（electrohydraulic framework），将电场（electric fields）、渗透压（osmotic pressures）和流体流动（fluid flows）结合起来，考虑一个活跃的可渗透界面驱动周围本体中的电液场。通过该框架分析了空间异质性离子输运作为分布式电流源的行为。

Result: 空间异质性的离子输运可以产生长程电场、渗透梯度和流体流动；外部电场与内部偶极泵浦模式在物理上等价；诱导的偶极渗透压可通过本体渗透耦合驱动自推进；强场下非线性耦合可导致空心细胞球各向同性膨胀；离子输运与电场的反馈可驱动自发对称性破缺，产生偶极或多极场和模式。

Conclusion: 该工作强调了电液耦合（electrohydraulic coupling）在生物系统电流和场涌现中的重要性，为理解生理学中的电场和流体流动模式提供了统一的理论基础。

Abstract: Living cells and tissues can generate complex patterns of electric fields and fluid flows which can play important role in physiology. Both, fields and flows are rooted in ion transport across biological interfaces: cell membranes and epithelial cell layers. Here we develop a unified electrohydraulic framework that combines electric fields, osmotic pressures, and fluid flows, emphasising their couplings. We consider an active, permeable interface that drives electrohydraulic fields in the surrounding bulk. We show that spatially heterogeneous ion transport acts as a distributed current source, generating long-range electric fields, osmotic gradients, and fluid flows. Using this framework, we show that patterns of ion pumping at cell and tissue boundaries can simultaneously produce large-scale electric fields and fluid flows due to electrohydraulic coupling. A key insight is that an external electric field and an internal dipolar pumping pattern can be physically equivalent and can generate the same pattern of ion current and fluid flows. The induced dipolar osmotic pressure can drive self-propulsion through bulk osmotic coupling, with a mobility determined by interfacial permeability and system size, a mechanism distinct from classical electrophoresis or electro-osmosis. We further show that for strong fields a new effect emerges. Nonlinear coupling can lead to isotropic swelling of a hollow ball of cells. This can explain recent experiments on epithelial organoids. Finally, we show that feedback between ion transport and resulting electric fields can drive spontaneous symmetry breaking, generating dipolar or multipolar fields and patterns. Our work highlights the importance of electrohydraulic coupling in the emergence in currents and fields in the biological systems.

</details>


### [173] [The exact solution of the Koga-Widom-Indekeu model and related models of wetting in fluid mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22084)
*A. O. Parry,C. Rascón*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过复分析和代数曲线理论，精确求解了Koga-Widom-Indekeu（KWI）模型的三组分润湿问题，得到了表面张力和密度分布路径的精确解，证实了该模型中临界点润湿（critical point wetting）的缺失，并揭示了润湿行为受序参量分量的普适性（universality）和对称性（symmetry）原则控制：若序参量分量描述伊辛型（Ising-like）临界性，则临界点润湿存在；若存在局域XY对称性（local XY symmetry），则临界点润湿缺失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 澄清二元和三元混合物中临界点润湿存在与否的根本原因，解决此前数值研究和猜想中相互矛盾的结果，建立润湿转变与临界端点处普适性及对称性原则之间的关联。

Method: 采用复分析和代数曲线理论，对Koga-Widom-Indekeu（KWI）模型及其两个相关变体模型进行精确求解，推导表面张力和密度分布路径的解析表达式，并分析润湿转变的位置与级次。

Result: 精确解确定了表面相图中润湿转变的位置和级次，证实临界点润湿在该模型中缺失；微观密度分布可通过共形变换映射为满足Neumann三角形的宏观液滴形状；两个相关模型表明，若序参量分量具有Ising型临界性则临界点润湿存在，若存在局域XY对称性则缺失。

Conclusion: 润湿行为受序参量分量的普适类和对称性控制，这统一了此前关于临界点润湿的矛盾结论，并对更微观模型和实验中的润湿转变具有重要启示。

Abstract: We show how a broad class of two-component square-gradient models of wetting may be solved exactly for the surface tensions and density profile paths, and clarify how the presence or absence of critical point wetting, in binary and ternary mixtures, is related to universality and symmetry principles at critical end points. We begin by solving a model of fluid interfaces, first introduced by Koga and Widom, in ternary mixtures showing three phase coexistence. Numerical studies had revealed interesting wetting transitions, as well as curious geometrical properties of the profile paths in the density plane, and led these authors to conjecture expressions for the surface tensions. These conjectures were extended by Koga and Indekeu and predicted that partial wetting may persist up to the line of critical end points, i.e. critical point wetting was absent. Here, we obtain the exact density profiles and surface tensions for the Koga-Widom-Indekeu (KWI) model using complex analysis and drawing on the theory of algebraic curves. The exact solution determines the location and order of wetting transitions in the surface phase diagram, confirming that critical point wetting is absent. The model also displays the remarkable property that microscopic density profiles are mapped, by a conformal transform, onto the shape of a macroscopic drop near the contact line whose tensions satisfy the Neumann triangle. Two related models, which illustrate the role of the component isotropy, are also discussed. These models suggest that a universality principle governs wetting in fluid mixtures, resolving contradicting results from earlier studies: Critical point wetting is present if the order-parameter components of the mixture describe Ising-like criticality, but is absent if there is a local XY symmetry. Implications for wetting transitions in more microscopic models and in experiments are discussed.

</details>


### [174] [Self-organization and memory formation in two-dimensional jammed deformable matter under cyclic compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22398)
*Rahul Nayak,Satyavani Vemparala,Pinaki Chaudhuri*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究通过准静态压缩实验，发现可变形环状颗粒组装体在堵塞（jamming）之后发生屈曲（buckling），导致宏观机械软化；在循环压缩下，单分散体系趋向有序可逆路径，而多分散体系收敛至滞后极限环并编码训练历史的鲁棒记忆，且宏观滞后源于微观尺度上方向性不对称的非仿射变形（non-affine deformations）


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究可变形环状颗粒在堵塞后的力学响应及循环加载下的自组织和记忆形成机制，理解颗粒可变形性如何主导堵塞软物质（jammed soft matter）的集体行为

Method: 对单分散和多分散的可变形环状颗粒组装体施加准静态压缩（quasistatic compression），并在堵塞点之后进一步致密化，同时进行循环压缩实验，对比单分散与多分散体系的响应差异

Result: 堵塞后致密化导致环状颗粒屈曲并引起宏观力学软化；单分散体系在循环压缩下退火至接近可逆的有序路径，多分散体系则收敛至稳定的滞后极限环（limit cycles），且极限环编码的训练记忆在后续过度驱动（overdriving）下仍能保持；宏观滞后源于微观尺度上方向性不对称的非仿射变形，同时接触网络基本保持不变

Conclusion: 颗粒可变形性在堵塞软物质中起着调控集体自组织和记忆形成的关键作用；无序堆积中的宏观滞后由微观非仿射变形的不对称性驱动，而非接触网络的显著重构

Abstract: We study the athermal mechanical response of deformable ring assemblies to quasistatic compression. Beyond jamming, further densification induces buckling of rings, resulting in macroscopic mechanical softening. Under cyclic compression, monodisperse systems anneal toward a nearly reversible path passing through an ordered state, whereas polydisperse systems converge to stable, hysteretic limit cycles. These limit cycles encode a robust memory of the training history that is retained even under subsequent overdriving. We show that macroscopic hysteresis in the disordered packings originates from directionally asymmetric non-affine deformations at the microscale while keeping contact network largely intact. Our findings demonstrate how particle deformability governs collective self-organization and memory formation in jammed soft matter.

</details>


### [175] [Topological cell-openness index for porous materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22761)
*Michał Bogdan,Paweł Dłotko*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于贝蒂数（Betti numbers）估算多孔材料中开孔与闭孔比例的方法，定义了一个细胞开放指数τ，并探讨了其与气体比重法（gas pycnometry）的差异及与物理量的相关性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有孔隙类型表征的金标准——气体比重法仅能报告开孔体积比例，缺乏对孔隙拓扑结构的直接测量信息。本文旨在提出一种基于拓扑学（topology）方法的新指标，以提供互补或替代性的结构表征手段。

Method: 通过测量多孔结构的贝蒂数来估算开孔与闭孔的比例，并基于此定义细胞开放指数τ。此外，利用贝蒂曲线（Betti curves）估计多孔结构中的特征尺寸。

Result: 讨论了τ与气体比重法测量结果之间可能出现不匹配的结构类型，并说明这种不匹配可提供额外的结构信息。在数值生成的结构中，初步展示了τ与可测量物理量之间存在显著相关性。

Conclusion: 细胞开放指数τ可作为气体比重法的补充或替代指标，用于多孔材料的孔隙类型表征；贝蒂曲线还可用于估计特征尺寸，为进一步的结构-性能关系分析提供新的拓扑工具。

Abstract: We propose a method of estimating the proportion of open and closed cells in a porous material based on measuring Betti numbers on the structures. Based on this method, we define a cell-openness index τ which can be used instead of or complementary to the proportion of open-celled volume reported by gas pycnometry, which is the current gold standard for pore type characterization. We discuss in what types of structures mismatches between the two measures can occur and how such mismatches convey additional information about the structure. We also demonstrate initial examples of significant correlations between τ and measurable physical quantities in numerically generated structures. We also discuss how Betti curves can be used to estimate characteristic feature sizes in porous structures.

</details>


### [176] [Hollow Needle Puncture Mechanics for Biopsy Sampling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22790)
*Yiting Wu,Frederic Lechenault,Matteo Ciccotti,Mattia Bacca*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文基于脆性断裂力学（brittle fracture mechanics）并引入针-组织界面摩擦相互作用（frictional interactions），建立了一个简明的能量模型，描述空心钝针穿刺软组织的力学机制，解决了活检取样中芯样形成（coring）过程理解不足的问题。模型预测了五个关键量并通过实验验证，揭示了摩擦对力估计和穿刺模式的重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 活检取样依赖空心针穿刺软组织并扩展圆柱形裂纹，但控制这一芯样形成过程（coring process）的力学机制尚未被充分理解。该研究的动因正是填补这一认识空白。

Method: 基于脆性断裂力学（brittle fracture mechanics）构建了一个简单的基于能量的模型，并将其扩展以包含针-组织界面的摩擦相互作用（frictional interactions）。模型将穿刺描述为断裂能（fracture energy）与弹性能（elastic energy）之间的竞争，该能量平衡受针几何参数（半径与壁厚）、材料属性（韧性与弹性模量）及界面参数（粘附与摩擦）共同调控。

Result: 模型提供了芯样尺寸（core size）、无摩擦力（frictionless force）、摩擦力斜率（frictional force slope）、临界插入深度（critical insertion depth）和临界插入力（critical insertion force）五个关键量的半解析预测。实验验证表明，摩擦显著改善了力的估计精度，并改变了穿刺模式（puncture regime）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为组织芯样形成（tissue coring）和活检过程中的力产生机制提供了定量洞察，为针具设计、取样性能评估以及机器人辅助活检与针插入系统的实时控制奠定了预测基础。

Abstract: Biopsy sampling relies on hollow needles that puncture soft tissues by propagating and opening a cylindrical crack, yet the mechanics governing this coring process remain only partially understood. Motivated by this gap, we develop a simple, energy based model for puncture by blunt hollow needles, grounded in brittle fracture mechanics and extended to include frictional interactions at the needle tissue interface. The model describes puncture as the competition between the fracture energy and the elastic energy. This energetic balance is controlled by the interplay among needle geometry (radius and wall thickness), material properties (toughness and elastic modulus), and interfacial parameters (adhesion and friction). This model provides semi analytical predictions for five key quantities, core size, frictionless force, frictional force slope, critical insertion depth, and critical insertion force. Model predictions are validated against experiments, demonstrating that friction significantly improves force estimation and alters the puncture regime. These results offer quantitative insight into the mechanics of tissue coring and force generation during biopsy, providing a predictive foundation for needle design, sampling performance, and real time control in robotic biopsy and needle insertion systems.

</details>

### [177] [Refocusing spacetimes need not be strongly refocusing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21871)
*Friedrich Bauermeister*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 该论文证明了存在全局双曲时空（globally hyperbolic spacetime）是重聚焦（refocusing）但非强重聚焦（strongly refocusing）的，并进一步证明了满足某种勒让德重聚焦（Legendrian refocusing）条件的全局双曲时空可以配备强重聚焦度量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 回答Chernov、Kinlaw与Sadykov提出的公开问题：是否存在全局双曲时空是重聚焦（refocusing）但非强重聚焦（strongly refocusing）的。

Method: 通过构造与度量形变的方法，证明对于任一维数至少为3的全局双曲强重聚焦时空，均可构造出其上的全局双曲度量，使其变为重聚焦但非强重聚焦。同时引入勒让德重聚焦（Legendrian refocusing）这一新概念，并证明满足该条件的全局双曲时空允许强重聚焦度量。

Result: 成功构造出全局双曲重聚焦但非强重聚焦的时空，正面回答了Chernov–Kinlaw–Sadykov问题。此外，勒让德重聚焦的全局双曲时空均可配备全局双曲强重聚焦度量。

Conclusion: 重聚焦与强重聚焦这两种全局双曲时空性质之间存在严格层次关系，而新引入的勒让德重聚焦条件则为强重聚焦的存在性提供了充分条件。

Abstract: We prove that there are globally hyperbolic spacetimes $(X,g)$ which are refocusing but not strongly refocusing. In fact, every globally hyperbolic strongly refocusing spacetime of dimension at least $3$ admits globally hyperbolic metrics which are refocusing but not strongly refocusing. This answers a question by Chernov, Kinlaw, and Sadykov. We then prove that globally hyperbolic spacetimes which are Legendrian refocusing (a notion introduced in this paper) admit globally hyperbolic strongly refocusing metrics.

</details>


### [178] [Complex spinorial forms, Brinkmann four-manifolds, and self-dual bundle gerbes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22798)
*Alejandro Gil-García,C. S. Shahbazi*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文发展了一套与不可约复旋量（irreducible complex spinors）关联的复旋量形式（complex spinorial forms）的微分理论，适用于任意维度与符号差（signature）。该框架将不可约复旋量的约束平行性条件（constrained parallelicity conditions）重新表述为Kähler-Atiyah丛中指定半代数体（semi-algebraic body）上的外微分系统（exterior differential systems）。作为应用，本文改进了低维spin-c Killing旋量方程的结果，证明了Freedman规范超引力（gauged supergravity）中所有拟超对称解（quasi-supersymmetric solutions）属于一个显式的四参数测地完备（geodesically complete）的陀螺化Brinkmann波（gyratonic Brinkmann waves）族，并研究了六维最小超引力中的拟超对称解，同时证明了具有可积屏丛（integrable screen bundle）的斜挠率平行旋量（skew-torsion parallel spinor）的Lorentzian六维流形必然允许一个叶状结构（foliation），其叶片为局部共形Kähler复曲面（locally conformally Kähler complex surfaces）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发展不可约复旋量的复旋量形式的微分理论，以统一处理其约束平行性条件，并将该框架应用于超引力（supergravity）中的超对称（supersymmetry）条件分析，从而推广和精化现有结果。

Method: 通过将不可约复旋量的约束平行性条件重新表述为Kähler-Atiyah丛中半代数体上的等价外微分系统，建立了一套适用于任意维度与符号差的微分理论框架。

Result: 改进了低维spin-c Killing旋量方程的结果，放松了单连通性（simply connectedness）和完备性（completeness）的标准假设；证明了Freedman规范超引力中所有拟超对称解都属于一个显式的四参数测地完备、全局双曲（globally hyperbolic）的陀螺化Brinkmann波族，具有球面波前（spherical wave fronts）；证明了一个Lorentzian六维流形若具有可积屏丛的斜挠率平行旋量，则必然允许一个叶片为局部共形Kähler复曲面的叶状结构。

Conclusion: 本文所建立的复旋量形式微分理论为研究不可约复旋量的约束平行性条件提供了一个统一且强有力的框架，并在超引力和微分几何中获得了新的重要结构与分类结果。

Abstract: We develop the differential theory of complex spinorial forms associated with irreducible complex spinors across all dimensions and signatures. This framework enables the study of constrained parallelicity conditions for irreducible complex spinors by reformulating them as equivalent differential systems for exterior forms within a prescribed semi-algebraic body of the Kähler-Atiyah bundle. To illustrate this approach, we first apply it to the spin-c Killing spinor equation in low dimensions, refining existing results by relaxing standard assumptions of simply connectedness and completeness. Then, we proceed to apply our framework to supersymmetry conditions in supergravity, and we prove that every quasi-supersymmetric solution of Freedman's gauged supergravity belongs to an explicit four-parameter family of geodesically complete, globally hyperbolic gyratonic Brinkmann waves with spherical wave fronts. Finally, we study the quasi-supersymmetric solutions of six-dimensional minimal supergravity, defined by a system that couples a self-dual curving on a bundle gerbe to a Lorentzian metric with an irreducible chiral spinor parallel under a metric connection with totally skew-symmetric torsion given by the curvature of the aforementioned curving. Along the way, we prove that a Lorentzian six-manifold admits a skew-torsion parallel spinor with an integrable screen bundle only if it admits a foliation whose leaves are locally conformally Kähler complex surfaces.

</details>

### [179] [Two bodies left behind](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22805)
*Raúl A. Briceño,Caroline S. R. Costa,Hans-Werner Hammer,Daniel R. Phillips*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了高能探针作用下浅束缚态（shallow bound state）的准自由碎裂（quasi-free breakup）过程，涵盖两体与三体束缚态、局域流与强子散射四种场景，证明了碎裂振幅由重粒子传播子的近壳极点主导，并导出了封闭解析形式，从而在理论上严格论证了从准自由核敲出过程中提取中子形状因子（neutron form factors）及多中子相互作用（multi-neutron interactions）的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有实验在高能氘核碎裂中提取中子形状因子，以及在包含晕中子（halo neutrons）的核体系中研究中子-中子相互作用，但缺乏严格的场论依据来证明准自由运动学（quasi-free kinematics）下碎裂振幅的主导项形式及其与束缚态波函数的关系。本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 分别考虑局域流与强子散射作用于两体束缚态（重粒子+轻粒子）与三体束缚态（重粒子+两个轻粒子）四种场景，在准自由运动学下对振幅进行解析分析，证明其由重粒子传播子的近壳（on-shell）极点主导，并导出封闭表达式。对二体剩余子系统，证明振幅可分解为轻粒子散射振幅、与探针有关的动力学函数及与束缚态波函数相关的实函数的乘积。此外提供了互补的非相对论推导。

Result: 证明重粒子被敲出是准自由运动学下的主导效应，修正项被探针动量的负幂次压低。引入相对论振幅，该振幅对剩余子系统的幺正性（unitarity）严格满足。当剩余两个轻粒子时，主导振幅包含轻粒子间的散射振幅，从而为提取多中子相互作用提供了入口。

Conclusion: 本文从理论上为利用高能准自由敲出反应提取核子形状因子及多中子相互作用提供了严格的形式化证明。结果仅依赖于准自由敲出运动学，不依赖于特定粒子间动力学，因此可自然推广到有自旋的系统。

Abstract: We consider scenarios in which a shallow bound state undergoes breakup by a probe whose energy is high compared to the binding energy. The first two scenarios, which serve as warm-up exercises, involve a single heavy particle bound to a light particle, analogous to a core nucleus bound to a neutron. We show that in quasi-free kinematics, the leading effect comes from the heavy particle being knocked out by the probe, with corrections suppressed by inverse powers of the probe momentum. This formally justifies extracting neutron form factors from high-energy deuteron breakup in quasi-free kinematics. In Scenario 1, the probe is a local current; in Scenario 2, it is hadron scattering. In Scenarios 3 and 4 we consider, respectively, a local current and hadron scattering, but now on a three-body bound state of a heavy particle and two light particles. Hard knockout of the heavy particle leaves two low-energy particles behind, which can interact with one another. In all four scenarios, we prove that the amplitude is dominated by the nearby on-shell pole of the heavy-particle propagator and derive a closed-form expression for this contribution. When two bodies are left behind, the leading amplitude is the product of the scattering of the two light particles, a dynamical function depending on the probe, and a real function related to the bound-state wavefunction. Thus, quasi-free removal of a core nucleus from a system with halo neutrons provides access to on-shell data on multi-neutron interactions. The resulting amplitudes are relativistic and satisfy unitarity for the remnant subsystem exactly. We also provide complementary non-relativistic derivations. While the derivations are for spinless particles, the generalization to spin is straightforward, since the results depend only on quasi-free knockout kinematics; we make no assumptions about the inter-particle dynamics.

</details>

### [180] [The Restricted Schatten-class Grassmannian $\mathrm{Gr}_{\mathrm{res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ as affine coadjoint orbit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22512)
*Amin Tahiri,Alice Barbora Tumpach*

Main category: math.FA

TL;DR: 本文研究受限 p-Schatten 类格拉斯曼流形（restricted $p$-Schatten class Grassmannian）$\mathrm {Gr}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$，证明对于 $1\leq p\leq 2$，它是无限维受限酉群（restricted unitary group）$\operatorname{U}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ 的仿射（共）伴随轨道（affine (co-)adjoint orbit），且具有自然的弱辛结构（weak symplectic structure），其关键在于该酉群的李代数（Lie algebra）存在非平凡的 2-上循环（2-cocycle）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在揭示受限 p-Schatten 类格拉斯曼流形 $\mathrm {Gr}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ 在 $1\leq p\leq 2$ 条件下的几何与代数结构，特别是证明其作为无限维受限酉群 $\operatorname{U}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ 的仿射（共）伴随轨道以及弱辛结构的存在性。

Method: 通过分析无限维受限酉群 $\operatorname{U}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ 的李代数结构，利用该李代数上非平凡的 2-上循环（2-cocycle）构造弱辛形式，并建立格拉斯曼流形与群作用之间的伴随轨道对应关系。

Result: 证明了对于 $1\leq p\leq 2$，受限 p-Schatten 类格拉斯曼流形 $\mathrm {Gr}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ 是无限维受限酉群 $\operatorname{U}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ 的仿射（共）伴随轨道，并且该流形上存在自然的弱辛结构。

Conclusion: 该流形的上述几何性质源于受限 p-Schatten 类酉群 $\operatorname{U}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ 的李代数具有非平凡的 2-上循环，这一结果将受限格拉斯曼流形的经典辛几何推广到了 Schatten 类指标 $p$ 介于 1 和 2 之间的情形。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider the restricted $p$-Schatten class Grassmannian $\mathrm {Gr}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ consisting of infinite-dimensional and infinite codimensional subspaces $W$ of a polarized complex separable Hilbert space $\mathcal{H} = \mathcal{H}_+\oplus \mathcal{H}_-$ such that the orthogonal projection from $W$ onto $\mathcal{H}_+$ is Fredholm and the orthogonal projection from $W$ onto $\mathcal{H}_-$ is in the Schatten ideal $L_p$, $p\geq 1$. The aim of this paper is to show that, for $1\leq p\leq 2$, the restricted $p$-Schatten class Grassmannian $\mathrm {Gr}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ is an affine (co-)adjoint orbit of an infinite-dimensional restricted unitary group $\operatorname{U}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$, and that it admits natural weak symplectic structures. These results follow from the fact that the Lie algebra of the restricted $p$-Schatten class unitary group $\operatorname{U}_{{\rm res}, p}(\mathcal{H})$ admits a non-trivial $2$-cocycle.

</details>

### [181] [The Limitations of the Notion of `Observable' in Diffeomorphism-Invariant Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22260)
*Álvaro Mozota Frauca*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 本文区分了规范变换（gauge transformation）的局域与全域两种含义，论证了可观测性（observable）概念仅适用于局域规范变换，而微分同胚不变性（diffeomorphism invariance）仅在全球意义上可被理解为规范对称性，因此可观测性概念在广义相对论（general relativity）等微分同胚不变理论中仅能有限适用，并以此反驳了“物理内容由关联性（correlations）编码”等流行观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将规范理论中的“可观测性”概念应用于微分同胚不变理论（如广义相对论）时，在经典理论的诠释与量子版本的构建中都产生了大量概念性与技术性难题。本文旨在厘清这些难题的根源。

Method: 通过区分规范变换的局域（local）与全域（global）两种含义，分析可观测性概念各自适用的范围，并将该框架应用于微分同胚不变性的分析。

Result: 可观测性概念在局域规范变换下自然成立，但微分同胚不变性仅在全球意义上可被视为规范对称性，因此可观测性概念在此类理论中只能有限适用。基于这一结论，文献中“物理内容由关联性编码”等主张缺乏依据。

Conclusion: 微分同胚不变理论（如广义相对论）中的可观测性概念不能照搬规范理论中的对应概念，相关流行观点需要重新审视。

Abstract: The application of the notion of `observable' from gauge theory to diffeomorphism-invariant theories -- most relevantly to general relativity -- has led to numerous conceptual and technical issues when interpreting classical theories with this symmetry and building quantum versions of them. In this article I distinguish between two senses of gauge transformation: local and global, and I argue that the notion of observable appears more naturally in the local sense of gauge transformation. Then, I argue that diffeomorphism invariance can be understood as a gauge symmetry only from a global point of view, and hence, that the concept of observable applies only in a restricted manner. This has the consequence that some popular claims in the literature, such as the claim that the physical content of diffeomorphism-invariant models is encoded in correlations, are unfounded.

</details>

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [182] [Markov Renewal Theory for Transfer Operators and Point Processes on the Line](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.21638)
*Yoon Jun Chan,Markus Heydenreich,Sabine Jansen*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明：当一维平稳点过程（stationary point process）的间距序列满足马尔可夫条件、几何遍历性（geometric ergodicity）及指数矩条件时，该过程的配对关联函数（pair correlation）必然呈指数衰减。主要技术工具是带有指数收敛速率的马尔可夫更新定理（Markov renewal theorem），证明结合了经典再生技术（regeneration technique）与一般状态空间马尔可夫链的几何遍历性。应用实例包括硬核有限程对势能的吉布斯点过程（Gibbs point process）以及与自回归高斯过程相关的谐振子原子链。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 点过程的配对关联衰减速率决定了系统的短程有序性、相变行为及宏观物性，目前尚缺乏针对一维间距序列服从马尔可夫结构时指数衰减的一般性条件。本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 首先将点过程转化为平稳间距序列，并利用Palm分布（Palm distribution）描述其统计律。然后基于马尔可夫条件、几何遍历性和指数矩条件，借助经典再生技术与一般状态空间马尔可夫链的几何遍历性理论，推导出带有指数收敛速率的马尔可夫更新定理，最终证明配对关联的指数衰减。

Result: 在间距序列满足马尔可夫条件、几何遍历性及指数矩条件的前提下，一维平稳点过程的配对关联函数必然指数衰减。

Conclusion: 该理论结果成功应用于统计力学中的两类模型：硬核有限程对势的吉布斯点过程和谐振子原子链（与自回归高斯过程相关），验证了条件的普适性和实用性。

Abstract: We prove exponential decay of pair correlations for 1D stationary point processes when spacings satisfy a Markov condition, geometric ergodicity, and a condition on exponential moments. The conditions are phrased for stationary sequences of spacings (intervals between consecutive points) whose law comes from the Palm distribution of the point process. The key technical ingredient is a Markov renewal theorem with exponential convergence rate. The proofs combine classical regeneration techniques with the notion of geometric ergodicity for Markov chains with general state space. We apply the result to two models from statistical mechanics: (1) Gibbs point processes with a hard-core, finite-range pair potentials and (2) a harmonic chain of atoms, related to an autoregressive Gaussian process.

</details>


### [183] [Persistence of asymptotic variance under transport: from hyperfluctuation to stealthy hyperuniformity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22803)
*Luca Lotz,Michael A. Klatt*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文引入 $p$-均匀性（$p$-uniformity）来刻画 $\mathbb{R}^d$ 中空间随机系统密度涨落的标度行为，覆盖从超涨落到隐蔽超均匀性。核心定理给出了在输运下保持 $p$-均匀性的充分条件：输运距离的有限 $(d+p)$ 阶矩及相应控制条件。该结果解决了此前提出的开放问题，并推广到任意维度的 $p$-均匀源，且源与输运可以相关。作为应用，构造了各向同性且具有任意高 $p$ 的新点过程类，可在线性时间内模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在空间随机系统（spatial random systems）中，密度涨落的标度行为可以从超涨落（hyperfluctuation）一直延伸到隐蔽超均匀性（stealthy hyperuniformity），但缺乏统一的刻画框架。此前存在一个关于输运保持超均匀性的开放问题（open problem），本文旨在解决并推广该问题。

Method: 引入 $p$-均匀性（$p$-uniformity）概念统一刻画密度涨落的标度。核心方法是通过输运距离的有限 $(d+p)$-阶矩（finite $(d+p)$-th moment）实现输运的泰勒展开（Taylor expansion），并施加相应控制条件，从而证明在输运下 $p$-均匀性的保持。

Result: 建立了输运保持 $p$-均匀性的充分条件定理，解决了并推广了先前开放问题——适用于任意维度的 $p$-均匀源，且源与输运可依赖。利用该定理构造了各向同性（isotropic）且具有任意高 $p$ 的 $p$-均匀点过程（point processes）新类别，可在线性时间（linear time）内模拟。

Conclusion: 本文给出 $p$-均匀性在输运下的保持条件，并构造了可高效模拟的新点过程类。未来展望是对逆命题（converse statement）的探讨。

Abstract: We introduce $p$-uniformity to characterize the scaling of density fluctuations in spatial random systems in $\mathbb{R}^d$, ranging from hyperfluctuation to stealthy hyperuniformity. Our central theorem establishes sufficient conditions to preserve $p$-uniformity under transport. The first condition, a finite $(d+p)$-th moment of the transport distance, allows for a Taylor expansion of the transport. The second condition controls the corresponding terms. We thus solve a previously stated open problem; indeed we extend it, since our result applies to a general $p$-uniform source in any dimension, and the source and transport may be dependent. As an application, we construct new classes of point processes that are isotropic and $p$-uniform with arbitrarily high $p$, and that can be simulated in linear time. We conclude with an outlook on a converse statement.

</details>

# math.OC [[Back]](#toc)

### [184] [Characterization of Normalizer of Lie Superalgebra and its Application to Control Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22694)
*Aroonima Sahoo,Kishor Chandra Pati,Tofan Kumar Khuntia*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了以李超群（Lie supergroup）为构型空间、同时包含玻色和费米变量的动力系统的控制问题，利用左不变向量场的李超子代数正规化子对控制系统进行刻画，并提出了线性控制系统及其能控性判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 同时包含玻色子（bosonic）和费米子（fermionic）变量的动力系统在超对称理论（supersymmetry）中具有重要地位，但这类系统在控制理论中的研究尚不充分，因此本文旨在将控制问题扩展到李超群这一更一般的构型空间。

Method: 首先，利用左不变向量场（left-invariant vector fields）的李超子代数（Lie subsuperalgebra）在所有光滑向量场的李超代数（Lie superalgebra）中的正规化子（normalizer）来刻画控制系统。随后，对线性控制系统进行详细分析，并在此基础上提出能控性判据（controllability criterion）。

Result: 提出了适用于李超群上同时包含玻色和费米变量的线性控制系统的能控性判据，并通过具体示例加以说明。

Conclusion: 本文为超对称框架下包含玻色和费米变量的控制系统提供了系统的数学刻画方法，所提出的能控性判据为后续相关控制问题的研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: The dynamical systems having both bosonic and fermionic variables play an important role in the theory of supersymmetry. This article addresses the control problems including both bosonic and fermionic variables on Lie supergroup as the configuration space. Here, the control systems are characterized using the normalizer of Lie subsuperalgebra of left-invariant vector fields in the Lie superalgebra of all smooth vector fields of Lie supergroup. Then, the linear control system is studied in detail and its controllability criterion is proposed along with suitable examples.

</details>
